Chapter 1531: The System of the Great Celestial Venerable

The current Heavenly Dao of the Profound Yellow Realm had not yet been corrupted by the paradoxical reforms of the Law Enforcement method. Especially with its former overlord, the Immortal Realm, already in ruins. It could be said that at this present time node, the Heavenly Dao of the Profound Yellow Realm was at its most powerful.

Although it might not be able to perceive that Li Fan was from the future, its innate rejection of "outsiders" was still something it could sense. When Li Fan attempted to comprehend the Dao of the Profound Yellow Realm, it naturally felt resistance.

However, with Li Fan's cultivation level, it was not as if the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao could obstruct him simply by refusing. Even though Li Fan, currently, had been reduced to a state akin to a mortal by the scouring of the River of Time, he still possessed countless methods to properly "handle" the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao.

"Under the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao's rejection, cultivation is met with resistance at every turn, making efforts twice as hard with half the results. However, this is easily resolved. As the saying goes, if heaven does not give, I shall take!"

With his extensive experience in cultivating new methods, Li Fan, even in his mortal body, could force his way into comprehending the Heavenly Dao. Furthermore, at this time node, the Law Enforcement should have just begun its proselytizing, with only the Law Enforcement Immortal Venerable spreading its teachings. As long as he attained Longevity before the Law Enforcement Immortal Venerable, he could replace them, becoming another Law Enforcement Heavenly Venerable!

However, doing so also carried immense risks. Law Enforcement was the Heavenly Physician borrowing the Heavenly Demon's power, controlling the body of the Profound Yellow native, Xuanyuan Tuo. When the Ten Immortal Dao Sects investigated Law Enforcement's identity, the charade of being a Profound Yellow native bought Law Enforcement precious time to rise to power. But if Li Fan, a complete outsider, were to emerge as the "leader," he would likely face the most brutal suppression from a combined effort of the Ten Sects. Before Li Fan could recover his cultivation, he still harbored some apprehension towards the Ten Sects in their prime.

"Besides, the old path of the new methods also has many drawbacks. Even if perfected, it would merely allow one to act arrogantly within the Profound Yellow Realm. Once one transcends this world, their strength would be greatly diminished."

"Far inferior to my Myriad Forms Dao Net."

"It's a pity..." Li Fan sighed inwardly. Leaving aside the fact that the inspirations that formed the Dao Net had been lost and needed to be re-observed and re-established, the most crucial aspect was that the power of the core Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul had been washed away during the crisis of the convergence of Mountains and Seas.

"However, I might be able to use the power of True and False Illusion to manifest it again, without needing to re-initiate the sublimation of the Profound Yellow Realm into an Immortal Realm."

Thus, after a roundabout journey, the key point returned to comprehending the Profound Yellow Dao. Only by first creating the soil for the operation of the Transformation of True and False could Li Fan's various methods find their utility.

"Being rejected to this extent, even absorbing spiritual energy into the body is fraught with difficulties, no less easy than when I first began cultivating."

"However, traces of the Great Dao of Longevity still remain within me, perhaps I can use this as a starting point."

When Li Fan officially resumed his path of cultivation and felt the extremely strong rejection from the Profound Yellow Realm once more, although he was enraged, a sense of confusion arose within him. While it was an instinctive rejection of outsiders, to suppress Li Fan to such a degree...

"It's not entirely the work of the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao alone."

"It's as if someone else is manipulating and orchestrating it from behind."

Li Fan suddenly looked up again, a realization dawning upon him.

"Who could it be? Capable of commanding the consciousness of the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao at this time node..."

Several figures flashed through his mind instantaneously. Finally, his gaze stopped at a scene. It was from a past simulation, depicting Li Fan in the process of sublimating the Profound Yellow Realm into an Immortal Realm. At that time, even with the nourishment of the boundless life force of the Star Sea, it was insufficient to support the sublimation of the Profound Yellow Realm. Thus, Li Fan performed a ritual, invoking the illusory projections of the past Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerables left within the Profound Yellow Realm's heavenly spaces. Eight illusory figures stood tall in the heavens and earth. The furthest one was the Nameless Heavenly Venerable, whom Li Fan had personally facilitated. Before the Nameless Heavenly Venerable was Su Bai. And before Su Bai... was not King Profound Heaven. Between King Profound Heaven and Su Bai, there existed a mysterious Heavenly Venerable of unknown identity. One could only see their silhouette, their faces being a void. This Heavenly Venerable seemed to have appeared out of nowhere and disappeared just as mysteriously, leaving no trace other than the illusory projection imprint of a Heavenly Venerable. Li Fan had once tried to investigate, but even with his Half-Immortal means, he found nothing.

"It's likely this time node, before Su Bai attained enlightenment and succeeded the Heavenly Venerable, that he was in power..." Li Fan mused thoughtfully. "With the invasion of heavenly demons from beyond, instructing the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao to retaliate is also a duty of the Heavenly Venerable. However, this means that every time I forcefully pursue enlightenment, it will be extremely dangerous!" Li Fan's heart grew cold. Although not exposed for now, every act of seeking enlightenment could be seen as a conspicuous signal sent to the outside world. When his realm was low, it was manageable. But at the Nascent Soul or God Transformation stage, he would be as conspicuous as a light in the darkness, inevitably attracting the attention of that mysterious Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerable. Of course, it wasn't as if Li Fan would be doomed at that point. As long as he explained that he was from the future, tasked with the heavy responsibility of saving the mortal world of Mountains and Seas, given the extremely high moral standards required for holding the position of Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerable, Li Fan would most likely survive. However, Li Fan naturally did not wish to take such a risk. Entrusting his life and fortune to the moral integrity of others. It was far from the conduct of a gentleman.

"I never expected that a simple path of re-cultivation would be fraught with so many difficulties," Li Fan couldn't help but press his temples. "I wonder how other beings who traveled upstream resolved this matter."

After careful consideration for half a day, Li Fan finally settled on his temporary cultivation strategy. Since he could not actively comprehend the Dao of heaven and earth himself, he could only borrow the comprehension of others. It was also timely that the Crimson Cloud Prefecture was on the verge of upheaval, offering a perfect opportunity to experiment. Relying on the means of Illusion is True, Li Fan "borrowed" quite a few resources from the Crimson Cloud Prefecture's sect treasury. He then went to the artifact refining workshop and cajoled the formation master Wang Yi into laboriously crafting a hundred palm-sized thin plates for him.

"Brother Ping, what's the use of this item? It can't defend against attacks, nor can it be used for offense," Wang Yi asked, wiping the sweat from his brow, full of confusion. Li Fan did not answer the chatterbox formation master's question, merely smiling and using Illusion is True to distort the formation master's memories of him. "Hmm? Who are you? Why are you in my workshop!" "Get out! Don't disturb my research on the sect's grand formation!" Wang Yi rudely kicked Li Fan, a stranger, out. Crimson Cloud Prefecture had many alchemy cultivators, but artifact refiners and formation masters were extremely rare. Wang Yi's status within the sect was considered high, and he was accustomed to bossing around disciples like Li Fan who appeared to be newly admitted. Li Fan quietly withdrew, leaving behind a sore and weak Wang Yi, utterly perplexed.

Returning to his residence, Li Fan arranged the hundred thin plates in front of him. Holding spirit stones, he began to rework them. After half a day, these hundred originally bare plates had undergone a drastic transformation. In the center of each plate, engraved in a font resembling True Immortal script, were the four characters [Supreme Dao Scripture]. Surrounding the four immortal script characters were countless intricate patterns and depictions of strange beasts, filling the plates. And in the background, a scene of continuous mountains and seas could be vaguely glimpsed. However, this mountain and sea scene was extremely concealed, hidden within the complex and ornate patterns, making it difficult for ordinary individuals to detect.

After completing the carving of the hundred thin plates, all the spirit stones Li Fan possessed had been depleted. Li Fan himself was also on the verge of exhaustion, even feeling faint. Although it was partly due to the effort of forcefully creating these items in a mortal body, the primary reason was that these hundred [Supreme Dao Scriptures] represented the culmination of Li Fan's current formation attainment. Far surpassing countless generations, though they were mortal formations, they could rival immortal formations! Due to the loss of his enlightenment experiences, Li Fan's actual attainment in formations had been greatly reduced, his power diminished to less than one-tenth. However, his foundational array concepts remained. Thus, with the help of Wang Yi, the Crimson Cloud Prefecture's formation master, he crafted various basic formations. He then rewove and combined these formations, transforming the mundane into the extraordinary. Ultimately, he created these hundred [Supreme Dao Scriptures]. Though merely thin plates, they possessed infinite uses. Most importantly, they served as mediums, allowing real-time communication with Li Fan even across the High Wall and the Star Sea! The four characters [Supreme Dao Scripture], though perhaps exaggerated, were not entirely baseless. Any who obtained this scripture, if they felt confusion during their enlightenment and cultivation, could seek answers from the scripture. For every question asked, an answer would be given. With Li Fan's experience spanning multiple lifetimes, and having re-cultivated to True Immortal, having personally experienced the fusion of the three Daos—Mountains, Seas, Longevity, and Reversion—there was likely nothing in the entire primordial possibility that he could not answer, let alone the mere Profound Yellow Realm. In other words, obtaining the [Supreme Dao Scripture] was akin to having a peerless expert as a personal tutor. The extent of help this would provide in cultivation was self-evident. If not for Li Fan's current predicament, he would not have devised such a mutually beneficial plan.

After a short rest, Li Fan began to act. Of course, he did not distribute all the Supreme Dao Scriptures at once. Enlightenment was about quality, not quantity. "Brother, please wait!" Baili Shan, the chief disciple of Crimson Cloud Valley, heard the sound and turned back to look. He saw a cultivator guiding him to a secluded corner, then mysteriously taking out a thin plate. "Who are you?" Baili Shan looked at the person, who seemed somewhat familiar, likely a member of the sect. However, he couldn't recall his specific identity. Without further thought, Baili Shan was captivated by the thin plate in his hand. "This item is called the Supreme Dao Scripture, possessing infinite profoundness. Although I have obtained this treasure, I know I am not destined to fully benefit from it. Therefore, I offer it to you, Senior Brother..." Li Fan whispered. Baili Shan found it slightly amusing. Judging by the cultivator's aura, he was merely at the Qi Refining stage. Yet, he dared to boast of possessing a supreme treasure. However, the name Supreme Dao Scripture was indeed formidable. Carefully examining the thin plate, he became engrossed in the mysterious patterns upon it. When he came to his senses, the treasure-offering individual had already vanished. "His name was..." "What was it again?" Baili Shan frowned, realizing he couldn't recall.

Chapter 1532: The Burning Dao Furnace Burns the Dao

Soon, Baili Shan forgot about the treasure-offering individual, his attention deeply captivated by the thin plate in his hand. Although common sense told him that this item of unknown origin could not possibly be the true Supreme Dao Scripture, for some reason, Baili Shan's gaze was constantly drawn to it. He studied it for a long time but found nothing special about the plate, eventually giving up with a sigh, dismissing it as his own baseless fancy. It wasn't until three days later.

When Baili Shan returned from his master, still pondering his master's teachings, he unconsciously took out the plate called [Supreme Dao Scripture] again to fiddle with it. "The third layer of the Four Seasons Evergreen Scripture, the sentence [Heaven has four seasons, follow them for everlasting green, defy them for eternal life]—what does it mean? Isn't evergreen just eternal life..." As he was tormented by such questions, a mysterious green light quietly emanated from the plate in his hand, engulfing Baili Shan's thoughts.

When Baili Shan came to his senses, he found himself in a vast and boundless starry sky. Faintly, he could see the illusory form of continuous mountains and seas standing against the backdrop of the starry sky. Above him, countless mysterious characters floated, shining brilliantly like stars, or like the Great Dao descending, revealing its true form! Baili Shan's mind roared, and his thoughts were momentarily blank. "Supreme... Supreme Dao Scripture? It's actually real?"

Just as he stood there dumbfounded, a streak of light streaked across the myriad stars above him, entering his body. "Green represents the order of heaven and earth. Longevity means transcending heaven and earth. When heaven and earth have an end, longevity is boundless..." A majestic and sacred voice simultaneously echoed in Baili Shan's mind, resounding endlessly. Baili Shan was struck with enlightenment, overcome with joy. "So that's how it is!"

Just as the first user of the Supreme Dao Scripture finally established contact with Li Fan, its creator, Li Fan, successfully glimpsed the Dao of this time node through Baili Shan's mind. Although it was like observing flowers through a mirror or the moon reflected in water, Li Fan, who was already intimately familiar with flowers and moons, only needed a fixed entity for auxiliary anchoring. At this moment, with the veil covering the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao being lifted with the help of others, Li Fan followed suit, comprehending the reality Dao of this space-time to the greatest extent possible.

In the blink of an eye, Li Fan mastered all the Daoic scenes Baili Shan had glimpsed in his cultivation journey. By using the illusory Dao perceived by other cultivators to infer the true Dao in reality, this was Li Fan's ability as a former quasi-Transcendence expert. It was a natural progression; Li Fan's realm instantly completed a three-level jump from mortal, Qi Refining, and Foundation Establishment, synchronizing with Baili Shan's late-stage Foundation Establishment.

Li Fan's late-stage Foundation Establishment was incomparable to Baili Shan's. "Even against Nascent Soul cultivators, I can easily dispatch them. This can be considered barely enough self-preservation." Li Fan examined his physical condition and nodded slightly. "However, this so-called realm is not particularly important. What matters is the degree of comprehension of the Dao. Baili Shan is after all only a disciple of Crimson Cloud Valley, with limited vision. I still need to expeditiously disseminate more Supreme Dao Scriptures..."

Li Fan first checked the progress of his Transformation of True and False. The path of enlightenment Baili Shan glimpsed was like a drop in the bucket for the advancement of the Transformation of True and False. However, it proved the feasibility of Li Fan's plan. Through the path of enlightenment re-enacted by Baili Shan, it had not attracted the attention of the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao, nor the Heavenly Venerable lurking behind the scenes. "Next, I need to go to the gathering place of heroes from all under heaven..." Li Fan looked into the distance and departed gracefully.

A month later, the Great Dao Sect was faintly in sight. Along the way, Li Fan did not吝啬 the Supreme Dao Scriptures in his hand. He would proactively give them to any slightly talented individual he encountered. Meanwhile, his strength also increased from the Foundation Establishment stage to late-stage Golden Core. However, this seemed to be the limit for ordinary disciples outside the Ten Sects.

During this period, Li Fan encountered quite a number of cultivators. Those below Golden Core were commonplace, but those at Nascent Soul and above were extremely rare. Even if he occasionally encountered one, they were mostly elderly, not meeting Li Fan's requirements. "The ancient Profound Yellow Realm was considered a great era for cultivation. It shouldn't have such a desolate and talent-scarce scene. Could it be..." Recalling Elder Song's words from Crimson Cloud Valley about impending chaos, Li Fan speculated that perhaps at this very moment, the Ten Sects were initiating wars against other immortal cultivation worlds. The elite disciples of the Ten Sects had all been mobilized. "No wonder the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao's rejection is so intense." "I just don't know if they are currently fighting against the Heavenly Law Realm where Heavenly Physician is located."

After several tribulations, the history of the Profound Yellow Realm had long been shattered and distorted, as if hidden in mist. Even with the records on stone tablets, its original true appearance could not be restored. Only by returning to the past and experiencing it personally could one witness its original form. Li Fan's arrival at the Great Dao Sect this time was primarily to find Zhao Ruoxi within the Great Dao Sect. She who would ultimately achieve the Longevity Heavenly Venerable in the future, Zhao Ruoxi's talent could absolutely be considered top-tier in the Profound Yellow Realm. Although he was already intimately familiar with Zhao Ruoxi's memories, he could not determine the specific time node of her existence. "However, I didn't see any mention of external wars in his memories. Could it be that she hasn't been born yet?" Li Fan couldn't help but feel a sense of regret.

Chapter 1533: The Lost Battle of the Fallen Immortal

In the Profound Yellow Realm, Li Fan's main body, within the secret chamber of the Grand Tutor's mansion, had already exploded into a pool of flesh and blood due to the immense pressure.

The aura of longevity continuously flowed from the remaining corpse, attempting to repair the injuries. However, the turmoil that suddenly erupted in Li Fan's mind this time had already exceeded his capacity to bear. Even the Great Dao of Longevity he upheld seemed unable to save him.

"Revert All! Revert All! Revert All!" Seeing that it was futile and helpless, Li Fan could only cry out in his heart. But a familiar scene occurred again. Revert All seemed not to have heard him and did not respond at all.

Li Fan called out several more times, unwilling to give up. The result remained the same. In a state of shock and anger, looking at his body being gradually swallowed, Li Fan inevitably felt despair.

But, in a daze, Li Fan recalled the Heaven Emperor's words just now. "Such a person, even without any hope, will still struggle with all their might!" The panic gradually subsided, and Li Fan's eyes were filled only with unwavering determination. In an instant, he had found his path to survival. The Contra-Flow Boat!

Although the upper half of his body had become a pool of flesh and blood, Li Fan could still "feel" that the Contra-Flow Wooden Boat gifted by the Heaven Emperor still quietly existed within his "mind."

At this moment, as Li Fan's desire for contra-flow intensified, the Contra-Flow Boat began to emit a crystalline, warm white light. A wisp of green also seemed to accompany the white light.

The scene in the real world began to dissolve and distort, like a painting splashed with water. An almost unbearable pain also appeared in Li Fan's mind. It was as if billions of chains were simultaneously piercing his skull. Then, with high-speed rotation, these billions of chains churned within Li Fan's mind.

"Aaaaaah!" Even without a head, Li Fan's remaining flesh and blood began to convulse and tremble from this indescribable pain. Although the Heaven Emperor imparted all his insights into the Dao of Contra-Flow, he had never mentioned that the side effects of activating the Contra-Flow Boat were so terrifying.

Li Fan vaguely recalled that in his past simulations, he had also endured various painful torments, but none of them were even one-thousandth of what he was suffering now. The pain synchronized with his flesh and blood, divine soul, and will, and memories. It seemed to have spread to Li Fan's true core.

Faint sounds of wind and rain could be heard gradually from all around, and countless "water droplets" struck him head-on. Each drop was like the sharpest blade in the world, cutting Li Fan. Li Fan felt even more pain.

However, the invisible, immense power from his memories had already completely crushed his remaining body. With flesh and blood gone, Li Fan, who wanted to survive, had no retreat. Amidst boundless pain, he managed to maintain a sliver of clarity and continued to maintain the power of the Contra-Flow Boat from dissipating.

The sound of wind and rain grew louder. The water droplets hitting him were no longer isolated, but connected into lines. The Contra-Flow Boat let out loud rumbling sounds amidst constant collisions. It seemed on the verge of disintegration.

Fortunately, at the critical moment, the hidden green lights erupted, quickly repairing the damage to the boat. After enduring for nine breaths. The lines of water droplets finally converged into a river.

In an instant, Li Fan fell into it. All the pain he felt disappeared at this moment. He seemed to detach himself from the entire world. His perspective rose from the minor Great Xuan world and the Profound Yellow Realm. After a moment of stillness, it began to rewind.

Li Fan saw the scene of himself entering the sealed village below the Mountains and Seas Fishing Ground, saw the scene of himself suppressing and subduing the Profound Yellow Ruo Mu. He saw himself as the Grand Tutor, dominating the world. He saw himself regaining his memories and being forced to drink disgusting talisman water…

The river of time flowed turbidly, and the Contra-Flow Boat traveled upstream precariously. It seemed that with the slightest carelessness, it was in danger of capsizing. However, precisely because of his experiences in past years, these existences were like anchors, allowing Li Fan to "borrow strength" every time he traveled upstream for a period, stabilizing his figure in the river.

But when Li Fan returned to the anchor point of one year ago, and wanted to travel further upstream, things changed. The moment he passed this important temporal node, the scouring of the river of time instantly became thousands of times more violent. It was as if he had entered a more muddy and turbulent area from a clear, rushing river channel.

Li Fan could no longer see any scenes from the river of time. The surroundings were filled with swirling lines formed by the fusion of millions of colors, obscuring the perception of Li Fan, the upstream traveler. The terrifying power that suddenly erupted in the river almost directly destroyed the unprepared Contra-Flow Boat.

The white light on the boat was too weak compared to the surging river, even less than a single drop of water in the river. However, it desperately maintained the white light, preventing the boat from being crushed on the spot.

Li Fan knew the consequences of failing to travel upstream. It was not as simple as returning to reality. He would completely disappear from history, leaving no trace of his existence in the world. Li Fan desperately tried to reverse his fate. But a single person was too small compared to the vast river of time.

Even with the understanding of the Dao of Contra-Flow, being in the river at this moment, he could only obey fate. It seemed like a desperate situation. However, Li Fan still did not give up on surviving and continued to operate the Contra-Flow Boat, adhering to the Dao of Contra-Flow.

While struggling, Li Fan also had many unanswered questions in his heart. According to the Heaven Emperor's inheritance, the contra-flow journey should not have been so difficult. At the very least, when backtracking within a thousand years, even a damaged and almost disintegrating Contra-Flow Boat should have been able to handle the waves in the river.

But now, Li Fan had only traveled upstream for about fifty years, and the waves in the river had already reached a scale comparable to traveling ten thousand years back! Remembering the Heaven Emperor's experience, the further one traveled back in time, the greater the pressure would be, increasing exponentially. And now, Li Fan had just started, but he had encountered such great resistance... It was hard to imagine how great the waves would be when he traveled back ten thousand or thirty thousand years!

"How could this be!" Li Fan was extremely puzzled in his heart. Suddenly, he recalled the images of his own experiences that he had glimpsed in the river before. When these images were present, the river's behavior was within the normal range. But after the images disappeared, the river of waves surged, wanting to choose him and devour him!

"Perhaps, it's because I never truly experienced this period of time. Without the anchor as support, the resistance has increased a millionfold?" Li Fan's inspiration struck, and this thought arose in his heart.

However, even knowing the reason for the sudden surge of the river, Li Fan was now in a predicament. The river of time was murky, making it impossible to distinguish directions. The immense scouring force was constantly "cutting" Li Fan. It made it impossible for him to find a safe temporal node to "land."

Amidst the waves, the light of the Contra-Flow Boat grew dimmer and dimmer, seeming on the verge of collapse. It seemed like it would be destroyed in the next moment.

Just at this critical juncture, a boundless and infinite green light suddenly erupted out of nowhere. Like a wave-suppressing pearl, it temporarily suppressed the storm in the river. This green light seemed to originate from Li Fan's body, but in the endless river of time, countless dots of green light simultaneously flashed from ancient times to the present.

They were like beacons, illuminating the path forward for Li Fan. Although their effect seemed slightly inferior to his own anchor, they were undoubtedly Li Fan's lifelines. The Contra-Flow Boat followed the direction of the green light and moved forward.

One hundred years, three hundred years, five hundred years… Until one thousand years, five thousand years… Li Fan's green light was already beginning to be depleted. The green beacons in the river grew dim again, gradually disappearing into the surging history. However, Li Fan still could not find a safe landing point outside the illumination of the green light.

"If I were to forcibly leave the river of time and return to reality right now, there might be two outcomes."

"One is unfortunate death, being crushed into dust by the scouring of time, becoming a speck of dust in history."

"The second is to luckily succeed in landing…"

"Let's wait a bit longer."

Although Li Fan's experience in traveling upstream was mostly derived from the Heaven Emperor's inheritance, their encounters in the river of time were vastly different. Li Fan had endured more turbulent waves, but in contrast, he did not feel much of the erosion and stripping sensation of the river of time that the Heaven Emperor had so feared. Keep in mind that the Heaven Emperor's first attempt at traveling upstream, which lasted only three thousand years, made him feel like he was about to completely dissolve into the river of time and had to return to reality.

But now, Li Fan's first attempt had already traced back several thousand years. Moreover, Li Fan did not feel much pressure from this so-called stripping. If it weren't for the protection and guidance of the Great Dao of Longevity, and the waves in the river being too fierce, making it difficult to navigate upstream. Li Fan even felt that he could continue to backtrack like this.

Although the pressure of erosion was small, the further back in time Li Fan went, the greater the pressure he endured. When time was traced back to about eight thousand years ago, the waves in the river of time had completely lost the conditions for navigation. Li Fan was swept into it, unable to even discern the direction of time.

He carefully observed every detail in the river of time, striving to find a glimmer of hope at the last moment. However, he was ultimately not a lucky person.

Bang! The Contra-Flow Boat began to disintegrate. Without the protection of the treasure boat, Li Fan, directly exposed to the river of time, faced pressures that were thousands of times greater. Li Fan finally understood what the Heaven Emperor meant by the sensation of melting.

With each scouring of the river, Li Fan lost a part of himself. Cultivation, divine abilities, enlightenment experiences... These were like external objects, gradually shedding away with the scouring of the river. Only the core within continued to struggle.

When the true core was damaged, Li Fan instinctively felt an extreme fatal threat. He knew he couldn't delay any longer. Even crashing "land" prematurely was better than dying in the river of time.

Manipulating the dilapidated Contra-Flow Boat, Li Fan gradually broke free from the insights of the Dao of Contra-Flow. The scene of the river of time slowly receded from his vision. Instead, it was replaced by a torrential downpour.

In an instant, Li Fan almost lost his direction. In the transitional zone between the river of time and reality, he was caught in a dilemma of advancing or retreating. Advancing rashly might lead him to plunge back into the river of time. Staying here, still within the range of the river of time's scouring, with the core continuously being eroded, was also a dead end.

Just as Li Fan was hesitating, he suddenly saw a familiar ray of light amidst the pouring rain before him. This perhaps represented that in the time node eight thousand years later, he had once had contact with this ray of light. Although it did not exist in the past timeline, through this contact, a cross-temporal anchor point was formed.

Li Fan knew how difficult it was to find something related to himself amidst the pouring rain eight thousand years ago. Seizing the opportunity, Li Fan did not hesitate. He immediately controlled the dilapidated Contra-Flow Boat and flew towards the fleeting ray of light.

With the anchor point as his guide, before the Contra-Flow Boat completely disintegrated, Li Fan finally traversed the wind and rain of the river of time. And arrived in the real world. The Profound Yellow Realm. 8,643 years before the initial anchor point!

"That beam of light... is it from the Medicine King Sect?! How dare they run away?"

"Quick, go inform the Elder!"

"Wait! Although the Medicine King Sect is not a large sect, its assets are quite substantial. They wouldn't possibly pack all their treasures when fleeing in such a hurry..."

"Let's go. Don't let others get there first!"

"Wait, what is that? Is it another beam of light?"

"Could it be that the Medicine King Sect had a disagreement and decided not to run anymore?"

"Let's go and see!"

When Li Fan woke up from his coma, he was already surrounded.

"Hmm?" In a daze, Li Fan had not yet fully recovered. He only noticed the cultivators around him, while counting their spoils, occasionally glancing at him.

"You're finally awake, kid."

"Quickly tell us what happened to the Medicine King Sect. Confess honestly, and we might spare your life. Otherwise..."

"Stop talking nonsense with him, just search his soul directly!"

"You idiot, these two beams of light are so conspicuous. We can't hide them. How will we explain to the Elder when he asks!"

These people were whispering among themselves, completely ignoring Li Fan, who was tightly bound. Li Fan ignored them for now and first checked his current condition. Although his body had almost completely disappeared in the river of time, as soon as he returned to reality, the Great Dao of Longevity within him re-evolved into a new body.

However, to Li Fan's regret, after this voyage, the Great Dao of Longevity seemed to have suffered great damage. And this damage seemed irreversible. At least, for now, it could not be restored.

"After all, it's not truly mine, but a gift from Shou Qiu Gong," Li Fan said with a self-deprecating smile.

"Hmm?"

"Shou Qiu Gong?" A moment later, Li Fan reacted. He had traveled eight thousand years upstream in the river of time. Although his cultivation and divine abilities, as well as the Great Dao of Longevity, had been completely scoured and tempered, in return, his lost memories had all been recovered. The events of these two lives played out one after another before Li Fan, causing him to sigh softly.

"Due to a momentary greed, it led to infinite variables."

"The consequences of the fusion of the three Daos—Mountains and Seas, Longevity, and Revert All—were indeed beyond my current capacity to bear."

"Fortunately, my luck is not bad. Even when I lost my memories, I found great opportunities."

"The Dao of Contra-Flow..." Li Fan lowered his head, recalling everything he had experienced in the river of time, a peculiar light appearing in his eyes.

"Revert All." After thinking, Li Fan first called out in his heart. The repeated failure of Revert All caused Li Fan a sense of extreme unease. There was still no response. However, after careful sensing, Li Fan finally confirmed that Revert All was still within him. It was just that for some reason, it seemed to be in a dormant state.

Chapter 1534: Spacetime Anchor Point

Even a minuscule ripple from the River of Time held more destructive power than any heavenly tribulation in the mortal world. The Profound Yellow Realm remained tranquil, yet in Li Fan's perception, space was being forcibly folded by an external, immense force. The clearly demarcated boundaries seemed like incredibly sharp blades, slicing at Li Fan's body and soul. Even though this wasn't his first encounter with the waves from the River of Time, Li Fan's expression still shifted slightly.

In this moment of crisis, Li Fan made the most correct choice. He utilized his comprehension of the Transformation of True and False to simulate the protection of [Illusion is True]. Fortunately, his recently recovered Harmonious Dao cultivation had allowed his comprehension of the Transformation of True and False to advance a small step, thus increasing the efficiency of Illusion is True slightly.

It was akin to putting on a straw raincoat amidst a storm; Li Fan could at least move and discern directions. The ripples in the River of Time persisted, as if waiting for the storm of Li Fan's induced changes to subside. Under the baptism of the wind and waves, Li Fan was like a butterfly in a tempest, constantly at risk of being torn apart.

In a flash, Li Fan thought of a way to save himself. He recalled how he had traveled upstream in the River of Time, the perilous journey where he almost got lost, and how he had eventually discovered a familiar point of light representing the Medicine King Cauldron, which allowed him to land safely.

"Even after arriving at this time node, I am still like duckweed in the wind, without roots. To survive in the ripples of time, I urgently need to find my [Anchor Points] in this era and fully integrate into them. It's like being in a rushing river, needing to grab onto a reef to survive..."

The spatial folds grew increasingly dense, and Li Fan was almost at a standstill. There was no more time to waste.

Almost instantly, Li Fan found the most stable anchor point in this time node that he could utilize. "Originally, if that Lei Fanzhi hadn't acted, the Great Dao Sect would have been the best choice. Unfortunately, the identity I was playing is already dead."

A realization surged within Li Fan. Pushing his 遁法 to its limits, he sped back towards Evergreen Valley. The speed of Harmonious Dao was a hundred times faster than in the Golden Core stage. A month's journey was completed in an instant.

Above Evergreen Valley, after briefly sensing Elder Song's location, Li Fan suppressed his aura and quietly descended.

"Elder Song, it's me!" Blocking Elder Song's path, Li Fan, while resisting the ripples of time, tried to maintain a calm demeanor and said, "You are..."

Elder Song narrowed his eyes, scrutinizing Li Fan before looking confused. Due to the prior effect of Illusion is True, he had not recognized Li Fan. The anchor point failed, and the temporal ripples showed no signs of abating. The increasingly dense lines filled the entire world. Li Fan felt that he would be completely submerged by the River of Time in the very next second.

In this critical moment, Li Fan had a flash of inspiration and retrieved the magical artifact Elder Song had previously bestowed upon him. It was fortunate that his frugal habit of not discarding the artifact just because it seemed useless, and keeping it on his person, proved to be a crucial lifeline.

Elder Song, though he didn't recognize Li Fan, recognized the artifact he had crafted, recalling Li Fan's identity. "Oh, it's you." With his words, Li Fan's identity was finally confirmed. In an instant, he fell from the River of Time back into real space. The ripples in the River of Time gradually dissipated. Even with some aftershocks remaining, Li Fan could now handle them himself.

Having narrowly escaped death, Li Fan coughed lightly and quickly stepped forward, "Yesterday, during a fight, this magical artifact saved my life at a critical moment. That's why I've come to thank you, Elder Song..."

As Li Fan spoke, he subtly created a crack on the artifact. Simultaneously, he compressed and condensed the surrounding spiritual energy into a top-grade spirit stone and offered it to him. The Harmonious Dao of a former True Immortal acting was naturally beyond the perception of Evergreen Valley's Elder Song. He looked at the glittering spirit stone, which clearly was no ordinary item, presented before him and smiled slightly, "You are indeed thoughtful." He accepted the spirit stone.

The relationship between the two became closer, and Li Fan sensed that the temporal ripples outside of reality had lessened further. The crisis was temporarily averted, and Li Fan breathed a sigh of relief.

"You don't need to be so nervous. We have very few disciples like you in Evergreen Valley who are filial and sensible. It's rare," Elder Song said with a kindly smile, looking at the significant emotional change in Li Fan, and he genuinely lamented. "Since that magical artifact is damaged, I will bestow another upon you. However, you must not rely on superior tools to seek conflict. These are troubled times; steady cultivation is the right path."

Elder Song said solemnly, taking out another artifact from his storage ring. Or rather, a treasure. Its quality was clearly a notch above the one bestowed upon Li Fan, a simple, ancient, dark-golden bronze bell. Elder Song looked at the bell with a hint of reminiscence in his eyes. "This bell accompanied me for a long time. However, due to the limitations of its crafting materials, it is of little help to me now. Today, I shall bestow it upon you." "It can withstand attacks below the Nascent Soul stage. There should be no problem."

Li Fan was overjoyed and quickly accepted the bronze bell. While thanking Elder Song, he had already refined the bell in an instant. What Li Fan desired was naturally not the bronze bell's efficacy as a magical treasure, but the time it contained. Associated with Elder Song's entire life, and now refined, this connection was now linked to Li Fan.

The storm in the River of Time completely subsided. Li Fan had safely resolved the first backlash from altering history. "Elder Song's kindness today, I shall repay it greatly in the future!" Li Fan said solemnly. Elder Song waved his hand, "It's good to have this intention." With that, he slowly departed.

Li Fan watched him leave, then found a courtyard in Evergreen Valley to temporarily settle down. First, he re-refined the dark-golden bronze bell. For Li Fan, the flaws in the natural materials were not a limitation. With the inscription of complex formations, even mundane objects could rival immortal artifacts.

While helping the bronze bell complete its transformation, Li Fan reflected on his slightly reckless actions earlier. "Looking back, it is most detrimental for those who travel upstream against the current to be like rootless trees and un-sourced water." "It's not that changing history is impossible. After all, the River of Time is vast and boundless, containing infinite possibilities." "But rather, while changing things, one must possess the ability to withstand the backlash of the River of Time's course change." "Besides one's own strength, the most crucial element is the anchor. Simply put, it is the connection with other people, events, and objects within the space-time."

"Tai Tian Di's inheritance, given to me before, uniquely lacked this critical aspect..." Li Fan pondered for a long time, excluding the possibility of Tai Tian Di intentionally harming him. "Tai Tian Di traveled upstream for at most tens of thousands of years. He was once an Immortal Emperor of the Immortal Realm. Countless True Immortals in the Immortal Realm could be considered his anchors. Naturally, he didn't need to worry about the storms caused by the River of Time's course change." "King Profound Heaven is the same. The myriad beings under the rule of the Profound Heaven Sect, and possibly several Law Kings who were reincarnations of Nameless True Immortals." "As for me, whether it was ten thousand years later, or now, I have always been alone..." "It is only natural for the storms of the River of Time to be so fierce."

Li Fan's thoughts raced, and after sorting them out, he couldn't help but let out a long sigh. He hadn't fallen into self-pity due to his absolute loneliness. Since there were no anchors, he would create them. "First, I will stabilize my existence within this time node. Then, I will consider other matters." Li Fan made up his mind.

The next day.

"The Senior Brother's might is divine!" "Looking at Senior Brother's prowess, he must be close to breaking through to the Nascent Soul stage! Truly the fortune of our Evergreen Valley!" "Hmph, perhaps Evergreen Valley is too small to contain such a great deity." "What nonsense are you spouting? How could Baili Shan be such a disloyal person!"

... In the sky, Baili Shan displayed immense power, repelling a group of wicked cultivators who coveted the Medicine King Sect's treasures. Below, the disciples of Evergreen Valley were discussing amongst themselves. Baili Shan seemed to pay no mind to the opinions of others, gracefully leading his fellow disciples back to report. He also solemnly declared to their master, Zou Yunhao, the Sect Leader of Evergreen Valley.

"Master, please rest assured. Once a master, always a father. Evergreen Valley is also my eternal home. Even if I advance to Nascent Soul, God Transformation, or even Harmonious Dao in the future, I will never leave Evergreen Valley." Baili Shan said with unwavering resolve.

Zou Yunhao stroked his beard and nodded with great satisfaction. Then, he said with a hint of disappointment, "Actually, with your talent, Baili, if you could go to the Ten Immortal Dao Sects, you would have a much brighter future. Perhaps you could even compete for supremacy in the world. Staying in our Evergreen Valley..."

Baili Shan said proudly, "Master, please don't worry. Even if I stay in Evergreen Valley my entire life, I will not be weaker than those so-called prodigies of the Ten Sects!"

Zou Yunhao sighed and said no more. He merely thought that Baili Shan, being young and arrogant, lacked the experience of the Ten Sects' true strength. Recalling Baili Shan's nervous yet observant demeanor when he first adopted him, Zou Yunhao thought to himself, "It's rare for Evergreen Valley to have such a rising star. We can't truly hinder his future. Perhaps going to Supreme Sect this time can help him find a better path." "The orthodox immortal methods are all within the Ten Sects. Everything else is merely heterodox..." Zou Yunhao sighed inwardly.

Baili Shan, of course, was unaware of his master's thoughts. His absolute confidence and reluctance to go to the Ten Immortal Dao Sects stemmed from the [Supreme Dao Scripture] he had unexpectedly obtained. After studying this treasure for some time, Baili Shan was convinced that its name, [Supreme], was indeed well-deserved. He had only glimpsed less than a billionth of its brilliance, yet his cultivation had already advanced by leaps and bounds.

"If I can fully comprehend the Dao Scripture, True Immortal might be within reach!" "What are the Ten Immortal Dao Sects? They are utterly insignificant!" Going to the Ten Immortal Dao Sects would expose his secret of possessing a supreme treasure, whereas in Evergreen Valley, he enjoyed absolute trust. The choice was clear.

Baili Shan returned to his modest courtyard and was about to enter seclusion to further study the Supreme Dao Scripture when he was startled to find someone inexplicably in his room. "Who's there?" Assuming his secret had been exposed, Baili Shan didn't hesitate. He unleashed his Evergreen spiritual energy, transforming it into a medical blade, and fiercely stabbed forward.

"Senior Brother, you have such a poor memory. It's okay if you don't remember me, but surely you don't forget the Supreme Dao Scripture I gifted you?" Li Fan smiled faintly and effortlessly dissolved Baili Shan's attack. The keywords [Supreme Dao Scripture] awakened Baili Shan's almost lost memories.

"It's you?!" Instantly, a myriad of thoughts flashed through Baili Shan's mind. There was killing intent, fear, and confusion. Baili Shan was still young, and all his thoughts were evident on his face. "Senior Brother, don't overthink it. Look at this."

Li Fan smiled and extended his palm. Baili Shan peered intently and saw a mesmerizing thin plate lying in his palm, one he was extremely familiar with—the [Supreme Dao Scripture]! Baili Shan's heart leaped. His instinctive reaction was to check his own body. Finding no loss, he breathed a sigh of relief. He was not foolish; after some thought, he finally understood. "You... you found two thin plates?" Baili Shan suddenly realized.

"Precisely! Senior Brother, you are indeed intelligent." Li Fan clapped his hands in praise. "However, I vaguely know this treasure is extraordinary, but I could never find the correct way to activate it, so I hardened my heart and gave one to Senior Brother." "And Senior Brother's performance over the past month has confirmed my conjecture," Li Fan said with a smile.

"Are these two thin plates the same?" Baili Shan squinted and examined Li Fan, then asked, "I'm not sure. But I guess they should be identical. Senior Brother, please take a look?" With that said, Li Fan offered the thin plate he held with both hands. Baili Shan, filled with suspicion, took it and examined it. After a moment, he exhaled and returned the so-called [Supreme Dao Scripture] to Li Fan. "You guessed correctly. Yours and mine are identical," Baili Shan said in a deep voice.

"Please teach me how to use the Supreme Dao Scripture, Senior Brother." After some deliberation, Baili Shan gradually recounted his own insights. Li Fan gripped the thin plate tightly in his right hand, closed his eyes, and pondered. After a moment, he opened his eyes, a look of wild fervor appearing. "So it was this simple. All my arduous searching was in vain; I only needed to follow the Dao!"

Baili Shan let out a snort of disdain. Li Fan remained unfazed, smiling, "Senior Brother, what are your plans for the future? With such a treasure in hand, you can go anywhere in the world, can't you?"

Holding the Supreme Dao Scripture together, they now shared a common secret. Although Baili Shan looked down on Li Fan somewhat, to prevent his secret from being exposed and implicating him, he sternly warned, "For you and me, as long as we have the [Supreme Dao Scripture] in hand, it makes no difference where we cultivate. Our strength is still too weak. If our secret is exposed, we won't even have the power to protect ourselves..." Baili Shan continued to counsel. Li Fan sensed that after Baili Shan began to treat him as "one of their own," the anchor points he had established in this space-time had increased.

Chapter 1535: Taixuan Revival Furnace

Li Fan could clearly feel that Baili Shan's "anchor point" was much more stable than Elder Song's. This was not merely because his relationship with Baili Shan seemed closer now, but because of the "thickness" of the "ink" left behind by the anchor point in the River of Time.

"If there are no accidents, Elder Song will only reach the Nascent Soul stage in this life. He is not much different from the common beings in the Profound Yellow Realm, and his ultimate end will be to perish like an ant in the impending cultivation tribulation."

"Whereas Baili Shan, who obtained the [Supreme Dao Scripture], will undoubtedly reach the Harmonious Dao stage, the pinnacle of the Profound Yellow Realm. He will live longer, leaving a deeper mark."

Li Fan's gaze seemed to pierce through the mists of history, penetrating the vast River of Time, glimpsing the scenes of ten thousand years later.

...

The verification of his guess confirmed, Li Fan changed his previous approach of using Illusion is True to conceal his identity, and began to frequently appear in public. Baili Shan was the center of attention in the current Evergreen Valley, and Li Fan, as Baili Shan's newly befriended companion, naturally attracted considerable attention.

Compared to Baili Shan, a rising star, Li Fan was an unknown nobody with no distinguishing features. Therefore, most Evergreen Valley disciples couldn't understand why he had such a close relationship with Baili Shan. Some insidious disciples, after failing to undermine their relationship, began to spread insidious rumors in Evergreen Valley.

"Don't bother with these foolish people. You and I are ultimately beings from different worlds." Baili Shan disdained to pay them any mind. Sensing the insights into the [Supreme Dao Scripture] that Li Fan transmitted to him, he was overjoyed.

"Indeed, the Great Dao is like the heavens; seeing it from different angles yields different perspectives. You and I sharing our insights and verifying them mutually will increase our cultivation efficiency by several times compared to working in isolation!"

Initially, Baili Shan only regarded Li Fan as a "fellow traveler" who shared a common secret. However, after witnessing Li Fan's rapid cultivation progress upon understanding the Supreme Dao Scripture, Baili Shan's attitude gradually shifted. He began to see Li Fan as a fellow seeker of the Dao who could mutually assist each other.

"Rumors are like floods; if not stopped, they will only spread further. I don't mind, but you, as the chief disciple of Evergreen Valley, are destined to inherit the position of Sect Leader. If these rumors are allowed to spread, eventually..." Li Fan shook his head slightly.

Baili Shan's expression gradually froze. After pondering for a moment, he frowned and said, "What you said makes sense. I will report this to Master immediately..."

Li Fan waved his hand. "Brother Baili, you need to learn to put yourself in the right position. The current situation is not you begging to stay in Evergreen Valley, but Evergreen Valley needing you to stay. If you can't resolve such a trivial matter yourself, then there's no need to stay in Evergreen Valley!"

"But..." Baili Shan said, feeling conflicted. What Li Fan said seemed reasonable, yet it ran counter to his long-held way of conducting himself.

As if sensing Baili Shan's dilemma, Li Fan took the initiative to volunteer, "Brother Baili, you don't need to worry. Just continue to play the role of the brilliant Senior Brother."

"The villain, I will be."

Baili Shan looked at Li Fan's calm expression, utterly stunned.

In the following days, Evergreen Valley experienced considerable bloodshed. The creators and spreaders of rumors were ruthlessly executed and annihilated in front of the assembled disciples. The rumors ceased instantly.

As for Li Fan's blatant violation of sect rules and his act of slaughter, the Sect Leader and all the Elders of Evergreen Valley chose to turn a blind eye. They all assumed that Baili Shan, valuing his reputation, had instructed Li Fan to act in his stead. Compared to Baili Shan, the creators of the rumors were the least of their concerns, and thus no punishment was meted out. In fact, they even actively supported the two, claiming they had brought them back.

The storm gradually subsided. However, Li Fan's cold, murderous figure lingered like a nightmare in the hearts of the Evergreen Valley disciples.

"Indeed, this method of leaving anchor points is also effective."

"And compared to conventional methods, the effect is even better."

In the seclusion chamber, Li Fan felt the gradually stabilizing connections between himself and the mortal world, a dangerous glint appearing in his eyes. However, after careful consideration, he extinguished it.

"Using it occasionally is acceptable, but it cannot be the primary method. The most crucial aspect is still the existence of people, events, and objects within this space-time as anchor points. If all of them are slaughtered, or if their numbers are too few, the anchoring effect will be reduced..."

Li Fan stood up and stretched, feeling the stability after establishing the anchors. He nodded with satisfaction. "Although Evergreen Valley is only a small sect, it influences a radius of ten thousand miles. With my current reputation, the anchors established within the sect are temporarily sufficient for my activities."

Li Fan did not intend to linger here for too long. During this period, he had also secretly gathered some information about the brutal war currently being waged by the Ten Sects. The immortal cultivation world that the Profound Yellow Realm was fighting against was called [Tai Yuan]. Compared to the Profound Yellow Realm, the Tai Yuan Realm, whether in scale or overall cultivator strength, was not on the same level.

Since the beginning of the war, the overlords of the Profound Yellow Realm, the Ten Immortal Dao Sects, had not taken them seriously, believing the war would end quickly. As expected, facing the sudden invasion of the Profound Yellow Realm, the Tai Yuan Realm suffered heavy losses. Several of their largest sects were almost wiped out. Only a few survivors united to resist with their lives.

Initially, the Ten Sects did not pay much attention to these insignificant resistance forces, only intending to plunder the Tai Yuan Realm's resources as quickly as possible. However, no one expected that the surviving resistance army would grow rapidly, dealing a heavy blow to the Ten Immortal Dao Sects. Not only did they almost annihilate the Profound Yellow vanguard cultivators, but they even managed to counter-attack into the Profound Yellow Realm.

And all of this was due to a world- trấn [world- trấn] immortal artifact within the [Tai Yuan Realm]!

The Tai Yuan Chaos Furnace! This was information painstakingly obtained by the Profound Yellow Realm at a great cost. Any cultivator who perished in the Tai Yuan Realm could be resurrected in the Tai Yuan Chaos Furnace by activating its flames, seemingly at full condition. It was rumored that the entire Tai Yuan Realm was initially used as a testing ground for the Tai Yuan Chaos Furnace's efficacy. Later, after the destruction of the Immortal Realm, the Tai Yuan Chaos Furnace was actually controlled by its own experimental subjects. The enemy would be resurrected endlessly, while their side would lose one person and never gain them back. How could such a war be won?

The moment this news spread, the morale of the Ten Immortal Dao Sects plummeted. Most of them were ready to abandon the attack on the Tai Yuan Realm. However, Qu Yi Xing, the Sect Leader of the Yi Shi Sect, spoke a word of truth at the critical moment. The news regarding the Tai Yuan Chaos Furnace was deliberately leaked by the enemy, precisely to force the Profound Yellow Realm forces to retreat.

The Tai Yuan Chaos Furnace did possess resurrection capabilities, but immortal artifacts required immortal spiritual energy to activate. The Tai Yuan Realm had no True Immortals. The general condition of the Tai Yuan Chaos Furnace should be similar to the remaining immortal artifacts in the Profound Yellow Realm. Each use diminished its power. Resurrection was not without limitations. Many sacrifices had already been made in the attack on the Tai Yuan Realm; would they abandon it halfway? Furthermore, if the Tai Yuan Chaos Furnace truly possessed such resurrection effects, after successfully conquering it in the future, they might even be able to resurrect the Ten Sects' cultivators who had perished in the Tai Yuan Realm. Whether out of self-interest or righteousness, continuing the attack became the only option for the Ten Sects. Thus, they chose to continue investing their forces and engage in a war of attrition with the Tai Yuan Realm. However, they might have misjudged the amount of immortal spiritual energy remaining within the Tai Yuan Chaos Furnace. The cultivators of the Tai Yuan Realm were resurrected wave after wave. Yet, they seemed inexhaustible. Consequently, the war fell into a stalemate.

After organizing the information he had gathered, Li Fan's expression became somewhat subtle. "Not True Immortals, lacking the attribute of infinite immortal spiritual energy."

"Choosing to fill the gap with lives..."

Not all immortal cultivation worlds are like the Profound Yellow Realm, which is special. As one of the most important experimental grounds in the Rotten Chessboard Dao Field, it was strictly supervised. Even with immortal artifacts, they were only half-finished products with 阉割 (castrated) functions. Judging the Profound Yellow Realm's situation based on other immortal cultivation worlds would likely lead to unpleasant outcomes.

What intrigued Li Fan was the location of this so-called [Tai Yuan Realm]. Li Fan, as a disciple of Shou Qiu, had obtained the highest authority of the Rotten Chessboard Dao Field. However, among the star fields of various experiments, he did not find the existence of the [Tai Yuan Realm].

"Either, at this time node, it was occupied and subsequently annihilated by the Profound Yellow Realm."

"Or, this Tai Yuan Realm is not located within the High Wall."

When Li Fan was at the Great Dao Sect before, he had closely observed the golden lock connecting to the Floating Crossing Star Sea Great Formation that spanned through the sky. Judging by its displayed power, it might indeed be able to penetrate the High Wall and connect to the outer starry sky.

"It's a pity that it seems to have been activated forcefully at a certain cost."

"It's only usable once, no wonder the Ten Sects are fighting so desperately."

"Their luck is truly terrible."

"An immortal artifact that can resurrect infinitely..."

In Li Fan's understanding, such an immortal artifact, even in the Immortal Realm, would be considered top-tier. Only the ruling Immortal Emperors who held the power of the Immortal Realm could forge such items and bestow them upon the Immortal Ministers of various star regions.

"Could it be the legacy of another Hidden Emperor?" Li Fan looked towards the faint image of the Floating Crossing Star Sea Great Formation on the sky screen, murmuring to himself.

"In this time of crisis, someone must emerge to turn the tide and save the collapsing situation..."

Li Fan murmured, his mind already made up. He sent a single message to Baili Shan, and Li Fan once again drifted away gracefully.

Entering the battlefield of the Tai Yuan Realm was not a difficult task. With insufficient manpower, the Ten Immortal Dao Sects were forcibly recruiting soldiers. After obtaining the verification token from the Sect Leader of Evergreen Valley, Li Fan arrived at the mountain gate of the Supreme Sect. Compared to what he had seen in paintings before, it was even more magnificent. Peaks hung in the sky, forming a vast formation. The disciples of the Supreme Sect looked down upon the mortal world like immortals from above. Unfortunately, the current Supreme Sect was rather desolate.

"Are you here to volunteer?" Duan Yuxiao, a God Transformation cultivator from the Supreme Sect, looked at Li Fan in utter surprise. He carefully examined Li Fan, matching his appearance with the description given by Zou Yunhao, the Sect Leader of Evergreen Valley, and dismissed his doubts. He said earnestly, "Good! Currently, all sects fear war and hesitate to join. We need exemplary figures like you! Rest assured, we Ten Sects will definitely not mistreat you!"

"Follow me!"

Duan Yuxiao was not lying. He directly led Li Fan to the treasure vault of the Supreme Sect and, pointing to the vast sea of cultivation techniques and magical treasures, generously said, "You may choose any three items from here!"

"If you return alive, I will report to my Uncle-Master, the Sect Leader, and you will be accepted as a direct disciple of our Supreme Sect!"

Li Fan cupped his hands and wandered through the Supreme Sect's treasure vault. Clearly, this was only the outermost layer. Despite boasting of countless treasures, it was only so for cultivators below the God Transformation stage. With Li Fan's current vision, he found none of it appealing and discovered no extraordinary treasures. He casually selected a cultivation technique and two magical treasures as a pretense.

Li Fan was then personally led to the battlefield by Duan Yuxiao. Within the Supreme Sect, there was also a golden chain from the Floating Crossing Star Sea Great Formation. However, compared to what Li Fan had seen before, the situation seemed even more precarious. In Li Fan's view, this chain was clearly nearing its limit, capable of collapsing at any moment. Duan Yuxiao, however, was oblivious, filled with joy as he led Li Fan along the golden chain, completing the spatial translocation.

The moment they entered the Tai Yuan Realm, Li Fan keenly sensed wisps of immortal spiritual energy flowing through the world.

"Without the Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerable causing trouble, would it still resist my comprehension?" Li Fan sensed the revealed Dao within this realm. After a moment, he couldn't help but frown. Although the situation was much better than in the Profound Yellow Realm, it wasn't optimistic either. This was because the Dao within this realm was incredibly solid and integrated. Li Fan almost thought he was facing a Nameless True Immortal who had attained enlightenment!

"Moreover, the Dao of this realm is actually within my blind spot, not familiar to my former Myriad Forms Dao Net..." Li Fan felt a mix of surprise and joy in his heart.

In contrast, Duan Yuxiao was not so pleased. Seemingly having discovered something, his expression became serious the moment he entered the Tai Yuan Realm. Grabbing Li Fan, he flew rapidly towards a building standing on the ground ahead. This place was likely once the stronghold of a sect in the Tai Yuan Realm, now occupied by the Profound Yellow Realm. It had undergone untold numbers of brutal battles, to the point where its original appearance was almost unrecognizable.

"Senior Brother Duan, why have you come?" a somewhat surprised voice rang out. The speaker was a female cultivator radiating a dense aura of bloodlust. She had an ordinary appearance, but her heroic spirit was unforgettable.

Duan Yuxiao pointed at Li Fan and explained the situation truthfully. The female cultivator nodded slightly at Li Fan, "Although your cultivation is a bit low, you can still rally the troops and boost morale."

"What is the current battle situation?" Duan Yuxiao asked.

Chapter 1536: The River Anchor Point

"It's the same as ever," the female cultivator named Cao Yingyue sighed. "We've barely managed to repel one wave, and they'll likely be back in about seven days."

Duan Yuxiao comforted her, "You've worked hard, junior sister. The situation at other outposts isn't optimistic either. This place isn't even the front line..."

The two exchanged glances and fell into silence.

"But there's good news. It's said that by pooling their efforts, they've finally deduced the exact location of that item. They're preparing for a surprise raid to end this in one decisive battle..." Cao Yingyue whispered.

Duan Yuxiao heard this and felt a sense of relief. "I hope this time, we can finally end this war. We've shed too much blood on this land."

"However, even if that item is destroyed, the enemy's final counterattack will be even more ferocious. Junior sister, you must be careful," Duan Yuxiao warned.

"I understand that principle, of course," Cao Yingyue nodded.

The two exchanged words, but even though they were transmitting their voices, it was all within Li Fan's perception.

"As the saying goes, success is achieved through secrecy. To directly target the Tai Yuan Furnace, such a confidential matter, was exposed so easily. After fighting for so long, the front lines of the Ten Sects are still at this level..." Li Fan inwardly grumbled.

Suddenly, his thoughts came to an abrupt halt.

"Something's wrong!"

"At this time node, the Ten Immortal Dao Sects are the unified overlords of the Profound Yellow Realm, a colossal entity, and they are at their zenith before the Great Tribulation. Moreover, they possess immortal artifacts like the Burning Dao Furnace. If they truly wanted to keep it a secret, they could have."

"Therefore, it was deliberately spread, making it common knowledge."

Li Fan's thoughts turned, and he instantly understood.

"The Ten Sects have always been unable to pinpoint the location of the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace, so they released the news, intentionally trying to flush out the enemy."

"Hoping the Tai Yuan Realm would move the Tai Yuan Furnace, thus exposing its location..."

"They've actually reached this stage of using such tactics. It seems the situation for the Ten Sects is indeed not optimistic."

From just a corner of the battlefield, Li Fan had already glimpsed the entirety of the war situation.

However, at this moment, Li Fan still feigned ignorance, his face showing a mix of nervousness and fear.

After Duan Yuxiao delivered Li Fan, he quickly took his leave.

Cao Yingyue watched the figure of her senior brother as he flew away, her expression somewhat complex.

At this very moment...

A beam of light shot out from the depths of the Tai Yuan Realm with astonishing speed, instantly piercing Duan Yuxiao's body!

Without even a whimper of struggle, Duan Yuxiao turned into a pool of flesh and blood, exploding with a boom.

His soul scattered, his life extinguished, and his path vanished!

Cao Yingyue was stunned at first, then finally realized what had happened.

"Senior Brother!"

A heart-wrenching cry erupted from her throat, and Cao Yingyue frantically rushed towards the scene of the tragedy.

However, she stopped abruptly mid-air.

"Enemy attack!"

"Form ranks!"

Cao Yingyue's voice resounded throughout the Profound Yellow Realm's fortress. She seemed to have regained her composure in a short span of time, but her slightly trembling body betrayed her inner turmoil.

Shortly after Cao Yingyue issued her orders, Li Fan saw hundreds of thousands of cultivators, like a tidal wave, surging from the depths of the Tai Yuan Realm, fearlessly charging towards the Profound Yellow Realm's defenses.

The fortress where Li Fan was stationed also became one of the insignificant targets battered by this terrifying onslaught.

The situation changed so rapidly that Cao Yingyue and the cultivators within the fortress had no time to attend to Li Fan.

Furthermore, with the enhancement of the Illusion is True divine ability, Li Fan appeared to have been forgotten by the battlefield.

However, Li Fan's situation was not exactly pleasant.

Because of his actions, Duan Yuxiao met an accidental death. And the backlash from the River of Time, triggered by this chain reaction, was even more ferocious than he had anticipated.

"It seems that this Duan Yuxiao from the Supreme Sect held a pivotal position in the original future. But it's understandable, after all, even at such a critical juncture of the war, he managed to remain in the rear and avoid the front lines." Li Fan watched the sudden turmoil around him, struggling to maintain his balance.

Fortunately, the foundation he had laid in Evergreen Valley previously allowed him to withstand the erosion of this storm.

"If there are no accidents, the Profound Yellow Realm should suffer a great defeat in this battle and ultimately retreat in disgrace."

"And then erase all records of this humiliating defeat."

"From then on, the fortunes of the Ten Sects would begin to decline, from prosperity to ruin. After experiencing calamities such as the rise of the Myriad Immortal Alliance, the conflict of incompatible cultivation methods, and the miasma between immortals and mortals, they would eventually be completely submerged by history."

"This crucial node happens to be where I laid my foundation!" A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

If it were an ordinary person, after narrowly escaping death in the turbulence caused by the rerouting of the River of Time, they would first seek a stable method to solidify their anchor points and then plan further.

However, Li Fan did the opposite, seeing in it a method to quickly establish a solid anchor.

"If this anchor point is successfully built, even if the River of Time reroutes and creates a completely different future, I will remain safe amidst the changes. Because all future Profound Yellow cultivators will remember my deeds."

"Not just establishing an anchor point for a moment or a lifetime. It will resound through history, spanning across the ancient and present times!"

The power of the Great Dao, like lighthouses standing tall, that Li Fan had witnessed in the River of Time, gave him inspiration.

Within moments, he made his decision.

"However, it's not advisable to make drastic changes right from the start."

"The butterfly's wings will begin to flap from this fortress."

Li Fan looked towards the distant battlefield, where Cao Yingyue, under siege by three Tai Yuan Realm cultivators and in an increasingly dire situation, was about to follow in her senior brother's footsteps.

With a flick of his finger.

Cao Yingyue, who was already severely injured and on the verge of losing consciousness, suddenly saw the scene of her admired Senior Brother Duan's tragic death again.

He, who was supposed to have an infinite future, now died in vain on this battlefield. A surge of ferocity suddenly rose within Cao Yingyue's heart, accompanied by an boundless power burning like a flame.

Her body and soul seemed to be burning, and Cao Yingyue, driven into a frenzy, took down the three Tai Yuan Realm cultivators who were besieging her with a single strike of her blade.

Then, she continued to charge towards the attacking cultivators of the Tai Yuan Realm fearlessly.

The Ten Sects' cultivators stationed here, witnessing Cao Yingyue's valiant display, were all inspired and began to resist with all their might.

After a long and brutal day of defense, the Tai Yuan Realm cultivators, who had been attacking like locusts, were finally repelled for the time being.

The cultivators all believed it was their resistance that paid off.

They never expected that this was all Li Fan's covert orchestration.

Not just this fortress, but if one were to look at the entire Tai Yuan Realm from a higher perspective, one would see that the Tai Yuan Dao, which was originally a cohesive whole, seemed to have had impurities mixed into it, causing it to become turbid.

An invisible, narrow line, like a沟壑 (gully), spanned across the entire Tai Yuan Realm, dividing the battlefield.

The Tai Yuan Realm cultivators who sensed the anomaly were thus forced to retreat.

The Ten Sects' cultivators, having survived the ordeal, lay weakly on the ground, enjoying what might be their last moments of peace.

And Li Fan, just like them, was on the verge of exhaustion.

Not only because of the influence he exerted through his own enlightenment and the formations he had subtly laid, which had altered the overall situation of the Tai Yuan Realm, but also because he had to simultaneously contend with the renewed turbulence from the River of Time.

"This is the limit of what I can do now."

"The foundation I laid earlier is no longer sufficient against such waves."

As Li Fan felt his precarious state, he deliberately released a strong fluctuation.

Instantly, it attracted the attention of the surrounding surviving cultivators.

A moment of surprise drew murmurs: "This... is he breaking through?"

"Heh, Nascent Soul stage. It only slightly increases the probability of survival."

"However, to survive the surprise attack at the Golden Core stage and then achieve enlightenment and breakthrough after the battle... This person is extraordinary! Who is he? I don't seem to have seen him before."

"Between life and death lies great terror, but also great opportunity. Master, you were right!"

As the discussions continued, rumors about Evergreen Valley's "Li Ping" gradually spread.

Just the act of voluntarily charging into battle was enough to earn the respect of these Ten Sects' cultivators who had personally experienced the horrors of war.

Until the heavenly changes were completely resolved, the Tai Yuan Realm forces dared not launch another attack.

Everyone was able to enjoy a relatively peaceful night.

By nightfall, Cao Yingyue, who was in a deep sleep, was once again plagued by nightmares of Senior Brother Duan's tragic death.

"Senior Brother!" she cried out instinctively.

Senior Brother Duan seemed to sense her call, and before vanishing, he gave her a loving look.

Then, a point of light flew from his body and entered Cao Yingyue's mind.

*Boom!*

The nightmare was instantly swept away, and a starry, magnificent scene appeared before Cao Yingyue's eyes.

This incomparably beautiful sight made her temporarily forget her pain.

"Tai Shang Dao Scripture?"

Before this supreme beauty, Cao Yingyue was lost in a daze.

...

When Cao Yingyue regained her senses, Li Fan proactively came to apologize.

"What crime have you committed?" Cao Yingyue said coldly.

"If you hadn't sent me to the battlefield, Senior Brother Duan wouldn't have..." Li Fan said guiltily, lowering his head.

"..."

In reality, Cao Yingyue did have such thoughts initially. However, she also knew that this matter could not be blamed on him. Life and death were unpredictable. On the battlefield, one's life was not their own. It was all up to fate. Was Duan Yuxiao's life more precious than the lives of countless disciples of the Ten Immortal Dao Sects? Moreover, Li Fan was a loyal cultivator who voluntarily went to battle. If she used this as an excuse to cause trouble, the countless Ten Sects' cultivators on this battlefield would not agree. Cao Yingyue knew this principle and had already let it go. Now that Li Fan brought it up himself, it was as if a gentle breeze had blown it away, settling the matter.

"Live well."

"Live well for Senior Brother Duan as well."

Cao Yingyue said expressionlessly.

...

In the following half-year, dozens of battles, large and small, occurred between the Tai Yuan Realm and the Profound Yellow Realm.

While the Ten Sects still suffered heavy losses, relying on the Profound Yellow Realm's strong replenishment capabilities, they could barely hold on.

The Tai Yuan Realm cultivators could be resurrected, but the occasional anomalies in the Tai Yuan Realm's heavenly laws greatly affected the efficiency of their resurrection. Before they could fully understand the source of these anomalies, they did not dare to launch a full-scale counterattack.

Thus, the war entered a stalemate.

Facing the future direction of the war, disagreements began to emerge within the Ten Sects.

It now appeared that the immortal spiritual energy within the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace was clearly not something that would be depleted in the short term. Although they were unwilling, they had to admit that they had made a fatal misjudgment.

However, as things stood, they could only pursue responsibility after the war ended. The key now was how to proceed. Having already missed one opportunity, the Profound Yellow Realm could not afford another mistake.

There were quite a number of people advocating for a retreat. And those who remained silent, harboring the same thoughts, were even more numerous. However, the primary reason the Ten Sects publicly maintained a stance of fighting to the death was the Floating Crossing Star Sea Great Formation inherited from the ancient Profound Sky Sect. Originally intended as a means of escape from the Immortal Ruins, the golden chain of the Floating Crossing Star Sea Great Formation brought them hope. But unexpectedly, it became a quagmire of misfortune. And now, they were trapped in this quagmire, unable to extricate themselves. The so-called quagmire referred not only to the war itself but also to the golden chain! The Profound Yellow Realm side had naturally also noticed the heavenly changes in the Tai Yuan Realm. They were unclear about the specifics of the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace, but they could see the changes in the Floating Crossing Star Sea Great Formation. The originally strained golden chain, on the verge of complete destruction, was actually slowly recovering! This was initially a cause for celebration for the Ten Sects. However, no one in the Ten Sects could truly be happy. Because the cost of the golden chain's recovery was its gradual integration into the heavens and earth of the Tai Yuan Realm! The reason for this extremely strange phenomenon left everyone, including the Sect Leaders of the Ten Sects, completely baffled.
