All that was left was a fait accompli: even if they wanted to withdraw now, they couldn't. As a part of the Floating Crossing Star Sea Great Formation, the golden chain connected to the Profound Yellow Realm. Even if they retreated from the Tai Yuan Realm, if they didn't retrieve the golden chain, the Tai Yuan cultivators could still attack and invade through the chain. And if they severed the chain... The Floating Crossing Star Sea Great Formation was already at the level of an immortal formation. Although the Ten Sects often claimed their heritage from the Immortal Realm, they had not reached the point where they could freely modify immortal formations. All they could do was activate and manipulate the formations. More crucially, the Profound Yellow Realm was still situated in the Abyss of the Immortal Ruins. Forcibly severing the chain could potentially inflict severe damage on the Profound Yellow Realm, causing it to fall into the Immortal Ruins. Thus, the Ten Sects collectively rejected this option. Therefore, the Ten Sects were left with only one path. From now on, even if they didn't continue to attack the Tai Yuan Realm, they would have to establish defensive fortresses to prevent a counterattack from the Tai Yuan Realm. For this, they needed to commit more forces. "My lords, have you heard of organizations called the Myriad Immortal Alliance appearing in various parts of the Profound Yellow Realm?" "They are merely a bunch of rogue cultivators causing trouble." "Originally, we planned to suppress them after the Tai Yuan Realm issue was resolved. Now it seems..." "Perhaps we can bring them into the battlefield."

Chapter 1537: Intact Nine Star Pearl

"Sect Leader Qu speaks wisely. After all, the Profound Yellow Realm is not solely the Profound Yellow Realm of our Ten Sects," stated Fang Dingge, the Sect Leader of the Great Dao Sect, with an implied meaning.

Qu Yixing, however, appeared oblivious and continued, "The leader of the Myriad Immortal Alliance, known for his fame, has a unique approach to his methods. However, with the Great Heavenly Venerate overseeing the world, his sect is destined to falter. If they cause too much of a stir, they might not even need our intervention; this so-called Myriad Immortal Alliance would vanish in an instant."

"Since they are all fated to die, why not make the best use of them? However, the Myriad Immortal Alliance's techniques are unique, making it unsuitable to recruit cultivators above the Nascent Soul stage. Otherwise, after they die, their residual essences will only nourish the Primordial Realm...

"Leave this matter to me. I will persuade them well." A voice brimming with heroic spirit suddenly rang out, taking on the task. It was Situ Yao, the Senior Disciple of the Heavenly Sword Sect.

He gazed towards a certain location in the Profound Yellow Realm, silently picked up the gourd in his hand, and drained it in one go.

...

With just a few words, the leaders of the Ten Sects decided the fate of the Myriad Immortal Alliance in this epoch.

And in a corner unseen by them, a master was also weaving their future.

"So that's how the Primordial Rebirth Cauldron works."

"I was wondering why there was a Dao that I, who have experienced countless possibilities, did not recognize!"

In the Dark Blood Fortress, Li Fan sat cross-legged, a blurry, distorted image of a furnace flickering in his palm.

Over the past six months, he had used the Heaven-Scanning Golden Lock of the Floating Crossing Star Sea Grand Formation as a medium to analyze and dissect the Dao of the Primordial Realm.

The results were somewhat unexpected, but upon reflection, they were entirely logical.

The so-called infinite resurrection occurring in the Primordial Realm was not true resurrection. It was "creation."

This was exactly the same situation as in the Profound Yellow Realm.

Deep within the Primordial Realm lay a magnificent and vast ancient Immortal Formation.

The Nine Star Red Pearls, the unstable circular rings, the endless frozen sea of corpses...

All of this was almost identical to the Profound Yellow Realm. The only difference was that the Primordial Realm's Nine Star Red Pearls had not gone missing, unlike in the Profound Yellow Realm. They remained intact at the core of the ancient formation, maintaining its operation.

When cultivators in the Primordial Realm died, the Nine Star Red Pearls, which recorded the data of all living beings in the Primordial Realm, would recreate new copies through the Immortal Formation.

Both the "resurrected" and those who fought them would believe they had been "resurrected."

Only those who could pierce through all veils and glimpse the Immortal Formation behind it could see the truth.

"As expected of an experimental ground once overseen by an Immortal Emperor. With a complete ancient Immortal Formation as its core, powered by the Nine Star Red Pearls, it has already achieved [Dao Painting Through Formations]."

"Tai Tian Di, Tai Tian Di, you didn't even mention such an important matter."

Of course, this was just Li Fan's playful remark. In Tai Tian Di's view, compared to the mission of reversing time and saving all ages, the lives of all beings within the experimental ground were utterly insignificant. An array that merely simulated life was naturally not related to the word "important."

"The so-called resurrection is a complete lie. This must not be revealed to the Ten Immortal Dao Sects. Otherwise, the belief that supported the Profound Yellow Realm cultivators in continuing to fight after resurrecting their fallen comrades would instantly disappear, and the Profound Yellow Realm's front line would likely collapse instantly."

Li Fan examined the phantom image of the furnace in his hand, slowly caressing it.

Although it was merely a phantom, ripples truly stirred with Li Fan's gentle touch.

This was naturally Li Fan attempting to modify the Primordial Realm's Immortal Formation after successfully infiltrating and deciphering it.

Even with the Immortal Formation's core intact, it was ultimately no match for a True Immortal from ten thousand years later.

Li Fan did not exert much effort before infiltrating the core of the Primordial Realm's Immortal Formation.

However, aside from secretly modifying the details of the formation, he hadn't taken any significant actions. The reason was the presence of two Immortal Realm array guardians still alive within the formation.

Under the concealment of the World-Protecting Ancient Immortal Formation, Li Fan glimpsed the true forms of these two figures.

One was the Immortal Realm Overseer, who had also appeared in the Profound Yellow Realm. However, this one in the Primordial Realm clearly maintained his complete and clear consciousness.

The other, perhaps it once existed in the Profound Yellow Realm. But it had already vanished with the damage to the Immortal Formation.

It was the Immortal Formation Repairer.

Their human bodies merely had heads replaced by books that seemed to have countless pages constantly flipping.

The so-called Overseer and Repairer, in Li Fan's opinion, were merely Immortal Servants.

Of course, in the eyes of mortal cultivators, even if they were just "servants," as long as they were associated with the word "Immortal," they were far beyond what ordinary mortals could contend with.

Even Li Fan, who had now recovered his Harmonious Dao realm, could not compete with these two head-on.

He could only temporarily avoid their锋芒.

However, it was clear that the Immortal Servants stationed within the formation did not understand the World-Protecting Immortal Formation itself. They could only follow the instructions given by True Immortals in the past and use it step by step.

They were completely unaware of the subtle changes occurring within the formation under Li Fan's direction.

"I must solidify the belief that the Primordial Resurrection Furnace can resurrect Profound Yellow cultivators who died on the battlefield. Only then can their will to fight be maintained." Having spent half a year in the fortress on the battlefield, Li Fan understood this point very well.

"I painstakingly set up the stage for this play. If the audience walks away now, wouldn't that be a pity..."

"If the Immortal Formation cannot do it, I will!"

Li Fan gently waved his left hand, and the phantom image of the furnace flew forward, spinning rapidly in the air.

With each movement of Li Fan, countless rays of light emerged from it.

Unbeknownst to anyone, changes were slowly occurring within the Primordial Realm.

When a cultivator's soul scattered, the Immortal Formation would actively capture their life data and record it in the Nine Star Red Pearls. With this data, it would not be difficult to recreate new ones.

Of course, since it was not the original template data, there would inevitably be some discrepancies between the data captured by the Nine Star Red Pearls and the cultivator's true life data.

The "resurrected" Profound Yellow cultivators would have slight deviations from their original selves. It was less like resurrection and more like reincarnation.

However, even with such deviations, it was likely that the Profound Yellow cultivators would be satisfied.

After several days of meticulous refinement, Li Fan finally completed the initial modifications to the Primordial Realm's Immortal Formation.

During this process, he also completed a certain degree of calibration between the Dao of the past and future, using the Dao contained within the Immortal Formation.

The previously blurred boundaries of Immortal Arts, which were like being seen through a layer of frosted glass, became clear once more.

Li Fan could almost feel the boundless sea beyond the mortal realm again.

After all, a True Immortal cannot be suppressed.

Even with the Profound Yellow Realm's resistance and suppression, as long as Li Fan received an opportunity, he could rise again in an instant.

"Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao, I will deal with you when I return."

Chapter 1538: Sowing the Seeds of Immortal Cultivation

"The idea is right, it's just that the position is not correctly understood." Li Fan commented thus.

The great Dao starry sky he displayed on that thin plate was too far beyond the mortal world, even exceeding the limits of what cultivators in the Profound Yellow Realm could imagine. For ants on the ground, they naturally couldn't distinguish the difference between the first heaven and the thirty-third heaven. That old Daoist thought he had missed out on a method to become an immortal. He never imagined it was a highway straight to the other shore!

"He still retains his unique arrogance. Perhaps when he eventually perishes at the end of his life, he will regret it immensely," Li Fan shook his head slightly.

For Li Fan, walking his own Great Dao and learning from other powerful beings were not mutually exclusive. He could learn the transformation of truth and falsehood from Huan Zhen, comprehend the infinite immortal laws from the Mountains and Seas, and study the Great Dao of Longevity from Duke Shou Qiu. However, none of this prevented Li Fan from ultimately forging his own path. Even the Sect Leaders of the Ten Sects were, in Li Fan's eyes, merely insignificant ants in the drops of the River of Time, not worthy of excessive attention. Li Fan cared more about the grand play he had meticulously orchestrated.

As Li Fan’s fingers subtly moved, the scales of victory gradually tipped towards the Tai Yuan Realm. The “abnormal malfunction” of the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace seemed to have finally been repaired, and its resurrection efficiency was even better than before. Although he didn't understand the reason for such a bizarre phenomenon, it did not hinder the Tai Yuan Realm cultivators from seizing this excellent opportunity to counterattack swiftly and secure victory.

The Profound Yellow cultivators on the battlefield immediately felt the pressure. In the previous six months, the Tai Yuan Realm cultivators’ attacks usually lasted for five to six days before temporarily retreating. However, this attack was unprecedentedly fierce. Enemies died in waves, but they seemed inexhaustible. There were even instances where the same person’s two or three incomplete corpses appeared on the same battlefield, which was deeply unsettling.

Even though the Ten Immortal Dao Sects reacted quickly and mobilized their reserve forces, their battle lines were still forced to retreat continuously. The territories painstakingly occupied by the Profound Yellow Realm through countless sacrifices were lost inch by inch. The surviving Profound Yellow Realm cultivators were gradually compressed into the innermost defensive perimeter.

It seemed that after successive battles lasting dozens of days, the Tai Yuan Realm forces had also reached their limit. A rare moment of tranquility descended upon the battlefield, and all the Profound Yellow soldiers seized this last chance to breathe and recover their strength. However, under such high-pressure circumstances, not a shred of despair emerged in their minds. Only a firm belief remained: to fight to the death when the enemy charged again soon.

In the center of the Profound Yellow formation, Qu Yixing, the Sect Leader of the First Origin Sect, sat cross-legged in mid-air with a solemn expression. Above his head, the Five Elements energy twined with Yin and Yang essence, rotating rapidly like a Tai Chi diagram. Mysterious fluctuations emanated from this vortex, influencing and altering the mindset of the Profound Yellow cultivators on the battlefield.

“Brother Yixing’s method is ingenious, but it’s not a long-term solution,” Situ Yao said with a heavy heart. “It can last for another month at most. Otherwise, they will all turn into monsters who have completely lost their minds, with only killing in their heads.”

“A month… I don't think the situation can even hold for that long. Perhaps everyone should make a decision sooner,” said Fang Dingge, the Sect Leader of Great Dao Sect. “I have already asked Stone Mother to perform a hundred trillion calculations. There is a 56% probability of success. With the advantage on our side, why not take a gamble!”

A 56% probability seemed like a sure victory to Fang Dingge. No one present responded.

“Of course, if any of you are confident that you can sever the Horizontal Golden Chain while ensuring the safety of the Profound Yellow Realm, you can disregard my plan,” Fang Dingge’s sharp gaze swept across everyone.

“The safety of the Profound Yellow Realm cannot be fully guaranteed. But if it’s just the safety of the Ten Sects, perhaps that can be achieved.”

After a moment of silence, the one who spoke was a wrinkled yellow paper effigy. The paper effigy regarded Fang Dingge with a strange and distorted expression, neither smiling nor crying.

Fang Dingge’s face flashed with anger upon hearing this, “Yijue! Don’t try to peddle your Tribulation Crossing plan again. You’re asking us to fight such a bloody war, yet you don’t contribute a single soldier. Now you’re trying to sow discord and shake morale?!” “If you continue like this, don’t blame my Burning Dao Furnace for being merciless!”

Faced with Fang Dingge’s threat, Daoist Yijue of the Tribulation Crossing Sect remained unfazed. He chuckled and said, “Sect Leader Fang, you misunderstand. To speak of preempting defeat before seeking victory. You are always so fond of gambling. Perhaps you can win countless times, but if you fail even once, you will face utter destruction. Who in this world can always win?”

Fang Dingge said coldly, “Words are useless! Facts will prove everything. Besides, apart from my strategy, is there a better method? Are we all supposed to become monsters like you, neither human nor ghost?”

“Neither human nor ghost, isn't that immortal? Since you are unwilling, I will not force you. But don’t count on our Tribulation Crossing Sect. This old Daoist is leaving~” Daoist Yijue chuckled with an unclear meaning.

The originally vivid expression on the paper effigy instantly froze, then slowly drifted to the ground. Daoist Yijue of the Tribulation Crossing Sect had transformed into the most ordinary piece of paper.

The remaining people in the venue were all silent.

“Hmph, I see that influenced by that old madman Yijue, the entire Tribulation Crossing Sect will eventually turn into paper figures. Why don’t we…” Fang Dingge’s eyes flashed with a dangerous glint.

Situ Yao laughed heartily and quickly interjected, “The Ten Sects have always been united. We have experienced tribulations far more dangerous than this in the past, so why should we ruin our camaraderie over this matter?”

Fang Dingge did not concede at all, “Times have changed. After several major battles, how much energy is left in the immortal artifacts you all possess? Without immortal spiritual energy, what difference are they from scrap metal? Relying on these immortal treasures, we have been lucky enough to survive in this starry sky. In the future, when we can no longer use these immortal artifacts, where will we go?”

……

The leaders of the Ten Sects argued endlessly. Finally, a female cultivator clad in black gauze, with a graceful figure but a voice like tearing metal, ended their argument.

“Since everyone has a point, let’s bet on both sides. Everyone, don’t forget, we have one captured immortal artifact.” Xiahou Yan, the Lord of the Boundless Prison, scanned the crowd.

The crowd instinctively narrowed their eyes as if struck by invisible swords, avoiding Xiahou Yan’s direct gaze.

“That immortal artifact is too bizarre. It’s best not to use it lightly…” Even Fang Dingge shook his head in rejection after some hesitation.

Xiahou Yan let out a cold laugh. In front of the Sect Leaders of the Ten Sects, he openly mocked, “The leaders of the Ten Sects should be the most heroic figures in the world. Yet, you turn out to be indecisive and deceitful cowards.”

Although the words were harsh, they included himself. The others merely showed awkward expressions and couldn't retort.

“But we can’t blame you. The more power one wields, the more considerations one has. Such as sects, the world, and all beings…”

“It’s far less enjoyable than when I was alone and roamed the world freely!” Xiahou Yan said calmly.

It seemed to evoke memories of the past, and the scene momentarily fell silent.

Xiahou Yan broke the silence, “Consider it. Although the [Two Part Immortal Seed] is strange, it can divide all of us into two without any loss. It provides one more option, one more retreat, one more chance at survival.”

“It shouldn’t have reached such a severe point yet,” Jiang Yixing and the others still did not agree with Xiahou Yan’s opinion. “Although the Two Part Immortal Seed is immensely mystical, its side effects are truly too great. We used it once back then, and it took almost a hundred years to digest it. Lu Chenghong and Yijue from the Tribulation Crossing Sect, who were still relatively normal back then, have all become the madmen they are now…”

“But we ultimately won, didn’t we? And those three immortal cultivation worlds have long turned to dust. Since we could endure it once, we can endure it a second time,” Xiahou Yan insisted.

Only when the doubtful gazes fell upon him did Xiahou Yan realize he had lost his composure. He then let out a cold snort and fell silent.

Another long period of silence.

Situ Yao drained his gourd of wine and said impatiently, “I think Brother Dingge’s plan is feasible. I witnessed the entire process of Stone Mother’s deduction. It offers some hope for ending the Tai Yuan Realm war.”

“If you are unwilling, then let me do it.” “Death is just death, after all. When has Situ Yao ever been afraid of death!”

“Good!” Fang Dingge was overjoyed to finally gain a supporter. As opinions began to unify, the rest had no choice but to consider it.

Just then, a weak voice came from a corner. “My Master said that he agrees with Sect Leader Fang’s plan. However, our Supreme Sect will only send three people as support.” The speaker was Jiang Yingyue. This female cultivator, who had been a killing machine on the battlefield, was like a child in front of the Sect Leaders, having not dared to utter a word previously. Only after receiving a message from her Master did she speak hesitantly.

Originally, everyone had some reservations about the old Daoist’s absence. Now, hearing that the plan concerned the survival of the Profound Yellow Realm, the Supreme Sect was only willing to send three participants. Their expressions were even less pleased. However, upon seeing the three names formed by the starlight appearing in Jiang Yingyue’s hand, the others had no objections. This was because these three were the most elite combat forces of the Great Dao Sect. The strength of any one of them would not be inferior to that of the current individuals present.

After some argument, a consensus was slowly reached. The Ten Sects began to discuss the specific operational details, and Fang Dingge reiterated, “The reason we have been unable to win and have been persistently entangled by the Tai Yuan Realm is precisely because of the existence of that immortal artifact, the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace.”

“The Tai Yuan Realm cultivators, in terms of scale and strength, are far inferior to our Profound Yellow Realm. Yet, they are inexhaustible. Even if we, when facing a dozen Harmonious Dao cultivators sacrificing themselves to exchange for grievous wounds, would need considerable recuperation. Yet they can appear on the battlefield perfectly fine after a few days.” Fang Dingge said with a tinge of resentment, clearly having suffered losses before.

“The key to breaking the stalemate is to destroy the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace. We didn’t act before because we could never ascertain its exact location. We tried probing with various schemes multiple times, but to no avail. However, now…” Fang Dingge’s eyes flashed with a sharp light.

“Perhaps it’s truly related to the safety of the Profound Yellow Realm that the Great Heavenly Venerable, who has always been silent and detached from worldly affairs, has finally decided to offer guidance.”

Fang Dingge waved his hand, and a phantom image of the Tai Yuan Realm appeared in the center of the hall. Within it, flashing points of light indicated the location of the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace.

“According to the Great Heavenly Venerable, this so-called Resurrection Furnace is actually an ancient immortal-grade formation. As long as we destroy several key nodes of the formation, we can affect its resurrection effect for a period of time.”

“Enough for us to completely sweep this realm!” Fang Dingge said solemnly.

“The corresponding location here is…” Jiang Yingyue looked at the image before her and suddenly became lost in thought. “Indeed, deep within the Tai Yuan Realm, at the former location of Tai Yuan’s largest immortal cultivation sect, the Heavenly Art Palace.”

“The entire Tai Yuan Realm is within the scope of the immortal-grade formation. To infiltrate and successfully destroy the formation is fraught with danger…”

“However, our chances of success are still higher!” Fang Dingge said. “Since the start of the war, all cultivators who have appeared on the Tai Yuan battlefield have been included in Stone Mother’s deductive calculations. We have even added a third of their strength as a redundancy…”

“Even so, we still have a 56% probability of success.”

As Fang Dingge spoke, hundreds of densely packed light spots appeared on the Tai Yuan phantom. Each light spot represented a cultivator at the peak of God Transformation or above, capable of threatening their plan. When divine sense focused on these light spots, the information of the corresponding cultivators also appeared. Besides their appearance and strength, their various divine abilities and techniques displayed on the battlefield were also revealed.

“Their ability to resurrect infinitely is their absolute advantage, but it is also their fatal weakness.”

“They are currently unaware of us, but we know everything about them.”

The crowd in the hall was captivated by the scene before them. Even Xiahou Yan and others, who did not agree with Fang Dingge's risky plan, watched and contemplated silently.

And not far away, through Jiang Yingyue’s eyes, Li Fan, who had overheard the Ten Sects' secret discussion, shook his head slightly.

“Even without me, with the strength they’ve brought, they still wouldn't be able to break through the heavy defenses of the Tai Yuan Realm cultivators and destroy the Immortal Formation.” Li Fan immediately saw the fatal flaw in their plan. The defensive Immortal Formation blessed by the Nine Stars Red Pearls was not merely capable of creating life. Setting aside other abilities, the Overseer and Repair Officer within the Tai Yuan Immortal Formation might not know how to activate them, but they could definitely temporarily stimulate the potential of the created beings, greatly increasing their combat power in a short period. Although the cost was the rapid burning of the created beings' lifespans, as long as they could hold off the Profound Yellow Realm adventurers for a few moments, it would be enough to make their plan fail. It might even result in the annihilation of the Profound Yellow Realm's elites.

“This is exactly the same as the Ten Sects’ decapitation strategy in the past.”

“However, it seems that without my involvement, they would all lose their gamble.”

Chapter 1539: Boundless Life

Li Fan seemed to have foreseen the end for the Immortal Sect members. "But the Immortal Sect does not represent the Profound Yellow Realm. As long as I am here, the Profound Yellow Realm will not lose."

"It's just that the process will be more tragic."

The persona Li Fan was playing completed his final preparations before the Immortal Sect's surprise attack plan was launched. As usual, he was besieged and on the verge of death before suddenly breaking through. Thus, the rumor of him being a "Conquering Sacred Body" was thoroughly confirmed. His status instantly underwent a sky-high transformation as he advanced from the God Transformation stage to Harmonious Dao. No one dared to scoff anymore; instead, they showed outward respect.

Of course, such terrifying progress, no less than Jiang Yingyue's, naturally attracted the attention of the Ten Sects' high-ranking officials. Jiang Yingyue had the Sect Leader of the Supreme Sect shielding her, but Li Fan, coming from the ordinary Evergreen Valley, had no backing. Therefore, secret investigations were inevitable.

However, Li Fan merely allowed the Ten Sects to investigate him. His strength far surpassed that of the Ten Sects as a whole. After all their investigations, they could only conclude that Li Fan had a special constitution and extraordinary talent.

After the investigations concluded, the Ten Sects simultaneously extended olive branches to him. Facing the recruitment efforts of the Ten Sects, Li Fan politely declined, citing his desire to continue fighting on the Tai Yuan Realm battlefield. He even ignored the generous offer of being allowed to withdraw from the battlefield and return to the rear of the Profound Yellow Realm.

"Until the enemy is defeated, I will not return."

"My countless comrades have sacrificed themselves on this battlefield; how can I flee out of fear of death?"

Li Fan said resolutely and turned away, leaving behind a noble back for the Ten Sects' cultivators. His decision moved everyone present. Thus, no one mentioned recruitment again, and they all generously gifted him various magical artifacts and divine abilities, hoping to increase Li Fan's chances of survival in the decisive battle. After all, a loyal and righteous individual like "Li Ping" was something every sect wished to recruit. Not only did he possess formidable combat power gained through life-and-death struggles, but he also had absolute sincerity. Crucially, his growth trajectory and background were beyond reproach. He was undoubtedly a reliable force for any sect. This was extremely important for the Ten Immortal Dao Sects, who had suffered heavy losses in the successive battles. Therefore, in their recruitment efforts, the Ten Sects spared no expense.

"Great Dao Sect's [My Dao is Like Me], Heavenly Sword Sect's [Shattering Heaven Sword], First Origin Sect's [Myriad Forms Return to One], Boundless Prison's [Ethereal Divine Movement]..."

Li Fan casually glanced at the divine abilities gifted by the Ten Sects and couldn't help but reveal a playful smile. "Although these are still a step away from the Ten Sects' secret inheritances, they are still top-tier important divine abilities. They are truly generous..."

"Then I shall not disappoint you."

Li Fan's mind rapidly deduced and improved these divine abilities. In a short time, enhanced versions of the Ten Sects' divine abilities were produced. The core principles remained the same, but after Li Fan's optimization, their actual power had doubled. Any one of them, if released independently, would be comparable to the Ten Sects' most treasured secret techniques.

Li Fan waved his hand, and the countless starry points of illusory text in his mind flew out like streaks of light, transforming from illusory to tangible reality before him. They became numerous physical divine ability secret manuals. Li Fan arranged these manuals neatly, placing them under his pillow in his room. Then, he pushed open the door and rejoined the battlefield.

Several days of tranquility passed, followed by the Tai Yuan Realm cultivators launching a series of attacks like a tsunami. Harmonious Dao cultivators, rarely seen on the battlefield before, were now appearing one after another, participating in the slaughter. Only Harmonious Dao cultivators could withstand Harmonious Dao cultivators. However, the number of Harmonious Dao cultivators on the Profound Yellow Realm's side was clearly insufficient. Therefore, almost from the very beginning of this final battle, the Profound Yellow Realm fell into a disadvantage.

"Damn it, what is the sect thinking, not sending more people!"

"Cultivated for five hundred years, yet I don't want to die on the battlefield today, destined to be estranged from the Great Dao."

"I knew I shouldn't have stepped into this mess for that meager reward. It's all my fault!"

……

Faced with desperation, cultivators displayed different reactions. However, the vast majority harbored negative emotions. The Ten Sects' plan to attack the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace was a top secret, hence the cultivators on the battlefield were unaware that most of the Ten Sects' Sect Leaders had already arrived. Thus, in this seemingly isolated situation, it was inevitable for their morale to falter. Their overall strength was already weaker, and with their morale plummeting, the battle situation quickly began to spiral out of control.

"Everyone, the Profound Yellow Realm is behind us. We have nowhere to retreat but to fight to the death!"

Just then, a resounding voice echoed across the entire Tai Yuan Realm battlefield. Countless gazes in the heavens and earth turned towards the direction of the voice. Amidst a blinding flash of white light, two Harmonious Dao cultivators were instantly killed and exploded into mist.

Li Fan roared.

Li Fan held his blade, pointing menacingly towards the countless enemies ahead. He let out a contemptuous smile. "Villains, come up and receive your death!"

Such arrogant behavior naturally ignited the fury of the Tai Yuan Realm cultivators. Li Fan's power, capable of instantly killing Harmonious Dao cultivators, was undoubtedly immense. However, the Tai Yuan Realm cultivators could be resurrected infinitely; how could they be intimidated by Li Fan?

But after just a moment, no less than twenty streams of light flew from all corners of the battlefield towards Li Fan's location. On the battlefield, there were no fair duels; only life and death.

Soon, under siege, Li Fan seemed to be in a perilous situation. However, with Li Fan stepping forward to absorb the pressure, the burden on the other Profound Yellow cultivators on the battlefield was greatly reduced. Inspired by Li Fan, everyone managed to regain their composure.

And at this moment, from the rear of the main battlefield, a group of people was speeding towards the depths of the Tai Yuan Realm. Leading them was naturally Fang Dingge, the Sect Leader of the Great Dao Sect. He looked at Li Fan's posture, facing the siege of several people without faltering, even holding his own, and a gleam of admiration flashed in his eyes.

“This is… our Great Dao Sect’s [My Dao is Like Me]? I recall only recently teaching him this secret technique? How has he mastered it so proficiently?”

The Ten Sect Leaders were naturally well aware of the situation surrounding Li Fan, this shining new star on the Tai Yuan battlefield. Witnessing Li Fan single-handedly contend against more than ten Harmonious Dao cultivators and twenty God Transformation cultivators, they were all amazed. Although these Tai Yuan Harmonious Dao cultivators were only at the early stage of Harmonious Dao, Li Fan’s ability to achieve this undoubtedly proved his peerless combat strength.

Under the cover of the First Origin Sect's [Primordial Innate Great Formation], they bypassed the Tai Yuan Realm cultivators' reconnaissance. They were getting closer and closer to their destination, the Heavenly Art Palace.

Soon, a ninety-nine-story towering structure standing precariously on a cliff face appeared before their eyes.

“Everyone, the formation core is beneath this towering building, inside the mountain.”

“Once we enter the core of the towering building, this concealment formation will likely become ineffective. At that time, we will have to force our way in…”

Amidst Fang Dingge's warning, they had already infiltrated the Palace. Perhaps because most of their forces had been deployed to the battlefield, the defense personnel within the Heavenly Art Palace were much fewer than expected. However, the deeper they went into the core of the Palace, the more cultivators they inevitably encountered. Their good fortune ended here. As a piercing alarm rang out, dark red clouds gathered and enveloped the Palace.

The Tai Yuan cultivators who were fighting on the battlefield were instantly stunned. Then, they moved in unison, intending to withdraw from the battlefield and return.

Just then, the Horizontal Golden Chain appeared in the void. Thousands upon thousands of figures, charging out from the Profound Yellow Realm.

“Profound Yellow cultivators, heed my command! Delay the thieves at all costs!”

As if prepared, resounding announcements like rolling thunder spread across the battlefield. Seeing the reinforcements from the Profound Yellow Realm arrive, and understanding the Ten Sects' Sect Leaders' surprise attack plan, they realized they were not abandoned and victory seemed within reach. The Profound Yellow cultivators on the battlefield were instantly morale-boosted. In contrast, the Tai Yuan Realm cultivators appeared somewhat panicked. After all, the anomaly above the Palace clearly indicated an attack. If the Resurrection Furnace were to be destroyed, they would no longer be able to resurrect. Thus, they instinctively wanted to rush back to provide support. However, they quickly seemed to receive some notification. In an instant, they abandoned all thoughts of support and instead turned back, launching an even fiercer attack.

From afar, sounds of breaking through the air whistled, composing a roaring symphony. Countless figures, like a dark cloud pressing down, flew towards them at extreme speed.

“This… are all the Tai Yuan cultivators attacking us?”

Such a terrifying sight shocked everyone present. But the motivational effect from earlier was still present, and they firmly believed that as long as the Ten Sects' Sect Leaders took action, they could definitely turn the tide. The Profound Yellow cultivators collided with this rolling dark cloud with resolute faith. Explosions, wails, curses, the clash of metal… mixed with the heavy smell of blood. The battle for conquest reached its most intense moment.

However, looking at the twelve figures standing before them, Fang Dingge and his group involuntarily felt a sense of despair. Just moments ago, they had joined forces, sacrificing their own blood to unleash their strongest ultimate moves, and had already slain these twelve Harmonious Dao cultivators.

But just as they were about to advance with overwhelming joy, a storm swept through the empty space. Amidst the turmoil, the twelve figures reappeared. They seemed completely unharmed, and even their aura was stronger than before. Fang Dingge and the others’ faces were extremely grim, but with victory only one step away, they could hardly give up now.

“Everyone, let’s give it our all!”

Crimson light, like ripples, surged from Fang Dingge's body, charging forward again. “Great Dao is Like Me!”

All the divine abilities unleashed by the Tai Yuan Twelve Harmonious Dao cultivators were swept away and absorbed by this crimson light. Fang Dingge, who forcibly endured the combined attack, only had a slightly flushed complexion and suffered no serious injuries. The others, seizing this opportunity, unleashed their killing divine abilities. Giant sword shadows, splitting into two, then into ten thousand. They surrounded the Tai Yuan Twelve Harmonious Dao cultivators. Winds stirred, whipping up yellow sand, each grain of sand seeming to contain a sealed god or demon. The others all flew forward. But after only a few steps, the familiar storm descended again. One, two, three, four… The figures they had just killed reappeared out of thin air. Even their flesh and blood remnants lay quietly not far away. The Tai Yuan Twelve Harmonious Dao cultivators stood like an insurmountable wall, blocking the Profound Yellow group. With mocking expressions.

“Since they can revive, let’s kill them even faster!”

A three-legged furnace image quietly appeared in his hand. A flicker of heartache flashed in his eyes, and Fang Dingge tapped the furnace body. As milky white flames spewed out from the three-legged furnace, the twelve Harmonious Dao cultivators who had once again revived and blocked their path, even stronger than before, didn’t even have the slightest power to resist. They turned to ashes in the milky white flames.

Seizing the opportunity while the flames were still present, the Profound Yellow group pressed onward. This sudden assault achieved excellent results. As long as the final defensive restriction was broken, the formation core could be destroyed. The Ten Sects' group was filled with hope.

Just then, the rebirth storm struck again. This time, the gestation process took longer than before. And it seemed that Fang Dingge's activation of the Burning Dao Furnace had triggered some unexpected factors within the formation.

When the Tai Yuan Twelve Harmonious Dao cultivators stood tall once more, the breaths of the Ten Sects’ group inevitably became more rapid. This time, it was not just simple revival. Judging solely by their aura, these twelve individuals had become more than twice as strong as the last time they appeared. Moreover, they were all clad in some flowing, colorful defensive armor and magic treasures. They clearly weren't ordinary items.

“Sect Leader Fang…”

Fang Dingge gritted his teeth and remained silent. He released another burst of milky white flames.

Chapter 1540: All Heavenly Pride Bows Their Heads

“The idea is right, it’s just that the position is not correctly understood.” Li Fan commented thus. The great Dao starry sky he displayed on that thin plate was too far beyond the mortal world, even exceeding the limits of what cultivators in the Profound Yellow Realm could imagine. For ants on the ground, they naturally couldn't distinguish the difference between the first heaven and the thirty-third heaven. That old Daoist thought he had missed out on a method to become an immortal. He never imagined it was a highway straight to the other shore!

“He still retains his unique arrogance. Perhaps when he eventually perishes at the end of his life, he will regret it immensely,” Li Fan shook his head slightly. For Li Fan, walking his own Great Dao and learning from other powerful beings were not mutually exclusive. He could learn the transformation of truth and falsehood from Huan Zhen, comprehend the infinite immortal laws from the Mountains and Seas, and study the Great Dao of Longevity from Duke Shou Qiu. However, none of this prevented Li Fan from ultimately forging his own path. Even the Sect Leaders of the Ten Sects were, in Li Fan's eyes, merely insignificant ants in the drops of the River of Time, not worthy of excessive attention. Li Fan cared more about the grand play he had meticulously orchestrated.

As Li Fan’s fingers subtly moved, the scales of victory gradually tipped towards the Tai Yuan Realm. The “abnormal malfunction” of the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace seemed to have finally been repaired, and its resurrection efficiency was even better than before. Although he didn't understand the reason for such a bizarre phenomenon, it did not hinder the Tai Yuan Realm cultivators from seizing this excellent opportunity to counterattack swiftly and secure victory.

The Profound Yellow cultivators on the battlefield immediately felt the pressure. In the previous six months, the Tai Yuan Realm cultivators’ attacks usually lasted for five to six days before temporarily retreating. However, this attack was unprecedentedly fierce. Enemies died in waves, but they seemed inexhaustible. There were even instances where the same person’s two or three incomplete corpses appeared on the same battlefield, which was deeply unsettling. The territories painstakingly occupied by the Profound Yellow Realm through countless sacrifices were lost inch by inch. The surviving Profound Yellow Realm cultivators were gradually compressed into the innermost defensive perimeter.

It seemed that after successive battles lasting dozens of days, the Tai Yuan Realm forces had also reached their limit. A rare moment of tranquility descended upon the battlefield, and all the Profound Yellow soldiers seized this last chance to breathe and recover their strength. However, under such high-pressure circumstances, not a shred of despair emerged in their minds. Only a firm belief remained: to fight to the death when the enemy charged again soon.

In the center of the Profound Yellow formation, Qu Yixing, the Sect Leader of the First Origin Sect, sat cross-legged in mid-air with a solemn expression. Above his head, the Five Elements energy twined with Yin and Yang essence, rotating rapidly like a Tai Chi diagram. Mysterious fluctuations emanated from this vortex, influencing and altering the mindset of the Profound Yellow cultivators on the battlefield.

“Brother Yixing’s method is ingenious, but it’s not a long-term solution,” Situ Yao said with a heavy heart. “It can last for another month at most. Otherwise, they will all turn into monsters who have completely lost their minds, with only killing in their heads.”

“A month… I don't think the situation can even hold for that long. Perhaps everyone should make a decision sooner,” said Fang Dingge, the Sect Leader of Great Dao Sect. “I have already asked Stone Mother to perform a hundred trillion calculations. There is a 56% probability of success. With the advantage on our side, why not take a gamble!”

A 56% probability seemed like a sure victory to Fang Dingge. No one present responded.

“Of course, if any of you are confident that you can sever the Horizontal Golden Chain while ensuring the safety of the Profound Yellow Realm, you can disregard my plan,” Fang Dingge’s sharp gaze swept across everyone.

But if it’s just the safety of the Ten Sects, perhaps that can be achieved.” After a moment of silence, the one who spoke was a wrinkled yellow paper effigy. The paper effigy regarded Fang Dingge with a strange and distorted expression, neither smiling nor crying.

“If you continue like this, don’t blame my Burning Dao Furnace for being merciless!”

Faced with Fang Dingge’s threat, Daoist Yijue of the Tribulation Crossing Sect remained unfazed. He chuckled and said, “Sect Leader Fang, you misunderstand. Who in this world can always win?”

This old Daoist is leaving~” Daoist Yijue chuckled with an unclear meaning. The originally vivid expression on the paper effigy instantly froze, then slowly drifted to the ground. Daoist Yijue of the Tribulation Crossing Sect had transformed into the most ordinary piece of paper.

Situ Yao laughed heartily and quickly interjected, “The Ten Sects have always been united. We have experienced tribulations far more dangerous than this in the past, so why should we ruin our camaraderie over this matter?”

Fang Dingge did not concede at all, “Times have changed. After several major battles, how much energy is left in the immortal artifacts you all possess? Without immortal spiritual energy, what difference are they from scrap metal? Relying on these immortal treasures, we have been lucky enough to survive in this starry sky. In the future, when we can no longer use these immortal artifacts, where will we go?”

The leaders of the Ten Sects argued endlessly. Finally, a female cultivator clad in black gauze, with a graceful figure but a voice like tearing metal, ended their argument.

Yet, you turn out to be indecisive and deceitful cowards.” Although the words were harsh, they included himself. The others merely showed awkward expressions and couldn't retort.

“But we can’t blame you. The more power one wields, the more considerations one has. Such as sects, the world, and all beings…”

“It’s far less enjoyable than when I was alone and roamed the world freely!” Xiahou Yan said calmly. It seemed to evoke memories of the past, and the scene momentarily fell silent.

Xiahou Yan broke the silence, “Consider it. Although the [Two Part Immortal Seed] is strange, it can divide all of us into two without any loss. It provides one more option, one more retreat, one more chance at survival.”

“It shouldn’t have reached such a severe point yet,” Jiang Yixing and the others still did not agree with Xiahou Yan’s opinion. “Although the Two Part Immortal Seed is immensely mystical, its side effects are truly too great. We used it once back then, and it took almost a hundred years to digest it. Lu Chenghong and Yijue from the Tribulation Crossing Sect, who were still relatively normal back then, have all become the madmen they are now…”

“But we ultimately won, didn’t we? And those three immortal cultivation worlds have long turned to dust. Since we could endure it once, we can endure it a second time,” Xiahou Yan insisted. Only when the doubtful gazes fell upon him did Xiahou Yan realize he had lost his composure. He then let out a cold snort and fell silent.

Another long period of silence. Situ Yao drained his gourd of wine and said impatiently, “I think Brother Dingge’s plan is feasible. I witnessed the entire process of Stone Mother’s deduction. It offers some hope for ending the Tai Yuan Realm war.”

“If you are unwilling, then let me do it.”

“Death is just death, after all. When has Situ Yao ever been afraid of death!”

Chapter 1541: Xuanhuang Gives Birth to True Immortal

Within the Profound Yellow Realm, there was first a deathly silence, then a great uproar.

"What exactly is happening?"

"Can he still fight? Give up, it's too tragic. There's no hope of winning."

"Where are the cowards of the Ten Sects! Let me in, I want to go to the Primordial Realm and die alongside the God of War!"

...

Most cultivators in the Profound Yellow Realm only saw "Li Ping" stand up once more, seemingly intending to continue the fight. Only a very few understood the meaning behind the inexplicable aura erupting from Li Ping.

They were all aghast, rising to their feet with a clamor.

"Sect Leader Fang, if I'm not mistaken, that is..." Boundless Prison Lord Xiahou Yan asked with some disbelief.

Fang Dingge, too, lost his former composure, scrutinizing for a long time with an air of suspicion, fearful he might be mistaken.

But as the distorted scene above the sky-screen became more pronounced, he finally confirmed: "A breakthrough. It's actually a sign of a breakthrough?"

"He's clearly already at the Harmonious Dao peak; if he takes another step..."

Fang Dingge's mouth hung open, utterly astonished.

"Immortal?"

The few individuals in the hall looked at each other, their hearts filled with shock and incomprehension.

However, they quickly and simultaneously looked up, fearful of missing any detail.

Above the sky-screen, the distorted ripples grew fiercer, all swirling around Li Ping's standing figure.

It was like a stone dropped into a vast lake, causing circles of turbulence on the surface.

The Primordial Realm cultivators, who had been silently grieving, also noticed this anomaly. Disregarding everything else, they immediately launched another attack.

Alas, around Li Fan, a tumultuous storm had risen.

Any living being attempting to approach was inevitably swept up by the fierce winds, spinning uncontrollably in the air like ants. Even Harmonious Dao cultivators were no exception!

Even with their full might, they could not approach by an inch, let alone harm Li Fan.

At the very center of the storm, Li Fan's vitality and aura seemed to climb incessantly, even transmitting through the Transverse Golden Lock to the Profound Yellow Realm.

All living beings gazing at the figure in the storm's core instinctively felt a sense of oppression, compelled to prostrate themselves in worship.

Though they didn't understand why, they knew something monumental was about to happen.

The Profound Yellow Realm fell into a deathly silence. In the Primordial Realm, all cultivators, fueled by the rising fear in their hearts, made a final struggle, attempting to hinder Li Fan's transformation.

Alas, it was ultimately futile.

When the storm finally subsided, Li Fan's unharmed body reappeared before everyone.

Cleansed of the bloody stench from his previous continuous battles, he was ethereal and elegant, like a celestial being.

"Immortal!"

All beings of both realms who saw Li Fan simultaneously had this word leap into their minds.

Their bodies trembled uncontrollably.

Since the severance of the Immortal Path, there had been no True Immortal in the world for tens of thousands of years.

Unexpectedly, today, an Immortal was born before the eyes of all!

The beings of the Profound Yellow Realm could not help but prostrate themselves, worshipping with fervor.

And the cultivators of the Primordial Realm, though still fearful, still attacked Li Fan, this "Immortal," without a trace of fear of death.

However, once Li Fan achieved enlightenment, the battlefield situation immediately underwent an earth-shattering change.

The overwhelming divine abilities and magic spells of the Primordial Realm cultivators were originally impossible for Li Fan to evade.

But now, he merely stretched out his hand silently towards the front.

Countless rays of promised colorful light were all deflected and absorbed into his palm.

Then, he lightly blew a breath.

All these released killing moves were instantly reflected back, assaulting their casters.

Caught off guard, the Primordial Realm cultivators suffered heavy losses. Especially as they were all gathered together, unleashing their divine abilities in concert, leading to massive casualties.

The area around Li Fan, which had been tightly besieged, was now directly cleared out after the divine abilities backfired.

If Li Fan's tactic of "using their own methods against them" had not instilled much fear in the Primordial Realm cultivators, then what happened next plunged even these infinitely resurrecting cultivators into deep despair.

Li Fan gently raised his left hand upwards.

Scattered throughout the battlefield, the relics of the Profound Yellow cultivators seemed to respond, flying into the sky.

As if summoned, illusory figures emerged from these relics.

These were precisely their original owners, the cultivators of the Profound Yellow Realm who had fallen in battle!

Even with their faces not perfectly clear, the beings of the Profound Yellow Realm recognized these resurrected friends and family. Many wept uncontrollably on the spot.

The illusory figures of the Profound Yellow warriors all saluted Li Fan respectfully. Then, gripping their weapons, they boldly charged towards the Primordial Realm cultivators.

Reality and illusion, the forces of the two realms collided fiercely once more.

This time, the dynamics of attack and defense had reversed!

It must be remembered that, whether in overall scale or average combat power, the Primordial Realm cultivators were far inferior to those of the Profound Yellow Realm. It was only by relying on the infinite resurrection ability of the Primordial Rebirth Furnace that they had pushed the Profound Yellow Realm to its current desperate situation.

But now...

When the Primordial Realm cultivators exerted their full strength to shatter a Profound Yellow cultivator's illusory figure.

A stream of light flew from the centrally-commanding Li Fan, and just a moment later, those illusory figures reappeared. The "resurrected" Profound Yellow cultivators instantly caught their dumbfounded enemies off guard and slaughtered them.

Then, they charged towards other opponents on the battlefield.

Finally tasting their adversary's greatest reliance, the Profound Yellow cultivators, as if emboldened a hundredfold, slowly forced the Primordial Realm cultivators back.

The illusory figures who died in battle would soon be replenished by Li Fan.

On the battlefield, streaks of light continuously flashed, like a grand meteor shower blooming in the sky above the Primordial Realm.

When the meteor shower ended, the Primordial Realm cultivators who had gathered nearby were either dead or had fled in panic.

"Kill!"

Li Fan did not stop there; he pointed his sword forward and uttered only this single word.

The direction his sword pointed was precisely the Heavenly Art Palace, where the Primordial Rebirth Furnace was located!

Thus, countless streams of light slowly pushed deeper into the Primordial Realm.

Irresistible, unstoppable.

Anyone who stood before this surging torrent would be instantly torn to pieces.

This breathtaking scene stirred the blood of countless beings watching from the Profound Yellow Realm.

They yearned to participate.

Only a handful of individuals could see through the passion and excitement of the scene to the true mysteries hidden beneath.

Although the resurrected Profound Yellow cultivators were all illusory figures, the divine abilities and magic spells they unleashed undoubtedly possessed true destructive power.

On the Primordial battlefield, there were more than hundreds of thousands of cultivators resurrected from death.

And "Li Ping" alone was able to sustain their consumption?

As if thinking of something, Fang Dingge completely lost himself, no longer able to conceal the shock in his heart, murmuring, "Infinite, the infinite of an Immortal. Could it be that he truly is an Immortal?"

All cultivators who had any understanding of a True Immortal's nature displayed the same reaction as Fang Dingge at this moment.

And amidst this shock, Li Fan had already led a million illusory figures, pushing step by step towards the Heavenly Art Palace.

Before this magnificent army of millions, the greatest combat advantage of the Primordial Realm no longer existed.

You can resurrect, but I resurrect even faster than you.

You have an unyielding will, your commands are obeyed, and you won't collapse even in desperation. But my warriors don't even have subjective will; they are merely the existing obsession for revenge.

...

Although Immortal spiritual energy is infinite, the operating efficiency of an Immortal Formation has its limits.

After continuous, prolonged resurrections, the pressure on the ancient defensive Immortal Formation of the Primordial Realm finally reached its critical point.

Visibly, the speed at which Primordial Realm cultivators were resurrected slowed significantly.

A wave of cheers erupted from the Profound Yellow Realm.

However, the expressions on the faces of the several Ten Sects' leaders and elites who had entered the Heavenly Art Palace remained grave.

The combat power displayed by "Li Ping," this Half-Immortal, had indeed exceeded their imagination. But the Immortal Formation deep within the Palace was equally despairing.

However, Li Ping's next action once again surprised them.

Instead of leading his forces into the Palace,

he unleashed a sword strike directly at the ninety-nine-story towering structure on the mountain peak.

A dazzling light illuminated the entire sky, blinding all onlookers.

A terrifying roar, like continuous thunder, echoed through the heavens.

The immense tremor even passed through the distant space-time, reaching the Profound Yellow Realm.

Both worlds trembled under the sword light unleashed by Li Fan.

When sight was restored, the Heavenly Art Palace and the Primordial Realm cultivators had all disappeared.

Only a deep, bottomless gully, dark and profound, remained embedded in the earth.

Only Li Fan's ethereal figure stood amidst it.

And...

A strange tripod cauldron in his hand.

Silence once again enveloped heaven and earth.

"Is this the might of a True Immortal?"

All living beings' minds went blank, utterly astounded by the immense power of the True Immortal's single sword strike.

But the Ten Sects' members, after recovering from their shock, thought of more.

With a True Immortal descended, how should the Ten Sects conduct themselves from now on?

This question seemed to have no other answer.

Even if all the Ten Sects' cultivators combined, they probably wouldn't be a match for this True Immortal. Even deploying all their remaining immortal artifacts might not yield any advantage.

They just didn't know if this True Immortal would blame them for their previous abandonment.

The hearts of the Ten Sects were troubled.

In the Primordial Realm, another anomaly occurred.

The tripod cauldron tightly held in Li Fan's hand suddenly erupted with a heaven-piercing, multicolored auspicious light.

Illuminating the entire horizon of the Primordial Realm.

Li Fan looked at the Profound Yellow illusory figures below, who had completed their mission of revenge and seemed a little lost.

Then, he smiled faintly.

The multicolored auspicious light pouring from the cauldron, like waterfalls, cascaded upon them.

After receiving the infusion from the Primordial Rebirth Furnace, a remarkably significant change began to occur in the million Profound Yellow illusory figures.

Their ethereal faces gradually cleared.

Their faint outlines solidified.

The vitality unique to living beings emerged in these illusory figures.

They...

Were truly coming back from the dead, undergoing resurrection!

Even though they had experienced so much astonishing phenomena today, the beings of the Profound Yellow Realm were still overjoyed when they witnessed this scene.

Especially when they saw their deceased friends and family, after being resurrected, disbelievingly examining their bodies, also shedding tears of extreme joy.

A million Profound Yellow warriors, risen from the dead, wept with joy.

After the initial exhilaration, they quickly reacted.

They prostrated themselves before the True Immortal above them, who had saved them and bestowed new life.

However, after a long time, the True Immortal remained motionless.

The cultivators couldn't help but look up.

And witnessed a scene that would forever be etched in their memories.

Dots of starlight began to emerge from the True Immortal's figure.

As a gentle breeze blew, these starlights floated away from the True Immortal.

At first, there were only几十 hundred points of starlight.

Then, more and more.

Like stars from the Nine Heavens, falling upon the mortal world.

High in the sky, when the stars filled the heavens, the True Immortal was no longer to be seen.

The beings of both realms collectively fell into a daze.

It took half a day for them to understand what had happened.

Then, sounds of pain and wailing echoed throughout both realms.

Lasting endlessly.

...

A month later.

The war that changed the fate of the Profound Yellow Realm had long since ended, but the beings of the Profound Yellow Realm still had not emerged from their grief.

Without the infinitely regenerating enemy, the Profound Yellow Realm successfully occupied the Primordial Realm.

Having successfully opened up another safe habitat for themselves at the ends of the stars, the threat of the Immortal Ruins outside the Profound Yellow Realm slowly began to become known to the world.

However, compared to the Immortal Ruins, the beings of the Profound Yellow Realm were more concerned about what had happened to the [Profound Yellow True Immortal].

After deductions by the Ten Sects' leaders, combined with observations of the scene, a preliminary conclusion was reached.

The Immortal Path was severed; this was an unchangeable fact. The Immortal attained by "Li Ping" was not a True Immortal in the true sense.

It was merely because of his unparalleled talent that he forcibly pushed himself into a realm between Harmonious Dao and True Immortal, perhaps best called a Half-Immortal.

If he had become a True Immortal, he might have been able to reverse his grievous injuries and death.

Alas...

Before his demise, he had held on.

He not only led his forces to enact revenge on the Primordial Realm.

He even utilized the Primordial Rebirth Furnace to resurrect as many of the fallen Profound Yellow cultivators as possible.

However, in the end, he could not defy the will of Heaven and passed away.

Compared to a living True Immortal, this True Immortal who sacrificed himself to save the beings of the Profound Yellow Realm would undoubtedly be remembered more profoundly.

Every household erected commemorative tablets and statues for the [Profound Yellow True Immortal], burning incense and offering prayers.

Even within the large and small immortal cultivation sects, halls dedicated to the Profound Yellow True Immortal were erected.

There were originally a few dissenting voices, but they quickly disappeared.

Though the True Immortal had passed, his lingering influence remained, long and unceasing.

The improved versions of the Ten Sects' ultimate techniques, left under Li Fan's pillow, were also found.

They were listed as top-secret by the Ten Sects.

The day these ultimate techniques were returned to the Profound Yellow Realm, the leaders of the Ten Sects gathered to discuss and study them.

"As expected of one capable of attaining True Immortalhood, these improved divine abilities even surpass our sect's secret core techniques..."

The Ten Sects' members were all filled with admiration.

In the common populace, however, rumors secretly spread.

Those who attain the Grand Dao Scripture can achieve True Immortalhood!

Chapter 1542: The Identity of the Great Heavenly Venerate

Within the Profound Yellow Realm, a deathly silence first descended, followed by a great uproar.

"What exactly is happening?"

"Can he still fight? Give up, it's too tragic. There's no hope of winning."

"Where are the cowards of the Ten Sects! Let me in, I want to go to the Primordial Realm and die alongside the God of War!"

...

Most cultivators in the Profound Yellow Realm only saw "Li Ping" stand up once more, seemingly intending to continue the fight. Only a very few understood the meaning behind the inexplicable aura erupting from Li Ping's body.

They were all aghast, rising to their feet with a clamor.

"Sect Leader Fang, if I'm not mistaken, that is..." Boundless Prison Lord Xiahou Yan asked with some disbelief.

Fang Dingge, too, had lost his former composure, scrutinizing for a long time with an air of suspicion, fearful he might be mistaken.

But as the distorted scene above the sky screen became more pronounced, he finally confirmed: "A breakthrough. It's actually a sign of a breakthrough?"

"He's clearly already at the Harmonious Dao peak; if he takes another step..."

Fang Dingge's mouth hung open, utterly astonished.

"Immortal?"

The few individuals in the hall looked at each other, their hearts filled with shock and incomprehension.

However, they quickly and simultaneously looked up, fearful of missing any detail.

Above the sky screen, the distorted ripples grew fiercer, all swirling around Li Ping's standing figure.

It was like a stone dropped into a vast lake, causing circles of turbulence on the surface.

The Primordial Realm cultivators, who had been silently grieving, also noticed this anomaly. Disregarding everything else, they immediately launched another attack.

Alas, around Li Fan, a tumultuous storm had risen.

Any living being attempting to approach was inevitably swept up by the fierce winds, spinning uncontrollably in the air like ants. Even Harmonious Dao cultivators were no exception!

Even with their full might, they could not approach by an inch, let alone harm Li Fan.

At the very center of the storm, Li Fan's vitality and aura seemed to climb incessantly, even transmitting through the Transverse Golden Lock to the Profound Yellow Realm.

All living beings gazing at the figure in the storm's core instinctively felt a sense of oppression, compelled to prostrate themselves in worship.

Though they didn't understand why, they knew something monumental was about to happen.

The Profound Yellow Realm fell into a deathly silence. In the Primordial Realm, all cultivators, fueled by the rising fear in their hearts, made a final struggle, attempting to hinder Li Fan's transformation.

Only alas, it was ultimately futile.

When the storm finally subsided, Li Fan's unharmed body reappeared before everyone.

Cleansed of the bloody stench from his previous continuous battles, he was ethereal and elegant, like a celestial being.

"Immortal!"

All beings of both realms who saw Li Fan simultaneously had this word leap into their minds.

Their bodies trembled uncontrollably.

Since the severance of the Immortal Path, there had been no True Immortal in the world for tens of thousands of years.

Unexpectedly, today, an Immortal was born before the eyes of all!

The beings of the Profound Yellow Realm could not help but prostrate themselves, worshipping with fervor.

And the cultivators of the Primordial Realm, though still fearful, still attacked Li Fan, this "Immortal," without a trace of fear of death.

However, once Li Fan achieved enlightenment, the battlefield situation immediately underwent an earth-shattering change.

The overwhelming divine abilities and magic spells of the Primordial Realm cultivators were originally impossible for Li Fan to evade.

But now, he merely stretched out his hand silently towards the front.

Countless rays of promised colorful light were all deflected and absorbed into his palm.

Then, he lightly blew a breath.

All these unleashed killing moves were instantly reflected back, assaulting their casters.

Caught off guard, the Primordial Realm cultivators suffered heavy losses. Especially as they were all gathered together, unleashing their divine abilities in concert, leading to massive casualties.

The area around Li Fan, which had been tightly besieged, was now directly cleared out after the divine abilities backfired.

If Li Fan's tactic of "using their own methods against them" had not instilled much fear in the Primordial Realm cultivators, then what happened next plunged even these infinitely resurrecting cultivators into deep despair.

Li Fan gently raised his left hand upwards.

Scattered throughout the battlefield, the relics of the Profound Yellow cultivators seemed to respond, flying into the sky.

As if summoned, illusory figures emerged from these relics.

These were precisely their original owners, the cultivators of the Profound Yellow Realm who had fallen in battle!

Even with their faces not perfectly clear, the beings of the Profound Yellow Realm recognized these resurrected friends and family. Many wept uncontrollably on the spot.

The illusory figures of the Profound Yellow warriors all saluted Li Fan respectfully. Then, gripping their weapons, they boldly charged towards the Primordial Realm cultivators.

Reality and illusion, the forces of the two realms collided fiercely once more.

This time, the dynamics of attack and defense had reversed!

It must be remembered that, whether in overall scale or average combat power, the Primordial Realm cultivators were far inferior to those of the Profound Yellow Realm. It was only by relying on the infinite resurrection ability of the Primordial Rebirth Furnace that they had pushed the Profound Yellow Realm to its current desperate situation.

But now...

When the Primordial Realm cultivators exerted their full strength to shatter a Profound Yellow cultivator's illusory figure.

A stream of light flew from the centrally-commanding Li Fan, and just a moment later, those illusory figures reappeared. The "resurrected" Profound Yellow cultivators instantly caught their dumbfounded enemies off guard and slaughtered them.

Then, they charged towards other opponents on the battlefield.

Finally tasting their adversary's greatest reliance, the Profound Yellow cultivators, as if emboldened a hundredfold, slowly forced the Primordial Realm cultivators back.

The illusory figures who died in battle would soon be replenished by Li Fan.

On the battlefield, streaks of light continuously flashed, like a grand meteor shower blooming in the sky above the Primordial Realm.

When the meteor shower ended, the Primordial Realm cultivators who had gathered nearby were either dead or had fled in panic.

"Kill!"

Li Fan did not stop there; he pointed his sword forward and uttered only this single word.

The direction his sword pointed was precisely the Heavenly Art Palace, where the Primordial Rebirth Furnace was located!

Thus, countless streams of light slowly pushed deeper into the Primordial Realm.

Irresistible, unstoppable.

Anyone who stood before this surging torrent would be instantly torn to pieces.

They yearned to participate.

Only a handful of individuals could see through the passion and excitement of the scene to the true mysteries hidden beneath.

Chapter 1543: The Final Chapter of the Fable

Those who obtain the Supreme Dao Scripture can attain true immortality!

This statement was not mere fantasy but had a solid basis.

The foundation was none other than the [Profound Yellow True Immortal] who now possessed immense prestige in the Profound Yellow Realm!

One must understand that the Profound Yellow True Immortal did not appear out of thin air. He had progressed from a mere Foundation Establishment cultivator to the realm of a true immortal, with his entire growth trajectory traceable.

Therefore, after discovering this fact, people were even more astonished.

For the Profound Yellow True Immortal had only taken a few short years to complete the journey from mortal to immortal!

Although the Ten Sects had officially declared that this was due to his exceptionally special physique, constantly evolving and regenerating through battles, it was still difficult to quell the doubts in some hearts.

Even within the Ten Sects, meticulous investigations began in secret into the True Immortal's background before his rise.

No matter how composed the chief disciple of Evergreen Valley was, he could not hide himself from the methods of the Ten Sects. Consequently, his past dealings with the True Immortal were exposed to everyone.

"Supreme Dao Scripture..."

Jiang Yingyue of the Supreme Sect, responsible for the secret investigation, looked at another familiar thin plate in her hand, her expression unreadable.

"It's exactly the same as the one in my mind."

"According to Baili Shan, he also possessed a similar thin plate during his lifetime. No wonder I always felt there was something indescribably strange about him. So that's how it is..."

"A special constitution, coupled with the guidance of the [Supreme Dao Scripture]. Was that how he achieved this unprecedented feat of ascending to immortality?" Jiang Yingyue clenched the thin plate, a hint of determination flashing in her eyes.

Since that individual could ascend to the immortal realm, she too could achieve it.

Perhaps not as quickly...

After ruthlessly killing Baili Shan to safeguard the secret as much as possible, Jiang Yingyue had just brought the thin plate back to her sect when she received her Sect Leader's summons.

"The Supreme Dao Scripture concerns the future path of the Profound Yellow Realm. It must be shared by the Ten Sects."

The old Daoist, who had originally declined the brilliant starry sky of the Great Dao, choosing to forge his own path, finally couldn't maintain his resolve after witnessing Li Ping's ascension to immortality in just a few years.

Jiang Yingyue felt a sense of inexplicable loss, yet also relief.

Carrying the captured thin plates of the Supreme Dao Scripture, she slowly departed.

From then on, the Supreme Dao Scripture became a treasure shared by the Ten Sects. Furthermore, combined with the experiences of Jiang Yingyue and others, the Ten Sects concluded that other thin plates might still be scattered in the outside world.

Regardless of the reason, the Ten Sects could not stand by and allow such a supreme treasure as the Supreme Dao Scripture to fall into the hands of others. Therefore, a secret organization was formed within the Ten Sects to search for them covertly.

For three years after the great war subsided, the Profound Yellow Realm remained peaceful.

Even though the Profound Yellow True Immortal had resurrected most of the cultivators who died on the Tai Yuan battlefield, the overall losses of the Profound Yellow Realm were not particularly severe. However, that great battle had undoubtedly left an extremely profound psychological scar on the cultivators, requiring time to heal.

The atmosphere between the Ten Sects and the Myriad Immortal Alliance, which had been growing tense, temporarily eased due to their shared experience fighting alongside each other on the Tai Yuan battlefield.

More importantly, with the successful occupation of the Tai Yuan Realm, a new gateway to another part of the starry sky was opened. The Profound Yellow Realm was no longer a trapped Griever from which there was no escape. The outside starry sky held infinite possibilities.

The conflict between the two sides was no longer irreconcilable.

The River of Time, at this temporal node, took a sharp turn, rushing towards a completely different trajectory.

And amidst the surging waves caused by the river's diversion, a figure struggled desperately.

If not for the faint threads appearing in the river, tightly entwining him, he would have long been swallowed by the overwhelming power of time.

"What is the Way of Contra-Flow? How to define front and back, forward and reverse, smooth and contrary? Is the end of this river predetermined, or are there still different outcomes?..."

Amidst the surging waves, Li Fan tried desperately to maintain his form, finding solace in suffering and meditating on the Dao.

Although his grand performance as a "lying-deceiving" play to earn the admiration of countless beings in both realms had been satisfying, the price was also agonizing.

The River of Time, having completely flowed in a different direction, was constantly moving away from its original trajectory.

Thus, the backlash was incessant.

It was even a hundred times more intense than the waves Li Fan encountered when he traveled upstream in the river of time previously.

The reason was that previously, he had mostly been in the same stream. Now, Li Fan's actions had pushed him horizontally to another end of the River of Time.

If going upstream before was "contra-flow," then now it was "crossing."

Fortunately, his meticulously orchestrated play was so brilliant that it deeply imprinted itself in the minds of all beings in the Profound Yellow Realm. With so many sufficient and weighty anchor points, no matter how strong the waves, as long as this branch of the River of Time remained, and as long as the Profound Yellow Realm was not completely destroyed.

It would temporarily guarantee Li Fan's safety within this segment of the River of Time.

"This is what is meant by 'immovable for ten thousand generations, eternal true name'!"

From now on, no matter what choice he made, whether to continue upstream or remain still, he had a safe point to establish himself.

Just as Great Xuan was to the Profound Yellow Realm, the Profound Yellow Realm was to the Darkest Sea, and the realm within the High Wall was to the Primordial Possibility.

Of course, given the general moral standards of Profound Yellow cultivators, and the high probability of future cataclysmic changes, Li Fan did not expect this stable anchor point to remain perfectly preserved forever.

Therefore, in addition to the name "[Profound Yellow True Immortal]," he also left behind the [Supreme Dao Scripture] as a backup anchor point for emergencies.

Moreover, besides the beings of the Profound Yellow Realm, there was also the Tai Yuan Realm.

In that earth-shattering white sword light, Li Fan had not destroyed all the Tai Yuan cultivators and the Resurrection Furnace.

Instead, he had temporarily sealed them all in the depths of that extremely deep fissure.

Adoration from the masses was an anchor point; desperate fear was also an anchor point.

Li Fan would naturally not waste them.

On the contrary, slaughtering them would be of no benefit to Li Fan.

With the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace, the Tai Yuan cultivators who could repeatedly resurrect and inherit the memories of their past lives were destined to be more suitable anchor carriers than the Profound Yellow cultivators.

Perhaps many years later, as time passed, the renown of the Profound Yellow True Immortal would gradually be forgotten by the beings of the Profound Yellow Realm. The statues erected and worshiped everywhere would eventually be neglected.

But his heroic figure, who, with one sword, led the masses to counterattack and overturn Tai Yuan in a desperate situation, would be forever etched in the hearts of those Tai Yuan cultivators. Even if they died, they could not erase it.

It took another two years, a total of five years, for Li Fan to barely stabilize himself amidst the turbulent currents of the altered River of Time.

Stepping onto solid ground back in reality, Li Fan had a completely different feeling than before.

No longer like a rootless duckweed, connected only by a few anchor points. He was deeply rooted within the river, becoming a part of this spacetime.

"As long as enough anchor points are established, one can shed the identity of an illegal immigrant and become one of our own," Li Fan realized.

The benefits of completely integrating into this spacetime were obvious.

His cultivation had almost returned to its pre-upstream level, and even his comprehension of the Great Dao had been completely recalibrated by the constant scouring of the temporal tides in this period.

Li Fan had a premonition.

The Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul, the Transformation of True and False... and other abilities that were once close to him would soon be fully reproducible in this period of spacetime.
