In great spirits, Li Fan did not return to the Profound Yellow Realm immediately.

Instead, he looked at the fissure he had cut with his sword beneath him.

In five years, the Ten Sects had completely sealed off this area and had even attempted multiple times to probe the fissure's interior.

But the sealing techniques Li Fan had employed before falling into the river's current were not something the Immortal Dao Ten Sects could break through.

The people of the Ten Sects were destined to return empty-handed.

"Besides the Immortal Dao Ten Sects..."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, flipping through the images recorded by the array.

The screen flickered rapidly, and when a figure appeared, it suddenly stopped.

"Found you, Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable!" A hint of excitement flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

As Li Fan had expected.

After the path to immortality was broken, a true immortal inexplicably descended. This was unbelievable for any cultivator, especially for those with higher cultivation, closer to the realm of true immortals, who would undoubtedly be incredibly curious.

The Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable, who held an official position in the immortal realm, was even more so.

Therefore, he was willing to personally travel to the Tai Yuan Realm, despite the immense danger, hoping to glean some understanding from the traces left by the true immortal.

However, he never expected to be captured by the methods Li Fan had set up.

Even though this Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable instinctively concealed herself, she could not escape Li Fan's surveillance array.

Wearing a plain, elegant pink dress, with a thin veil covering her face. A small red plum blossom-shaped scar at the corner of her temple.

Li Fan was certain that this was the Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable who had mysteriously disappeared from Profound Yellow history.

Similarly, Li Fan felt a strange sense of familiarity towards her.

"It's not that I've truly faced her, but in whose memory..."

After some recollection, Li Fan finally remembered.

The figure before him overlapped with Bai Sensei's mortal lover in Ningyuan City.

It was precisely because his lover tragically died in the battle between Zhang Qianmo and Song Hesong, the rebellious disciple of the Purple Heavens Sect, that Bai Sensei embarked on his subsequent cultivation path.

"It seems likely that Song Hesong's inexplicable rebellion was also influenced by this Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable's guidance. What a Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable, resorting to such despicable means," Li Fan sneered inwardly.

However, he could also understand.

As she held the position of Grand Celestial Venerable, even if she wanted to escape, she couldn't simply abdicate. At the very least, she had to find a suitable "successor."

And she couldn't simply appoint one; she had to find someone who met all the requirements for succeeding the Grand Celestial Venerable.

Su Bai, perhaps, was the most suitable candidate she had secretly identified.

"Indeed, there are no coincidences in this world. Even if Su Bai had exceptional talent and could instantly transform from mortal to Nascent Soul and then to Harmonious Dao within days, the Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable is not someone who can be chosen based solely on talent and cultivation."

Just like the succession of the Nameless True Immortal.

Su Bai's succession was also filled with the shadow of manipulation.

"Perhaps Su Bai had a faint inkling of this himself. But precisely because the guide was his mortal beloved, he was willing to bear it all silently." Recalling the fragmented memories he had glimpsed in the Profound Yellow ill will and Su Bai's eternal lingering thoughts, Li Fan couldn't help but think so.

Shaking his head, Li Fan destroyed all the recorded images.

Taking a step forward, he arrived at the very bottom of the fissure.

Where the Tai Yuan cultivators were imprisoned.

For the Tai Yuan cultivators, death was not a terrible thing. It was the inability to live or die that was terrible.

The torment they had endured over these five years surpassed their past experiences a hundredfold. Even dying repeatedly in battle was far less painful than this.

Trapped within a small space, unable to move half a step.

A place devoid of sunlight, filled with deathly silence.

All methods were exhausted, yet the restriction could not be broken. Even if they committed suicide in despair, they would immediately be resurrected by the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace above.

Compared to the battlefield, this place seemed to be the true eternal purgatory.

Li Fan's arrival did not alarm anyone.

Looking at the overall condition of the Tai Yuan cultivators below, he frowned slightly.

Li Fan's fundamental goal was to forge an anchor point from their fear.

However, Li Fan discovered that the Tai Yuan cultivators' fear of him was gradually diminishing in such a situation.

"This is not a good thing."

"We need to remind them from time to time."

Li Fan gently pointed towards the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace in the sky.

A radiance suddenly bloomed, illuminating the dark, deep space.

In the radiance of a great sun, the Tai Yuan cultivators seemed to see Li Fan's god-like figure, sword in hand, once more.

As if returning to the battlefield of yesteryear, the once lifeless, confined space was suddenly filled with waves of fear and despairing screams.

Li Fan nodded with satisfaction.

He then flashed into the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace in the sky.

Overseer, Repair Officer.

These two immortal servants responsible for the Tai Yuan Realm's protective formation did not attack Li Fan upon seeing him.

Instead, they respectfully knelt and bowed.

It was acknowledged that, purely based on strength, the previous Harmonious Dao stage Li Fan was not a match for these two immortal servants.

But even the most powerful immortal servant was merely a servant.

As a disciple of Shou Qiu and the successor of Tai Tian Di's legacy, Li Fan had numerous methods to directly gain control of them.

This was also why they, the immortal servants, had never appeared from beginning to end, even when the Tai Yuan Realm was pushed to its limits and the Tai Yuan cultivators begged for mercy.

Without paying attention to the two immortal servants, Li Fan directly entered the core hub of the ancient immortal formation.

As expected, he saw the indeterminate circles and the shining Nine Stars Red Pearl at the center.

At the heart of the immortal formation, Li Fan truly felt the inexplicable pressure emanating from the Mountain and Infinite Sea above.

A strange look flashed in his eyes. His purpose here was not this pearl that recorded the information of all cultivators and beings in the Tai Yuan Realm.

But the complete immortal formation itself.

"Although I cannot directly access the Infinite Sea myself."

"I can indirectly steal the infinite immortal power from the Infinite Sea through this immortal formation."

"Just as I did through my clone before."

"Now that the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul is gone and the Myriad Forms Dao Net does not exist, I must first use this method to temporarily restore my True Immortal cultivation."

Chapter 1544: Capturing the Great Heavenly Venerate

Overjoyed, they trembled; excited, they quivered; in fear, they despaired.

Ultimately, they vanished above the mountains and seas, transforming into a bridge.

Creating a path for their people to enter the mountains from the sea.

...

Li Fan painstakingly re-read this passage from the allegory dozens of times, attempting to grasp the imagery it depicted. However, the allegory was vague about details, only mentioning the fate of this first being.

But it was understandable.

The ancient events of the mountains and seas recorded in this allegory were already secrets far beyond the mortal world. If it also involved things beyond the mountains and seas...

Then Li Fan would first doubt the authenticity of this allegory.

After all, the allegory recorded that the fate of the first being who looked beyond the mountains and seas was to perish and transform into a bridge, connecting the mountains and seas. Unless this deceased being was resurrected, and recorded what they saw, no one else in the world of mountains and seas could know what they had truly seen.

In fact, Li Fan was not particularly curious about things beyond the mountains and seas. Because they were too distant from his current self. Unfounded speculation was useless and would only increase his troubles.

What Li Fan cared more about was this passage in the allegory.

"Born from the sea, standing in the mountains. Therefore, their gaze could extend beyond the mountains and seas..."

"It seems to elucidate the way to transcend mountains and seas," Li Fan mused inwardly.

The first being's past events recorded in the allegory bore a resemblance to the deeds of the two Sage Monarchs, Lian Shan and Gui Hai, from the Immortal Realm.

If one looked at the deeds of connecting mountains and seas, it seemed they possessed the characteristics of both Sage Monarchs. But the two Sages were still within the mountains and seas, and did not perish to become a bridge as described in the allegory.

"If there was a true connection between them, perhaps it was precisely because of the existence of the [Bridge] transformed from this primordial first being, that the two Sage Monarchs, countless years later, achieved the Dao."

"It was also from this corpse named [Bridge] that the two Sage Monarchs glimpsed the past of the mountains and seas," Li Fan made a reasonable guess in his heart.

"Then the author of this allegory is worth pondering. They knew of the future apocalypse, understood the primordial past, and had a deep relationship with the two Sages..."

Invisible flames arose in his hand, completely burning the allegory.

This allegory was indeed not made of any special material, and in moments, it turned into nothingness.

Even though he had verified it once in his previous life, Li Fan still felt some disappointment in his heart.

"It seems there are no other hidden secrets."

Although the physical entity was gone, the words of the allegory were deeply imprinted in Li Fan's mind. Recalling it carefully, Li Fan attempted to deconstruct part of the allegory based on his own experiences.

"If being born from the sea and standing in the mountains already possessed the qualifications to transcend mountains and seas, then in reality, any [Immortal] created by the two Sage Monarchs after they established the Immortal Realm would have met this condition."

"Its essence is the merging of two Daos."

"However, most so-called True Immortals only achieved their Dao by borrowing the power of the two Sage Monarchs. They did not truly comprehend the Dao of Mountains and Seas."

"The extreme of the two Daos is transcendence of mountains and seas."

"In my previous experiences, the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, along with the Great Dao of Longevity and the Transformation of True and False, should have been of the same level. This implies that..."

"Cultivating either one to its extreme would grant the power to transcend mountains and seas. Then my previous act of merging three Daos..."

Li Fan shook his head slightly.

Judging from the content of the allegory, the mountains and seas themselves would undergo constant refinement during the fusion.

It was likely that even the Infinite Sea and the Upper Mountain could not withstand the consequences of three Daos merging in such a short period.

"This is also why Huan Zhen was so severely [injured] this time. I was indeed too reckless before. To have survived by chance after attempting it was truly thanks to Huan Zhen's protection."

"Ignorance is bliss."

Looking back at his past actions from his current perspective, Li Fan truly felt fortunate and fearful.

"What was Sun Piaomiao's purpose in leaving this allegory?"

"Normally speaking, the content involved in this allegory far exceeds the Profound Yellow Realm. Even a True Immortal might not recognize the true form of the mountains and seas. Most cultivators would simply treat this allegory as a mere story and not think too much of it."

"Except..."

Li Fan raised his eyebrows: "Except for me, there is also the person who will tear a few pages from this allegory in the future."

With a thought, an identical book appeared in Li Fan's hand.

He placed it back in its original position within the treasure vault.

Although Li Fan's actions had drastically altered the historical trajectory of the Profound Yellow Realm, he could not be certain whether the mysterious person who tore pages from the allegory would appear again.

However, it was necessary to leave a contingency.

Perhaps it would bring Li Fan unexpected surprises?

Having dealt with the matter of the mountain and sea allegory, Li Fan's next plan was to find the Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable.

Previously, in the Tai Yuan Realm, the immortal formation had captured a trace of her aura.

Even if she deliberately concealed her existence within the Profound Yellow Realm, she could not escape Li Fan's grasp.

Locking onto her location through the unseen threads, Li Fan smiled slightly and took a step.

In the next moment, he appeared out of thin air near her.

Without rushing to alert her, he first hid in the shadows and observed carefully.

This was a serene and ordinary mountain in the Profound Yellow Realm.

Due to its location in a slightly cold region, instead of tall trees, emerald green short grass grew abundantly, stretching endlessly to the horizon. It was like a grassland in the heavens, refreshing and uplifting, making one feel expansive.

The Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable sat quietly on the mountaintop.

Before her stood an easel.

The Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable was meticulously recording the beautiful scenery before her with brush and ink.

For the Grand Celestial Venerable, who could search and save all the scenes in the Profound Yellow Realm with a single thought, such an action seemed meaningless.

But Li Fan could see that this Grand Celestial Venerable seemed to be enjoying herself.

Every stroke was meticulous. Occasionally, if she was not satisfied, she would frown and repaint.

A gentle breeze blew on the mountain, and time slowly flowed by.

Just as the painting in the Grand Celestial Venerable's hand was nearing completion, and the look of pleasant satisfaction on her face was clearly visible.

In the painting, countless corpses inexplicably appeared amidst the vast expanse of grass.

A mountain of corpses and a sea of blood, with an overwhelming aura of malevolence.

Above, a blood moon also rose into the sky.

Completely destroying the fresh and beautiful artistic conception.

"Who's there!" The Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable, shocked and enraged, spun around suddenly, scanning her surroundings.

She happened to see Li Fan's half-smiling expression.

From a rational standpoint, approaching without her noticing and being able to intentionally alter her painting,

Li Fan's strength was definitely far superior to hers.

If Li Fan were her, he would never easily attack such a powerful being.

But the Grand Celestial Venerable before him, seemingly driven by rage due to her ruined painting, had somewhat lost her reason.

She still chose to attack Li Fan.

The smile at the corner of his lips gradually receded, and Li Fan uttered a single word lightly.

"Still!"

In her furious state, the Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable, who had launched a fierce attack, was instantly rendered immobile!

Only then did she slowly regain her senses.

The look of horror on her face was evident.

She was the Profound Yellow Celestial Venerable, and the power of the entire Profound Yellow Realm could be manipulated by her at will. But now...

Before this person.

Her connection with the world seemed to have been severed.

Or rather, even with the entire Profound Yellow Realm's power added, she was still being severely suppressed by this person.

The Grand Celestial Venerable was not dull. She instantly connected the prior inexplicable descent of the [Profound Yellow True Immortal].

Only an Immortal could possess such power.

Compared to a True Immortal, the Grand Celestial Venerable was clearly not on the same level.

Inheriting the Grand Celestial Venerable's responsibilities, she understood very well that the so-called Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable was merely an immortal servant acting under orders.

Therefore, she immediately put away her arrogance.

Even though this True Immortal's actual age should be far less than hers.

Li Fan had only frozen her movements, not her speech.

Upon realizing this, the Grand Celestial Venerable spoke, "Senior, why are you toying with me?"

As the voice drifted out, Li Fan already vaguely understood why Mr. Bai held such an unforgettable affection for a mortal.

Even after later discovering that he had been deceived, he still did not change his resolve.

It was just that such methods would not work before Li Fan.

"Profound Yellow soldiers are fighting to the death on the front lines. As the Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable, you are here indulging in poetry and painting..." Li Fan snorted coldly.

Using the Transformation of True and False to simulate the power approaching the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul, he poured it into the Grand Celestial Venerable's body.

The Grand Celestial Venerable's expression was initially quite calm, and she explained skillfully, "The duty of the Grand Celestial Venerable is only within the Profound Yellow Realm. The long-range attack on Tai Yuan is not my..."

She only spoke halfway before her voice involuntarily changed.

The power of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul could annihilate everything. The Grand Celestial Venerable's connection with the Profound Yellow Realm could not escape it either.

Even though her body and soul felt no pain, cold sweat streamed down her face.

Although in her heart she no longer wished to hold the position of Grand Celestial Venerable and had begun looking for a successor, the active loss was different from a passive deprivation.

For the first time in a long while, she felt an intense fear that almost overwhelmed her. However, she endured the fear in her heart and did not directly beg for mercy.

She only held on, explaining one by one the reasons why she had not gone to the Tai Yuan front line.

Objectively speaking, her reasons were indeed logical.

But Li Fan had only come to find fault with her, so these reasons were all useless.

The method of reduction continued unabated.

Seeing this, the Grand Celestial Venerable sighed softly, "Junior knows she has failed in her duties. Whatever punishment Senior wishes to inflict, I will accept it. However, I am worried that there is no successor yet for the next Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerable. If there is no Heavenly Venerable to manage the affairs of the Profound Yellow Realm, trouble might arise in this world."

"Of course, if Senior has the leisure and inclination to handle these trivial matters of billions of mortals and the Ten Immortal Dao Sects, then consider my words as having been unsaid."

It seemed she truly wished to accept punishment. Until the very last moment before her connection with the Profound Yellow world was completely severed, she did not show any hostility towards Li Fan.

She merely endured in silence.

This made Li Fan look at her with a renewed respect.

Leaving a final thread of connection, Li Fan finally stopped.

"How long have you served as the Grand Celestial Venerable?" he asked, gazing at her.

"Since King Xuan passed away, it has been sixteen thousand three hundred and forty-two years," the Grand Celestial Venerable replied swiftly.

"According to Immortal Realm regulations, each Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerable's term shall not exceed ten thousand years. In reality, I have already exceeded my term. However, with the Immortal Realm's destruction, the normal appointment and removal procedures have long been defunct."

"And I have been unable to find a suitable successor..."

The Grand Celestial Venerable spoke softly, her tone filled with helplessness.

"Senior, please see. During my tenure, I have always been diligent and conscientious. I have maintained the stability and prosperity of the Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth, fulfilling my duties responsibly. The Ten Immortal Dao Sects can all attest to this." Soon, she turned the conversation to her contributions.

"But I see you have the intention to leave," Li Fan glanced at her and said lightly.

This was the Grand Celestial Venerable's most confidential matter, yet Li Fan saw through it in an instant. The Grand Celestial Venerable was deeply shaken.

However, her reaction was swift, and she immediately admitted, "After ten thousand years of hard work, I have grown weary. My duty is fulfilled, and I wish to withdraw, which is only human nature."

"Even the first Grand Celestial Venerable did not serve from beginning to end. Although my actions are somewhat unfeeling, they are within the rules," she defended herself.

"The First Grand Celestial Venerable?"

Upon hearing this, Li Fan's mind immediately went to the You Clan people beneath the Profound Yellow Realm.

Because they possessed the bloodline of the first Grand Celestial Venerable, these You Clan people were transformed by King Xuan into neither human nor ghost and were doomed to accompany the Dark Sea eternally as punishment.

Li Fan inferred that King Xuan must have been deeply angered by the actions of the Grand Celestial Venerable, hence this decision.

But Li Fan did not know what the Primordial Grand Celestial Venerable had truly done, hence this question.

This woman softly explained, "The First Grand Celestial Venerable foresaw the tribulation of the Immortal Realm long ago and voluntarily transformed from immortal to mortal. Within the Profound Yellow Realm, she established an earthly immortal dynasty, calling herself Emperor, and caused chaos among mortals."

"Even though immortals have shed their mortal form, they are still not ordinary mortal cultivators who can resist. Therefore, they could only obediently follow her orders."

"Although the Primordial was no longer an immortal, she still viewed mortal cultivators as ants, ordering them around and treating them like slaves. At that time, although the major immortal cultivation sects had grievances, they were powerless to resist."

"Later, with the connection methods of the major sects reaching directly into the Immortal Realm, the matter was reported to the Immortal Realm. Only then did the Primordial restrain herself somewhat, but she voluntarily reduced the scope of the earthly immortal dynasty, her behavior remaining unchanged."

"Within the immortal dynasty, cultivators were treated like livestock, at her mercy."

"After transforming from immortal to mortal, the Primordial's temperament became even more tyrannical. She frequently vented her desires. Countless mortals, and even cultivators, could not escape her claws. However, she forbade herself from having any mortal bloodline descendants. If she found anyone pregnant, she would kill them on the spot. Only one branch, through a fortuitous encounter, escaped and remained hidden. Only after the Primordial departed did they reveal their identity."

"Relying on her immortal bloodline, she had the momentum to establish a second immortal dynasty. Fortunately, she was stopped in time by the other sects of the Profound Yellow Realm uniting against her."

...

The Grand Celestial Venerable softly narrated the Primordial's atrocities.

These were events not recorded in later history, and Li Fan listened with great interest.

Chapter 1545: The Past of the Great Heavenly Venerate

"Before the rise of King Xuan of the Mysterious Heavens, the families established by the primeval bloodline were among the most powerful on the Profound Yellow Continent."

"They were even comparable to some ancient sects. People speculated that, in addition to their True Immortal bloodline, they might have pilfered some Immortal treasures when they fled from the Primeval Era."

The voice of the Immortal Grand Celestial Venerable of the Profound Yellow was indeed "melodious."

It flowed like a clear mountain spring, a gentle breeze, subtly permeating and giving a sense of intimacy.

"From what you say, I fear the fate of the descendants of that Primeval Grand Celestial Venerable was not so good."

"Senior indeed has keen insight. When King Xuan returned from the Immortal Realm and swept across the Profound Yellow with his Twelve Dharma Kings, it was this primeval bloodline family that led the resistance, hoping to revive their ancestors' legacy as the alliance leader. Strictly speaking, they did possess some power to rally the masses. In the beginning, they truly caused King Xuan no small amount of trouble."

"However, this was also due to King Xuan's unnecessary compassion. Once he later made up his mind, there was nothing in the world that could stop him." The Grand Celestial Venerable seemed to have a unique affection for King Xuan; her tone showed a slight fluctuation when mentioning him.

Li Fan keenly discerned that this was not merely admiration, but also held a hint of resentment.

Yet, this Grand Celestial Venerable seemed unaware, continuing, "This primeval bloodline family, though not inheriting the True Immortal's strength, conducted themselves in a manner strikingly similar to their ancestors. When King Xuan's forces breached their territory, the wicked deeds occurring within were brought to light."

"To ensure the purity of the True Immortal bloodline, only incestuous relations were permitted within the family; innately gifted children were secretly rounded up and their talents usurped by secret arts; other cultivators were enslaved and controlled by restrictions to work for them; and even at regular intervals, vast numbers of living beings were sacrificed to maintain the stability of their bloodline... Their crimes were too numerous to count and absolutely atrocious."

"In a fit of rage, King Xuan transformed and suppressed all members of the primeval bloodline family..." The Grand Celestial Venerable spoke eloquently.

Unexpectedly, Li Fan suddenly waved his hand, interrupting her. "Don't stray. Let's talk about that Primeval Grand Celestial Venerable. If I'm not mistaken, her transformation into a mortal wasn't achieved by ordinary means. She preserved her immortal body, leaving herself a retreat. Is that correct? If the time was right, she could use this immortal body to reascend from mortal to immortal."

"Indeed, worthy of one entrusted with important tasks by the Immortal Realm, able to advance and retreat freely between immortal and mortal."

"And in your description, the sole purpose of portraying her as utterly worthless was to make me overlook her as much as possible, to conceal the existence of the Grand Celestial Venerable's immortal body..."

Li Fan's gaze gradually turned cold.

Though exposed, the female Grand Celestial Venerable before him showed no hint of panic. She merely looked at Li Fan with a calm expression, remaining silent.

Li Fan seemed unconcerned. "Actually, I can tell that you're saying all this to stall for time. A method that can escape my confinement..."

Li Fan's gaze drifted towards the distance.

The female Grand Celestial Venerable's expression changed slightly for the first time.

Li Fan continued, "And why would I be willing to listen to you for so long, if not to wait?"

The moment had arrived, and Li Fan no longer hesitated.

The suppressed power of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul instantly surged forth, engulfing the female Grand Celestial Venerable's body.

The astonished expression remained on her face, but in the next second, she became like a petrified statue.

Her vitality completely extinguished.

Li Fan did not kill her; he still preserved a trace of activity in her body and soul.

He merely adopted a Heavenly Pillar sealing method, temporarily freezing her.

"Asking questions one by one is far less convenient than observing myself," Li Fan shook his head slightly.

He would never readily believe a woman's words.

He took everything the Grand Celestial Venerable had just said as mere amusement.

The truth would require Li Fan's personal investigation.

The reason he hadn't made a move earlier was due to her position as the Grand Celestial Venerable of Profound Yellow.

The Grand Celestial Venerable of Profound Yellow was closely tied to the safety of the Profound Yellow Realm. Rashly inflicting heavy injuries or killing her might trigger unrest in the Profound Yellow Realm.

And chaos in the Profound Yellow Realm was not what Li Fan desired.

After all, all his anchor points in this spacetime were established here. How could he destroy his own foundation?

Thus, during the period when he severed her connection with the Profound Yellow Realm, he first utilized the power of a True Immortal to temporarily gain authority as the acting Celestial Venerable of Profound Yellow.

Ensuring that removing the female Grand Celestial Venerable would not cause any damage to the Profound Yellow Realm. Only then did he make his move.

Li Fan had not forgotten her antagonistic actions towards him, along with the Heavenly Dao of Profound Yellow, when he first arrived in this spacetime.

"Let me observe."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes. The female Grand Celestial Venerable was like a book, which he turned leaf by leaf, savoring every detail.

During Li Fan's scrutiny, the Heavenly Dao of Profound Yellow, regarding the female Grand Celestial Venerable's mysterious disappearance and Li Fan's sudden replacement, exhibited instinctive caution and curiosity.

And also confusion and interrogation.

Above the sky, dark clouds gathered.

A consciousness fluctuation, an absolute behemoth compared to ordinary cultivators, descended upon the mountain where Li Fan was located.

It was as if heaven and earth had instantly overturned, and the entire weight of the Profound Yellow Realm pressed down on his shoulders.

Li Fan merely snorted coldly, stamping his foot firmly.

In the next moment, the inverted heaven was immediately righted.

His divine sense soared skyward, instantly suppressing the Heavenly Dao of Profound Yellow, which had dared to manifest its consciousness fluctuation.

The current Heavenly Dao of Profound Yellow had not yet experienced the later great tribulation and the erosion of other immortal cultivation realms. Its temperament was not so strange.

Even the later twisted Heavenly Dao of Profound Yellow could be handled by Li Fan with ease. How much more so the present one?

The oppressive power of a True Immortal, the nourishing vitality of immortal spiritual energy, the manifested power of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul that devoured all...

Under a combination of coercion and enticement, the Heavenly Dao of Profound Yellow instantly retreated, no longer making any movement.

Li Fan then continued to examine the "book" before him.

The female Grand Celestial Venerable was sealed as a Heavenly Pillar, her past memories solidified page by page.

Though merely countless static images, this did not hinder Li Fan from delving into her past.

The female Grand Celestial Venerable was named Yi Yutong, originally an ordinary mortal in the Profound Yellow Realm.

Because her family was protected by the Sect of Mysterious Heavens, her household worshiped the faceless statue of the Mysterious Heaven God. Later, although the Sect of Mysterious Heavens issued an order to confiscate the statues and cease worship.

Out of the simple gratitude of mortals, Yi Yutong's parents secretly kept the statue. They worshiped it in secret, day and night.

Initially, everything was peaceful. Although the Sect of Mysterious Heavens had issued the order, they did not conduct a large-scale investigation. It seemed to be merely a formality.

However, one day, upon waking up, Yi Yutong was horrified to find that both her parents had suddenly died in their bed.

The cause of their death was that their faces, like the statue of the Mysterious Heaven God, had disappeared. Lacking facial features, they could not breathe and were suffocated to death.

Fortunately, all these bizarre changes occurred in their sleep. They experienced no pain and departed peacefully.

Under the rule of the Sect of Mysterious Heavens, a mortal's life was still a life.

A couple dying suddenly, and the involvement of the Mysterious Heaven God statue, caused an immediate sensation.

People discussed it widely, filled with confusion.

Why would worshiping the Great Compassionate, Suffering-Saving Mysterious Heaven God statue lead to disaster?

The Sect of Mysterious Heavens quickly sent people to calm the storm. They claimed that the family had violated the Mysterious Heaven's Edict, maliciously worshiping, and thus suffered backlash.

Yi Yutong was also brought before King Xuan of the Mysterious Heavens.

Yi Yutong still remembered the immense surprise on King Xuan's face when he first saw her.

He then took her in at the sect.

It was only later that Yi Yutong understood the reason for King Xuan's surprise.

It was because he had found a qualified successor.

In fact, the young Yi Yutong had daily followed her parents in worshiping the faceless Mysterious Heaven God statue. Yet, no changes had occurred to her.

According to King Xuan and Yi Yutong's own speculation, it was likely that she had been subtly influenced by the faceless statue while still in the womb.

Not only did she not die from it, but she was safely born. Thus, she developed a natural adaptability to the statue's power.

It was precisely this inherently unique constitution that allowed her to survive the subsequent calamity and then be noticed by King Xuan.

To be "noticed" did not mean she received much special care.

Or perhaps, to prevent others from noticing her unique qualities. In any case, Yi Yutong's early life was spent growing up alongside countless orphans adopted by the Sect of Mysterious Heavens.

Aside from King Xuan occasionally visiting in secret to impart cultivation techniques and check her physical condition, her treatment was no different from other orphans.

Thus, Yi Yutong slowly grew into an adult.

For some reason, her cultivation speed was far slower than her peers. Even though her talent was ten or a hundred times greater than others, it was as if an invisible hand constantly suppressed her from above.

This meant her progress could only proceed according to a predetermined schedule.

The ridicule of her peers and the pressure from the sect caused Yi Yutong to break down and cry countless times.

During her rare solitary moments with King Xuan, she couldn't help but question him.

King Xuan only said, "Slowly, therefore one lives, therefore one triumphs. Triumph bestows longevity." This was a truly difficult statement to comprehend.

Filled with grievances.

Fortunately, she persevered through it all.

In her twenty-ninth year, she finally achieved the Golden Core stage, officially stepping into the threshold of a cultivator.

Although it was slow, she could at least serve the sect in the future.

Only, later...

That day, the sect was suddenly thrown into chaos.

Countless terrifyingly powerful auras attacked.

And the Sect of Mysterious Heavens, usually heavily guarded, was unable to organize a decent counterattack for a time.

As a small Golden Core cultivator, she could only drift with the tide, fleeing in panic with the others.

In a trance, she seemed to hear King Xuan's voice.

But the situation was too chaotic then, and she wasn't sure if it was an illusion.

Outside the Sect of Mysterious Heavens, countless cultivators were besieging and slaughtering. These sects, who usually followed the Sect of Mysterious Heavens, seemingly loyal, were now mercilessly slaughtering the disciples of Mysterious Heavens.

Fortunately, Yi Yutong was only a Golden Core cultivator, not an important figure in the sect.

Gambling her severely injured life, she barely managed to escape.

Later, due to her severe injuries, she fainted directly.

During this time, she seemed to have a very long dream.

When she woke up...

She had inexplicably become the Grand Celestial Venerable of Profound Yellow.

Aside from the memories of past Venerables' records of the Profound Yellow Realm, there was also a message from King Xuan.

It roughly stated that this was a fallback plan left by King Xuan.

If he met with misfortune, then the means he had placed on Yi Yutong would activate.

She would automatically succeed to the position of Grand Celestial Venerable.

Succeeding the Grand Celestial Venerable, according to established practice, required passing specific trials. However, according to King Xuan, she had passed the Grand Celestial Venerable's trial and become a Venerable candidate when she was very young, upon first entering the sect.

Yi Yutong, however, had no memory of this at all.

Originally just a Golden Core cultivator, she woke up to inherit the power of the Grand Celestial Venerable.

The power to effortlessly suppress Harmonious Dao cultivators with a mere gesture made Yi Yutong tremble uncontrollably.

The first thing that came to her mind was to seek revenge on those treacherous and shameless individuals of the Ten Immortal Dao Sects.

But the inherent warnings of being the Grand Celestial Venerable immediately surfaced.

Now that she was the Grand Celestial Venerable, she could not, for personal grievances, wantonly kill innocents.

This meant that even though she possessed immense power, she couldn't even exact revenge.

And she couldn't even abandon this responsibility.

The tragic deaths of her companions, who grew up with her, at the hands of the Ten Sects were still vivid in her memory.

To ask her to forsake this hatred, and even to help and coordinate with the Ten Immortal Dao Sects, who had replaced the Sect of Mysterious Heavens, to protect the Profound Yellow Realm's safety.

How could she accept this?

She had tried to resist the restrictions of the Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable on her.

But before the heart-fire punishment that would instantly incinerate her if she disobeyed, Yi Yutong still flinched.

She couldn't abandon her own life for revenge.

This made her feel even more ashamed.

Every day as Grand Celestial Venerable was for Yi Yutong an ordeal comparable to purgatory.

Facing the eager requests for an audience from her hideous enemies, Yi Yutong could only refuse.

Out of sight, out of mind.

While managing the affairs that maintained the Profound Yellow Realm's safety, Yi Yutong secretly searched for news of King Xuan.

She truly wanted to return the position of Grand Celestial Venerable to him.

And then openly seek revenge on the Ten Sects.

But she traversed the entire Profound Yellow Realm and found no trace of Xuan Yuanhong.

It seemed he had fallen in that turmoil.

However, an intuition told her that King Xuan was still alive.

So, over the years, Yi Yutong had never given up hope of finding him.

Only...

She had originally thought she would forever remember her hatred for the Ten Sects.

But time, after all, possesses the power to heal all.

Fifty years, one hundred years.

Eight hundred years, three thousand years.

As long stretches of time passed, the figures of her former companions had already blurred.

And the culprits of that turmoil, she didn't even need to act.

Most had already died of old age.

Only then did Yi Yutong begin to understand what King Xuan had once said to her.

"Slowly, therefore one lives, therefore one triumphs. Triumph bestows longevity."

The thought of revenge slowly faded.

But the position of Grand Celestial Venerable of Profound Yellow was something Yi Yutong always wished to relinquish.

Chapter 1546: The First Generation Immortal Puppet

For ten thousand years serving as the Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerable, Yi Yutong, in theory, should have been able to end her mission.

However, finding a suitable successor proved to be no easy feat.

When the probability dwindles to a certain extent, it becomes indistinguishable from impossibility. Yi Yutong diligently searched for over six thousand more years, scouring nearly the entirety of the Profound Yellow Realm, yet she could never find anyone who met the requirements for succession.

Only then did Yi Yutong truly understand why the Profound Yellow King had been so surprised and lost his composure upon discovering her.

After a prolonged fruitless search, Yi Yutong gradually grew resigned. In her spare time, while handling Profound Yellow affairs, she found solace in the mountains and rivers, preparing herself to live and die alongside this world.

Until…

The war between the Profound Yellow and Tai Yuan realms erupted. A rift tore through the void, and the Profound Yellow True Immortal's breakthrough in the midst of battle, turning the tide, unfolded before the world.

As one of the individuals in the Profound Yellow Realm most knowledgeable about "immortals," the moment that figure displayed their power, she recognized the unique aura belonging to the True Immortal realm.

This sparked immense confusion within her.

The path to immortality had been severed, and even prodigies like the Profound Yellow King could only achieve the state of a Half-Immortal. How could a new True Immortal possibly exist in this world?

Later, when that True Immortal shone with unparalleled brilliance, only to vanish like a meteor moments later, she finally found some peace.

However, at the same time, an uncontrollable impulse surged within her.

"If I possessed the power of a True Immortal, perhaps I could disregard all these Great Heavenly Venerable constraints. After all, the Immortal Realm has long since been destroyed…"

Once the thought arose, it could no longer be suppressed.

Thus, risking great danger, she left the Profound Yellow Realm for the first time in her life and ventured to the Tai Yuan Realm.

It was essential to remember that the vast majority of her power stemmed from the augmentation of the Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerable. Outside the Profound Yellow Realm, she was no different from an ordinary Harmonious Dao cultivator. She was acutely aware of how many Harmonious Dao cultivators had perished in that land. Even though the war had now subsided, and the threat of Tai Yuan cultivators was gone, one could never be sure what dangers lay in foreign lands.

Yet Yi Yutong went.

She not only went to the location where the Profound Yellow True Immortal had fallen to pay her respects and worship, but she also gazed upon that world-shattering sword mark.

Upon her return, Yi Yutong indeed seemed to have gained subtle insights.

The residual aura of that Profound Yellow True Immortal evoked a sense of profound familiarity within her.

This familiarity originated from her interactions with the Profound Yellow King in the first half of her life, and also from the Faceless God effigy she had worshipped since childhood.

"So that's how it is. I was wrong."

"Since there are still immortals surviving in this world, it means the path to immortality has not been severed. The final destination, known as becoming an immortal, is still there. What was destroyed was merely the Immortal Realm. Only one path leading to that destination was destroyed…"

Drawing upon this feeling of familiarity, Yi Yutong seemed to be able to vaguely touch the boundary of immortality.

While painting, her thoughts, following the connection of familiarity in her heart, drifted beyond the Profound Yellow Realm.

In a trance, she witnessed a vast, continuous landscape of mountains and seas!

Li Fan slowly closed the book of Yi Yutong, a look of solemnity on his face.

To have glimpsed the scenes of the Infinite Sea and the Upper Mountain during her enlightenment was truly remarkable.

This was clearly beyond Yi Yutong's innate talent. The only plausible explanation was the influence of that so-called feeling of familiarity.

Just as Li Fan himself had occasionally seen a solitary silhouette standing on a mountain, gazing at the sea.

This vision was not something he had personally witnessed.

It was a transformation that occurred after he began practicing the Great Dao of Shou Qiu and entered the path of inheritance left by Duke Shou Qiu.

"So the source of Yi Yutong's enlightenment on mountains and seas is…"

Now that Yi Yutong had transformed into a Heavenly Pillar, existing like a crafted artifact,

Li Fan, using her as a medium, fully occupied her mind. He meticulously studied the origin of her feeling of familiarity.

"It's not the Profound Yellow King."

"It's the Faceless Immortal…"

After careful differentiation, Li Fan reached his conclusion.

After all, Li Fan had been deeply entangled with both these figures in his past cycles of reincarnation.

Especially the Faceless Immortal, with whom he had even fallen into their grasp at one point, losing his own visage along with Yi Yutong's tragically deceased parents.

But the current Li Fan was vastly different from his past self. He had already met powerful beings like Shou Qiu, Zi Yi, and Tai Tian Di, who could traverse the Eternal Void.

Why then should he fear this insignificant Faceless Immortal?

"Such a close connection indicates that they are still within the 'Primordial' possibility. They are not transcendents…"

Li Fan's eyes flickered as his thoughts churned.

But ultimately, he set aside these notions for the time being. He would deal with other matters in the Profound Yellow Realm first.

Upon reviewing Yi Yutong's memories, her account to Li Fan was indeed a mixture of truth and falsehood.

The first-generation Great Heavenly Venerable had indeed displayed tyrannical tendencies, but this was merely a residual effect of the Immortal-Mortal bifurcation. As the symptoms worsened, the first generation chose to isolate themselves, no longer meeting the world and beginning to search for a successor for the Heavenly Venerable position early on.

The reason the first generation's bloodline managed to escape was also a result of their intentional leniency.

It was precisely because of the first-generation Great Heavenly Venerable's past merits that, despite the heinous crimes of their descendants, the Profound Yellow King showed leniency during his cleanup, refraining from total annihilation.

"Knowing that ascension to immortality was hopeless, the first generation eventually abandoned any plans of returning to immortality."

"They decided to gift their immortal body to the successor Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerable as a trump card for critical moments."

"An immortal artifact, an immortal body, and the power of the Profound Yellow. These laid the foundation for the supreme status of the Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerable within the Profound Yellow Realm."

"The current location of the first-generation immortal body…"

Li Fan found the answer within Yi Yutong's memories. In the next moment, he instantly teleported to the corresponding location.

"So it's here."

In Li Fan's mind, time and space shifted, connecting this location with the scene ten thousand years later.

It was the Heavenly Spirit Prefecture within the Five Elements Great Cave Heaven, built by the First Origin Sect.

However, at this particular point in time, the space known as the "Root of Heaven and Earth" had not yet been occupied by the First Origin Sect.

And the first-generation immortal body lay quietly within.

Traces of immortal energy emanated from the immortal body, nourishing the Profound Yellow Realm.

With Yi Yutong's memories, Li Fan encountered no obstacles and successfully broke through the numerous restrictions.

He arrived before the first-generation immortal body.

"Not weak. No wonder they were entrusted with such important responsibilities by the Immortal Realm," Li Fan commented nonchalantly from a distance.

Judging by the aura emanating from this body, while it did not reach the level of the Nameless Realm, it was still stronger than the two immortals he encountered in the Pluto Star Sea previously.

"A True Immortal's husk, a body completely devoid of self-awareness. Truly the best material for refining puppets," Li Fan's heart stirred with temptation.

The first-generation immortal body had lain quietly in the Profound Yellow Realm for ten thousand years, undisturbed.

This was undoubtedly due to the efforts of successive Great Heavenly Venerables who, despite their inability to directly intervene, possessed the foresight to protect it.

Even without consciousness, the naturally emanating immortal spiritual energy provided a protective barrier that no one could breach.

But it could not stop Li Fan.

"Perhaps the Profound Yellow King could have achieved this as well, but given Xuan Yuanhong's character, he likely wouldn't have done so."

Li Fan, however, was unconcerned.

In his view, everything in the world could be utilized by him. And he would do so without any psychological burden.

This "world" referred not only to the Profound Yellow Realm.

But also to the entirety of the Mountains and Seas.

Although he intended to make full use of it, Li Fan did not let his guard down.

He thoroughly inspected the first-generation immortal body from all angles, then set up a formation on the spot. Ensuring that there would be no issues, he then began the refinement of the immortal puppet.

This time, Li Fan deeply absorbed the advanced experiences from his previous cycles of reincarnation in refining puppets and clones. He adopted a state between a clone and an independent puppet.

The immortal puppet would still possess its own independent consciousness, but Li Fan would also have complete control over it.

Even every thought born in his mind would be under his control. If necessary, Li Fan could temporarily freeze the puppet's consciousness and seize control of the body.

The ability to obliterate the puppet's consciousness with a single thought and create new intelligence, starting everything anew, was also within its functionalities.

This refinement of the immortal puppet was truly a culmination of Li Fan's abilities.

At his current Half-Immortal realm, refining it required considerable effort.

Fortunately, with the support of immortal energy from the Tai Yuan Realm's ancient defensive immortal formation, he finally completed the refinement of the first-generation immortal puppet.

As the puppet's consciousness slowly awakened, the natural nourishment of immortal energy it had been emitting towards the Profound Yellow Realm was retracted.

Almost instantaneously, the Profound Yellow world, which had been vibrant like a blooming flower, seemed to lose its color.

It became somewhat different.

If it had previously been in a state of flourishing prosperity, it now, without the sustenance of the first-generation immortal body, rapidly declined from its peak.

Although this change was still extremely subtle now, perceptible only to a few individuals in the entire world, it was anticipated that as time passed, this transformation would become increasingly evident, and its acceleration would increase.

"No wonder Su Bai didn't take the first-generation immortal body with him when he tried to escape the High Wall. Without the support of the immortal body, it's uncertain if the Profound Yellow Realm could survive for even ten thousand more years."

While Li Fan was contemplating, the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao's consciousness, having newly sensed the celestial anomaly, hurriedly descended.

A palpable sense of shock and fury could be felt.

But upon glimpsing Li Fan, it instantly froze. Subsequently, it shifted to resentment and a flattering demeanor.

"Very good. It seems you've learned quickly."

Li Fan nodded with satisfaction.

He then channeled a small portion of immortal energy, extracted from the Tai Yuan ancient immortal formation, and established an immortal formation here to supply the Profound Yellow Realm.

Since immortal energy was infinite, even by partitioning a portion, it had no substantial impact on Li Fan. Moreover, as his foundational anchor point in the River of Time, Li Fan would not stand idly by and watch the Profound Yellow Realm fall into turmoil.

The Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao, revitalized, instantly turned from sorrow to joy and happily departed.

Completely unaware of the terrifying implications of its lifeline being controlled by Li Fan.

Li Fan, however, paid little heed to the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao.

He was attempting to glean insights into the life of the first-generation Great Heavenly Venerable through the residual memories within the immortal puppet.

It had to be said that the first-generation Great Heavenly Venerable possessed considerable skill.

The method of Immortal-Mortal bifurcation was indeed quite thorough.

Even after Li Fan had completely purged the body, he only found a few deeply ingrained memory fragments.

These fragments occupied crucial portions of the first-generation Great Heavenly Venerable's life, deeply imprinted on his essence, and could not be erased even by the Immortal-Mortal bifurcation.

"Is this the Tribulation of the Dao's Demise…" The first generation watched as the Immortal Realm in the distance silently collapsed. Palatial heavenly structures, once brilliant, were instantly plunged into darkness and stillness.

And this stillness was rapidly spreading towards his location.

Innumerable immortals vanished in this terrifying calamity like ants, unable to even cry out for help or wail, disappearing completely.

Despair filled the first generation's heart. He didn't even have the urge to flee.

Because he knew there was nowhere to escape.

Just as he closed his eyes, awaiting death, a figure, appearing somewhat frail but in reality immensely majestic, suddenly appeared between heaven and earth.

All the immortals scrambled backward in panic.

Only he faced the encroaching tide of Dao's Demise head-on.

Alone, like a mountain. Like a dike.

He stood there, and the terrifying, all-consuming surging tide before him could not advance an inch!

A distinct dividing line bisected the field of vision.

Beyond the dividing line lay death and void.

While this side, where the first generation was located, represented life and light.

Like all the saved immortals, the first generation stared blankly at the standing silhouette ahead, unable to recover for a long time.

Only after a considerable time did the first generation learn the name of this peerless expert.

Shou Qiu Gong.

…

"Shou Qiu Gong couldn't accomplish it, yet Tian Luo Di can?"

The first generation seemed to be arguing with someone.

Even though the other party was making fervent appeals, the first generation's anger remained uncontrollable.

"No self-awareness! Yet he still leads a group of followers…"

"No wonder even Shou Qiu Gong had to leave."

"The Immortal Realm is beyond saving."

Once this thought arose, it reverberated in the first generation's heart like thunder, never to be silenced.

"I heard Tian Luo Di is rigorously investigating activities against the Immortal Administration, especially regarding True Immortals who escaped from the lower realms…"

The voice of a friend reached the first generation’s ear at this moment.

…

"This is the Broken-Chess Dao Field."

"Since you have come seeking refuge, choose any immortal cultivation world at your leisure."

The first generation's divine sense swept through countless segmented block spaces. Suddenly, upon seeing one realm, he froze.

"If I'm not mistaken, that figure seems to be…" The first generation discovered an extremely familiar individual in this world.

He had vaguely seen them standing beside an Immortal Emperor when he followed in Shou Qiu Gong's footsteps.

"Shh…" A knowing, unspoken chuckle came from the person beside him.

The first generation could only stop speaking.

"Indeed, my choice was correct."

"Then I shall choose this place. Being in the vicinity of such great figures, it can't be wrong."

…

"He is dead."

"Such a powerful being, yet he also dies."

"And he died in the mortal realm."

The first generation looked at the slowly forming, illusory Profound Yellow Realm, his heart filled with shock and confusion.

The other party's demise was indeed unexpected.

But the birth of this illusory world astonished him even more.

"Though illusory, it is substantial."

"It does not require a foundation in reality."

"Even if the Tribulation of Dao's Demise arrives, it can float upon it like a wooden boat!"

Chapter 1547: The Long River is Forever Lost

With a single thought, another Profound Yellow Realm, like a mirror, was reflected.

Even the first generation could see his own shadow within it.

Although that shadow lacked the true essence of an immortal, it was still undeniably real, a reflection of his mortal self.

Such power, even for the first generation, a True Immortal, was deeply shocking.

...

The last scene from the residual memories of the first generation's immortal body was his final moment of using the Immortal-Mortal Bifurcation technique.

He looked at his reflection ahead, his heart filled with mixed emotions.

Ultimately, all dissolved into a sense of relief.

“There’s a reason all my immortal friends fled. The Heavenly Emperor’s plan has reached its most frantic stage. I can feel that the day the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation erupts on a large scale may be drawing nearer. If my immortal body still existed, even if I were in the lower realm, it would likely attract Dao Annihilation. Only by shedding my immortal body can there be a glimmer of hope…”

The first generation pondered silently. After bidding farewell to his past self, he plunged into the mortal body.

“I truly hope that one day, I can return.”

This was the first generation’s last thought after transforming from immortal to mortal.

...

Li Fan emerged from the first generation’s memories.

It was clear that the first generation had not achieved his wish.

Once the sky collapses, how easy would it be to salvage it?

“The most crucial point is the abandonment by the Three Sages.”

“Because it concerns neither the final outcome, the Three Sages, even if they possessed the ability to save, would not ‘waste’ their power on such trivial matters. Are there no powerful beings who can break beyond the primordial possibility, who can only choose to save themselves? Or perhaps they simply left directly.”

Li Fan shook his head slightly: “Speaking of which, I still don’t know what the Heavenly Emperor’s plan actually is. To completely resolve the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, and for the entire Immortal Realm to transcend…”

Before, Li Fan couldn’t even conceive of a possible method, let alone think about it.

However, after reading the complete allegory of mountains and seas, Li Fan found a possibility.

Born from the sea, standing in the mountains. Then, one’s gaze can extend beyond the mountains and seas.

If this theory is correct, then as long as one finds a “Great Dao of Mountains and Seas” like Longevity or True Transformation, and merges it with the Immortal Realm.

Then it is possible for the entire realm to transcend beyond the mountains and seas.

Naturally, there would be no need to suffer the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

But this was only a theory.

Beyond the mountains and seas, there seemed to be another great terror. The fate of the first being in the allegory who looked beyond the mountains and seas proved that there was immense danger involved.

“Even if it can be achieved, the outcome is likely no better than being swallowed by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.”

Li Fan was still somewhat curious about the ultimate fate of the Heavenly Emperor and the Immortal Realm. It was a pity that at this temporal node, everything was already destined and could no longer be investigated.

“Perhaps by following the River of Time upstream, more clues could be found. But it would be meaningless.”

Li Fan reined in his thoughts, gazing intently at the first generation’s immortal body before him, stimulating its sentience.

The first generation opened his eyes, and after a moment of confusion, he quickly understood his current situation. He bowed towards Li Fan.

And Li Fan, using the first generation’s body, observed the state of the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation outside the Profound Yellow Realm.

“Hmm, it’s much more stable than ten thousand years later.”

“The situation of the ‘tower collapsing’ that the first generation worried about before becoming mortal did not occur. It should be due to the bones of the previous starved immortal buried beneath the Immortal Ruins silently supporting it.”

After observing for a while, Li Fan withdrew his gaze.

He had no intention of provoking the starved immortal for the time being.

In the past, he acted with impunity, destroying worlds with a raise of his hand if he disagreed. After all, he had True Transformation to back him up. But not now.

With this immortal body, coupled with the immortal array, capturing the starved immortal should not be a problem.

But Li Fan could not guarantee that he could safely protect the Profound Yellow Realm while both sides were fighting.

If the Profound Yellow was harmed, all his hard-earned anchor points in this spacetime would be destroyed. At that point, forget capturing the starved immortal, he might not even be able to protect himself.

“Staying at the edge of the Immortal Ruins is still a bit too dangerous.”

“Next, I need to find a way to safely transfer the Profound Yellow Realm first.”

Li Fan had prior experience in this regard. After a moment of thought, a plan formed in his mind.

“In this era, the Ten Sects still hold a certain degree of ruling power. Some trivial matters can be handed over to them.”

“However, before that…”

Li Fan’s mind stirred, and he instantly gained control of the first generation’s immortal body.

His figure flickered, leaving the space of the Root of Heaven and Earth. He arrived next to the mountain where the fishing pond was located.

Standing in the air, he gazed down at the underground.

“Still maintained by the life force of Ruomu?”

“Does this mean there is still a Tai Tian Di present here?”

Li Fan’s eyes narrowed, taking full precautions, and he slowly walked into the underground village.

It was almost identical to what he had seen ten thousand years later.

It seemed time had frozen in this small village.

However, when Li Fan, following his memories, arrived before the painting where Tai Tian Di hid, his steps abruptly halted.

The painting was still the same painting.

The young Profound Yellow King, his childhood sweethearts, and the many children from the mountain village were all in the painting.

But an old man lying down to rest was missing!

“Vanished.” In an instant, Li Fan felt a sense of loss.

And a trace of relief mixed in.

The place where Tai Tian Di had been lying was empty.

Even the Reverse Flow Boat had disappeared.

But the life force absorbed by the Profound Yellow King’s secret technique was still tirelessly nourishing this scroll.

Without Tai Tian Di, all the life force was absorbed by it alone.

Therefore, this painting had undergone rather miraculous changes. In Li Fan's ears, he seemed to hear the sounds of Xuanyuanhong and his childhood sweethearts playing.

Even the two young children in the painting seemed to notice Li Fan’s approach from outside the painting.

They slowly turned their gazes towards Li Fan.

Seeing such a bizarre scene, Li Fan couldn't help but think of the fate of Xuanyuanhong's descendants.

After a moment of contemplation, Li Fan temporarily put away the painting.

After isolating himself from the prying eyes of the figures within the painting, he first pondered Tai Tian Di’s disappearance.

“It seems that after mastering the Way of Reverse Flow, and traveling upstream against the River of Time, falling anywhere in the river leads to the simultaneous disappearance of existences at other temporal nodes.”

It seemed difficult to understand.

But Li Fan recalled his own experiences when traversing the River of Time, and slowly began to understand.

“Originally, I was merely a drop of water in the River of Time, able to go with the flow.”

“But when I gained the ability to travel against the flow, and went upstream along the River of Time, a line was formed in the River of Time.”

“This line is my complete self now. In a sense, I have now become a life form similar to the River of Time.”

“However, my main consciousness is currently trapped in this segment of the River of Time, unable to perceive the fate of other parts of my body. It is like my five senses are sealed.”

“This is also because my Way of Reverse Flow has only just begun. If this Way were to reach its peak, I would be able to leap above the river, and all my experiences within the River of Time would be fully understood…”

As Li Fan stood in the place where Tai Tian Di had disappeared, numerous realizations surfaced in his mind.

The Reverse Flow Boat within his body, which had been shattered, began to slowly repair itself.

Even though the repair speed was very slow, it was already a qualitative change compared to the previous state of complete self-repair.

“Generally speaking, once the Way of Reverse Flow is mastered, ordinary methods cannot kill it.”

“Only a drop of water in the River of Time dies. As long as the River exists, and the drop forms a line, it is immortal.”

“Unless the scouring of the River of Time itself assimilates self-consciousness. Or the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation engulfs the entire spacetime. Or, like Tai Tian Di, actively giving up one’s own life.”

Only now did Li Fan understand what sacrifice Tai Tian Di had made to help him comprehend the Dao.

Indeed, due to excessive reverse flow, Tai Tian Di’s body and soul had decayed, leaving only a remnant phantom barely surviving.

But this did not mean he had no chance of complete recovery.

He didn't even need the intervention of Gong Shou Qiu’s Great Dao of Mountains and Seas to be saved. All he needed was for the River of Time, blocked by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, to flow smoothly again.

The “water flow” from upstream would then irrigate downwards, and Tai Tian Di could immediately recover to his peak state in the previous temporal period.

Although this seemed more difficult to achieve than Gong Shou Qiu’s intervention, it was not.

Because it was not the entire River of Time that needed to be connected, but only the connection with the previous temporal period.

Since Gong Shou Qiu could traverse the Eternal Void, taking Tai Tian Di’s remnant and bringing him to a previous temporal period could easily save him.

After all, the plan of passing down the torch of hope to the past had been ongoing. It was merely a matter of convenience.

Even if no one was willing to help with this, Tai Tian Di himself didn't need to do anything. He just needed to patiently survive and wait.

Until the day the River of Time reconnected.

If one were to take a longer view, the ultimate fate of the entire world of mountains and seas was nothing more than two possibilities.

Either it would be completely merged into the mountains and seas, and swallowed by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

Or, the sparks of life within the mountains and seas would succeed in saving themselves.

If it was the former, then all beings would share the same fate. Death was death. If it was the latter, Tai Tian Di would naturally be resurrected.

“Tai Tian Di must have understood this principle. Yet, he insisted on giving up this opportunity.”

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, recalling Tai Tian Di’s epiphany before his disappearance.

“Lingering here is meaningless. So today, I will impart what I have comprehended, the Way of Reverse Flow, to you!”

“If, one day, you can go to the Eternal Void in my stead and offer assistance, then my sacrifice today will not be in vain!”

Tai Tian Di’s resolute expression seemed to reappear before Li Fan’s eyes.

Li Fan repeatedly shook his head: “Although he saved my life, I still cannot understand.”

“Giving up the only, yet very stable, chance of survival…”

“Perhaps in the future, when the River of Time reopens, new Tai Tian Dis may appear in other temporal nodes. But the one who experienced repeated rescues in this spacetime, destined to save the world, will never return.”

“This one has the grace of teaching me and saving my life. As for others, that Tai Tian Di, is not this Tai Tian Di.”

“Perhaps, the only way to restore him in the entire Mountains and Seas is through True Transformation.” Li Fan’s heart suddenly stirred.

However, his comprehension of True Transformation and Falsehood was currently insufficient, even to fully restore his own peak cultivation.

Let alone creating an Immortal Emperor from nothingness who had completely vanished.

Li Fan helplessly abandoned this thought for the time being.

Solemnly sealing the underground village here with an immortal formation, Li Fan left the underground. Instinctively, he glanced towards the nearby fishing pond.

At this temporal node, a Daoist temple had not yet been built outside the fishing pond.

It was just a solitary pond lying in the mountains. Perhaps no one would have imagined that such an ordinary pond would involve an existence beyond the Nameless Realm.

“It even surpasses the Nameless Realm.”

“After all, Tai Tian Di referred to it as the [Mountain Sea Fishing Ground].”

Even though he was currently controlling an immortal body, Li Fan did not approach. He only observed from afar.

“Since there is a Mountain Sea Fishing Ground, the fishing pond is not connected to a single possibility. Instead, it has opened up the entire Upper Mountain…”

“What a grand undertaking. The Fishing Immortal behind it must at least be a transcendent being. I wonder if they can traverse the Eternal Void like Gong Shou Qiu.”

However, Li Fan suddenly remembered that besides the stone tablet attempting to comprehend the Way of Fishing and then being suddenly sucked away, Xuan Tian Wang had also disappeared into this fishing pond.

“The one who can fish with such ‘leisurely elegance’ should still be within this spacetime. Not yet reaching the level of traversing the Eternal Void. However, even so, it is not someone I can provoke at present.”

A hint of dread flashed in Li Fan’s eyes.

Even with the protection of True Transformation, Li Fan was still wary of the fishing pond and the being behind it. Not to mention that he now only had a piece of Reverse Flow wood board for defense.

“No rush. Sooner or later, I will have to face this [Fishing Immortal].”

Li Fan suppressed his emotions and returned to the space of the Root of Heaven and Earth.

He handed the painting over to his main body.

The main body slowly unrolled the painting, and almost instantly, he met the gaze of the young Xuan Tian Wang in the painting.

It seemed the other party had anticipated someone outside the painting.

Li Fan was not surprised. Without Tai Tian Di inside, he wouldn't be intimidated by a mere painting.

Ignoring the probing gaze of young Xuanyuanhong, Li Fan listened carefully to the rustling sounds that reached his ears.

“Indeed, it is exactly the same as the demonic sound, like a curse, from the Xuanyuan clan’s bloodline that I heard before, only clearer.”

“Is Xuan Tian Wang trying to convey something through this method?”

If True Immortal inscription was to engrave the Dao with characters.

Then this demonic sound was to depict the Dao with melody.

In the primordial possibility, Li Fan had only encountered this art of drawing the Dao with sound in the Great Magician.

Most True Immortals followed the path of inscribed Dao Immortal Arts.

“It seems that perhaps this Way of Profound Sound does not originate from the primordial, but from the place where Xuan Tian Wang disappeared to in another possibility.”

“The Great Magician learned from the Three Sages. The Three Sages already existed in myriad possibilities, so it is understandable.”

Li Fan attempted to decipher the melody transmitted by Xuan Tian Wang.

When the three Daos merged, he had united with the mountains and seas.

Now, comprehending the Great Dao within the mountains and seas was much easier than before.

Moreover, his comprehension was not weak in the past.

However, after a short period, a general result was achieved.

Chapter 1548: Gaze of Mountains and Seas

"...Empty words, life and life. Intent, spirit, body, soul, born from chaos, return to chaos."

"One exists eternally. Both lost and existing."

"Without front or back, without ancient or modern. Ordinary yet extraordinary, a sage yet not born..."

...

Through the painting before him, Li Fan heard the profound sounds of the Great Dao, even more detailed and clear than what he had obtained from the memories of the Heavenly Physician and the Law-Transmitter.

The profound sounds of the Great Dao transmitted by King Xuan held infinite mysteries. They could influence the past from the present, and alter reality through illusion. In the past, although Li Fan had learned this profound sound divine ability, he could never understand how it achieved its effects.

It wasn't until Li Fan used the Reverse Flow Boat, traversing the River of Time, that he began to understand.

"This profound sound actually merges with a bit of the Way of Reverse Flow. However, it's not the main body traversing the river, but the sound itself. It's like a cry from downstream echoing upstream."

"Speaking of which, King Xuan once piloted the Reverse Flow Boat. Having this method is not surprising. If I wanted to..." Li Fan narrowed his eyes.

His thoughts instantly returned to the moment he had first fallen into this period of time.

Because he came from the future, his upper limit in this time and space was precisely this moment.

"You brat, you're finally awake."

"Quick, tell us what happened to the Medicine King Sect. Confess honestly, and we can spare your life. Otherwise..."

"Stop wasting time with him, just search his soul!"

This was precisely when the disciples of Evergreen Valley had surrounded Li Fan.

The current Li Fan, silently chanting the profound sound divine ability.

This faint, profound sound that penetrated the heavens, passed through the waves of the vast River of Time, and traveled upstream for a short distance, reaching the ears of these Evergreen Valley disciples.

Their expressions immediately became somewhat dazed. After carefully observing Li Fan for a moment, they suddenly realized: "So it's you, kid. Why did you come here alone?"

It was Li Fan, using the profound sound to distort and rewrite their perceptions.

Thus, this calamity, which would have required Li Fan to use his Illusionary True power to resolve, was invisibly averted.

The "past" Li Fan, looking at the inexplicable changes in the people before him, seemed to realize something. His gaze crossed the River of Time, meeting the eyes of the "future" or "present" Li Fan.

Buzz buzz buzz...

To the current Li Fan's ears, faint immense roaring sounds could be heard. Like surging rivers, like rolling thunder. It did not originate from the Profound Yellow Realm, but from this very segment of spacetime itself.

Without the slap that struck Li Fan's head, these Evergreen disciples would not have died.

Although it was the lives of a few insignificant Foundation Establishment cultivators, it would not cause a major deviation in the River of Time. However, it still created some ripples.

Of course, with Li Fan's current level of deep-rooted anchor points, this slight tremor could no longer affect him. No matter how the river roared, he remained unmoved.

After completing this profound sound divine ability that traversed time, Li Fan was filled with pleasant surprise and lingered in his thoughts for a long time.

In the past, he had also used the profound sound divine ability to successfully influence and alter the minds of He Zhenghao and others. But at that time, he had only grasped the divine ability itself, and had no idea about the principles behind its success.

Now, Li Fan, as if witnessing it firsthand, saw the entire process of the profound sound flowing in reverse and traversing time.

He had even achieved a momentary connection with his past self.

Although this connection only lasted for a brief moment before being obscured by the River of Time again.

But Li Fan still felt something different about himself.

Looking out at the River of Time, his vision seemed to extend slightly further.

Not just the past.

But also the future.

For a predetermined past, the future is actually in constant change, with innumerable possibilities. What Li Fan saw was not a single future.

But a collection of countless possibilities.

After just a few more glances, he felt a bit dizzy and had to withdraw from this wondrous state.

However, it did not dampen his inner joy.

"It seems that those who grasp the Way of Reverse Flow can, while having the ability to manipulate any time they are in, also need to face the backlash of the river. As the saying goes, to kill one's enemy by a thousand cuts, one also injures oneself by eight hundred. Of course, if one is extremely stable within the river, one can ignore this tremor and backlash."

"As for why I didn't suffer any backlash when I used the profound sound divine ability before. Firstly, I was still under the protection of Illusionary True at that time. Naturally, I could ignore such disturbances. Secondly..."

"At that time, I had not yet jumped out of the river. I was still considered a part of the river. Even if the river changed course, the impact on myself was not significant."

"But once I jump out of the river, the meaning immediately changes. No longer belonging to the river, I must face the storms alone." Li Fan recalled the situation at that time, with a sense of realization.

"If before, I was merely a drop of water outside the river, then now, I can barely be considered to have transformed from a water droplet into a segment of the river." Li Fan felt a sense of pride.

"It's just that it's still too short."

"However, as I follow the River of Time, flowing downstream, it will naturally become longer and longer. But, correspondingly, the self-control required will become increasingly strict..."

Li Fan sensed that as time passed, the imprint he left in the river was slowly growing.

"As long as I occasionally use this profound sound divine ability to exercise my ability to connect the head and tail, I can maintain this current state."

"The longer I live, the stronger I become."

"A thousand years, ten thousand years, a hundred thousand years."

If the Great Dao of Longevity from Shou Qiu was about becoming strong through longevity, then this Way of Reverse Flow was somewhat about becoming strong through longevity.

"Ordinary longevity would certainly not achieve such a state of becoming stronger the longer one lives. But refining the body into a single line, swimming in the River of Time, is entirely different."

Li Fan looked towards the heavens, as if glimpsing the River of Time he was in. All comprehension surged into his heart like waves.

His aura fluctuated unstably.

When Li Fan's consciousness cleared, he felt that his adaptability to the river had further improved.

This time, it was not through external means like spacetime anchors.

But Li Fan himself had become more accustomed to surviving in the River of Time.
