Just like a fish in water, a bird in the sky.

Having stepped into a forbidden zone that was previously unreachable, he had advanced further, merging himself into it.

"Now, even if all anchors are lost and the Reverse Flow Boat is destroyed, I can still struggle alone in the river for a while, and not be instantly destroyed by the river's turbulence."

This was undoubtedly a great reassurance for Li Fan.

The current Li Fan had very low trust in all "external things." He couldn't be blamed for being so suspicious.

After all, even "Illusionary True" could fail, so what could be guaranteed to be useful forever?

Only rely on oneself.

Pure self.

Li Fan's thoughts returned to this profound sound divine ability.

"The profound sound is deeply hidden within the Xuanyuan clan's bloodline, it should be King Xuan's message conveyed through the bloodline connection between himself and his descendants."

"It can not only traverse possibilities but also pass through ten thousand years of time."

"But, where did the source of this profound sound originate, and when?"

Li Fan tilted his ear again.

Like a sound from beyond the heavens, it became clearer and clearer.

Li Fan felt as if his body was soaring, following the sound, drifting out of the Profound Yellow Realm.

Leaving the Darkest Sea, crossing the High Wall, and jumping out of the Primordial Possibility.

Arriving beyond the mortal world, facing the mountains and seas directly.

The vast River of Time that could be observed in the mortal world instantly became empty. It disappeared.

From this perspective, the mountains and seas seemed to possess the attribute of frozen time.

Whether it was ten thousand years ago, or a hundred million years later.

Everything was within the mountains and seas.

This was an indescribable and wondrous experience. Although somewhat unbelievable, even defying common sense, Li Fan knew that everything he knew, had experienced, and had heard, past, present, and future,

was all frozen within the mountains and seas.

"The Tribulation of Dao Annihilation affects all time periods."

"All beings at all time nodes are destined to escape the catastrophe. So that's how it is."

As if in a state of absolute rationality, Li Fan thought calmly, even forgetting the reason why he had come here.

After his doubts were resolved, another question naturally arose.

"Then, what does the 'outside of the mountains and seas' truly represent?"

"What is the 'star' recorded in that allegory that suddenly appeared at the end of the time of the mountains and seas?"

As if sensing something involved in Li Fan's thoughts.

The originally calm and frozen mountains and seas suddenly came alive.

Li Fan could even clearly sense, emanating from all around him, inescapable, spine-chilling gazes.

Shocked in his heart, he decisively stopped his actions, which were drifting towards a certain place in the mountains and seas following the sound.

In an instant, he returned to reality.

Li Fan looked up at the sky, observing with a lingering sense of fear for a long time.

It took a full half of a day before the intense sense of crisis slowly subsided.

"Fortunately, I am accustomed to using Illusionary True to enhance myself. Even if it's a simplified version now, it still saved my life." Knowing that Illusionary True was currently in a state of slumber and ineffectiveness.

Li Fan had undoubtedly narrowly escaped death this time.

Even after experiencing the crisis of three Daos merging, he had not expected the "senses" of the mountains and seas to be so keen.

"It shouldn't be like this?"

Li Fan's brows furrowed.

This was not the first time he had faced the mountains and seas.

But Li Fan could be almost certain that before, for a being like him, who couldn't even be called an ant compared to the mountains and seas, the mountains and seas had definitely not been so sensitive.

"It seems my previous premonition was correct."

"After the merging of three Daos, even though it was distorted by Illusionary True, I became different from ordinary existences in the mountains and seas."

"Hiding in the mortal world was fine. But if I rashly left the mountains and seas, I would probably face the scrutiny of the mountains and seas at any time. Just like what I just experienced." Li Fan's heart grew heavy at this thought.

But he could not think of any good way to deal with the might of the mountains and seas at the moment.

"Fortunately, I didn't rashly ascend to the Immortal Realm, but used an Immortal Puppet and Immortal Formation instead. Otherwise, I would truly be in mortal danger." Li Fan's expression was somber.

Since recovering his memories, he had been treading on thin ice.

Not only did he have to constantly worry about the backlash of the River of Time, but he also had to guard against the scrutiny of the mountains and seas.

This made Li Fan, who had become accustomed to acting recklessly with Illusionary True in hand, feel greatly restricted.

However, the situation was stronger than the individual.

Whether it was the River of Time or the mountains and seas, they were not forces that he could contend against at the moment.

He could only temporarily lower his head and behave like a commoner.

"Let's take it slow," Li Fan sighed. "First, I need to reach a point where I can be completely stable in the River of Time."

His thoughts refocused on the profound sound.

Li Fan recalled what he had seen in the mountains and seas just now.

"The source of the sound seems to be from a more distant past?"

"But it should still be within this spacetime of ours. Not beyond the Eternal Void."

"Could it be that King Xuan is also trying to traverse the void and go to the past to save the world? Does he already have such strength?"

"Also, rather than saying this profound sound is some message King Xuan wants to convey, it's more like a marker, guiding those who come later. Could it be..."

A thought flashed through Li Fan's mind in an instant: "Has he already perished? Otherwise, under normal circumstances, he wouldn't be so persistent and stable in traversing the River of Time to send profound sounds and establish connections."

Li Fan pondered for a long time, and finally shook his head slightly, choosing to block the profound sound.

Even if this speculation were true, he would never go to investigate out of curiosity. King Xuan's strength perished there, so it was likely that Li Fan would not fare any better.

Especially now, without the protection of Illusionary True, he would not take such risks.

"Perhaps in the future, when my strength is sufficient, and I can roam freely between the mountains and seas, I will go and find out." Li Fan thought to himself.

Slowly putting away the painting, Li Fan did not casually store it away.

Instead, he suppressed it in the space of the Root of Heaven and Earth.

"The second matter is also concluded."

"Next..."

"Black Sky Physician, Evil Su Bai."

When the beings to be faced changed from colossal entities like the mountains and seas to such transcendent experts, everything seemed much easier.

At the very least, the mountains and seas made the current Li Fan unable to resist, or even maneuver.

He could only flee in a hurry.

But Black Sky Physician and Evil Su Bai were at least beings for whom countermeasures could be considered.

These two transcendent experts were like time bombs for the entire Darkest Sea. As soon as Su Bai and the Heavenly Physician took a step beyond the High Wall, the bombs would be instantly detonated.

Li Fan, who regarded the Profound Yellow Realm as his foundational anchor, naturally had to eliminate this risk completely and early on.

Through the previous search of the Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerable's memories, Li Fan had roughly pinpointed the current temporal node.

The Heavenly Law Realm had not yet been completely destroyed and was in a period of recuperation after a great war.

"I don't know if the Heavenly Physician has already activated the Heavenly Soul Rebirth technique. As for Su Bai, he has not yet been born."

"But it's all happening soon."

Li Fan pondered for a long time, and decided to first meet the Law-Transmitter of the current temporal node.

King Xuan's descendant, Xuanyuan Tuo.

The Myriad Immortal Alliance, as a fresh force, had participated in the Great Tai Yuan Realm War. The relationship between the New Law Cultivators and the Ten Immortal Dao Sects had eased considerably compared to the original timeline.

Especially the powerful combat strength displayed by the New Law Cultivators in the deathmatch had directly attracted many Ancient Law Cultivators to switch their cultivation paths.

And the Ten Sects, at this moment, were also focused on exploring the Tai Yuan Realm and the surrounding starry sky.

They had no time to pay attention to the Myriad Immortal Alliance.

Therefore, the Myriad Immortal Alliance grew more and more wild and unrestrained.

Chapter 1549: Benevolent Palm Heavenly Doctor

Although the Myriad Immortal Alliance's influence grew stronger, with the momentum to rival the Ten Immortal Dao Sects, their leader, Chuán Fǎ, became increasingly cautious.

He rarely appeared in public. The official explanation was that Chuán Fǎ, having witnessed the ascension of a True Immortal, experienced a profound realization and entered secluded meditation. However, Li Fan knew that while this might be partially true, it was more likely that Chuán Fǎ was trying to guard against the schemes of the Ten Sects. After all, their modus operandi had become widely known throughout the Profound Yellow Realm after the Tai Yuan conflict.

Despite Chuán Fǎ's seclusion, finding him was a simple matter for Li Fan. He didn't even need to use his divine sense for a search. With Li Fan now in control of the Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerable's authority, he could pinpoint Chuán Fǎ's location in an instant by leveraging the fundamental laws of heaven and earth that Chuán Fǎ had absorbed and refined.

"Chuán Fǎ built his Dao foundation with the [Profound Heaven Ten Thousand Spirits], achieved Golden Core with the [Heavenly Evolution Method], ascended to Nascent Soul in the [Primordial Celestial Dwelling], entered the God Transformation stage with the changes of [Myriad Forms Return to One], and finally reached Harmonious Dao with the essence of heaven and earth, [Jin Zhí]..."

"His foundation is not much inferior to my own accumulated experience from countless reincarnations. Truly a prodigy of the era, destined to dominate the Profound Yellow Realm for the next ten thousand years."

Jin Zhí was one of the foundational Dao principles used to control the Profound Yellow Realm when it was first created. Even though it had been absorbed and refined by Chuán Fǎ, it still maintained a subtle connection with the Profound Yellow Realm. This connection allowed Chuán Fǎ to partially control the heavens and earth. It was precisely this connection that had ironically become Chuán Fǎ's self-imposed prison.

"Found you."

Li Fan flickered, traversing thousands of mountains and rivers in an instant. He appeared beside Chuán Fǎ like a phantom. Xuanyuan Tuo, now in the guise of an old cowherd, was leisurely driving his cattle through the fields, propped on a green ox, holding a whip. Upon seeing Li Fan's sudden appearance, his expression turned grave.

"Xuanyuan Tuo..." Li Fan sized him up with a half-smile.

But before he could finish speaking, Xuanyuan Tuo suddenly attacked, taking the initiative. Thousands of golden chains materialized in the space between heaven and earth, stretching out from all directions and precisely locking onto Li Fan. In Xuanyuan Tuo's hand, he held aloft an ancient bronze mirror. The mirror was ancient and profound, its blurred surface seeming to reflect the Nine Heavens, Ten Earths, and the Profound Yellow World!

The golden chains were naturally Jin Zhí, the essence of heaven and earth. And the mirror in Chuán Fǎ's hand was the Heavenly Profound Mirror!

"Hmm?" Li Fan appeared somewhat surprised. According to the memories he had accessed from the Heavenly Profound Mirror in the past, it had been subdued by Chuán Fǎ and the Heavenly Physician after Chuán Fǎ had achieved True Immortality. Yet now, Chuán Fǎ had not yet attained longevity, and the Heavenly Physician should not have fully awakened.

"It seems my actions have caused a deviation. But it matters not. It is irrelevant to the final outcome." Li Fan remained composed. The golden chains, capable of capturing and restraining all living beings within the Profound Yellow Realm, were aimed at Li Fan with perfect precision. However, Li Fan seemed to be merely a phantom, and the countless golden chains passed through him, missing their target. The Heavenly Profound Mirror, which could reflect all profound secrets of the mortal world, also failed to reveal Li Fan's form. In fact, upon sensing something was wrong, the mirror suddenly emitted a green light, attempting to break free from Chuán Fǎ's control and escape.

Seeing both his ultimate moves fail, Chuán Fǎ's face was filled with bewilderment. After only a moment, he understood the realm and strength of the person before him. A True Immortal! Before he could resist further, Li Fan flipped his hand, suppressing both man and mirror. He then began to examine them closely.

Although Chuán Fǎ was his target this time, Li Fan first turned his attention to the Heavenly Profound Mirror. This was because the Heavenly Profound Mirror at this time was vastly different from the one Li Fan had seen tens of thousands of years later. It had not yet completely completed its mortal shedding process as an immortal artifact, and wisps of immortal essence still emanated from it.

"You have strayed from the path! The more ferocious the great tribulation, the more one must face it head-on. Only then will there be a sliver of hope for survival. You can escape for a moment, but can you escape a lifetime?" Li Fan shook his head and sighed. With a wave of his hand, he helped the Heavenly Profound Mirror complete its repair. As it reconnected with the Upper Mountain and Infinite Sea, the Heavenly Profound Mirror's efforts over the past nearly ten thousand years were all in vain. The ancient luster faded, replaced by the unique lustrous glow of an immortal artifact, as if imbued with the ultimate essence of heaven and earth, appearing mystical at first glance. Although it had become stronger, the Heavenly Profound Mirror felt indescribably depressed. If it weren't for being subdued by Li Fan at this moment and being unable to resist, it would have likely wished to pulverize him into ashes.

The shedding of an immortal artifact was a hundred times more arduous than a True Immortal's mortal ascension. After all, immortal artifacts were creations of True Immortals, forged to serve the immortals. They could not easily lose control. Only the Heavenly Profound Mirror knew the immense price it had paid to reach this stage, measuring the heavens and earth in the Profound Yellow Realm while slowly severing its own shackles. It never expected its efforts over the years to be erased by an immortal in a single day! The mirror body trembled with rage, but the immense force emanating from its surroundings, capable of shattering the Heavenly Profound Mirror, instantly sobered it. "My apologies, esteemed immortal," it said helplessly.

In the blink of an eye, Li Fan's divine sense had invaded the core of the Heavenly Profound Mirror, dispelling the restrictions Chuán Fǎ had placed upon it. "It seems the Heavenly Profound Mirror was not completely subdued by Chuán Fǎ, but rather, they reached some form of cooperation," Li Fan saw at a glance that the restrictions within the mirror were not enough to fully constrain it. "Awaken properly. Do not let down Xuanyuan Huang's expectations." Li Fan said, then suppressed and stored the Heavenly Profound Mirror, which was trembling and lost in thought once more. Only then did he turn his attention to Xuanyuan Tuo.

Despite being captured, Xuanyuan Tuo showed no fear. As Li Fan examined him, Xuanyuan Tuo was also silently observing Li Fan. Their gazes met. Xuanyuan Tuo appeared somewhat confused and puzzled. Li Fan's gaze, however, pierced directly through the surface of Xuanyuan Tuo's soul, reaching the depths within. Indeed, he discovered a faint, almost invisible transparent figure.

"Heavenly Physician..." Li Fan's lips curved into a sly smile. Golden light flashed in his hand, and a row of golden needles appeared out of thin air. Under Xuanyuan Tuo's horrified gaze, nine hundred and ninety-nine golden needles were precisely inserted into his body. Although pricked all over with golden needles, Xuanyuan Tuo felt no pain. Instead, his heart grew calmer, and his mind became clearer. With the help of the golden needles, he seemed to understand himself better and discovered the foreign presence within him!

"What is this?!" Xuanyuan Tuo was utterly astonished, never having known about such a foreign entity within him. As he watched, this seemingly dormant figure was gradually enveloped by golden light and pulled out. Aside from a slight discomfort in his soul, Xuanyuan Tuo felt no other discomfort. Instead, as this foreign object was expelled, he felt his soul and body become more harmonious and natural. The moments of contemplation and enlightenment that had always been abruptly halted at crucial junctures now seemed to erupt all at once. More importantly... the inexplicable murmuring voice that had only appeared during moments of severe injury and crisis now became clearer. Under the influence of this murmuring voice, Xuanyuan Tuo felt the invisible shackles on him begin to loosen!

Xuanyuan Tuo rejoiced inwardly but kept his composure, pretending to still be shocked by the expulsion of the foreign object. However, Li Fan's next words mercilessly shattered his illusions. "With your current cultivation, listening to this Profound Sound too much is detrimental. I will temporarily seal it for you." Before his voice even fell, the murmuring sound that had been lingering in Xuanyuan Tuo's ears completely vanished for no reason. The hope of escape that had just arisen was instantly dashed, leaving Xuanyuan Tuo momentarily stunned.

"The Profound Sound originating from the bloodline is even clearer and more direct than the one from that painting. Its directionality is stronger." Xuanyuan Tuo did not know that it wasn't that the Profound Sound had disappeared, but rather that Li Fan had intercepted all of it. Li Fan's thoughts did not follow the Profound Sound into the mortal world beyond. He merely observed from a distance. "Approximately fifteen thousand more years into the past. This seems to be... the period when King Xuan created the Profound Heaven Sect after escaping from the Immortal Realm. But the target is not the 'Primordial,' perhaps another similar possibility?" The guidance of the Profound Sound from his direct bloodline was too clear. Li Fan could vaguely glimpse the general direction of its destination. However, Li Fan had no intention of investigating it now. After observing for a while, he withdrew his gaze. Ignoring the extremely frustrated Xuanyuan Tuo, he first examined the transparent shadow in his hand. It resembled a thin film, its features difficult to discern. It was impossible to imagine that this was the Heavenly Physician who had once caused Li Fan immense psychological distress.

"Little friend, what are you expecting?" The scene from back then seemed to linger in his mind. However, recalling it now, it felt like a distant memory, as if a lifetime had passed. This sense of detachment made Li Fan quite emotional. In the past, he had desperately desired to reverse the situation with the Heavenly Physician, even intending to play pranks and startle him. But now that he had the strength to do so, he felt a sense of apathy. "After all, I have experienced too many frights on my path to longevity. The Heavenly Physician is nothing compared to them." Although he had mentally let go, Li Fan had no intention of releasing the Heavenly Physician.

"Heavenly Soul Rebirth." Li Fan was more interested in the unique creation known as the [Heavenly Soul] than the Heavenly Physician himself. "Heavenly Demon essence, even in the Immortal Realm, was a rare commodity. The Heavenly Physician could easily deceive the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao, and even suppress Xuanyuan Tuo's consciousness to gain control of his body. The Heavenly Demon played an indispensable role." Li Fan gently stroked the transparent tissue before him. His divine sense, like a blade or needle, slowly dissected it. Even with his current abilities, he proceeded with extreme caution. Under the Great Heavenly Soul Rebirth technique, the Heavenly Physician's soul remnant was almost completely fused with the Heavenly Demon, making it nearly impossible to separate without True Immortal means. "The Heavenly Demon, the ultimate heart demon. The myriad thoughts of the human heart, all resonate with the Great Dao of heaven and earth. And the demon of heaven is the heart demon born from the operation of the Great Dao of heaven and earth..." Under Li Fan's suppression, the Heavenly Physician remained dormant. However, the Heavenly Demon seemed to sense the external danger, and the transparent tissue, like boiling water, began to tremble violently. To avoid damaging the integrity of the Heavenly Demon, Li Fan did not resort to brute force. He only used immortal spiritual energy to gently suppress it. After considerable effort, he finally separated it from the Heavenly Demon. Without the Heavenly Demon's protection, the Heavenly Physician's soul finally revealed its original appearance. Although he was still white-haired and compassionate like in later generations, he perceptibly appeared much younger. "Perhaps it's because he hasn't experienced the tragedy of the Heavenly Law Realm yet," Li Fan mused. "In the Profound Yellow Realm I now control, the crisis of the Heavenly Law Realm's destruction is averted. This is a great blessing for both the Heavenly Physician and the Heavenly Law Realm." Recalling the sights he had witnessed in the Cloud Water Heavenly Palace, Li Fan nodded slightly. After suppressing the dormant Heavenly Physician, Li Fan's divine sense invaded the separated Heavenly Demon tissue, attempting to analyze its mysteries. Sensing the invasion of foreign matter, even though it seemed devoid of its own will and was in a state of suppression and封禁, the Heavenly Demon still managed to muster a resistance. Li Fan felt as if he had returned to the River of Time, his consciousness stirred by immense waves. The world spun, engulfed in chaos. All his past memories surged forth like snowflakes.

Sometimes, reflecting on the past and examining oneself can be beneficial. However, getting lost in reminiscing can lead to losing oneself. Li Fan clearly recognized the danger. His consciousness took form, and countless hands emerged from his surroundings, meticulously organizing the stirred memories, piece by piece. In fleeting images, Li Fan saw himself diligently and ardundantly exploring the small world of Great Xuan before he awakened his True Transformation ability. He saw himself leveraging his foresight from rebirth to become the Grand Tutor of Great Xuan and manipulate the court. He saw himself meeting Kou Hong and Dao Xuan Zi, realizing the existence of immortality, and after enduring countless hardships across multiple lifetimes, finally breaking through the grand formation and entering Profound Yellow. He saw himself establishing an incredibly solid foundation through a hundred lifetimes of Foundation Establishment. He saw himself navigating and exploring the treacherous Profound Yellow Realm step by step, from Foundation Establishment to Golden Core, and finally achieving the Half-Immortal realm by promoting the Profound Yellow Realm's ascension. Then, breaking through the barrier and crossing the High Wall. He encountered the transformation of three Daos, and had to start all over again. Assisted by Tai Tian Di, he traveled upstream against the River of Time, reaching the present day.

As Li Fan slowly gathered and integrated these fragmented memories of his past self, and examined his own past as a pure observer, he discovered some events that he had previously considered "natural" but now seemed extremely peculiar. Li Fan had always been confident in his spiritual intuition. In his past reincarnations, countless times, his intuition had warned him of danger at critical moments, saving his life. It could be said that Li Fan's trust in his intuition surpassed even his trust in [True Transformation]. If he had only relied on True Transformation and lacked such an incredibly keen and inexplicable intuition, Li Fan might have been captured several times before he could even activate True Transformation. In the past, Li Fan believed his intuition was innate, a natural occurrence. But was that truly the case?

Chapter 1550: Inheriting the Law of Ancestor

"Avoiding ill fortune and turning disaster into fortune."

"If it were only within a certain range, perhaps it could be explained as innate talent. But those risks that even True Transformation failed to detect, I often sensed and was warned of them beforehand…" Li Fan's expression was solemn, and he couldn't help but feel suspicious.

"Could it be that this spiritual intuition is somehow related to my infinite spiritual essence? What kind of innate talent is this? Is it related to my identity as a 'transmigrator'?"

Inevitably, a series of questions arose in Li Fan's mind.

The first stage of the New Law was called [Foundation Establishment with Myself]. Logically speaking, as Li Fan's cultivation and knowledge grew, he should be getting closer to achieving this goal.

But as more mysteries surrounding him were uncovered, Li Fan realized he seemed to be drifting further away from [Foundation Establishment with Myself], even disregarding the factor of [True Transformation].

Almost lost in this storm of self-doubt, until a familiar fluctuation emanated from the depths of his divine soul. Like sweet rain after a long drought, it instantly helped Li Fan regain clarity.

It was True Transformation, severely injured and dormant for a long time!

Although this fluctuation was fleeting and extremely weak, it was like a thunderclap on flat ground, shattering Li Fan's confusion instantly.

"I was being too attached."

"Whether it's talent or a cheat, as long as it can be used by me, that's enough. I am still struggling to survive in the River of Time, so why bother delving into its essence? It only adds to my troubles."

"Perhaps there will come a day when I can truly understand the deepest mysteries. But by then, I should be able to fully comprehend and achieve pure selfhood."

The emergence of True Transformation was like a stabilizing force.

Li Fan's self-reflection, triggered by the Celestial Demon, finally subsided completely.

It should be noted that Li Fan, having gone through numerous reincarnations and experienced immense changes in mountains and seas, possessed an exceptionally firm will. Yet, he was still affected by the Celestial Demon.

"This is the Way of the Celestial Demon."

"As long as one has not transcended the Great Dao of the mortal world, one will inevitably be plagued by inner demons. The strength of the inner demons even relates to oneself. The more secrets one harbors, the stronger the inner demons can become…"

The Celestial Demon truly lived up to its reputation as a unique creation, entirely different from the beings Li Fan had encountered before.

The Nameless, the Transcended beings, were powerful, but in Li Fan's view, they were merely strong in terms of numbers.

But the Celestial Demon belonged to the category of 'mechanics.'

It could be considered strong, or weak.

As long as one's heart was pure and sincere, even a Foundation Establishment cultivator would not be troubled by it. But if there were flaws in one's state of mind, even Nameless realm beings could not escape its influence.

"Moreover, the Celestial Demon in this state is…"

It seemed that as long as one could escape the inner demon, one could be free from its influence for a considerable period. Li Fan once again studied the transparent tissue extracted from Xuan Yuan Tuo.

It was like the amniotic fluid surrounding a baby in the womb, providing protection and nourishment.

It protected the Heavenly Physician, who was still in a deep sleep.

It was precisely because Li Fan separated it from the Heavenly Physician that he was attacked by the Celestial Demon's instinct.

"The Celestial Demon should also be one of the Venerables of the Heavenly Law Realm."

"However, this mass of transparent tissue does not contain its consciousness."

"Furthermore, if my memory serves me correctly, the real Celestial Demon should currently be sealed and stored within the Profound Immortal Boat."

The Transformation of True and False simulated the Heavenly Physician's life aura, and then slowly approached.

The transparent tissue quickly re-enveloped the 'Heavenly Physician.'

"Interesting."

"It seems the Heavenly Physician's successful Heavenly Soul Rebirth owes much to the Celestial Demon's assistance."

"This nurturing ground…"

Li Fan shifted his perspective, assuming the identity of the Profound Yellow Grand Celestial Venerable to examine it.

The protective shell formed by the transparent tissue was like a mirror. When viewed from the Profound Yellow Realm, it reflected only the scenes of the Profound Yellow Realm.

Suddenly remembering something, Li Fan checked the slumbering Heavenly Physician again.

As he had predicted.

"It's incomplete."

"Or rather, it's only a part of the Heavenly Physician."

"The Heavenly Soul Rebirth projected consciousness. However, the Heavenly Physician's original physical body is still hidden somewhere."

"It should be so. Although the Heavenly Physician possessed Xuan Yuan Tuo's body, he later still had his own physical body. This is also why for a long time, I was puzzled by the relationship between these two individuals. They appeared as one person, yet also like a main body and an avatar, full of contradictions."

"Such a complex experience; how could it be clarified without personally observing it through his memories?" Li Fan shook his head slightly.

"In the original historical trajectory, the Heavenly Physician sensed the crisis of the Heavenly Law Realm and forcefully seized control of the body. Upon returning, he witnessed the scene of the Heavenly Law Realm being completely slaughtered."

"Although the Heavenly Soul Rebirth plan was only half successful, his hometown was already destroyed first. The Heavenly Physician was greatly disheartened."

"However, even so, he did not give up and conceived the plan of 'borrowing a corpse to return the soul.' However, the difficulty of this plan was even greater than Heavenly Soul Rebirth. He could not have accomplished it alone, let alone with the unstable existence of Xuan Yuan Tuo's self-will."

"Therefore, the Heavenly Physician needed help."

"The Celestial Demon, having left the Heavenly Law Realm years ago, became his only helper."

"Fortunately, with the nurturing ground left by the Celestial Demon back then, relying on the faint connection with its main body, the Heavenly Physician was able to precisely lock onto its location in the vast starry sky, finding the elusive and deeply hidden Profound Immortal Boat."

"It took considerable effort to rescue the Celestial Demon. Then, the Celestial Demon and the Heavenly Physician joined forces to completely suppress Xuan Yuan Tuo's consciousness, with the Celestial Demon acting as the Law Transmitter and the Heavenly Physician returning to his original body."

"Together, they intended to save the Heavenly Law Realm from destruction."

"It can be said that for the next ten thousand years of the Profound Yellow Realm, this was their solo performance. The Ten Immortal Dao Sects, the Three Celestial Venerables of Unity, Truth, and Carefree, were merely supporting actors in this grand play."

"Unfortunately, with me present now, this grand play is destined not to be staged."

Li Fan looked at the Celestial Demon's nurturing ground and the slumbering Heavenly Physician, his gaze seeming to penetrate ten thousand years of time, catching a glimpse of their predestined future.

The feeling of being caught in a storm of self-reflection triggered by the Celestial Demon earlier bore a strange resemblance to falling into the turbulent currents of the River of Time.

Li Fan had a premonition that mastering the Way of the Celestial Demon might increase his safety during reverse-time travel.

Although he didn't know why the [Celestial Demon] had an inexplicable connection with the Way of Counter-Flow, it didn't prevent Li Fan from absorbing and refining it for his own use.

The refinement process was not complicated.

In fact, it was quite simple. Li Fan merely used a bit of his True-Illusion power, disguised himself as the Heavenly Physician,

And successfully assimilated the Celestial Demon's nurturing ground.

He encountered no resistance at all.

"This Celestial Demon is quite interesting. Although seemingly ruthless and distant, it left behind a portion of its power to help the Heavenly Law Realm overcome difficulties when necessary."

"Furthermore, it was willing to sacrifice itself to protect others…"

"A prime example of being cold on the outside but warm on the inside."

As Li Fan slowly absorbed the transparent Celestial Demon nurturing ground, the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao began to seem more "lively and dynamic" in his eyes.

If in the past, Li Fan saw the world as merely the Great Dao of heaven and earth, then now, he could faintly see the heavens and earth as if they had come alive, expressing their own emotions.

And this was not limited to the Profound Yellow Great Dao.

Li Fan's gaze leaped beyond Profound Yellow, looking towards the starry sea, the High Wall, and even the entire Primordial Possibility.

It was the same everywhere. This was not to say that the Celestial Demon's abilities could rival transcended beings. Rather, it was like a key, opening a door for Li Fan.

The reason he could see such magnificent and vivid phenomena was still because Li Fan was powerful enough.

After all, Li Fan had truly stepped out of the Primordial Possibility and faced the mountains and seas before.

"By mastering the Way of the Celestial Demon, it's like gaining an extremely perceptive heart, allowing one to perceive the emotional changes of the cold Heavenly Dao."

"This is highly beneficial for any cultivation path."

"However…"

Within the mortal world, the emotions of the Great Dao were all revealed. What about beyond the mortal world…

Once one reached the realm of mountains and seas, the Celestial Demon's seemingly heaven-defying ability instantly failed.

The Infinite Sea, the Mountain Above.

These two endlessly vast behemoths exuded an icy, life-repelling aura. Even with the Celestial Demon's full power, it could only glimpse the mountains and seas themselves.

Furthermore, Li Fan sensed.

Even when merely observing the mountains and seas from the mortal world, the Celestial Demon's Dao was still being counterattacked by the profoundly cold aura of the mountains and seas.

The previously warm Celestial Demon nurturing ground, which emanated life-giving energy, gradually cooled down.

It became equally icy.

In an instant, Li Fan felt as if his soul were about to freeze.

Fortunately, he had anticipated this and immediately withdrew his distant observation.

It took a considerable amount of time for the Celestial Demon nurturing ground to gradually recover from its rigidity.

Li Fan's brow furrowed. He once again recalled the content of the prophecy left by Sun Piaomiao.

The prophecy recorded that during the interaction between mountains and seas, there were emotions similar to those of humans.

Joy, anger, sorrow, fear, all were present.

"Prophecies are ultimately just prophecies."

"What the observers see may not represent the true mountains and seas."

Li Fan cautioned himself internally.

After spending half a day completely absorbing the Celestial Demon nurturing ground and transforming it into his own power.

Li Fan reaffirmed his judgment.

As a newly born "linear entity" in the River of Time, his adaptability seemed to have strengthened by nearly double, even without adding any new anchors.

If before it was a struggle, then now he could at least slowly pace himself.

He couldn't Fathom the principle behind this for the time being.

If he wanted further clarification, he would likely need to visit the Profound Immortal Boat.

But there was no rush.

The historical trajectory of the Profound Immortal Boat for the next ten thousand years was all within Li Fan's mind. The drastic changes in the Profound Yellow Realm would not affect them.

After finishing these trivial matters, Li Fan finally turned his attention to Xuan Yuan Tuo, who had been waiting obediently.

After personally witnessing the foreign object being extracted from his soul, Xuan Yuan Tuo was completely convinced. Knowing that he was absolutely no match for this mysterious True Immortal, he made no further futile resistance.

After all, judging by the opponent's actions, he didn't seem to harbor any malice. Xuan Yuan Tuo mused silently.

Therefore, while Li Fan was caught in the Celestial Demon storm and experiencing inner turmoil, Xuan Yuan Tuo remained silently by his side, making no attempt to escape.

"Do you know who your ancestor, the Xuan Yuan clan, is?" Li Fan asked.

Xuan Yuan Tuo hesitated for a moment, then slowly replied, "King Xuan Tian."

This was something he did not know originally.

It was only later, by chance, that he encountered the Heavenly Profound Mirror and learned about the Xuan Yuan clan's lineage.

Li Fan nodded. "In the past, I was close friends with Xuan Yuan Hong. Otherwise, I wouldn't have intervened to save you."

Hearing Li Fan's faint words, Xuan Yuan Tuo's heart trembled.

King Xuan Tian was his ancestor from many generations past. And the person before him was a close friend of King Xuan Tian. Then what was his辈分 (generation/seniority)...

Xuan Yuan Tuo felt somewhat constrained. "Then, may I ask what I should call you?"

"Just call me Grand Ancestor." Li Fan smiled.

"Grand… Ancestor…" Xuan Yuan Tuo hesitated, wanting to speak but stopping himself.

However, seeing Li Fan's expression, he hesitated for a moment before finally obediently uttering the words.

"Xuan Yuan Hong left in haste, and there were many matters he did not have time to explain. The original destiny became a calamity for your Xuan Yuan clan," Li Fan sighed and shook his head.

Xuan Yuan Tuo's heart was profoundly shaken.

He almost instantly thought of the eccentric uncle in his childhood village, Xuan Yuan Sheng.

Xuan Yuan Tuo's expression became solemn. "I implore Grand Ancestor to enlighten me."

Judging solely by his appearance, Li Fan looked much younger than Xuan Yuan Tuo.

Yet, Xuan Yuan Tuo addressed him as an ancestor, which felt quite peculiar.

However, Xuan Yuan Tuo did not mind, addressing him naturally, as if he had quickly accepted his identity as a junior.

And subsequently, the murmuring sounds Li Fan recited further convinced him of his choice.

Because these ethereal and profound sounds were exactly the same as those he had occasionally heard in his past!

"Kid, do you know what this Profound Sound is?"

Li Fan only recited a segment before stopping to inquire.

Xuan Yuan Tuo was naturally ignorant.

"This is your Profound Yuan ancestor sending you a message, guiding you where to go!" Li Fan gestured towards the heavens.

Xuan Yuan Tuo looked in the direction Li Fan pointed, momentarily bewildered.

Just a mere message? It almost led to the extermination of the Xuan Yuan clan. Xuan Yuan Tuo found it difficult to accept.

Since their Profound Yuan ancestor was still alive, why would such a simple message be so complicated?

Xuan Yuan Tuo looked at Li Fan.

Li Fan, after a period of silence, slowly explained the concepts of the Eternal Void, the River of Time, and the legend of sparks of life saving the world.

To prove that his words were not false, Li Fan even brought Xuan Yuan Tuo along for a brief "visit" to the River of Time.

However, Xuan Yuan Tuo, with his Harmonious Dao cultivation, had never witnessed such bizarre scenes, even in his dreams.

Even the small droplets splashing around him felt like a Maelstrom of destruction.

The intermittent waves threatened to engulf him at any moment.

Upon returning to reality from the River of Time, Xuan Yuan Tuo's face had turned extremely pale.

"Grand Ancestor, you…"

He understood now that the person before him was by no means merely a True Immortal!

Chapter 1551: Folding Paper Divides Immortals

The reason Xuanyuan Tuo initially believed the other party to be a True Immortal of this age was because, in his worldview, the strongest beings were called "True Immortals." However, Li Fan unfolded before him an even grander and more magnificent world.

True Immortals were truly like ants. There were those who transcended, those who flowed against the current, and even those who could contend with mountains and seas.

This left Xuanyuan Tuo's mind reeling and his spirit swaying.

It was fortunate that Xuanyuan Tuo was no ordinary person. Otherwise, such a blunt injection of knowledge, revealing the immense disparity between his understanding and reality, might have left him utterly despondent.

He barely managed to compose himself and detach from the massive influx of information. Xuanyuan Tuo asked somewhat cautiously, "May I ask what purpose the Old Ancestor Xuanyuan had in sending the Profound Sound message? For the Old Ancestor to undertake such a journey across mountains and seas to convey something to us descendants, it must be of paramount importance..."

Just a short while ago, Xuanyuan Tuo was carefully pondering how to capitalize on the neglect of the Ten Immortal Dao Sects of the Profound Yellow Realm to expand the Myriad Immortal Alliance's influence. But now, after witnessing the true nature of this world,

Xuanyuan Tuo felt that everything in the Profound Yellow Realm had become utterly meaningless.

As the saying goes, "If the skin is gone, where will the hair attach?" If the entire mortal world were annihilated, then all his actions in the Profound Yellow Realm would be rendered meaningless.

Xuanyuan Tuo suddenly understood why the Old Ancestor had disappeared so abruptly and never returned.

Li Fan observed the changes in Xuanyuan Tuo's expression and nodded secretly. "You are correct. Xuanyuan Hong's sole concern is the continued existence of all beings in the mountains and seas. The reason he sent this message to summon you is likely deeply connected to this matter. He probably never imagined that so many changes would occur in the Profound Yellow Realm after his departure. Even for his own descendants, comprehending his message has become an impossible dream."

Li Fan's words made Xuanyuan Tuo feel somewhat ashamed. Then he couldn't help but say, "Even with Senior's guidance, I've only just realized the truth. However, my strength is too meager. Even if I ardently wish to follow the Ancestor's footsteps, I fear my heart is willing but my power is insufficient."

Li Fan waved his hand, interrupting Xuanyuan Tuo with an air of arrogance. "With this old man present, why need you worry?"

Xuanyuan Tuo was naturally delighted to hear this. However, Li Fan's next words made his heart sink.

"But you are indeed too weak now. Not only in your realm, but also in your temperament. You need to undergo thorough tempering. Otherwise, even if you can flow against the current and traverse it, you will struggle to shoulder the great responsibility and assist Xuanyuan Hong."

"Grand Ancestor's admonition is apt," Xuanyuan Tuo's expression flickered slightly, wanting to speak but holding back. In the end, he merely uttered this single sentence.

Li Fan continued, "The Ten Sects of the Profound Yellow Realm are the dominion that Xuanyuan Hong seized. Now, you shall emulate Xuanyuan's past actions and sweep them away. If you cannot even pass this test, any grand aspirations will only lead to futile self-destruction."

Xuanyuan Tuo's expression became solemn. "I shall not fail Grand Ancestor's command."

Li Fan, however, said, "You must understand one thing. This is something you must do yourself; it has nothing to do with me. Of course, you can prove yourself through other means. I will not force you. The ultimate goal is to forge a path of a strong individual, just like Xuanyuan of old. You are currently but a Harmonious Dao cultivator, but where the crux lies depends entirely on how you walk this path."

Xuanyuan Tuo seemed to understand something.

Recalling the various deeds of Xuanyuan Hong he had heard about, a renewed zeal for the cause of the Profound Yellow Realm surged within him.

"The Ten Immortal Dao Sects..." A cold glint flashed in his eyes.

"Xuanyuan Hong's Profound Sound is not merely a simple message. It also has the effect of interfering with the future from the past, and changing reality through illusion. You observe carefully!"

Along with Li Fan's words, Xuanyuan Tuo felt a slight dizziness.

A moment later, he was horrified to discover that his memories had undergone subtle changes.

That very conversation had been uttered by Li Fan the moment he first appeared before him.

He naturally felt somewhat bewildered.

It was only now, as time flowed normally and the loop closed, that Xuanyuan Tuo suddenly woke up with a shock.

"Is this the Ancestor's divine ability?"

Xuanyuan Tuo's mind reeled. Compared to this profound sound that could reverse time and space, all the so-called new methods he had created were almost like child's play.

"The Great Dao lies in refinement, not in multitude. If you can master the profound mysteries of this Profound Sound, sweeping away the Ten Sects will be a matter of mere moments." Li Fan's figure gradually faded, leaving only a thin piece of paper behind.

"When you have accomplished your task, hold this [Supreme Dao Scripture], call my name in your heart, and I will appear."

The voice slowly vanished, and Xuanyuan Tuo, holding the thin plate, saw before his eyes that magnificent and brilliant Dao star field.

"The Supreme Dao Scripture, it seems..."

Xuanyuan Tuo's eyes narrowed slightly, recalling the rumors he had heard about the Profound Yellow True Immortal.

"It is indeed so. I was previously puzzled by the emergence of that Profound Yellow True Immortal. Now, it seems, with assistance from a figure like Grand Ancestor, achieving True Immortality is an easy matter."

Filled with confidence in his future, Xuanyuan Tuo began to scheme in his mind how to settle scores with the Ten Sects.

Suddenly, Xuanyuan Tuo realized something, and his expression subtly changed as he looked in the direction where Li Fan had disappeared.

"My Heavenly Profound Mirror..."

Holding the Supreme Dao Scripture, Xuanyuan Tuo's expression shifted several times. In the end, he still lacked the courage to summon Li Fan directly and demand the Heavenly Profound Mirror back.

"Alas, after all, it is merely an immortal artifact. True might lies within oneself; that is the rightful path." Xuanyuan Tuo took a deep breath, trying to calm the emotional turmoil within him.

However, Xuanyuan Tuo did not know that at this moment, the mirror spirit of the Heavenly Profound Mirror, Jing Xuan, was crying out repeatedly: "Spare me, Celestial Immortal!"

Jing Xuan had initially believed that having his accumulated essence from shedding his immortal form revert to nothing was already an extreme misfortune. However, only after truly falling into Li Fan's hands did he realize that his misfortune had only just begun.

The other party seemed to understand the Heavenly Profound Mirror better than Jing Xuan, its own mirror spirit. The restrictions within the mirror were like empty fancies. Almost instantly, he permeated its core. Then, a figure nearly identical to Jing Xuan, but lacking a certain liveliness, appeared before him.

Almost immediately, Jing Xuan understood Li Fan's intention. He wanted to create a new mirror spirit and replace him!

An unprecedented sense of intense crisis surged within Jing Xuan. He knew that time was running out. Once this new mirror spirit was fully formed, only destruction awaited him.

He had to prove his worth to the other party before then! A unique value that the nascent mirror spirit could not provide!

Jing Xuan's thoughts raced. Connecting this Celestial Immortal's initiative to seek out Xuanyuan Tuo, an answer instantly formed in his mind.

"Celestial Immortal, please spare my life! I might be able to help Celestial Immortal find King Xuanyuan's former beloved!"

Sensing that the process of the new mirror spirit's creation had temporarily halted, Jing Xuan let out a long sigh of relief.

Li Fan's cold voice came through: "Why King Xuanyuan's beloved, and not King Xuanyuan himself?"

Jing Xuan quickly explained, "When King Xuanyuan departed, it was indeed too hurried. I truly do not know his whereabouts. But as for his beloved..."

"Before she left, she cast a divine ability, and actually separated another, identical mirror artifact from my body. She even named it [Profound Heaven], and renamed me [Heavenly Profound]."

Jing Xuan's tone carried a hint of indignation: "Although they have left, and I know not where they went, I can use this connection to vaguely sense their location."

"I can feel that the other me has become far stronger than before. If previously I was a dim star, now I am like the brilliant moon in the sky. It is precisely because of this immense disparity that I felt fear and accelerated my process of shedding immortality. Because I know that if I completely shed my immortal form, I will no longer be the same entity as her, and will forever lose the chance to compete."

Jing Xuan's resentment towards his other self seemed to even surpass his fear of Li Fan. As he spoke, he seemingly entered a trance, rambling on incessantly.

Li Fan had not expected Jing Xuan to be able to track Xuanyuan Hong's childhood sweetheart.

He temporarily halted the creation of the mirror spirit and carefully observed the immortal artifact Heavenly Profound Mirror at this specific time node.

Although the traces were extremely faint, Li Fan, upon careful inspection, still discerned faint "imprint" marks on the immortal artifact.

"Even for my current self, perfectly replicating the Heavenly Profound Mirror and creating another almost identical entity to the original mirror spirit is no easy feat."

"Xuanyuan Hong truly possesses profound foundations. His methods are endless."

Xuanyuan Hong's childhood sweetheart, though unnamed, likely had no complex background and was merely a mortal. To be able to cast such a divine ability, it must have been a gift from Xuanyuan Hong.

"Given Xuanyuan Hong's character, even if he were in danger, he would never allow her to accompany him. So, it's highly probable that the two of them are not in the same place."

To be honest, Li Fan had little interest in tracking someone's beloved. However, he was quite intrigued by the imprint divine ability she had used.

Among the many immortal artifacts, the Heavenly Profound Mirror was quite unique. To be easily replicated by a mortal...

This method bore some resemblance to the [Transformation of True and False] that Li Fan had mastered.

Li Fan carefully observed the traces left within the Heavenly Profound Mirror.

Having not undergone the shedding of its immortal form, the traces left on this immortal artifact were still preserved. Even if minuscule, they could not escape Li Fan's scrutiny and reconstruction.

Before Li Fan's eyes, a scene seemed to unfold.

A blank piece of paper suddenly floated through heaven and earth. It slowly settled upon the former Profound Heaven Mirror.

A slender, jade-like hand gently pressed the paper down.

Upon the white paper, the imprinted Heavenly Profound Mirror slowly manifested in the world.

"This is far superior to the first-generation Grand Celestial Venerable's 'Bifurcation of Immortal and Mortal'."

"It's somewhat similar to that immortal artifact the Ten Sects once discussed, the [Bifurcation Seed of Immortality]?"

He had previously paid no attention to these residual immortal artifacts in the hands of the Ten Sects. However, combined with the possibility that it was a method left by King Xuanyuan, it sparked Li Fan's interest.

His figure flickered, and a moment later, Li Fan had retrieved the [Bifurcation Seed of Immortality] from the tightly guarded custody of the Ten Sects.

He placed it alongside the Heavenly Profound Mirror, comparing them.

"Hmm, this thing..." Jing Xuan's startled and uncertain voice confirmed Li Fan's judgment.

According to the Ten Sects, this [Bifurcation Seed of Immortality] was acquired during a war against the [Dual Sky Realm]. The Dual Sky Realm was not large, but its scenery was quite peculiar.

It was not a normal heaven-and-earth structure, but a heaven-and-earth-heaven pattern. At the center of the world, there seemed to be a mirror, dividing the world into two halves. Not only the scenery, but even the beings in the world existed in pairs.

They were aware of each other's existence, and their fates and lives were intertwined.

At critical moments of life and death, they could achieve a twofold increase in strength through temporary "fusion," thus surviving tribulations. However, the side effect was intense. They would uncontrollably gravitate towards their other self in the other half of the world. In simple terms, their own existence would slowly disappear.

The reason the Dual Sky Realm was so unique was because of the existence of this [Bifurcation Seed of Immortality]. It is said that in ancient times, the Dual Sky Realm, like other immortal cultivation realms, had a normal heaven-and-earth structure. However, one day, the heavens and earth suddenly reversed, as if forcibly refolded.

Innumerable beings in the world died or were injured. When they finally came to their senses, they were horrified to find that beyond the earth, there was another sky. And another themselves.

From then on, the ultimate fate of all beings in the Dual Sky Realm was to gravitate towards and fuse with each other. Then, they would flow towards the [Bifurcation Seed of Immortality] between heaven and earth.

The Dual Sky Realm was already destroyed after being conquered by Profound Yellow. But this Bifurcation Seed of Immortality was acquired by the Ten Sects. As a trump card.

It could create another self, greatly reducing the risk of making choices at critical moments.

Li Fan looked at the immortal seed quietly floating before him.

If the traces on the Heavenly Profound Mirror were imprints, then this immortal seed was full of marks left by folding.

"Using the Great Dao of heaven and earth as paper."

"To be able to change it with one hand. What magnificent spirit, what extraordinary method."

Even though Li Fan's cultivation allowed him to reverse time, after witnessing this [Paper Folding] divine ability, he couldn't help but exclaim at its brilliance.

The path of [Paper Folding] was clearly no longer within the remnants of the primordial. Li Fan had never encountered it in his past reincarnations.

It was only through this journey upstream, arriving ten thousand years ago, that he finally glimpsed its traces.

"So, King Xuanyuan's childhood sweetheart was not an ordinary mortal either," Li Fan rubbed his chin.

"However, it's too early to draw conclusions."

For the current Li Fan, to further advance, the most important thing was to forge his own pure path.

But this path was not easily achieved.

Whether it was the horizontal transcendence of possibilities, the inverse flow of the River of Time, or the [True-False Transformation] where truth becomes falsehood and falsehood becomes truth, all seemed to be viable directions.

However, all of them were progressing with extreme difficulty.

It was as if he had arrived at a crossroads, and Li Fan was somewhat uncertain about which way to proceed.

From a rational perspective, the True-False Transformation was clearly the most suitable and most powerful Great Dao. After all, it could be compared with mountains and seas.

But True-False was in a state of slumber. Without the insights gained from each activation of True-False, comprehending the True-False Transformation became extremely difficult.

It was like a castle in the air, built upon crumbling foundations.

If Li Fan wished to touch upon it again, or even continue to ascend, he would inevitably need some steps to tread upon.

Chapter 1552: The Immortal Falls and Devours the Supreme Origin

The insights gained by Duke Shou Qiu from gazing upon the mountain while observing the sea, the backward-flowing profound sound of King Xuan, and even this art of paper folding could all be considered stepping stones for Li Fan's journey. He comprehended, he learned, then he felt and transformed, gradually touching upon the ineffable transformation between the true and the false.

Li Fan settled on a plan and flicked his finger on the surface of the Heavenly Profound Mirror. The nascent spirit of the mirror, which had been half-created, instantly turned to dust.

Jing Xuan, witnessing this, let out a long sigh of relief. However, after a moment, as Li Fan continued to lightly caress his side with his hand, emanating an inexplicable aura from the {Two-Part Immortal Seed}, an ominous premonition inexplicably surged within Jing Xuan's heart. It was not a mere illusion. Tendrils of power quietly sprouted from the {Two-Part Immortal Seed} beside him, like tentacles coiling around and binding the Heavenly Profound Mirror tightly. Then, countless even finer tendrils branched out from their points of contact. Under Li Fan's instruction, they scoured every inch of the Heavenly Profound Mirror's surface without restraint.

A sense of déjà vu washed over Jing Xuan. "Xuan Tian, I'm taking it away." For reasons unknown, the very words his childhood sweetheart, King Xuan Tian, had spoken to him echoed in his ear once more. "Could it be…" The Heavenly Profound Mirror instinctively trembled, and the power of the Two-Part Immortal Seed enveloping it vibrated even more violently, like boiling mud with ceaseless bubbling. Jing Xuan resisted with all his might but possessed not a whit of power to counter. He could only watch helplessly as another 'self' slowly grew within this "mud"! A third mirror descended into the world, in contrast to the Heavenly and Xuan Tian mirrors.

However, after Li Fan examined the mirror, he shook his head and dismissed it. "It has the form, but lacks the spirit and essence. A piece of trash!" His voice was icy as he applied slight pressure with his hand. Amidst horrifying creaking sounds, this newborn Heavenly Profound Mirror instantly turned to powder, returning to the Two-Part Immortal Seed. Jing Xuan could even vaguely hear the tragic wails of his other self.

Terrified, Jing Xuan, regardless of the bizarre feeling of being used as a replication test subject, quickly spoke of the differences he perceived between himself and the replica during the recent imprinting process, thereby proving his own value. "So that's how it is. Well done," Li Fan nodded, offering ungrudging praise. Having learned from the earlier lesson, Li Fan soon conducted a second experiment. The creation was indeed better than the first attempt, but still significantly fell short of the true Heavenly Profound Mirror.

"It seems this paper-folding imprinting technique is indeed an unfathomable divine ability. It cannot be mastered in a short time by merely relying on the traces it left behind. It requires repeated study." Li Fan had anticipated this and was not bothered. After all, with both the Two-Part Immortal Seed and the Heavenly Profound Mirror in hand, he had ample time for practice. The only thing he needed to be concerned about was that the power of the {Paper Folding} Dao condensed within the Two-Part Immortal Seed would be gradually consumed, diminishing with each use. If it were merely immortal spiritual energy, Li Fan could easily replenish it. But this {Paper Folding} Great Dao could only be created from nothingness through his {True and False Transformation} divine ability. Although the efficiency was slow, especially now that True Illusion was dormant and he could only rely on his own comprehension, Li Fan was optimistic. "But it can still be replenished, so it won't be completely depleted. And concurrently, it will increase my comprehension of the transformation between true and false."

However, from time to time during his research and experimentation, the shadow of Cat Treasure flickered in his mind. "I wonder if Cat Treasure's replication ability is the same as this Paper Folding Great Dao." "Indeed, there is no such thing as something without reason or logic in this world. Those seemingly incredible things are merely due to insufficient knowledge and shallow understanding." "Cat Treasure's Triple Transformation: item replication, lifeform mimicry, and marrow cleansing. The other two abilities…" Li Fan frowned in thought. A sudden idea bloomed in his mind: if he could fully grasp its Dao path, perhaps he could replicate {Cat Treasure} as well.

…

While Li Fan's main body was engrossed in comprehending the Dao, the Great Heavenly Venerable Immortal Puppet remained active. With no suitable successor for the next Profound Yellow Heavenly Venerable yet identified, Li Fan had to shoulder the responsibility of maintaining order in the Profound Yellow Realm. This was not due to any shackles from the Immortal Realm, but for his own sake.

His first priority was to transform the Profound Yellow Realm from the inside out. From his current perspective, the Profound Yellow Realm was still too fragile. Let alone the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, even if the starving immortals within the Immortal Ruins were to stir slightly, they could plunge the Profhen Yellow Realm into eternal damnation. Fortunately, Li Fan possessed ample experience in reconstruction. Moreover, this time, his plan went even further than before, aiming to forge the Profound Yellow Realm into an immortal ark capable of drifting and seeking new life even if the Primordial Sea was swallowed by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation!

Beyond methods like elevating the immortal domain and strengthening the Great Dao Pillar, Li Fan now set his sights on integrating the Fallen Immortal Realm. At this temporal juncture, the Fallen Immortal Realm was a closed-off place, not yet accessible to the beings of the Profound Yellow Realm. Only with the permission of the Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerable could their consciousnesses enter. Li Fan conducted a macroscopic observation of the Fallen Immortal Realm at this time and discovered that, compared to ten thousand years later, its scale was considerably smaller. It was merely a projection of the normal Profound Yellow Realm, with some world variations generated over years of evolution. It seemed to still be in its nascent stage, with many spacetimes that would exist later yet to be born.

However, Li Fan noticed some intriguing details. The Fallen Immortal Realm had recently seen a significant expansion of spacetime. Judging by its emergence time, it coincided precisely with the fierce war between the Profound Yellow and Tai Yuan realms. "Could it be…" Li Fan's heart stirred, and his divine sense traversed these newly born spacetimes. Upon returning, his expression turned unconventional: "Indeed. As the Tai Yuan Realm and the Profound Yellow Realm became completely connected, the Fallen Immortal Realm seemed to have infiltrated the Tai Yuan Realm." The bloody battlefield of the two realms had also quietly appeared within the Fallen Immortal Realm. The only thing that put Li Fan's mind at ease was that the Profound Yellow True Immortal, his own existence, was absent from this new spacetime. "Otherwise, my current concern wouldn't be about reconstructing the Profound Yellow Realm, but about fleeing for my life."

While contemplating, the Great Heavenly Venerable Immortal Puppet made another trip to the Tai Yuan Realm. As expected, above this world, he found the elusive phantom cloud of illusionary dreams. "Not just a momentary reflection of the world back then. It can also self-grow over time." "In the original timeline, the Profound Yellow Realm had been struggling for survival at the edge of the Immortal Ruins, lacking the conditions for growth. But now, it's different." "The Tai Yuan Realm, and even…" Li Fan's gaze shifted towards the surroundings of the Tai Yuan Realm. The Ten Immortal Dao Sects were enthusiastically exploring the unknown starry sky nearby. Li Fan also sensed life forces in the distant sea of stars. At the same time, he seemed to see the shadowy presence of the Fallen Immortal clouds, trailing the footsteps of the Ten Sects.

"It seems necessary to impose some restrictions." A premonition in the depths of his mind told Li Fan that simply watching it grow unchecked was not a wise move. "Though illusory, it is substantive. It does not require a foundation in reality, yet it can float upon the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation like a wooden boat!" The first generation's assessment of the Fallen Immortal Realm still echoed in his mind, and Li Fan dared not be careless. Although the Fallen Immortal Realm was bizarre, seeking to usurp the foundation he had painstakingly built in the Profound Yellow Realm was something he would not tolerate. In the past, with the protection of True Illusion, Li Fan could afford to retreat and start anew. He could simply evade. But now, Li Fan had no room to retreat. The Fallen Immortal Realm, despite its strangeness, would have to fight him first if it wished to displace Li Fan's painstakingly established anchor point. "No matter how you slice it, one cannot sleep soundly with the enemy sleeping next door." A cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. In the past, Li Fan had the protection of True Illusion, allowing him to choose to start anew at any time. He could simply evade. But now, Li Fan had no room to retreat. The Fallen Immortal Realm, despite its strangeness, would have to fight him first if it wished to displace Li Fan's painstakingly established anchor point.

The Fallen Immortal Realm, although strange, was not something that could simply usurp his anchor point and foundation in the Profound Yellow Realm. A battle would be necessary first! The expanding Fallen Immortal Realm, sensing the anomaly around it from Li Fan's restrictions, immediately reacted. It did not exhibit any emotions like living beings. Instead, it mechanically and instantly made corresponding adjustments. Under Li Fan's gaze, the Fallen Immortal clouds seemed to abandon their expansionist ambitions, quietly hovering above the Tai Yuan Realm to strengthen themselves. Almost visibly, the number of metamorphosed timelines within the Tai Yuan Fallen Immortal Realm increased. The source of the Fallen Immortal Realm's existence was not the Profound Yellow cultivators currently active in the Tai Yuan Realm. It even encompassed the Tai Yuan beings that Li Fan had sealed and suppressed! Even the two immortal servants responsible for overseeing the Tai Yuan Resurrection Furnace were reflected within the Tai Yuan Fallen Immortal Realm! This was the Fallen Immortal Realm's first deliberate "reflection." The reflected beings, however, were unaware of anything. But the observer, Li Fan, couldn't help but feel a chill. After a moment of contemplation, Li Fan sent a wisp of his consciousness into the newly formed Tai Yuan Fallen Immortal Realm. His objective was to examine whether the immortal formations and immortal servants within this realm were connected to the Infinite Sea and possessed infinite characteristics. His {Endless Reincarnation} function could indeed create spacetimes out of thin air. However, Endless Reincarnation was completely self-contained and did not connect to the mountains and seas. But this Fallen Immortal Illusion… Li Fan's expression turned solemn as he felt the pressure emanating from the Infinite Sea, a trace of apprehension flashing across his face. "It has actually connected to the mountains and seas?" While shocked, Li Fan also felt a sense of confusion. Connecting to the mountains and seas, in theory, already possessed the necessary conditions for creating immortals. This meant that the seemingly illusory timelines within the Fallen Immortal Realm truly had the potential to produce {True Immortals}. "This…" Theoretically, this was true. However, Li Fan still felt a subtle difference between the Tai Yuan Immortal Formation and the two immortal servants within the Fallen Immortal Realm, compared to their real-world counterparts. And this difference was particularly crucial.

"It only possesses the Infinite Sea, but not the Upper Mountain?" Gazing at the illusory Tai Yuan Realm before him for a long time, Li Fan finally experienced a moment of enlightenment and arrived at an answer. To verify his conjecture, Li Fan flashed into the location of the two immortal servants within the Fallen Immortal Realm. He deliberately revealed his aura as a {True Immortal}. In the real world, upon encountering a True Immortal, the immortal servants would be obligated to pay homage. This was an ironclad rule etched into the core of every immortal servant. But in this Fallen Immortal Realm, these two immortal servants completely ignored Li Fan's aura and, conversely, jointly attacked this intruder. "As expected." Li Fan calmly blocked their attacks, understanding dawning upon him. "It only possesses infinite power but lacks the 'potential' of the Upper Mountain." "Without climbing the highest mountain, one does not know the height of the heavens. Without being on the Upper Mountain, one does not know what an immortal truly is." Possessing infinite power, but lacking the support of 'potential,' the effectiveness they could unleash was greatly reduced. Their strength was merely one-tenth of that of the real immortal servants. This discovery unexpectedly relieved Li Fan. After suppressing the two unworthy immortal servants and casually destroying this Fallen Immortal spacetime, Li Fan quietly withdrew from the Tai Yuan Fallen Immortal Realm. For the Fallen Immortal Realm itself, the existence or destruction of individual spacetimes had no significant impact. In the blink of an eye, the spacetime destroyed by Li Fan had regenerated. Li Fan watched the scene unfold before him: "Although the Fallen Immortal Realm is illusory, it is built upon reality. Unless reality is swallowed by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation and beings cease to exist, the Fallen Immortal Realm will always regenerate." "And even if reality is encroached upon by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, the Fallen Immortal Realm can still survive for a period." At this thought, Li Fan was momentarily uncertain whether the real world or the Fallen Immortal Realm was the more "advanced" existence. "Since the Fallen Immortal Realm can connect to the Infinite Sea, then theoretically, it should also be able to connect to the Upper Mountain, but it has not…" "So it was done intentionally?" In the allegory of mountains and seas, the calamities of the world's beings originated from the connection between the sea and the mountains. The Fallen Immortal Realm abandoning the mountains and returning to the sea seemed like a method of escaping tribulation. "If that were the case, does a complete return to the mountains exist?" Li Fan naturally thought of this. "Possessing the 'potential' of an immortal, but lacking the 'infinite' attribute. Which is superior, and which is inferior, is hard to say." "But perhaps this is the original form of immortals." The sealed Tai Yuan Fallen Immortal Realm showed no signs of further regeneration or collision with the restrictions Li Fan had imposed. It simply hovered above the Tai Yuan and Profound Yellow realms, constantly evolving and growing. For the Fallen Immortal Realm, the spatial size in reality was not the key factor limiting its growth. As long as there were living beings within its coverage, the Fallen Immortal Realm could continue to propagate itself. Its previous outward expansion towards the starry sky was merely an instinctual mechanism for self-enhancement. Now, with its growth hampered by Li Fan's restrictions, it instinctively retreated, continuing to multiply within its original territory. Li Fan observed this peculiar creation, at a loss for a moment. The Fallen Immortal Realm as a whole seemed to lack subjective consciousness, unlike the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao. It operated merely on a "mechanical" instinctual judgment. However, it was the remnant left behind by a powerful immortal from the Immortal Realm. It might even transform into a breeding ground for their resurrection. Especially the Fallen Immortal Realm's characteristic of drifting upon the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation made Li Fan recall the Immortal Coffin he had encountered before. However, compared to the Immortal Coffin, which relied solely on the solidity of its Dao principles to resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, the Fallen Immortal Realm was clearly far more advanced. Li Fan cursed inwardly. Choosing to build his anchor point with the Profound Yellow Realm indeed had its pros and cons. Based on his understanding of the Profound Yellow Realm's past events, he could establish a foundation rapidly. However, the Profound Yellow Realm was riddled with hidden secrets, and even at his current level of power, he had to proceed with utmost caution. Otherwise, he might misstep and fall into disaster. "Regardless, one cannot afford to let the enemy rest easy beside them." A cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. In the past, Li Fan had the protection of True Illusion, allowing him to choose to start anew at any time. He could simply evade. But now, Li Fan had no room to retreat. The Fallen Immortal Realm, despite its strangeness, would have to fight him first if it wished to displace Li Fan's painstakingly established anchor point.

Chapter 1553: Heaven's Capital Transforms into Pillars Again

Li Fan did not act rashly.

Before making a move against the Fallen Immortal Realm, he needed time to accumulate and prepare.

The first order of business was to eliminate the hidden dangers around the Profound Yellow Realm one by one.

His divine sense returned to reality from the Fallen Immortal Realm. The Great Heavenly Venerable Immortal Puppet's first action was to gain control of the Astral Crossing Grand Formation.

The immortal formation set up by King Xuan back then had long been battered and broken during the Profound Yellow Realm's various external campaigns.

The golden chains that bound Tai Yuan were already the last great feat it could accomplish.

However, if the Ten Sects were powerless to repair it, it did not mean Li Fan was.

Amidst the roaring of the Profound Yellow World, the first to be rejuvenated and resurrected was the fallen [Xian Beast].

When the massive body of the Xian Beast appeared, the Ten Immortal Dao Sects were initially bewildered. They did not know the origin of this terrifying exotic beast. After a moment, someone recalled its identity from ancient memories tens of thousands of years ago.

Thus, great fear arose in their hearts.

Why had the Profound Heaven Sect's sect-guarding divine beast suddenly been resurrected? Could it be that the mysterious and unfathomable Half-Immortal King Xuan was returning?

The Ten Immortal Dao Sects fell into deep unease. Ignoring the opening of the Tai Yuan starry sky, the core cultivators of the Ten Sects returned to the Profound Yellow Realm overnight to convene and discuss countermeasures. They even attempted to send a message to the Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerable for consultation, but received no response.

The Great Heavenly Venerable was missing.

Just as their fear intensified, the Myriad Immortal Alliance suddenly declared war on the Ten Immortal Dao Sects. This strike left the members of the Ten Sects feeling a mixture of amusement and exasperation.

They indeed feared King Xuan, but what was a mere Myriad Immortal Alliance? The strongest in the Alliance, that Law-Transmitting Immortal Venerable, was only at the Harmonious Dao realm. Where did they get the courage to dare challenge the Ten Sects?

Both amused and enraged, just as the Ten Sects decided to suppress these insignificant rascals of the Myriad Immortal Alliance with thunderous force.

However, the series of actions by the Myriad Immortal Alliance suddenly caught the Ten Sects completely off guard.

First, the Law-Transmitter declared his true identity to the world: Xuanyuan Tuo. The former leader of the Profound Heaven Sect, descendant of King Xuan, Xuanyuan Hong. When the Ten Sects wreaked havoc on Profound Heaven's foundation, Xuanyuan Hong established the Profound Heaven Sect precisely to overthrow the rule of the Ten Sects and restore King Xuan's reign!

The Ten Sects had ruled the Profound Yellow Realm for ten thousand years, and the world had almost no knowledge of the Profound Heaven Sect. Therefore, for ordinary cultivators, this declaration from the Myriad Immortal Alliance was merely a pretext for "legitimacy."

But in the eyes of the Ten Sects, it held a completely different meaning.

The Law-Transmitter was actually a descendant of King Xuan?

A mere Harmonious Dao cultivator would certainly not have the courage to stand against the Ten Sects. But what if King Xuan himself stood behind the Law-Transmitter?

No wonder the Law-Transmitter, an outsider cultivator with no roots, could rise so rapidly. And could also create a method that was completely different from the current cultivation methods, yet was also exquisite.

Coupled with the loss of control of the Astral Crossing Grand Formation and the resurrection of the Xian Beast, the Ten Sects finally confirmed.

King Xuan had returned!

Ancient memories resurfaced, and fear followed suit.

How strong was King Xuan?

Even now, the Ten Sects still had Longevity cultivators who, ten thousand years ago, had personally witnessed King Xuan's sweeping victory across the world in his Half-Immortal state. They knew very well how powerful King Xuan was.

Even if all the Ten Sects joined forces, they would still not be King Xuan's match! If they attacked proactively, they would only be seeking their own demise!

Through analysis based on their perceived understanding of King Xuan, the core of the Ten Sects reached a conclusion: although King Xuan had returned, given his personality, even if he wanted revenge, he would require a righteous cause.

The reason he did not show himself, but allowed his descendant to provoke the Ten Sects, was to lure the Ten Sects into attacking proactively. Then, under the guise of counterattack, he would justly and ruthlessly slaughter and take revenge on the Ten Sects!

The awakened Ten Sects, believing they had discovered King Xuan's scheme, broke out in a cold sweat and hastily ordered their disciples to temporarily refrain from any conflict with the Myriad Immortal Alliance.

Thus, an extremely strange situation appeared on the Profound Yellow continent.
