The Myriad Immortal Alliance, under the banner of the Profound Heaven Sect, grew wildly and savagely. Meanwhile, the Ten Immortal Dao Sects, the actual rulers of the Profound Yellow Realm, turned a blind eye, playing the role of shelled turtles.

Such bizarre phenomena greatly boosted the morale of the Myriad Immortal Alliance. Their expansion rate accelerated once more.

The disciples of the Ten Sects' grassroots, however, were utterly depressed and confused.

Relying on their past prestige, the Ten Sects' core members temporarily suppressed the disgruntled emotions within the sects, knowing that this situation could not last long.

Thus, they jointly devised a plan: quickly invite the Grand Master Tiandu!

In fact, if King Xuan had not been heavily injured after his great battle with the Grand Master, they would not have dared to attack King Xuan.

Now that King Xuan had returned, they could only seek help from the Grand Master once more.

After all, the inheritances of the Ten Sects all originated from Tiandu. The Grand Master should not stand by and watch them perish.

This was the theory, but in practice, the Ten Sects had no guarantee. After all, it had been many years since anyone had seen the Grand Master. Even during several life-or-death crises for the Profound Yellow Realm, the Grand Master had never appeared.

In the secret chamber of the Great Dao Sect, more than half of the leaders of the Ten Sects gathered, discussing countermeasures.

Everyone wore gloomy expressions.

Fang Dingge coughed lightly: "Everyone need not be so worried. Don't forget our discovery in the starry sky near Tai Yuan. If it truly comes to the worst, what does it matter if we cede this corner of the Profound Yellow Realm to King Xuan? That place is far better than the edge of this Immortal Ruins."

This declaration of defeat before battle did not draw any objections from the group. Instead, everyone nodded in unison, agreeing with Fang Dingge's statement.

"Before we leave, we will empty out all the accumulations of the Ten Sects over the years. We will leave behind only an empty Profound Yellow for him. Hmph..." The speaker was an extremely aged person. His beard and hair were all white, and his facial skin had all shriveled together, making him look quite eerie. The light in his cloudy eyes seemed about to extinguish completely. It seemed that the so-called Longevity realm had also reached the end of life.

The others present, hearing the elder's veiled malicious words, did not echo them, merely displaying varied expressions.

However, given the elder's status and position, no one stepped forward to object.

The elder was named Ruan Tianliu, the Grand Elder of the First Origin Sect. When the sect leader of the First Origin Sect perished on the Tai Yuan battlefield and was not resurrected by the Profound Yellow True Immortal, this person regained control of the First Origin Sect's authority.

Ruan Tianliu was also one of the few cultivators among the Ten Sects who had witnessed King Xuan's power. He was extremely fearful of that Half-Immortal. Therefore, from the beginning, he had strongly opposed the Ten Sects taking action against the Myriad Immortal Alliance.

"Elder Ruan is correct. It can be said that the essence of the Profound Yellow has been largely extracted by our Ten Sects. Even if we transfer it, there will not be much loss. Actually, haven't we long made contingency plans for escape? However, if there were still those within the sect who opposed it, insisting on staying in the Profound Yellow Realm, then perhaps now, everyone's opinions have quickly unified due to King Xuan's appearance." Xiahou Yan, the Lord of Wuding Prison, said with a smile that was not a smile, looking at everyone.

"It's just hateful that the Two-Part Immortal Seed inexplicably disappeared. Otherwise, we could have pulled the wool over their eyes and left stealthily. The main body could have fled to the Tai Yuan starry sky, leaving behind only weaker clones to fight to the death with that Profound Heaven Sect!" A voice of regret sounded from the crowd.

"This Two-Part Immortal Seed disappeared strangely. It doesn't seem like its power dissipated, nor was it taken by King Xuan. After all, Xuanyuan Hong acted honorably and would never do something so underhanded."

"Could it be that he brought a helper back this time?"

The people in the room looked at each other suspiciously.

Not long after, they turned to the main topic: "Who will go to invite the Grand Master this time?"

It had to be known that the Grand Master Tiandu was not as approachable as they publicly claimed. One wrong move could lead to death.

"I will lead the way." Seeing everyone hesitate, Fang Dingge snorted coldly and spoke first.

After their expressions shifted, the rest of the Ten Sects finally decided on a team of five.

They would travel to Tiandu to invite the Grand Master out of seclusion.

"Ten thousand years have passed. Although we have sent messages and tributes to Tiandu regularly, we cannot be sure if the Grand Master still recognizes us. Based on the experiences of our ancestors, we still need to move Him with something He is interested in..."

The Ten Sects recorded all the recent anomalies in the Profound Yellow Realm onto shadow stones, and forcefully linked them to that King Xuan, using them as bargaining chips to invite the Grand Master.

"If only the Profound Yellow True Immortal had not perished on the Tai Yuan battlefield."

As the group was about to reach Tiandu, Cao Yingyue, the representative of the Great Dao Sect, suddenly looked at the distant sky and sighed softly.

The figures of the Ten Sects paused slightly.

"Profound Yellow True Immortal..." Everyone was momentarily lost in thought, then shook their heads, suppressing the myriad thoughts in their minds.

They continued to fly towards Tiandu.

According to the descriptions of those who had been there, they smoothly entered the city in the sky.

It was called Tiandu, but it was more like a dojo.

There were only a few scattered buildings.

Fang Dingge, holding an ancient token given by the Grand Master, led everyone into Tiandu smoothly.

"This is considered the first step successfully completed."

"It is said that even with the token given by the Grand Master back then, whether you can enter safely depends entirely on His mood. If you disturb Him, even a peak Harmonious Dao cultivator could disappear without a trace." The members of the Ten Sects exchanged glances and breathed a sigh of relief.

They continued to move deeper towards the location where the Grand Master was said to be seated, as described in the records. After pushing open the vermilion wooden door, two figures suddenly appeared before them.

The group of Ten Sects froze. They quickly prostrated themselves, shouting in unison, "Greetings, Grand Master!"

Inside the pavilion, there was absolute silence.

Cold sweat dripped from the foreheads of the Ten Sects' group.

The Grand Master did not respond for a long time.

Just as the Ten Sects' group was becoming uncertain, one of the figures suddenly spoke.

"Grand Master..."

"Are you referring to this pillar?"

The Ten Sects' group was instantly stunned and looked up sharply.

Indeed, in front of them, the scene was exactly as depicted in the records.

Two figures stood there.

One was seated and chanting.

But the other...

was not a young boy.

But a middle-aged man with an imposing aura, who looked like an immortal from the heavens.

The moment Fang Dingge saw him, he felt a sense of familiarity.

But the words the man spoke were too shocking, leaving him no time to think.

"Grand Master... pillar..."

"What does it mean?"

At this moment, the attention of the Ten Sects' group finally focused on a pillar being gently caressed by the middle-aged man beside him.

An almost impossible thought then emerged in the minds of the Ten Sects' group.

Thus, their bodies trembled uncontrollably from extreme fear.

A moment later, being stared at by the middle-aged man, their trembling was forcibly suppressed. But their hearts remained icy cold.

And the words that followed from the middle-aged man confirmed their suspicions.

"From now on, the Profound Yellow Realm will no longer have a Grand Master."

"Whatever you do, you will have to rely on yourselves."

"Go now."

Seemingly too lazy to waste words with the Ten Sects' group, the middle-aged man waved his hand.

The group felt a dizzying sensation of the world spinning, and then they were outside Tiandu. When they looked back, the building that had hovered above the Profound Yellow Realm for ten thousand years had actually vanished!

"Dingge... Brother Dingge."

After a long silence, the group finally regained their senses.

To them, the Grand Master Tiandu, who seemed omnipotent and descended from the Immortal Realm, had actually been turned into a pillar.

This event had impacted them too greatly.

To the extent that for a time, they even stammered when speaking.

But after all, they were leaders of the Ten Sects. No matter how shocked they were, after such a long time, they finally managed to accept it, albeit reluctantly.

Fang Dingge steadied himself and took a deep breath: "Let's discuss it when we get back."

On the way back, Fang Dingge suddenly stopped his flight and blurted out: "I remember who that person was just now! The First Generation Profound Yellow Great Heavenly Venerable!"

His words caused everyone to stare at each other in disbelief.

..."A bunch of clowns!" Li Fan in Tiandu shook his head slightly.

He no longer paid much attention to the Ten Immortal Dao Sects.

Instead, he shifted his focus to the sealed Grand Master.

Even though this was the second time he had sealed him, Li Fan could say he had fought a tough battle.

Even before this, Li Fan had already mobilized the power of the Astral Crossing Grand Formation, transferring the Profound Yellow Realm to the edge of the Darkest Sea, a safe distance from the Immortal Ruins.

Then, he activated the power of the Shou Qiu Gong's legacy phantom within the High Wall.

To deal with the Grand Master, ordinary Dao laws were all useless. Only the "Blade of Spiritual Reduction" from [True and False Transformation] was the only effective method.

Even with prior experience fighting him, there was no guarantee of no risk.

Fortunately, the extent of Li Fan's mastery over the transformation of true and false was too high a counter to the Grand Master's [Boundless] Great Dao.

Ultimately, he was sealed.

"With one Heavenly Pillar establishing the foundation, the Eternal Immortal Boat can be considered to have taken initial shape."

Li Fan, extremely satisfied, touched the Boundless Heavenly Pillar again.

This time, in the plan to reinforce the Profound Yellow Realm, Li Fan had excluded the Shou Qiu phantom.

After all, Shou Qiu Gong was now considered an unstable factor for the current Li Fan. Although the world said Shou Qiu Gong had noble character, Li Fan still would not place his life and death on anyone's morality.

"With Boundless in place, the next step is the Starving Immortal."

Although the Starving Immortal had not yet attained the Nameless realm, in terms of danger level, it was even above the Grand Master.

Chapter 1554: Morality Has True Immortals

The reason Li Fan could so easily suppress the Great Master was due to Li Fan's Blade of Spiritual Reduction, which inherently countered the Grand Master. The Grand Master's Grand Dao of Boundlessness was no match for the {True and False Transformation}.

However, he could not be so effective against the Starving Immortal.

Before the Starving Immortal's spiritual essence was reduced to its lowest point, its strength as a half-step Nameless realm cultivator would be enough to obliterate the First Generation Immortal Puppet. At present, without the safety net of True Restoration, Li Fan's main body would not easily intervene when eliminating the hidden dangers around the Profound Yellow Realm.

As for the Shou Qiu phantom…

In his previous life, Li Fan had used his clone, Li Buren, to gather all the Immortal Realm chess pieces, and then, under the heavy burden of a Nameless True Immortal, he was able to activate Duke Shou Qiu's legacy. However, this time, the actual Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul within his body had vanished along with the tribulation of the three Daos merging. While he could temporarily simulate the power of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul with the {True and False Transformation}, he was still unable to weave a complete and stable Myriad Forms Dao Net to accommodate the expansion of the Immortal Realm. Furthermore, the First Generation Immortal Puppet's strength was simply not enough to impress the Shou Qiu phantom.

Therefore, this time, Li Fan used the First Generation Immortal Puppet to display the power of "sitting on the mountain and gazing at the sea," which resonated with the Shou Qiu phantom within the High Wall, directly granting him partial control of the Broken Chess Dao Field. Although this made things much more convenient, it also had its drawbacks.

The Shou Qiu phantom was used to support and resist the Dao Annihilation tribulation in the nearby starry sky. To be able to summon it, one had to provide replenishment first. In his previous life, there was the support of the Primordial Bones. Besides, Li Fan could utterly disregard the safety of the starry sky within the High Wall, ignoring the tribulations of Dao Annihilation, and maximally draw upon the power of the Shou Qiu phantom. But now, there was only half a bone of the Primordial Bones within the complete Immortal Realm chess piece, which was hardly useful. Although the Grand Dao of Boundlessness held a high status, in terms of supporting the tribulations of Dao Annihilation, exchanging equivalent amounts, it was only equivalent to half a Heavenly Pillar. Combined, they could only replace the power of one Shou Qiu phantom, and Li Fan also had to consider his own safety. Therefore, dealing with the Starving Immortal still required careful preparation.

Even though Li Fan had easily suppressed the Starving Immortal in his previous life, making it a Heavenly Pillar, and had savored its power, he understood this point perfectly. Thus, he did not dare to be careless. Fortunately, in terms of understanding the Grand Dao of {Hunger}, Li Fan's comprehension level was likely even higher than that of the Starving Immortal at this moment! After meticulous planning, the perfect trap targeting the Starving Immortal was completed.

Three years later, in the Profound Yellow Realm's time, on the Immortal Ruins battlefield, the skeletal body meditating and comprehending the Dao suddenly opened its eyes. It looked towards the "distant" center of the starry sea.

"What is this... situation?"

"Someone is trying to seize ownership of the Grand Dao of {Hunger}?"

At first, it was somewhat confused. After a while, the Starving Immortal finally understood why it had inexplicably awakened from its enlightenment. The Starving Immortal found it incredible, even finding it somewhat amusing. After all, the skeleton of the previous {Starving Immortal} lay beneath its own feet. It was impossible in this world for someone to understand the Grand Dao of Hunger better than itself.

"Still stubbornly cultivating this path, they probably haven't discovered my existence yet. But they can wake me from enlightenment, indicating that this person's comprehension of the Dao of Hunger has already made considerable progress." The Starving Immortal found it interesting: "If I were to devour this person, perhaps it could save me some hardship in enlightenment." With a thought, the chains wrapped around the Starving Immortal retracted with a clattering sound. The Starving Immortal took its first step, and the lost flesh had already been restored.

Its form flickered, and it had already arrived near the location of another {Hunger} Dao cultivator it had sensed. "Hmm?" The Starving Immortal inexplicably felt that the escaping Dao principles in the nearby starry sky were somewhat familiar. But for a moment, it couldn't recall where this sense of familiarity came from. And the enlightened being that should have been here was nowhere to be seen. The Starving Immortal's heart sank, and it quickly scanned its surroundings. Suddenly, upon seeing a figure standing quietly in the star field not far away, the Starving Immortal's body froze rigid. Instincts from its body and soul almost made it blurt out the word "Master." This was because the figure, whether in terms of build or aura, was almost identical to its master, {Inaction}!

And as if sensing the probing gaze of the Starving Immortal, the back figure slowly turned around at this moment. A gaunt face, calm eyes. When this face fell into the Starving Immortal's eyes, it was no different from lightning strikes, shaking the Starving Immortal's soul and clouding its consciousness. "It's really Master?!" As shock and confusion, along with many emotions, surged simultaneously. The surrounding starry sky subtly changed. Faint, almost imperceptible thin lines crisscrossed, like an invisible net, enveloping the Starving Immortal. The figure of {Inaction} disappeared, replaced by scenes changing all around it. The heavens and earth were collapsing, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation descended! It was indeed the boundless disaster buried deep in the Starving Immortal's heart, from the past…

However, this time, even Master {Inaction} could not resist this monstrous calamity. It was swallowed by the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation as it recounted. "Master!" The Starving Immortal trembled in fear. The approaching Dao Annihilation aura from all directions made it instinctively want to flee. Moments later, it finally regained its senses. "No... this is a trap?" Although the Starving Immortal finally realized something, it was too late. The grand formation had already taken shape, and nothing could be undone. The Starving Immortal felt its vision gradually darken. It was as if an invisible giant hand was pressing down on it. And its connection with the bones of the previous {Starving Immortal} was inexplicably severed. All resistance was like a drop in the bucket. A Heavenly Pillar slowly formed within the formation. It was only at this moment, when the pillar was set, that Li Fan manipulated the First Generation Immortal Puppet to appear. "To attack the city is the worst strategy; to attack the heart is the best." He recited slowly with satisfaction. First, he used the trick of luring the tiger away from its mountain, then he shook its mind with the {Inaction} Immortal, and then, with his comprehension of the Grand Dao of Hunger, he severed its connection with the skeleton beneath the Immortal Ruins. This directly reduced the difficulty of capturing the Starving Immortal by more than half. If he had forcibly fought the Starving Immortal on the Immortal Ruins battlefield, it would not have been so easy.

"It's a pity that the Starving Immortal has not yet attained the Nameless realm." "It's still only half a Heavenly Pillar." Li Fan surveyed the three Heavenly Pillars he had collected so far, shaking his head slightly. {Primordial}, {Boundless}, {Hunger}. All of them were incomplete, far from the magnificent sight of them standing tall in the sea of stars in his previous life. "But one cannot be too demanding." "Although Nameless Heavenly Venerables are good, the risks are too great. With the slightest carelessness, my Eternal Immortal Boat might be overturned before it's even built. These three are barely adequate for now." "If the quality is insufficient, then make up for it with quantity." Li Fan comforted himself. Without the reliance of True Restoration, Li Fan had learned to compromise. He no longer pursued perfection but prioritized stability. After carefully storing the Starving Immortal Heavenly Pillar, Li Fan then proceeded to the Immortal Ruins battlefield. Although the Starving Immortal who comprehended the Dao was gone, the skeleton of the previous {Starving Immortal} still remained, and the Immortal Ruins' suction power towards the outside had not completely disappeared. In his previous life, Li Fan had chosen to achieve the status of Starving Immortal. After the Starving Immortal attained the Nameless realm, this skeleton had vanished. But now, the giant character {Hunger} was still quietly engraved on the Immortal Ruins battlefield! Li Fan did not attempt to move this skeleton. Because he keenly sensed the aura of Dao Annihilation tribulation supported by the skeleton. His experience from his previous life told him that if this skeleton were lost, the surrounding starry sky would immediately be affected by Dao Annihilation. "Being restricted like this is truly frustrating." Li Fan slowly uttered these words. Although he could not move it easily, it did not prevent Li Fan from meditating and comprehending the Dao, just like the Starving Immortal. Of course, Li Fan was not trying to become the next {Starving Immortal}. He was trying to comprehend the Dao path of this skeleton's owner before crossing the Dao Annihilation and arriving at the {Primordial} possibility. Li Fan had a vague feeling. Compared to the Grand Dao of Hunger, the original Dao path seemed to be able to expand his Myriad Forms Dao Net even further. Still sitting on the Immortal Ruins battlefield, in the center of the giant True Immortal inscription. However, Li Fan did not bind himself with chains. He was confident that with his own will, he could resist the influence of the Grand Dao of Hunger. As his comprehension gradually resonated with the skeleton beneath him, intermittent memories from the skeleton emerged in his mind. From distant to near. "It's happening again! It's happening again! The last time the heavens collapsed, I was fortunate enough to escape. This time, I'm afraid I won't be so lucky! Damn it, the {Immortal Coffin of Passage} is lost, and I haven't found it after so many years of effort!" In the distance, the continuous heavens disappeared without warning. The tide of Dao Annihilation was hidden in the darkness, pressing in from all directions. Faintly, he could hear the sounds of mountains and seas colliding and roaring from the darkness. This sound was too familiar. It was this sound, like a death knell, that had continuously sounded during the fall of his homeland. Ordinary people could not perceive it, only cultivators who could perceive the mountains and seas could hear it. Now, this symphony of mountains and seas echoed again, awakening the Starving Immortal's inherent fear. Without any intention of resisting, he wanted to flee. "The Immortal Realm has fallen, and it's already a foregone conclusion. I can only go to the lower realm to avoid the storm for now and think of other solutions." "Damn it, who took my {Immortal Coffin of Passage}!" As if he had long been prepared to flee, with a flash of light, the Starving Immortal arrived near the ascension passage before most immortals. As the connection point between immortals and mortals, as long as one passed through there, they would be temporarily safe. "The Immortal Realm's collapse will last for some time. I hope I can find a way to escape before the Dao Annihilation spreads to the lower realm." The Starving Immortal was filled with anxiety and was about to ascend to the lower realm. Suddenly, a voice called out to him. "Fellow Daoist, please wait!" The Starving Immortal's heart instinctively became vigilant, and he pretended not to hear, continuing to flee forward. But the journey that should have taken only an instant suddenly became so long that he could not reach the end no matter what! "Fellow Daoist turns a deaf ear, it seems you do not intend to give me face." "Originally, I wanted to discuss it with you, but now, there is no need!" The voice grew closer and closer, like a shadow. In a moment, it arrived beside the Starving Immortal. "The Immortal Realm is in distress, and the lower realm will not last long. Someone must stand up and endure the Dao Annihilation for everyone. Why can't it be you?!" "Sacrifice the individual for the greater good. We survivors will remember you." The figure spoke earnestly, and then the Starving Immortal felt a hand placed on his shoulder. Then, he could no longer move! First, there was shock, then a nameless rage surged in his heart. "You are seeking death!" Endless suction erupted from the Starving Immortal's body, madly devouring everything around it. Even the ascension passage began to waver. Many fleeing True Immortals, unable to beg for help, were devoured by the Starving Immortal. However, in the center of this all-stirring vortex, another figure, unaffected, looked at the Starving Immortal with regret. "It seems your realization is indeed too low." "There is no need to even mourn for you. It saves trouble." In a few words, the Starving Immortal's fate seemed to have been decided, and it completely disregarded the Starving Immortal's own thoughts. The Starving Immortal was both shocked and enraged. "If it weren't for trying to quickly integrate into the Grand Dao of this world, why would I have disguised myself and suffered such bullying!" "Damn it!" The weight on the Starving Immortal's shoulder grew heavier and heavier, and it felt itself gradually separating from the entire world. The ubiquitous immense force seemed to be crushing and grinding it inch by inch. In the last moment before consciousness disappeared, the Starving Immortal desperately tried to see the face of this figure. "It's you?! The Moral True Immortal?!" This was the last lingering thought echoing from the Starving Immortal's skeleton. It contained immense resentment and lingered for a long time. ... "Finally, I'm alive." "Everyone else is dead, only I am alive. The facts prove that I was right. Humph, Master, junior brothers, rest in peace in the afterlife." Having crossed the Dao Annihilation and endured hardships, arriving at a new possibility, the Starving Immortal looked at the familiar Immortal Realm scenery with exceptional joy. However, his good mood was quickly interrupted. "Strange, shouldn't the {Immortal Coffin of Passage} have descended into the present world with me? Why can't I see it?" "Moreover, the Grand Dao here seems to be somewhat resistant to me." "It seems I need to find a way." ... "What are Lian Shan Sage Monarch and Gui Hai, but hypocrites who try to monopolize the mountains and seas!" "The Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas is accessible to everyone. Today, I will devour mountains and seas!" In the shattered doomsday with rumbling thunder, the Starving Immortal roared to the heavens in madness. "You beast..." Beside him, an old man with only half a head muttered sternly. "Old man! How do you feel watching your disciples and grandchildren, and the Grand Dao of this world that you protected, being devoured by me one by one? Hahaha!" "You beast..." The half-headed skull did not respond, only repeating its reprimand. "Boring!" The Starving Immortal stomped the skull into pieces with a kick. Broken bone fragments, along with flesh and brain matter, instantly splattered. But at mid-air, they were adsorbed and stuck to the Starving Immortal's leg, then wriggled and disappeared into the leg. "I refuse to believe!" "I can even devour the Grand Dao, so why should I fear these mountains and seas!" The Starving Immortal looked at the symphony of mountains and seas quietly playing in the darkness ahead, its eyes turning crimson.

Chapter 1554: True Immortal of Morality

Li Fan’s Blade of Spiritual Reduction had a natural counter to the Great Master’s Grand Dao of Boundlessness, rendering his abilities ineffective against {True and False Transformation}.

However, the same could not be said for the Starving Immortal. Before its spiritual essence was diminished, its strength as a half-step Nameless realm cultivator was sufficient to obliterate the First Generation Immortal Puppet. With {True Restoration} no longer a safety net, Li Fan’s main body would not easily intervene when eliminating hidden dangers around the Profound Yellow Realm.

As for the Shou Qiu phantom…

In his previous life, Li Fan had gathered all the Immortal Realm chess pieces using his clone, Li Buren, and under the immense pressure of a Nameless True Immortal, he was able to activate Duke Shou Qiu’s legacy. However, this time, the true Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul within his body had vanished along with the tribulation of the three Daos merging. While he could temporarily simulate the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul’s power with {True and False Transformation}, he was still unable to weave a complete and stable Myriad Forms Dao Net to accommodate the expansion of the Immortal Realm. Furthermore, the First Generation Immortal Puppet’s strength was simply not enough to impress the Shou Qiu phantom.

Therefore, this time, Li Fan used the First Generation Immortal Puppet to display the power of “sitting on the mountain and gazing at the sea,” which resonated with the Shou Qiu phantom within the High Wall, directly granting him partial control of the Broken Chess Dao Field. Although this made things much more convenient, it also had its drawbacks.

The Shou Qiu phantom was used to support and resist the Dao Annihilation tribulation in the nearby starry sky. To be able to summon it, one had to provide replenishment first. In his previous life, there was the support of the Primordial Bones. Besides, Li Fan could utterly disregard the safety of the starry sky within the High Wall, ignoring the tribulations of Dao Annihilation, and maximally draw upon the power of the Shou Qiu phantom. But now, there was only half a bone of the Primordial Bones within the complete Immortal Realm chess piece, which was hardly useful. Although the Grand Dao of Boundlessness held a high status, in terms of supporting the tribulations of Dao Annihilation, exchanging equivalent amounts, it was only equivalent to half a Heavenly Pillar. Combined, they could only replace the power of one Shou Qiu phantom, and Li Fan also had to consider his own safety. Therefore, dealing with the Starving Immortal still required careful preparation.

Even though Li Fan had easily suppressed the Starving Immortal in his previous life, making it a Heavenly Pillar, and had savored its power, he understood this point perfectly. Thus, he did not dare to be careless. Fortunately, in terms of understanding the Grand Dao of {Hunger}, Li Fan’s comprehension level was likely even higher than that of the Starving Immortal at this moment! After meticulous planning, the perfect trap targeting the Starving Immortal was completed.

Three years later, in the Profound Yellow Realm's time, on the Immortal Ruins battlefield, the skeletal body meditating and comprehending the Dao suddenly opened its eyes. It looked towards the “distant” center of the starry sea.

“What is this… situation?”

“Someone is trying to seize ownership of the Grand Dao of {Hunger}?”

At first, it was somewhat confused. After a while, the Starving Immortal finally understood why it had inexplicably awakened from its enlightenment. The Starving Immortal found it incredible, even finding it somewhat amusing. After all, the skeleton of the previous {Starving Immortal} lay beneath its own feet. It was impossible in this world for someone to understand the Grand Dao of Hunger better than itself.

“Still stubbornly cultivating this path, they probably haven’t discovered my existence yet. But they can wake me from enlightenment, indicating that this person’s comprehension of the Dao of Hunger has already made considerable progress.” The Starving Immortal found it interesting: “If I were to devour this person, perhaps it could save me some hardship in enlightenment.” With a thought, the chains wrapped around the Starving Immortal retracted with a clattering sound. The Starving Immortal took its first step, and the lost flesh had already been restored.

Its form flickered, and it had already arrived near the location of another {Hunger} Dao cultivator it had sensed. “Hmm?” The Starving Immortal inexplicably felt that the escaping Dao principles in the nearby starry sky were somewhat familiar. But for a moment, it couldn’t recall where this sense of familiarity came from. And the enlightened being that should have been here was nowhere to be seen. The Starving Immortal’s heart sank, and it quickly scanned its surroundings. Suddenly, upon seeing a figure standing quietly in the star field not far away, the Starving Immortal’s body froze rigid. Instincts from its body and soul almost made it blurt out the word “Master.” This was because the figure, whether in terms of build or aura, was almost identical to its master, {Inaction}!

Chapter 1556: Refining the Profound Yellow Realm with Pills

As the memories of the previous Starving Immortal, or rather, the "Dao Devourer" from another possibility, flashed through Li Fan's mind, his skeletal remains transformed into streams of light, becoming another Heavenly Pillar.

Although it was only half a Heavenly Pillar, compared to what Li Fan had obtained previously, it undoubtedly represented a more fundamental condensation of the primordial Great Dao of "Starvation."

Li Fan did not uproot this Heavenly Pillar from the Immortal Ruins. Instead, he buried the half that sealed the Starving Immortal near it. He could sense that due to their mutual comprehension of the Great Dao of "Starvation," even though the cores of the two Heavenly Pillars were not from the same individual, there was still a tendency for them to merge.

"He could not achieve the Nameless Dao in life, yet he has a chance after death. It can be considered helping you fulfill your wish," Li Fan nodded to himself.

After temporarily settling the two Heavenly Pillars, Li Fan savored what he had just witnessed. Although the memories of the previous Starving Immortal were brief, there were three points that Li Fan found particularly noteworthy.

The first was the Dao of "Dao Devouring." Hidden within the Great Dao of "Starvation," its domineering desire to swallow mountains and drink seas was not Li Fan's illusion but the manifestation of this "Dao Devouring." Being able to devour an entire possibility Dao and turn it into one's own nourishment was undoubtedly an extremely terrifying existence.

"However, he overestimated himself and chose the wrong opponent. He had enough power to devour a single possibility. To face Mountains and Seas..." Li Fan sneered.

Without personally witnessing the Infinite Sea and the Mountain Above, one could not imagine their grandeur. Even the mortal world, encompassing all possibilities, was merely a corner of the Mountains and Seas. The previous Starving Immortal paid the price for his arrogance. After drifting for a long time in the Dao Annihilation, he embarrassingly arrived at the "Primordial," barely surviving. However, with the Three Saints of the Primordial present, he dared not act presumptuously. He had to change his guise, replacing "Dao Devouring" with "Starvation."

Although the two Dao paths had similarities, their power was clearly incomparable. His final fate was to be easily transformed into a pillar supporting the heavens.

The second point that concerned Li Fan was the "Immortal Coffin of Crossing Tribulations" that allowed the Starving Immortal to wander in the Dao Annihilation for so long. The Starving Immortal's remaining memories were not extensive, yet this Immortal Coffin was mentioned repeatedly. Clearly, the Starving Immortal deeply regretted the loss of the Immortal Coffin of Crossing Tribulations. A treasure that even a ruthless being like the Starving Immortal, who could destroy and devour single possibilities, cared so much about must possess its own mysteries.

"I wonder who stole this Immortal Coffin of Crossing Tribulations. Since the Immortal Realm is destroyed, if it still exists, it should be in some part of the lower stellar sea."

Although he had personally witnessed the destruction of the "Primordial," Li Fan had not yet explored all the surviving territories of the Primordial. His footsteps were currently limited to the High Wall, Suo Xing, and Guang Wu. The reasons for this were threefold: the obstruction of Dao Annihilation and the difficulty of travel; secondly, the forces that survived the destruction of the Immortal Realm were all formidable. In his previous life, the formidable weapons wielded by the Guang Wu Star Sea, such as Dao Swords, Dao Blades, and Dao Chronicle Projection Beads, all possessed world-destroying power. Guang Wu Star Sea was like this, and other star seas were as well.

Moreover, the backdrop of Dao Annihilation meant that these star seas were exceptionally repellent to outsiders. Exploring all the star seas of the Primordial was no easy task. Of course, the most crucial reason was that it was unnecessary. Li Fan's primary exploration objective in the future was to break free from the Mountains and Seas of the Primordial, and even to travel upstream to the Eternal Void. The High Wall, Suo Xing, and Guang Wu held no fundamental difference for Li Fan.

As for the last point that concerned Li Fan greatly, even causing him immense trepidation, it was the "Virtuous True Immortal." From the Starving Immortal's memories, Li Fan learned that this Virtuous True Immortal not only possessed extraordinary power but also acted entirely differently from the supreme experts Li Fan had encountered before.

The Duke of Shou Qiu, Emperor Tai Tian, Purple Robe, and the Three Saints were all powerful, but they all, to varying degrees, embodied the demeanor of "the strong" and acted according to certain rules. But this Virtuous True Immortal, despite his name, was utterly devoid of virtue in his actions! He habitually stood on the moral high ground to manipulate and control others, remaining indifferent to the lives and deaths of others. Anything that brought him benefit must be pursued; anything that threatened him must be ruthlessly destroyed...

Li Fan was all too familiar with this style of action! Although they had not yet met, Li Fan had a premonition that this Virtuous True Immortal would undoubtedly become his formidable adversary in the future!

"Interesting. Let's see who is more 'virtuous'!" The first-generation Immortal Puppet lightly stepped onto the ground of the Immortal Ruins. Under the sweep of the Dao Devouring power, the former ruins of the Immortal Realm were instantly shattered into countless fine particles and then rapidly devoured by the first-generation Immortal Puppet.

The Immortal Ruins would cease to exist in the future, leaving only two Starving Immortal Heavenly Pillars, one new and one old, to support the collapsing heavens of this place.

Using the body of the first-generation Immortal Puppet, Li Fan savored the essence of the Immortal Ruins. The entire Immortal Realm was carved out from the Mountain Above. Thus, as he slowly chewed, Li Fan's vision conjured images of vast, continuous mountain ranges.

"With this ability to gaze afar, one can indeed comprehend certain 'principles of mountains.' However, it is still far inferior to personally visiting the Mountains and Seas. Even Duke Shou Qiu's path of sitting on a mountain and gazing at the sea is vastly inferior."

Li Fan was not surprised by this, as he had only devoured an Immortal Realm. "It is like walking towards the mountain. The more you devour, the closer you get to the mountain."

The Immortal Realm was destroyed, and there were not many ruins left. Li Fan naturally turned his attention to the Immortal Domain Chess Pieces left behind by Sun Piaomiao. The temporal node of ten thousand years ago had subtle differences in the placement of the chess pieces compared to ten thousand years later, but they were all within the High Wall. During the three years he spent setting up traps and hunting the Starving Immortal, Li Fan had already collected them all.

The remaining disciples of the Medicine King Sect, overjoyed at having escaped the Immortal Ruins and regained new life, eagerly inquired about the situation from the cultivators ahead. To their shock, they discovered they had returned to the Profound Yellow Realm. Fortunately, the Ten Sects were now too busy dealing with the Myriad Immortal Alliance's offensive to bother with them. After much deliberation, the Medicine King Sect disciples, completely bewildered and terrified by what had happened, decided to join the Myriad Immortal Alliance. They thought that with their skills in treating illnesses, they could get by anywhere.

However, the characteristic of the New Law cultivators—their Dao foundations unbroken, their souls undying, and their bodies uncorrupted—rendered many of the Medicine King Sect's unique skills useless. Instead, some peculiar elixirs that were previously considered unorthodox became their capital for survival.

Li Fan did not pay much attention to these matters. He had merely tossed the Medicine King Sect aside instead of devouring them, out of consideration for their past relationship. After unfolding the Immortal Domains and devouring them all with the Dao Devouring method, the first-generation Immortal Puppet temporarily reached its limit. Although the image of the Mountain Above vaguely seen had become clearer, the immense pressure from the approaching mountains followed closely behind, descending upon the first-generation Immortal Puppet.

Immortals were, after all, creations that connected Mountains and Seas. The infinity of the Sea and the height of the Mountain balanced each other, creating True Immortals. Now, with the first-generation Immortal Puppet using the Dao Devouring method to devour an entire Immortal Domain, the mountain had subtly overshadowed the sea within him. Li Fan vaguely sensed that certain unpredictable changes were occurring within the first-generation Immortal Puppet. He could not yet determine whether these changes were good or bad.

Resolutely stopping his continuous devouring, Li Fan attempted to harness the power of the Infinite Sea to counteract the mountain. Amidst the sounds of the sea tides, the oppressive feeling brought by the image of the Mountain Above finally receded, and the first-generation Immortal Puppet barely regained its ability to act.

"That feeling, as if I were about to be swallowed by the shadows of the continuous mountains, was very similar to the experience I had when the Three Daos merged," the first-generation Immortal Puppet sat cross-legged, meditating, while Li Fan meticulously pondered. After a long time, he finally confirmed.

"When the Three Daos merged, I was dissipated into an unknown collection of mysterious forces."

"But what the first-generation Immortal Puppet experienced just now was merely being submerged by the Mountain Above..." Li Fan thought of the Fallen Immortal Realm. The Fallen Immortal Realm contained only the Infinite Sea and no Mountain Above.

"If one were to disregard the consequences and push the Dao Devouring method to its extreme, could one create another Fallen Immortal Realm centered on the Mountain Above, counterpart to the existing one?" Li Fan narrowed his eyes and rapidly deduced, based on his past experience of the Three Daos merging.

If one could maintain their sanity while being submerged by the image of the Mountain Above, they should be able to see this counterpart Fallen Immortal Realm. The Immortal Ruins, the Immortal Domain Chess Pieces, all the Immortal Realm soils that he had devoured before, reappeared intact, but not in their real-world forms. Instead, they appeared as they were on the Mountain Above! Scattered like stars in the endless mountain ranges. Like distant stars in the darkness.

"Being far from the place where Mountains and Seas intermingle, thus in a sense, one can also evade the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. However, the price..." Li Fan looked around like a ghost. Silence reigned in the mountains above. There was no sound of the sea representing life, only towering peaks.

"Absolute order and hierarchy."

"Life, here, is meaningless." Li Fan suddenly understood why all beings in Sun Piaomiao's prophecy about Mountains and Seas were born from the sea. Because the Mountain Above itself was inherently opposed to life.

"Even True Immortals can borrow the momentum of the mountains, but it does not mean merging with them. They merely stand upon them. Even the Three Saints of the Immortal Realm were like this."

"And the consequence of merging into the mountains..." The shadows of the mountains closed in from all directions. The scattered lands that he had devoured quickly disappeared into the endless mountains. Li Fan abruptly awoke from the illusionary deduction, a cold sweat breaking out on his forehead. Not out of fear, but out of a primal reverence for the Mountain Above that life possesses. The first-generation Immortal Puppet's body was covered in large swathes of shadows.

"Devouring mountains and seas is not mere hyperbole. It's just that one must simultaneously contend with the backlash from both mountains and seas."

"While devouring mountains and seas, one is also being devoured by them." Li Fan understood and connected the Infinite Sea to the first-generation Immortal Puppet to alleviate the pressure from the mountains. It took a full half-year to cleanse the shadows from the first-generation body. Li Fan could not help but sigh, "The two Saint Monarchs, Gui Hai and Lian Shan, were truly gifted. Even if one of them were missing, the so-called Immortal Dao, when cultivated to its extreme, would likely not end well."

"The only outcome would be to merge with Mountains and Seas, becoming one with them."

"But precisely because of the two Saints' heroic deeds, which opened up Mountains and Seas, the balance between them created a foothold for Immortals."

"However, consequently, having established a foothold within Mountains and Seas, one must also participate in facing the tribulations of Mountains and Seas themselves. The merging of Mountains and Seas, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation..."

The Great Daos of the world are merely the principles of Mountains and Seas. Li Fan, through the Dao Devouring method, directly devoured the ruins of the Immortal Realm, bypassing the process of enlightenment and directly confronting Mountains and Seas. Although his cultivation speed was fast, the side effects were unbearable for ordinary people. It was fortunate that Li Fan had the True Transformation, allowing him to survive the calamity of the Three Daos merging and escape intact. In this lower-level "sinking," he could maintain his stability.

"All things merge into Mountains and Seas, and Mountains and Seas merge into something higher."

"Even Longevity and True Transformation, which are on par with Mountains and Seas, are within this merging sequence..." Li Fan thought of the legend of the Creator God again.

"This legend seems to vaguely point to the greatest truth within Mountains and Seas."

"The so-called Creator God created Mountains and Seas, birthed all things in the mortal world. But in the end, everything in the world will return to its origin."

"The mortal world fades, Mountains and Seas merge. This is the trend, the destiny that the beings within Mountains and Seas must face." In Li Fan's mind, the scene that once made even Mountains and Seas tremble appeared. A lone star hung high, like the single eye of a god, looking down.

"The True Immortals who traversed time and space, passing on sparks of life, were they rebelling against such a fate?" Li Fan stood in the dark starry sky, gazing beyond the "Primordial" and falling silent.

"With my abilities, I can even uncover this truth. Let alone those transcended powerhouses, and even the Three Saints..."

"Even so, they showed no hesitation or despair..."

"Truly remarkable!" Li Fan exclaimed from the bottom of his heart. If there was something guiding the merging of Mountains and Seas in the darkness, perhaps it was the will of the supposedly vanished "Creator God." To save the mortal world and reverse the trend of merging Mountains and Seas was essentially to contend with the Creator God. For an ant in the Mountains and Seas to raise its antennae and attempt to confront a lone star hanging outside the Mountains and Seas was already an unbelievable feat.

"When the sky falls, the taller ones will hold it up. Since they can still persist, let us endure a little longer..." Li Fan muttered, suppressing the unease in his heart. Half of Li Fan's unease stemmed from the trepidation after glimpsing the truth of Mountains and Seas. The other half, however, came from his distrust. Li Fan was never one to entrust his fate to others. Even if they were beings far more powerful than him, like Purple Robe, Shou Qiu, and the Three Saints. When it came to his own life and safety, Li Fan could not help but harbor doubts: "Can these people really do it?" Until the great trend of Mountains and Seas merging was completely reversed, this doubt would never dissipate. "Perhaps, in the end, I will have to step in myself to be at ease." Li Fan's gaze was deep, as if piercing through the fractured River of Time, reaching the very source of everything.

Thank you to all the readers for your concern. The emergency check yesterday did not reveal any particular problems. I am currently wearing a 24-hour ECG monitor and await the results of the subsequent examination.

Chapter 1557: My Blood Nourishes the World

"When the Profound Yellow Realm was first created, it already contained the supreme Pill Dao within it."

"The Profound Yellow's ability to evolve itself, to recreate immortal artifacts, and even to nurture the power of Ink Slaughter, are all intricately linked to this innate Pill Dao."

Li Fan's gaze swept across the Profound Yellow world. In his vision, it was no longer ordinary scenery like mountains, rivers, lakes, and seas. Instead, it was a web of interwoven Great Daos. This vision often appeared when Li Fan was comprehending the Dao in the past. However, the Profound Yellow world's Great Daos were like a vast, intricate net before, but now...

All the Dao principles twisted and converged, ultimately forming a faint, ethereal, and elusive pill! The image of the pill shattered dramatically, and Li Fan's vision returned to normal. But Li Fan knew that what he had just seen was by no means an illusion. It was a trace of the Profound Yellow's essence that he had captured during his pill refinement of the Profound Yellow Realm.

"It seems Sun Piaomiao was also involved in the construction of the Rotten Chess Dojo..." A hint of understanding flashed through Li Fan's mind. Sun Piaomiao, as a reincarnated True Immortal who transcended the mortal realm, had an unfathomable origin. The items he left behind could even trigger True Transformation and possess various magical uses. For example, the Tri-forked Tree, which could trigger a True Transformation-like deduction once, providing effects like increasing True Transformation charging capacity and offering protection against death; the Dangling Eye Puppet, which offered protection against death; and the Broken-winged Gray Bird, which pointed to a specific time interval within the Rotten Chess Dojo. There was also the square pill stone containing the "Pill-Refining Medicine King Scripture."

All these clues indicated Sun Piaomiao's extraordinary nature. "It's a pity that apart from these, no other items were found. Even at this temporal node of eight thousand years ago." "After all, Sun Piaomiao was active in a distant era, a golden age of cultivation when the immortal path was not severed..." "Perhaps, by traveling upstream along the River of Time for another ten thousand years, more related clues can be found."

Amidst these thoughts, Li Fan's pill refining actions did not cease. Perhaps Sun Piaomiao had left some backdoors within this half-finished pill of the Profound Yellow Realm, but the current Li Fan had his own means to deal with them!

The Great Celestial Venerable Immortal Puppet's exhalation of vital energy was nearing its end. The furnace fire reached its peak but was weakening due to lack of fuel, about to fade. At this moment, the main body suddenly spat out a mouthful of blood, subtly scattering it across various parts of the Profound Yellow Realm.

"The furnace seals the heavens and earth to condense the wondrous essence..."

"I use my blood to refine the Profound Yellow!"

Li Fan's vital blood transformed into countless invisible red dots, enveloping the Profound Yellow Realm, forming the 雏形 (chúxíng - nascent form) of a pill, and isolating the entire Profound Yellow Realm from the outside. This "outside" did not merely refer to the connection between the Profound Yellow Realm and the Rotten Chess Dojo. It also referred to the Mountains and Seas, and the mortal world! And with Li Fan's current strength, he could achieve this... It was because this single expulsion of blood had drained almost all his vital blood. The power of the Great Dao of "Longevity" hidden within this vital blood was also being slowly refined and transferred to the Profound Yellow Realm along with this vital blood!

In his previous life, Li Fan suffered the calamity of the Three Daos merging. Although he was protected by True Transformation and narrowly escaped death, the price was severe. True Transformation fell into dormancy, and most importantly, Li Fan had not completely escaped the state of the Three Daos merging. In this life, a mortal body could achieve deathless bleeding, which was the best proof.

If anyone else obtained this divine power of Longevity, they would be overjoyed. However, having suffered a setback once, Li Fan wished he could expel it as soon as possible! After all, the Great Dao of Longevity ultimately belonged to Duke Shou Qiu. Even though he had gained Duke Shou Qiu's approval and received some of the divine power of Longevity, he was still merely a "guest." Since there was no hope of turning the tables for now, Li Fan decided to discard it directly.

"As long as I have True Transformation, even if the Great Dao of Longevity can rival the Mountains and Seas, I will not hesitate to part with it!" The Great Dao of Longevity from Duke Shou Qiu was truly one of the greatest creations in the mortal world of Mountains and Seas. Even though Li Fan had experienced the merging of the Three Daos, and only faint imprints remained within his body, he still possessed unimaginable divine abilities.

Li Fan, having expelled all his vital blood, felt no discomfort. In just a single breath, vital blood brimming with life and power regenerated from all parts of his body. The newly generated vital blood surged within his body, emitting sounds like dragon roars and tiger growls, showing a momentum of surpassing its predecessors. After spitting out all his vital blood and refining the Profound Yellow, Li Fan felt not weakened, but rather as if he had just had a good night's sleep and consumed a large amount of restorative supplements, becoming even more vigorous.

"This is Longevity..." Feeling the hidden potential for life within his body like an endless ocean, Li Fan could not help but let out a cold snort. The Great Dao of Longevity, he had obtained it in one fell swoop, yet it was incredibly difficult to expel. "The merging of the Three Daos was a misfortune, not a blessing, for me." "Using the effort of refining the Profound Yellow with pills, although it cannot completely remove it, it can minimize its influence as much as possible!" Li Fan had long wanted to resolve the hidden danger of the Three Daos merging, and it was only after much contemplation that he came up with this method that achieved two goals with one action.

Without further hesitation, he actively initiated it again, spewing forth his vital blood. Scattered across various parts of the Profound Yellow Realm. The vital blood generated by the power of Longevity was even more beneficial to the Profound Yellow Realm than the vitality of the stellar sea or immortal spiritual energy. After the Profound Yellow Realm absorbed it, the overall strength of the world increased exponentially.

As Li Fan continuously sprayed his vital blood and refined the pill, after three repetitions, the strength of the Profound Yellow Realm surpassed that of the Ascended Immortal Realm from his previous life. After five repetitions, it far surpassed the Great Desolate Immortal Realm of his previous life. However, Li Fan noticed that his extraction of the power of Longevity from his body had only just begun.

But as the Profound Yellow Realm gradually grew stronger, the power of Longevity within Li Fan also showed a slow but stable downward trend. Li Fan therefore had ample patience. "It's just a matter of persistence." With the Great Celestial Venerable protecting him, Li Fan sat cross-legged above the Profound Yellow Realm. With each breath, his blood mist erupted, nourishing the Profound Yellow. Thus, silently, a hundred years passed.

The Profound Yellow Immortal Pill was not yet formed, and all the changes were condensed within the pill. They had not yet formally manifested in the Profound Yellow Realm. In the world, only a handful of beings could dimly perceive the changes happening in the world. But their imaginations were insufficient to truly glimpse the future of the Profound Yellow Realm.

At the Myriad Immortal Alliance headquarters, the Law Transmitter looked up at the sky, his heart unsettled. A hundred years ago, he learned about his ancestor, King Xuan Tian, from "Grand Ancestor" and inherited the "Supreme Dao Scripture." He had intended to use this to sweep away the Ten Sects and avenge the past. However, the conflict dragged on for a hundred years. Although the Ten Sects repeatedly fell into disfavor, they were never completely defeated. This made Xuan Yuan Tuo, who was usually calm, gradually become impatient.

"Even the trivial Profound Yellow Realm cannot be cleared, how can I follow in the footsteps of my ancestor?" Xuan Yuan Tuo sighed. Theoretically speaking, he inherited Xuan Tian King's Profound Sound and received the aid of the "Supreme Dao Scripture." His strength and divine abilities should have far surpassed the mortal world, and the Ten Immortal Dao Sects should have been utterly defeated. In fact, it was true at the beginning. Wherever the Myriad Immortal Alliance went, the Ten Sects fled in fear. They gave up almost all their outer territories, confining themselves to their own sects and a few important grotto-heavens. At that time, it seemed only one step away from annihilating the Ten Sects and unifying the Profound Yellow Realm. But suddenly, one day, the situation changed drastically. The Ten Sects, as if they had a change of heart overnight, launched a fierce counterattack against the Myriad Immortal Alliance. As if they had been holding back for a long time, all the disciples of the Ten Sects exhibited astonishing killing intent. The previously weak rabbits, who were thought to be defenseless, instantly transformed into man-eating tigers. The Myriad Immortal Alliance, caught off guard, suffered heavy losses. In almost one month, they lost all the gains accumulated over the past few years. It was only by relying on the strong vitality of the New Law cultivators that they managed to barely survive.

Xuan Yuan Tuo was perplexed by the Ten Sects' erratic change in attitude. What bothered him even more was that he had not yet taken the final step in the New Law. Without proving Longevity, despite his marvelous techniques and divine abilities, he was still only a Harmonious Dao cultivator. He could fight against ten, but not against a hundred. The Ten Sects had profound foundations, and he alone did not have the strength to suppress them.

Xuan Yuan Tuo gazed at the Profound Yellow Realm's sky: "To defy the principles of heaven and earth, and prove Longevity." "With the number of peak New Law cultivators in the Myriad Immortal Alliance, I should have proven Longevity long ago, but I have consistently failed." "I originally thought that something was obstructing my path to enlightenment in the darkness." "But after a hundred years of contemplation, I finally realized." "It's not that my New Law deduction is flawed. It's that the Profound Yellow Realm itself is constantly strengthening." "And its rate of strengthening far surpasses that of all the New Law cultivators combined." Xuan Yuan Tuo's eyes flashed with a hint of terror: "What on earth..." This situation was far beyond his cognitive scope. After hesitating for a long time, Xuan Yuan Tuo ultimately gave up on seeking help from "Grand Ancestor" again. He gritted his teeth inwardly: "It's not yet a dead end. There should still be a way!"

"Since the world has changed, the New Law must also change!" As if returning to the day he first understood the New Law, Xuan Yuan Tuo sat in contemplation, feeling a sense of inspiration. Xuan Yuan Tuo fell into confusion, and so did the members of the Ten Sects. "Brother Xingji, what is the conclusion? Has Mother Shi derived any results after so much deduction?" Sect Master Fang Dingge of the Grand Dao Sect's tone revealed a rare, irrepressible sense of urgency. Even when surrounded and in a desperate situation on the Tai Yuan battlefield, he had never been so distraught. Daoist Xingji sighed, remained silent for a long time, and then quietly said, "My Tai Yan Sect has possessed the Dao Transformation Stone Mother for nearly ten thousand years, yet we have never encountered such a bizarre situation as this." "The Stone Mother's computational power is almost depleted. Even by overdrawing its own energy, it cannot deduce a scenario that aligns with reality." As soon as these words were spoken, the scene fell into dead silence.

"Bizarre, too bizarre." "We thought King Xuan Tian's return was just a false alarm, but we never expected that strange events would occur one after another over the past century." "The Ruomu Tree went out of control, the position of Longevity is no more, the stellar path of the Tai Yuan Realm was inexplicably severed, and the Profound Yellow Realm is in a state of isolation." "More importantly..." Senior Disciple Situ Yao of the Heavenly Sword Sect raised his wine gourd to his lips but then dejectedly put it down. It seemed the aged wine no longer tasted sweet. Fang Dingge continued, "As cultivators, our comprehension and control over the Great Daos of heaven and earth are growing weaker. If it were only one person, it could be considered an illusion." "But both you and I are experiencing this..." The people present exchanged glances, each seeing the heavy burden in the other's eyes. "If the situation continues to deteriorate at this rate, perhaps one day, we won't even be able to fly freely," said Xiahou Yan, the Master of the Boundless Prison, making a startling statement. "It shouldn't be that bad, should it?" The members of the Ten Sects exchanged glances, then felt an unbearable restlessness. Compared to this, the Myriad Immortal Alliance's problems were no longer significant. "Fortunately, before the Profound Yellow True Immortal achieved enlightenment, he left behind many improved cultivation techniques for the Ten Sects. Using these as a reference, we have managed to delay the loss of our control over the Great Dao," said Jiang Yingyue of the Supreme Dao Sect. Hearing this, everyone felt a sense of relief and recalled the figure who once stood tall on the Tai Yuan battlefield.

...

As if sensing the countless thoughts lingering around him in the Profound Yellow heavens and earth, Li Fan, who had been meditating and refining pills for a hundred years, finally opened his eyes on this day. In his vision, the illusory pill furnace that had been faintly visible outside the Profound Yellow Realm had long since become substantial. Although it was condensed from countless mouthfuls of vital blood spat out by Li Fan, it bore no trace of bloodiness. Instead, it emitted an infinitely pure, warm, white radiance. Li Fan felt an overwhelming sense of familiarity and an indescribable surge of vitality emanating from this radiance. Even Li Fan himself was momentarily lost in a trance.

"I never expected that the Longevity Great Dao power, which seems to have little remaining within me, is still so potent." "I've been drawing it out and expelling it with every breath, repeating this process. Yet, it has lasted for an entire century!" Amidst his astonishment, Li Fan finally gained a concrete understanding of the power of Duke Shou Qiu and the Great Dao of Longevity.

"Fortunately, after a century of arduous effort." "The hidden danger of the Three Daos merging has been temporarily resolved." Having lost the resonance of the Three Daos merging, Li Fan's sensitivity to the infinite immortal power of Mountains and Seas and the transformation of True and False had decreased significantly. In terms of his own performance, Li Fan found that his comprehension in all aspects had greatly diminished. It was as if he had transformed overnight from being extraordinarily intelligent to becoming dull and foolish. Although he felt unaccustomed to it, Li Fan had no regrets.

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless, only I can be the boat."

"The Great Dao of Longevity is indeed profound, but it ultimately belongs to another."

"Unless I can achieve the goal of becoming the master, I will not hesitate to discard it." Li Fan's expression was indifferent, his heart remaining unshaken by the loss of the Great Dao of Longevity.

Chapter 1558: I Am the Father of Profound Yellow

The Profound Yellow Realm, nurtured by vital blood filled with the power of Longevity for a hundred years, had reached an unimaginable level of vitality. However, as the pill had not yet been fully formed, all this vitality remained latent. In the Profound Yellow world, perhaps a few beings could dimly sense the changes occurring in the world, but only Li Fan, the alchemist, could truly see the power condensed within this Profound Yellow Great Pill.

"It is said that all living beings are born from heaven and nurtured by earth, with heaven and earth as their parents. Your growth to this point is entirely due to my vital blood."

"In a sense, it is 'I whoNourishes the world'," Li Fan said with a smile, sensing the subservient and flattering Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao consciousness serving him. Compared to the past, the Profound Yellow Realm's current flattery lacked a sense of deliberate artifice and was instead from the heart, stemming from instinct. It was like a hungry infant begging its parents for milk. The Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao knew very well that although the Profound Yellow world contained immense vitality, it could only erupt and be truly absorbed by the world with a single command from Li Fan.

For a full hundred years, it could only look but not consume, almost suffocating the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao. Now that Li Fan had spoken, and seemed to be on the verge of the final step of refining the pill, how could the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao dare to refuse? It directly acknowledged Li Fan's jesting words. At this very moment, Li Fan dimly sensed a connection, inexplicable and unclear, forming between himself and the Profound Yellow Realm.

"Since I nourish the world, I am its father."

"The bond is now formed..."

"Pill ~ Begin ~" Li Fan pointed into the air, and in an instant, the entire Profound Yellow world seemed to fall into absolute stillness. Plants, gentle breezes, ants, mortals, Foundation Establishment cultivators, Harmonious Dao cultivators. Even mountains, rivers, lakes, seas, earth veins, and spiritual energy. All were frozen. In Li Fan's eyes, the illusory pill furnace that had surrounded the Profound Yellow Realm for a hundred years shattered with a roar. Simultaneously, the warm white light surrounding the Profound Yellow Great Pill erupted. In the next instant, it retracted back into the Profound Yellow world.

In this world of absolute stillness, the aging Ruomu tree was the first to begin to thaw. As a new green leaf emerged from its branches, the Ruomu tree began to grow wildly, growing at an accelerated pace. It was as if a "fast-forward" button had been pressed on the Ruomu tree. This ancient tree, which originally reached the heavens, tore through the sky and propped open the firmament. It ascended infinitely upwards.

The Profound Yellow Realm did not fall into turmoil due to the rent sky, because the heavens and earth began to grow synchronously at this moment. The power of Longevity contained for a hundred years finally permeated every corner of the world. In just a single breath, the scale of the Profound Yellow Realm expanded to encompass the entire Darkest Star Sea. If Li Fan had not forcibly halted the Profound Yellow Realm's wild growth with his intent, it might have clashed violently with the five specters of Duke Shou Qiu in the next moment.

To other regions of the Darkest Star Sea, the appearance of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was incredibly strange. It forcefully integrated everything that was originally in the starry sky into the Profound Yellow Realm. It was more akin to devouring than covering. Everything in the original starry sky quietly appeared within the Profound Yellow Realm, resulting in various bizarre phenomena that defied logic. For example, continuous remnants of the great wall floated like dark clouds above the northern frontier of the Profound Yellow Realm. And the countless relics of various worlds gathered in the Sea of Relics outside the great wall were all swept up into the sky by an inexplicable force. Then, they drifted towards various parts of the Profound Yellow Realm with the flow of energy, finally falling like rain.

The nascent consciousness of the Darkest Star Sea, originally at the center of the sea, suddenly found its body usurped. After a moment of stupor, it instinctively tried to struggle fiercely. The Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao, however, paid no heed and swallowed it in one gulp. The consciousness of the star sea disappeared completely without any power to resist. For the original Profound Yellow Realm, the consciousness of the Darkest Star Sea was an unreachable, colossal existence. But now, it was merely equivalent to a candy that could barely satisfy a craving.

Although the size and scope no longer expanded, the changes within the Profound Yellow Realm were far from over. As the heavens and earth became higher and vaster, everything within the world also underwent a qualitative change. Li Fan sat cross-legged in the air, silently observing everything below.

...

Xuan Yuan Tuo, who was in the midst of enlightenment, suddenly awoke. He looked around in a daze. No outsiders had intruded or disturbed him. His location had not changed. But Xuan Yuan Tuo felt... the world seemed to have become somewhat different. Filled with unease, Xuan Yuan Tuo instinctively tried to use his divine sense to probe further. After a moment, his expression drastically changed. Because when his divine sense left his body, it could no longer advance an inch. It was as if the air was filled with incredibly hard, invisible barriers, blocking the progress of his divine sense.

"What's going on? What exactly?" A sense of foreboding arose in Xuan Yuan Tuo's heart. He tried to ascend, to search his surroundings, and to investigate. What shocked him even more was that he, who was at the peak of the Harmonious Dao realm, could not even ascend! "Have I lost all my cultivation?" The Law Transmitter instinctively tried to call upon the power of his Heavenly Soul's "Golden Seal." However, the moment he tried, it was like he had run headfirst into a solid rock. Stars flashed before his eyes, and his soul was violently shaken. "How could this be?" At this point, the Law Transmitter finally began to panic like never before. The Heavenly Soul's "Golden Seal" was still there, but he could no longer wield it!

If the original Heavenly Soul's "Golden Seal" was like a handy iron bar, then now it was like a colossal Heavenly Pillar, whose top was out of sight and whose end could not be seen in the distance. Just seeing it made Xuan Yuan Tuo tremble uncontrollably, let alone lifting or wielding it. Xuan Yuan Tuo, who considered himself knowledgeable, took half a day to calm down and accept this incredible reality. With his understanding, he could not deduce the cause of this change at all. However, he vaguely sensed that the immense Heavenly Pillar within his body seemed to be sealed by some force. Although he could not wield it, the other party also could not harm him. But... the seal was not permanent. It was continuously weakening with the passage of time.

"If the seal disappears, and I still cannot control it..." Xuan Yuan Tuo's expression turned pale. The scene of the colossal Heavenly Pillar collapsing and crushing him seemed to appear before his eyes. The foundation of his cultivation had now become a sharp blade that could take his life at any moment. This immense contrast was difficult for Xuan Yuan Tuo to accept. However, he quickly realized something and muttered to himself, "I wonder... is it that I have become weaker? Or..." Having not walked on the ground like a mortal for a long time, he stepped out with an awkward gait and slowly pushed open the door of his seclusion. He didn't know if it was his imagination, but even this door seemed more difficult to push than before. The door boomed open, and Xuan Yuan Tuo, the Law Transmitter of the Myriad Immortal Alliance, was struck dumb as he gazed upon the sight of the new world. The world had changed.

...

Compared to the Profound Yellow cultivators, Xuan Yuan Tuo's reaction was already considered the best. After the world recovered from its stillness, facing these sudden and drastic changes, most beings found it difficult to adapt. Many cultivators who were originally flying through the air plummeted to the ground. The formations of the major sects all lost their effectiveness. It was as if the world had been reset, and everything in the world had been completely reshuffled. It took a long time for the Profound Yellow cultivators to gradually get used to this new world.

The New Law and Old Law cultivators each had their advantages and disadvantages. For the Old Law cultivators, their past comprehension and control of the world became useless. Their past cultivation realms, whether Harmonious Dao or Longevity, were all turned to dust, rendering them no different from frail mortals. They had to start all over again. As for the New Law cultivators, although their devoured celestial objects and grotto-heavens remained, they had undergone drastic changes along with the world. They became powers that they could not wield at all at present and had to re-master them slowly. Moreover, if the sealing power within their bodies disappeared, and they had not yet grown strong enough, they would be crushed to death by their own cultivation.

As the overall scope of the Profound Yellow Realm expanded, communication between cultivators, which was previously easy, was now severed. Besides the fact that the vast distances between them made most flying and communication methods ineffective, the fundamental reason was the obstruction of various strange beasts that appeared on the Profound Yellow land. These strange beasts did not exist in the Profound Yellow Realm before, but emerged with the drastic changes in the world. They were the embodiment of the Profound Yellow world's power and possessed their own intelligence. For cultivators who had lost all their methods, these beings were utterly invincible. Fortunately, there seemed to be some inexplicable rules limiting the extent of these strange beasts' activities, which prevented the complete annihilation of the Profound Yellow cultivators by the beasts. However, the cultivators also keenly noticed that these strange beasts were slowly expanding their territories. It was expected that in the near future, a battle between the cultivators and these ubiquitous strange beasts would be inevitable. Under the threat of life and death, both New Law and Old Law cultivators felt immense pressure.

...

"The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm does not tolerate idlers."

"Giving you a hundred years to adapt is already showing great mercy!" The one who spoke these words with a cold snort was not Li Fan. It was a young girl serving Li Fan, the manifested consciousness of the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao! The moment the pill was formed, propelled by the power of the Great Dao of Longevity, the Profound Yellow Realm's Heavenly Dao consciousness finally managed to manifest a physical form. Her face was perfect, without a single flaw. However, there was a subtle incongruity between her eyebrows and tone, hinting at a hint of harshness. "You cannot be idle either." "The world is just beginning to be created; you still need to supervise various places and constantly transform them," Li Fan said indifferently. The young girl instantly changed her expression and quickly bowed, "Your command shall be obeyed." Li Fan had previously called the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao "Father," but Li Fan found the name awkward and told her to change it.

"As expected, old habits die hard." After dismissing the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao, Li Fan's gaze turned to a certain subterranean location within the current Profound Yellow Realm. Originally, the location of Yuan Dao Province. The origin of the Ink Slaughter power. The Profound Yellow Realm, nourished by the power of the Great Dao of Longevity, and all connected things within the world, underwent a transformation. The origin of the Heavenly Soul's Ink Slaughter was also transformed. However, compared to the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul derived by Li Fan during the Profound Yellow's sublimation, this "Ink Slaughter" in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm had its own unique changes.

Li Fan took a step forward and arrived beside the Ink Slaughter shadow. Because of Li Fan's special identity as the "Father of Profound Yellow," the Ink Slaughter did not attack him. However, it still maintained a subtle sense of hostility. Li Fan, however, was completely unfazed. He directly reached out and beckoned a patch of dark clouds towards him. As the architect who orchestrated the changes in the Profound Yellow Realm, Li Fan, who possessed the "Sitting Heaven Technique," was the biggest beneficiary of the drastic changes in the world. However, out of consideration for the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan had not yet taken the step of formally "becoming an immortal." But the unimaginable feedback force was enough for him to ignore the threat of the Ink Slaughter before him. With a slight exertion of force, he easily subdued the restless Ink Slaughter.

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, sensing the difference between it and the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul. "The Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul is the power of the merging of Mountains and Seas." "And this Ink Slaughter, influenced by the Great Dao of Longevity, has reduced its destructive power to annihilate everything slightly. But in return..." Li Fan held a mass of dark clouds in his hand and brought it above the Profound Yellow Realm's sky. The four Heavenly Pillars that originally stood in the Darkest Star Sea now stood in this place. With the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm as a solid foundation, even if these Heavenly Pillars had minor flaws, they would be largely sufficient to resist the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.
