However, they were still somewhat lacking compared to Li Fan's plan for an eternally indestructible Immortal Boat. This was only the end of the first phase of renovation. Li Fan did not rush to start the next phase. He would wait until the creatures of the Profound Yellow Realm had barely adapted to the world's transformation, which would be the beginning of the second phase of renovation. With a thought, the four Heavenly Pillars emitted rumbling sounds. It was Li Fan forcefully drawing out a portion of their power for an experiment. Four illusory images of Heavenly Pillars separated from their original positions and merged into a pitch-black broken pillar in the center. Then, Li Fan threw the Ink Slaughter cloud he controlled towards the broken pillar. As if sensing a tempting delicacy, the Ink Slaughter cloud, like a wild dog off its leash, frantically attacked the broken pillar. Countless dense black ink dots, like wriggling worms, constantly attempted to devour the Dao laws condensed within the broken pillar. Even the results of the Nameless Immortal's enlightenment were no match for the Ink Slaughter cloud. It took little effort to devour half of it. However, Li Fan seized the Ink Slaughter cloud at the critical moment when it was eagerly devouring. Then, he commanded the Ink Slaughter cloud to "spit out" the "food" it had devoured. Food already in one's mouth is hard to give up. Especially after it had been devoured and digested? The Ink Slaughter cloud was unwilling. Instantly enraged, it attacked Li Fan. Li Fan chuckled lightly. With his left hand spread open, countless overlapping illusions of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm appeared. The Ink Slaughter cloud, after all, was born from the Profound Yellow Realm. The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, like its parent, possessed a natural constraining power over it. And now, Li Fan held thousands upon thousands of its parents in his hand!

Chapter 1559: Worried About True Transformation

As if seeing its mortal enemy, the Ink Slaughter cloud trembled violently, wanting to distance itself from the overlapping illusions of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm in Li Fan's hand. However, Li Fan held it firmly, unable to advance or retreat.

What Li Fan held was by no means a simple illusion. It was the true power of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm formed by the feedback force of the "Sitting Heaven Technique." Although it was in an illusory state now, it could become substantial in an instant. Countless restraining forces were superimposed. No matter how special the Ink Slaughter cloud was, it was completely subdued.

The black cloud rolled and churned, and it actually "spat out" the merged broken pillar that it had previously devoured! Li Fan delicately sensed the Dao laws contained within it, which were no different from before it was devoured.

"The original Ink Slaughter, although possessing destructive power close to annihilation, the process of destruction was irreversible. It was impossible to achieve such free transformation."

"The Ink Slaughter influenced by the power of the Great Dao of Longevity is more suitable for refining the 'Myriad Phenomena Dao Net'." Li Fan flicked his finger, restoring the four Heavenly Pillars. He did not directly devour the origin of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's Ink Slaughter, but instead returned it. Using the connection with the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, he began to carefully sense the transformed Ink Slaughter cloud.

At the same time, within Li Fan's body, within the countless Profound Yellow overlapping illusions, specks of ink began to appear synchronously. This was Li Fan using the True-Illusion divine ability to directly remodel the countless illusory Profound Yellow Realms, constantly carving and refining them until they were infinitely close to the actual Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. This was used to generate the required infinite Ink Slaughter clouds.

Ink Slaughter, as one of the ultimate salvation answers provided by the Immortal Realm's experimental field, naturally possessed its unique miraculous properties. In a sense, it was a human-made, controllable wave, attempting to simulate the creation of the merging of Mountains and Seas with mortal realm materials. If Dao Annihilation was a tide that swallowed everything, then Ink Slaughter was a controllable wave. Whether used to resist the Dao Annihilation tide or to blend in, it could serve as a means of escape and avoiding disaster.

From a hierarchical perspective, Ink Slaughter, representing the power of the merging of Mountains and Seas, was even higher than the Nameless True Immortals in the mortal world. And based on Mountains and Seas, with the addition of the Great Dao of Longevity...

"Perhaps due to the special attribute of the merging of two Daos, after each consumption-transformation process of the Ink Slaughter cloud, it is equivalent to a cultivator's enlightenment." "Although it has not reached the point of complete analysis, as long as it is repeated a few more times." Li Fan narrowed his eyes, savoring the detailed Dao insights from the four Heavenly Pillars that it had just consumed and spat out.

"In my previous life, to decipher the divine abilities contained within the Dao Chronicle Projection Bead, I, along with Cheng Dao, used all the life forms in the High Wall-Suo Xing Star Sea as the basis to perform the 'Dao Returning Plan,' letting the countless heavenly prodigies and life forms in this star sea comprehend the Dao on my behalf." "Compared to my own solitary contemplation, the efficiency was not just thousands of times higher." "But now..." "If I master this new Ink Slaughter power, I will no longer need the help of these sentient beings. Where the Ink Slaughter cloud passes, the three thousand Great Daos will manifest themselves!" Li Fan's eyes flickered, thinking of more.

"This is merely the merging of two Daos. If another Dao is added..." It was merely a thought; as soon as it emerged, Li Fan actively suppressed it. He had not yet fully mastered the Ink Slaughter of two merged Daos. Adding another Dao would only bring unnecessary risks of losing control.

"Although I actively detached myself from the state of Three Daos merging, it does not mean I have given up." "Moreover, I have only temporarily suppressed the hidden danger. In the near future, I will inevitably have to face this problem again." "Using Ink Slaughter as a guide is an excellent method of exploration."

The overlapping Profound Yellow illusions in his hand slowly disappeared. Li Fan's thoughts in his mind did not stop: "The fundamental difference between me personally intervening and the Ink Slaughter experiment is that Ink Slaughter did not truly participate in the merging process of the Great Daos of Mountains and Seas. It merely 'imitated' based on its own characteristics." "Although I don't know how the Immortal Realm cultivators in the past found such a peculiar Ink Slaughter prototype, it doesn't prevent me from utilizing it."

In fact, Li Fan already had a vague guess about the origin of the Ink Slaughter prototype. "Either it is a being on par with Mountains and Seas, True Transformation, and Longevity, or it is the remnant of an earth-shattering powerhouse who comprehended the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas. Based on the characteristics displayed by Ink Slaughter throughout, I lean towards the latter." "If 'True Transformation' were still here, perhaps I could glimpse its reality under the 'Dao Concealment' state when activating True Transformation." "What a pity." Li Fan sighed inwardly. True Transformation had unfortunately fallen into deep slumber.

Besides the desire for Eternal Remnants, Sun Piaomiao's peculiar relics were also things that True Transformation craved, even more so than the Eternal Remnants. "In the Darkest Star Sea, True Transformation has already consumed all beings possessing Eternal Remnants, and even their seeds. Moreover, nurturing and cultivating Eternal Remnants is not something that can be achieved overnight. It cannot be forced." "In fact, outside the Darkest Star Sea, there is currently a ready-made feast."

Li Fan thought this and looked past the High Wall, through the Suo Xing Sea, towards the depths of the starry sea, the Guang Wu Star Sea. "In the Guang Wu Star Sea, there is the decaying body of a transcended powerhouse." "That decaying body still retains the transcendent path from its life: 'Lone Sail on Mountains and Seas'..." Eternal Remnants are essentially the nascent form of the transcendent path.

In his previous life, with the help of Purple Robe and Cheng Dao, Li Fan was fortunate enough to clearly see the 'Lone Sail on Mountains and Seas' and vaguely sensed True Transformation's stirring. However, at that time, Purple Robe was still present, and True Transformation maintained considerable restraint. "After the matter of the Suo Xing Sea is concluded, I might as well take the decaying body of that transcendent powerhouse. However, in my previous life, Purple Robe paved the way with the Tongtian Great Dao, but in this life, relying solely on myself might be somewhat difficult." The strength of the Guang Wu Star Sea should not be underestimated. Not to mention hundreds of True Immortals, just the Dao Chronicle Projection Bead alone was something the current Li Fan could not resist.

"However, if the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm is fully established, it might still have the power to fight." Li Fan temporarily suppressed these thoughts and refocused his attention on the creation of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. The new Ink Slaughter cloud also required considerable time to incubate.

Li Fan was not idle. His divine sense swept across the entire Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, instantly finding the target he sought. At this temporal node of over eight thousand years ago, besides the Profound Yellow Realm, other immortal cultivation worlds still survived in the Darkest Star Sea. However, with the sublimation and expansion of the Profound Yellow Realm, these immortal cultivation worlds were all devoured and merged into the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

Li Fan did not pay much attention to these fortunate beings who had newly joined the world. However, some discoveries within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm resolved some of Li Fan's long-standing doubts. His figure flickered, and Li Fan appeared in a secluded canyon. The canyon was bottomless, shrouded in mist, and eerie sounds echoed from time to time. And below the canyon, Li Fan saw the cultivators of the Heavenly Law Realm, Qin Tang, Tai Yi, and Han Hai, etc. They had arrived in this newly born canyon along with the swallowing of the Heavenly Law Realm.

Their situations were even more miserable than the Profound Yellow cultivators. The Heavenly Law Venerables who acted on behalf of Heaven, such as Tian Yin, Tian Jue, and Tian Yu, had completely lost all their authority, becoming no different from ordinary mortals. They had to start all over again, just like other cultivators. And they themselves had already deeply merged with the Heavenly Law Dao. How could it be easy to break free from their original shackles and forge a new path? Their rate of progress was even far slower than that of ordinary people.

"However, if they can comprehend the corresponding Dao paths within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm..." "They can soar to the heavens in one step." Li Fan did not feel pity and did not offer any special care to these old acquaintances. In his opinion, whether it was the Profound Yellow Realm, the Heavenly Law Realm, or any other immortal cultivation world, all beings were essentially the same in his eyes. If there were any difference...

Li Fan's figure flickered, and he arrived within an altar in the Heavenly Law Realm, undetected. Li Fan could vaguely sense the aura of the various Venerables of the Heavenly Law Realm that had once gathered here. And, beneath this altar, a body still lay dormant. It was the Heavenly Physician! It looked exactly like the white-haired, compassionate figure Li Fan saw in later generations.

Li Fan examined it carefully: "Consciousness is completely dormant, like an empty shell." "But the life force is still present. This is because he initiated the Heavenly Soul Rebirth technique and transferred his consciousness into Xuan Yuan Tuo, who is lurking in the Profound Yellow Realm." "The vitality of this body is maintained by the collective efforts of the Heavenly Law Realm's Venerables. Only under certain extreme circumstances would it be forced to awaken." "Like when the Venerables perish, and the Heavenly Law Realm is destroyed!"

"So, the Heavenly Physician I saw in the illusion within the Cloud Water Heavenly Palace was this body. No wonder the Heavenly Physician's consciousness, linked to Xuan Yuan Tuo, could perceive the tragedy of the distant Heavenly Law Realm." Li Fan nodded slightly, his doubts resolved. Previously, in the memories of Han Hai of the Cloud Water Heavenly Palace, Li Fan saw the scene of the Heavenly Physician rushing back after the Cloud Water Heavenly Palace was massacred by the "Heavenly Physician." Later, Li Fan learned that the Heavenly Physician who massacred the Heavenly Law Realm was actually Su Bai, manipulated by external forces from another possibility. But the latter Heavenly Physician inexplicably appeared in the Heavenly Law Realm. Because, from a chronological perspective, the Heavenly Physician should still be trapped within the body of the Law Transmitter of the Profound Yellow Realm at this time and should not exist in the Heavenly Law Realm.

"This makes sense now." "The reincarnation was only a branch soul of the Heavenly Physician. The Heavenly Law Realm still possesses the Heavenly Physician's physical body. After the Heavenly Law Realm's Venerables were all slaughtered by Evil Su Bai, the body was forced to awaken. Thus, he witnessed the tragedy of the Heavenly Law Realm." "This is also why the Heavenly Physician's consciousness in the Profound Yellow Realm knew about the tragedy in the Heavenly Law Realm. Disregarding the consequences, he forcibly took control of the Law Transmitter's body, all in order to return to the Heavenly Law Realm." "Upon returning to the Heavenly Law Realm, the Heavenly Physician's consciousness returned to its original form. Although his homeland was destroyed, the Heavenly Physician did not give up and devised the method of 'borrowing a corpse to return the soul' using the Profound Yellow Realm. And Xuan Yuan Tuo, the Heavenly Venerable Law Transmitter, naturally became a crucial part of this plan." "But he alone could not completely control the Law Transmitter. So, he eventually found a way to seek help from the Heavenly Demon in the Profound Immortal Boat."

The events that transpired in the River of Time in the past were all reconstructed by Li Fan one by one. Although, for the current Li Fan, all of this held little practical significance. It did, however, resolve some lingering doubts. With a subtle sense of enlightenment, Li Fan returned the Heavenly Physician's consciousness, which he had previously suppressed, to its original body. And then...

"When reality becomes illusion, and illusion becomes reality." A blade of True-Illusion struck down upon the Heavenly Physician's body! Li Fan had gone to such great lengths, how could he possibly just let the Heavenly Physician go? "The Black Heavenly Physician outside the High Wall possesses unfathomable power." "Perhaps this is a good opportunity to verify my previous conjecture."

Li Fan's expression was calm, without the slightest pity in his heart. The blade of Spirit Reduction, striking non-stop, continuously. Although the Heavenly Physician still appeared white-haired and benevolent like the one Li Fan saw in later generations, he invisibly seemed younger. "Perhaps it's because he hasn't experienced the tragedy of the Heavenly Law Realm." Li Fan mused. "The Profound Yellow Realm I rule no longer faces the crisis of the Heavenly Law Realm's extinction. This is a great fortune for both the Heavenly Physician and the Heavenly Law Realm."

Recalling the various scenes he had witnessed in the Cloud Water Heavenly Palace, Li Fan nodded slightly. He first suppressed and collected the slumbering Heavenly Physician. Then, Li Fan's divine sense invaded the separated Celestial Demon tissue. He attempted to decipher the profound mysteries of the Celestial Demon. Sensing the invasion of the foreign object, even without its own will, and despite being sealed and suppressed. This Celestial Demon could still exhibit a resistance.

Li Fan felt as if he had returned to the River of Time, and his consciousness was stirred by immense waves. The heavens and earth spun, shrouded in chaos. Countless past memories fluttered like snowflakes. Sometimes, when one reminisces about the past and reflects on oneself, it can be a good thing. But becoming overly immersed in memories can lead to losing oneself. Li Fan clearly recognized the danger.

Myriad hands, seemingly from nowhere, appeared around his spiritual form. They meticulously sorted through all these stirred memories, bit by bit. In fleeting glimpses, Li Fan saw himself diligently and arduvely exploring the Great Profound Minor World before his True Awakening. He saw himself using his foresight from reincarnation to become the Grand Tutor of Great Profound, wreaking havoc in the court. He saw himself encountering Kou Hong and Dao Xuanzi, learning of immortals, and after enduring hardships through multiple lifetimes, finally breaking through the Great Formation and ascending to Profound Yellow. He saw himself undergoing a hundred lifetimes of Foundation Establishment, laying an incredibly solid foundation. He saw himself navigating and exploring the treacherous Profound Yellow Realm step by step. From Foundation Establishment to Golden Core, ultimately facilitating the sublimation of the Profound Yellow Realm and achieving the Half-Immortal realm. Then breaking through the barrier and leaping over the High Wall. He then encountered the upheaval of the Three Daos merging, forcing him to start all over again. With the help of Tai Tian Di, he traveled upstream against the River of Time, reaching the present day. ...

As Li Fan slowly gathered and integrated these fragments of his past memories, examining his past purely as an observer. He discovered some things that he had always taken for granted, but now seemed extremely peculiar. Li Fan had always had great confidence in his spiritual intuition. In countless reincarnations, during critical moments of crisis, his spiritual intuition had alerted him, saving his life. It could be said that Li Fan's trust in his spiritual intuition surpassed even that in [True Transformation]. If he had only possessed True Transformation and lacked such an uncanny spiritual intuition, Li Fan might have been captured on several occasions before he could even activate True Transformation.

In the past, Li Fan believed his spiritual intuition was innate. A natural occurrence. But was that truly the case?

Chapter 1560: The Fate of Merging Can't Be Escaped

"And Su Bai..." Li Fan's eyes narrowed, and his gaze shifted to the distance. Su Bai had indeed been reborn. However, without the temptation of the Profound Yellow Great Celestial Venerable, his fate had undergone a tremendous change. Before the Profound Yellow realm's sublimation and dramatic changes, he had also been in Ningyuan City, caring for the orphans in the dilapidated temple. However, the battle between Zhang Qianmo and the New Law cultivators that destroyed Ningyuan City never happened, so Su Bai lived as an ordinary mortal until the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm descended, and all beings in the world stood on the same starting line once again. Su Bai's innate talent was beyond doubt. Even though the Profound Yellow Realm had changed its world, he still had the potential to attain enlightenment and achieve Dao. To protect the orphans of the dilapidated temple during the drastic changes in the world, Su Bai, who originally had no intention of actively cultivating, began to attempt cultivation as if destined. His adaptability to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was far superior to that of ordinary people. If Li Fan had not deliberately suppressed him, Su Bai would probably have already reached the Nascent Soul stage by now. It should be known that the "Nascent Soul" of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was by no means comparable to the Nascent Soul of the Profound Yellow Realm in the past. Currently, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm had not yet produced any True Great Cultivators. Even Li Fan, the "Father of Profound Yellow," was still unsure of the ultimate level of power that top cultivators in this realm could reach.

"Theoretically speaking, Harmonious Dao cultivators in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm are essentially weakened versions of [Nameless True Immortals]."

"And any cultivator in the Profound Yellow Realm who can refine Qi are actually seeds of True Immortals. As long as I grant them titles, they can immediately become Immortals! The process of refining Qi to Harmonious Dao is merely the process of comprehending and proving the Nameless Dao."

It had only been less than half a year since the creation of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, yet Su Bai had already traveled about half the distance, and this was despite being suppressed. How could Li Fan not be amazed?

"Let him grow like this. When he attains the Harmonious Dao, it will be the time for my new experiment to begin." Li Fan smiled slightly. The Profound Yellow Realm truly lived up to its reputation as one of the core experimental fields of the Rotten Chess Dojo. Besides Su Bai's rapid progress, the progress of other cultivators was also somewhat beyond Li Fan's imagination.

Li Fan's mind stirred, and he decided to loosen some of the restrictions on the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's strange creatures, increasing the pressure on them.

"Rapid cultivation alone is not enough. Only those who can survive the trials of life and death are truly useful."

Not long after, Li Fan looked at the invisible souls floating up in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's sky and nodded with satisfaction. The transformation and sublimation of the Profound Yellow Realm were comprehensive. And the process of cultivators' deaths within it was designed and modified by Li Fan himself. It could be said that during the hundred years of pill refinement and tempering, at least one-tenth of his effort was spent on this. Referring to the arcane changes of the Profound Yellow Realm's "Returning Dao to Heaven" in the future, and further improving upon it. Only Li Fan could perceive that these invisible souls of fallen cultivators were all slowly floating and gathering on a transparent net floating in the Nine Heavens. The scenes experienced by the cultivators during their lifetimes flickered within the net. Even their insights and thoughts were absorbed by the net. All these life experiences were classified and sorted, and then transmitted to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm through the net.

"It is not only the living beings that are slowly adapting to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, but the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm is also adapting to the beings within the world."

"Mutual contention and competition are the only ways to forge the indestructible Immortal Boat of my ideals." It was foreseeable that the cultivators of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm would find cultivation increasingly difficult. The Heavenly Dao of the world was not static but was constantly changing. The conventional method of cultivation based on summing up past experiences, step by step, would be completely useless. Progress could only be made through personal exploration. Besides promoting the "mutual transformation of heaven, earth, and living beings," the transparent net in the Nine Heavens also had another purpose. The foundation of the Desolate Immortal Realm was the Immortal Ruins and the Immortal Domain Chess Pieces scattered across the Mountain Above. However, with Li Fan irrigating it with vital blood containing the power of Longevity, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, this behemoth that grew from the ruins, had long surpassed the "foundation" on the Mountain Above. Therefore, even though the Great Desolate Immortal Realm had achieved its grand form, it was actually precarious and at risk of collapse at any moment. And this transparent net served to temporarily stabilize it.

"Even if, by accident, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm falls from the Mountain Above, with the great net as a buffer, it will not completely disintegrate. Of course, ultimately, a foundation must be re-established on the Mountain Above to achieve complete stability."

"But that is only after the Ink Slaughter cloud has fully matured."

"Outside the Mountain Above is the Infinite Sea." Four Immortal Ascension Platforms stood majestically at the four corners of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Although they had been ready for a long time, they had not yet been activated.

"We must consider that when Mountains and Seas resonate and recreate True Immortals, it will inevitably attract the attention of certain powerful beings."

"The Three Saints of Lian Shan, Gui Hai, and Tai Yi..."

"As well as other transcended powerhouses." Strictly speaking, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, this pill, was not yet fully refined because it had not officially connected with Mountains and Seas. It was still in a state of isolation and closure. Therefore, even Li Fan's actions of reducing the Heavenly Physician's spiritual essence would not be detected by the Black Heavenly Physician of the Primordial possibility.

However, the moment the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's first True Immortal is born and connects with Mountains and Seas. It would be like breaking an eggshell, losing its enclosure, and all potential dangers would come rushing in. This was also why Li Fan eagerly awaited Su Bai's growth to serve as experimental material, yet still had to suppress his progress. The four Immortal Ascension Platforms stood majestically, guarding the four corners of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, like mythical Heavenly Gates. Once the Heavenly Gates opened, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm would usher in vast, unknown changes. Even Li Fan could not predict much about the future.

"However, it is certain that most powerful beings are likely in the Eternal Void, like Duke Shou Qiu. Even if they are attracted by the commotion in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, as long as it does not threaten Mountains and Seas, those powerful beings should be too lazy to bother."

"After all, it is irrelevant to the final outcome."

"Therefore, I only need to guard against the Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai, who have inextricable ties with the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm." As the creator of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, Li Fan felt confident and fearless, even anticipating future confrontations with these transcendent powerhouses. The countless Profound Yellow Immortal Realm illusions generated by the Sitting Heaven Technique within his body, along with the True-Illusion divine ability, were his greatest assurances.

"The True-Illusion divine ability carries the risk of being seen through by other powerhouses. It should not be used lightly."

"However, with all the knowledge and skills I have learned in the past, combined with this immense feedback force, any one of them should be sufficient to contend with them." Li Fan said proudly. During the hundred years of refining the Profound Yellow Great Pill, Li Fan had also comprehensively reviewed all the divine abilities, Great Daos, and insights he had learned and understood in the past. The ultimate goal was to forge his own path of crossing.

"Theoretically speaking, True-Illusion is the most suitable for me. However, with True Transformation suddenly falling silent, and with the loss of its guidance in past critical moments, regardless of the reason. Moreover..."

"Even if I master True-Illusion, will it truly resolve the crisis of the merging of Mountains and Seas?"

"After all, even True Transformation itself seemed to be collecting more possible answers for salvation. If True Transformation alone could turn the tide..."

"The Mountains and Seas and the mortal world would not have become as they are now." Thinking this, Li Fan's thoughts naturally converged back to the merging of the Three Daos: Mountains and Seas, Longevity, and True Transformation. Subsequently, his personal experience of the Three Daos merging resurfaced in his mind. The power of Longevity within his body, which had become extremely thin after continuously expelling vital blood for a hundred years during pill refinement, surprisingly showed signs of rising and strengthening again! Fortunately, Li Fan awoke in time and instantly broke free from the immersion.

"It really is a persistent haunting!" A shadow flashed across Li Fan's eyes. Without hesitation, he spat out another mouthful of vital blood, scattering it towards the Profound Yellow. Only then did he alleviate the trend.

"The merging of the Three Daos is indeed not so easily suppressed."

"But the root cause is my own confusion."

"It seems there is no better path than the method of merging the Three Daos." Li Fan realized.

Chapter 1561: Infinite Improvement

If the merging of Mountains and Seas was an inevitable trend, then the merging of the Three Great Daos was a miracle that had never occurred in the mortal world of Mountains and Seas. The Mountains and Seas themselves, or perhaps even True Transformation, might have been silently awaiting its outcome.

It was already incredibly difficult to resist the Dao Annihilation that accompanied the merging of Mountains and Seas. How much more so the tribulation of the Three Great Daos merging? Once one entered a state of merging, without the power to transcend the Three Great Daos, it was almost impossible to fully break free, even with the assistance of True Transformation.

Even though Li Fan had sprayed his vital blood to dilute the power of the Great Dao of Longevity within him as much as possible, he still could not reverse the trend of merging. Any thought in his mind that touched upon "merging" would cause the trend to change again.

"The method of extracting vital blood only treats the symptoms, not the root cause. Only by finding and firmly believing in a more correct path can this inertial dependence be severed."

"However..." Li Fan frowned slightly.

Let alone Li Fan, even the Three Saints might not have the answer at this moment.

"I'll take it one step at a time and see what happens."

With his emotions calmed, Li Fan suppressed the numerous thoughts in his mind and focused on the present. In his mind’s eye, a remarkably divine alchemical furnace appeared. All his past knowledge was like alchemical materials. As Li Fan organized and stored them, they were slowly cast into the furnace.

His divine consciousness blazed like fire, slowly refining. Li Fan, like peeling an onion, analyzed the essence of these countless divine abilities. He stripped away the superficial aspects of the divine abilities, leaving only the core essence, within the pill he intended to refine.

Li Fan quietly watched the divine ability pill slowly taking shape before him, feeling an unprecedented clarity.

"Instead of seeking externally, it is better to seek within oneself."

"I desperately pursued the True Immortal transformation of [True Transformation], yet I almost forgot what True Transformation truly is, and why it has always been pinned on me."

Li Fan seemed to see, within his mind, outside the alchemical furnace. Besides the "alchemical materials" of the various divine abilities he had mastered through his reincarnation experiences, there was a gem that he had overlooked, yet was the most brilliant!

"Infinite Spiritual Essence..."

The other materials came from the Mountains and Seas, and the mortal world. No matter how exquisite the refining technique, it could not forge a pill that surpassed the Mountains and Seas and the mortal world. Only this gem, originating from beyond the Mountains and Seas, could. If it were added to the pill, it might have the effect of transforming decay into the miraculous!

Li Fan's heart roared, and the alchemical furnace trembled. The radiant gem instantly erupted with an incomparably bright glow. It flew directly into the alchemical furnace. All the original materials in the furnace spontaneously made way for it. The gem smoothly reached the very center of the furnace. It was as if it had always belonged there. Countless materials, like stars, encircled this brilliant stone. And by being stained by the radiance released by the gem, the materials within the furnace also began to undergo inexplicable changes.

"Infinite Spiritual Essence is not only what True Transformation craves. It also plays a crucial role in the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas."

Like a flash of light illuminating the darkness, Li Fan, in an instant, found another potential wonderful use for his Infinite Spiritual Essence.

"The Art of Formations."

As inspiration struck, Li Fan incorporated a bit of Infinite Spiritual Essence into one of the materials in the alchemical furnace. Almost instantly, Li Fan simultaneously felt a slight dizziness. Immediately, countless scenes appeared before his eyes.

These were scenes of one "Li Fan" after another, researching and analyzing the Art of Formations. From the fumbling steps of the Foundation Establishment stage to the innovation of the True Immortal stage. Although their realms were different, they all poured their life's effort into the research of Formations, with unwavering focus, shedding blood and tears, striving until death. Without exception, they were pure seekers of the Dao, as if they had no other pursuits besides the Art of Formations.

With the lighting up and extinguishing of each "Li Fan's" life, Li Fan felt as if he had personally experienced the lifelong research of that figure in the Art of Formations. Although it was like a fleeting dream, leaving no memories, Li Fan felt that his sense of familiarity with the Art of Formations had not diminished.

The speed of the illusory figures flickering and jumping became faster and faster, and the "Art of Formations" in Li Fan's eyes underwent incredible changes accordingly. They became increasingly familiar, closer, and simpler. As if they were intimate companions who had known each other for an unknown number of years. They were already telepathic and tacitly understood each other.

Li Fan knew that his talent in the Art of Formations had reached a level that countless beings in the Mountains and Seas could not hope to match. Moreover, this talent was still constantly climbing!

"The Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Grand Formation..." When Li Fan thought of this peerless immortal formation, the formations that had seemed incredibly complex to him before, even with the help of the Immortal Separation Disc, were now no longer so obscure and difficult to understand. Furthermore, through the relationship between the nine sets of the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Grand Formation, he could deduce the remaining ones based on the five known formations.

"The Profound Origin Beginning Spirit, knowing five out of nine. They are: Xuanji, Myriad Spirits Returning to Number; Desolate Fall, Void Chamber Blossoming; Immeasurable, Primordial Becoming Square; Dao Genesis, Unceasing Life; Feather Ascension, Life and Death Ascending and Descending."

"The remaining four are..." Before Li Fan's eyes, the five major formations automatically extended countless fine threads, reaching into the blank areas next to them, gradually filling in the unknowns.

The remainder of the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Grand Formation thus appeared in Li Fan's sight.

"Fixing the Caldron, Stabilizing Mountains and Seas."

"Spiritual Ruins, Myriad Daos Connecting to the Profound..."

"Ah!" As soon as he deciphered these two major formations, Li Fan suddenly felt a sharp pain in his head. This pain seemed to come from the deepest part of his soul, the very foundation of his consciousness. Words could not describe its intensity. All the suffering Li Fan had experienced in his mortal reincarnations was merely a drop in the bucket compared to it. In his mind, not only did the formations he was deducing shatter instantly, but even the image of the alchemical furnace from the divine ability of pill refining also shattered.

Pain! In Li Fan's consciousness, only this single concept remained. His soul, and even his physical body, seemed to begin to shatter due to this extreme pain! He did not know how long he could endure it, but when the pain began to subside, Li Fan finally regained some ability to think. Li Fan had a premonition that this sudden occurrence was not just mere pain. It was a terrifying crisis that would completely destroy the foundation of his Infinite Spiritual Essence.

"It seems I was too reckless. Utilizing Infinite Spiritual Essence is not as easy and carefree as imagined. It carries immense risks." "Although it can help me rapidly increase my talent, the short-term outflow of a large amount of spiritual essence will also shake the foundation of my existence." Li Fan felt lingering fear and decisively stopped this rash behavior for the time being. Fortunately, the infinite nature of Spiritual Essence ultimately existed. After pausing the consumption, the pain that lingered in Li Fan's heart quickly disappeared. Everything returned to normal, as if nothing had happened. However, the two major formations, [Fixing the Caldron, Stabilizing Mountains and Seas] and [Spiritual Ruins, Myriad Daos Connecting to the Profound], which he had just deduced, were clearly imprinted in Li Fan's mind. It was also like the exhaustion after fighting for three days and three nights on a bed, constantly reminding Li Fan that what had just happened was not a dream.

"Although I gained something, I also paid a price." The only thing that reassured Li Fan was that his own weakness was slowly receding at a perceptible rate. "I only need to recuperate for a period of time to recover." After meditating and resting for seven days, Li Fan, finally regaining his energy, began to test his talent in the Art of Formations. With the enhancement of Infinite Spiritual Essence, he could see through the reality of the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit Grand Formation at a glance and could deduce rapidly. Under normal circumstances, it was not this outrageously effective. However, he was currently almost at the pinnacle of the mortal world. It might still be some distance from achieving transcendence through the Art of Formations, but being able to understand everything by analogy and handle it with ease was no longer a problem. "Even though the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit is one of the most complex immortal formations in the mortal world, with my current talent in formations, I will only need a hundred years of deduction to fully comprehend it." "This is only if I dedicate my entire mind and body to it. Just like the fleeting illusory lives. In reality, I cannot be so completely focused. After all, there are still external distractions like the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm." "The more focused one is, the higher the efficiency. The more distracted one is, the lower the efficiency. But regardless, within a thousand years, I can completely analyze it." After inspection, Li Fan was quite satisfied with the improvement in his talent for formations. After all, before this, without the assistance of the Separation Disc, his talent in formations was only at an ordinary level. If quantified, with a total value of 100, his previous talent in formations was only 9 points, barely enough to start practicing. But now... it had reached the near-limit of 99. Going further would be the theoretical limit. And that remaining 1-point gap was almost more difficult to overcome than the entire journey from 1 to 99. Even with the nourishment of Infinite Spiritual Essence, it did not help Li Fan cross this threshold. "Those who can take this step are likely transcended beings." Li Fan lamented the pity. His attention then returned to the two major formations of the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit. As the name suggests. The Profound Origin Beginning Spirit is a tool derived by the Three Saints to conveniently create an immortal realm in the Mountain Above. These two formations are both related to the stabilization of the immortal realm after its creation. [Fixing the Caldron, Stabilizing Mountains and Seas] solidifies the immortal realm's foundation in the Mountain Above. [Spiritual Ruins, Myriad Daos Connecting to the Profound] weakens the influence of the power of Mountains and Seas on the beings within the immortal realm, allowing True Immortals of various levels, and even Nameless True Immortals, to have the capital for enlightenment, rather than being suppressed by the pressure of Mountains and Seas. "It has great reference value for me to build the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm." Li Fan nodded slightly. "If all nine formations of the Profound Origin Beginning Spirit were complete, I could truly create an immortal realm from nothing, reshape the world, and even, with my various means, perhaps complete the ambition of the former Emperor Tian Luo, creating a truly sublimated immortal realm and escaping the tribulation of Dao Annihilation." "Although the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm has merged with the Great Dao of Longevity, due to its congenital flaws, it can at most give birth to Nameless True Immortals. It is not enough to support the birth of transcended beings." Li Fan incorporated the two newly comprehended major formations into the renovation of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Subtle changes occurred again in the heavens and earth. "It's just a small outflow of my Infinite Spiritual Essence, and it has brought about such a huge change..." Li Fan pondered, and couldn't help but look at the other divine ability "materials" in the alchemical furnace in his mind. "Fully mastering a hundred Daos, excelling in all of them." Li Fan murmured, as if he saw himself, with the help of Infinite Spiritual Essence, transforming into the number one prodigy of the Mountains and Seas. "The growth of talent is by no means useless. Especially the simultaneous increase in all aspects of talent. Like water rising and boats floating, as the intensity of all my talents is perfected, I will inevitably be able to see my final destined path more clearly. Perhaps even True Transformation could be easily reproduced and wielded." After some deduction, Li Fan concluded in his heart. This was not his baseless speculation. The foundation of True Transformation was, in essence, all the existences of the Great Dao in the Mountains and Seas and the mortal world. And if one knew all the principles of all Daos, then mastering the Great Dao of True and False would certainly be child's play. However, this method of improvement seemed to have no practical significance for ordinary people. Because the difficulty of simultaneously improving all talents to the extreme was even greater than mastering the Great Dao of True and False! Only Li Fan's Infinite Spiritual Essence within him could support this seemingly unrealistic plan. "Although some accidents occurred during the process of improving talent with Spiritual Essence just now, it was because I was too hasty. If done gradually, all sorts of drawbacks could be avoided." Just as Li Fan was contemplating how to continue developing his Infinite Spiritual Essence, a familiar fluctuation, long unheard of, reappeared. "True Transformation?" Li Fan's heart instinctively rejoiced. But after a moment, his eyebrows raised, and his expression became strange. This was because, in an instant, Li Fan understood the meaning of True Transformation's inexplicable fluctuation. The reason True Transformation had awakened from its serious injury and dormancy was naturally due to Li Fan's use of Infinite Spiritual Essence just now, which prompted it to remind him. As for the reason for the reminder, it was not explicitly stated, and it fell back into slumber. Given Li Fan's personality, if someone dared to criticize his own things, he would definitely choose to ignore them. However, True Transformation's opinion could not be taken lightly. "Is it that True Transformation wants to monopolize Infinite Spiritual Essence alone, or is my method of using Spiritual Essence to improve talent harmful to myself?" Doubts arose in Li Fan's heart. Although he had stumbled upon the method of using Infinite Spiritual Essence by chance, Li Fan did not understand the essence of Infinite Spiritual Essence itself, nor did he know what it truly meant. After careful consideration, Li Fan finally decided to tentatively heed True Transformation's advice. He stopped all actions of improving his talent with Spiritual Essence. However, it was only temporary. Once he mastered this method of improvement, which was akin to cheating, when facing his own various shortcomings, it would be difficult to resist using it. "Although True Transformation has been my reliance all along," "It is not something I can blindly obey. Ultimately, the decision rests with me." After experiencing the merging of the Three Great Daos and the outflow of Spiritual Essence, Li Fan's trust in True Transformation finally began to waver.

Chapter 1562: One Hand Covers The Bright Moon

If [True Transformation] did not possess independent consciousness but was merely Li Fan's own ability, then trust would naturally not waver.

But past facts had proven that [True Transformation] possessed its own independent consciousness, so Li Fan's lack of trust was justified. This was Li Fan's innate nature. Being able to heed [True Transformation's] advice and temporarily cease using his Infinite Spiritual Essence was already a display of Li Fan's trust in [True Transformation].

"It seems my spiritual essence is extremely important to [True Transformation]. Even though it was in slumber, it forcibly revived to remind me. But this also implies that [True Transformation] was indeed severely injured. Even for such an important matter, it only had time for a hurried reminder before falling back into slumber."

Putting this sudden incident aside, Li Fan refocused his attention on the changes within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. After deciphering the two major formations, [Fixing the Caldron, Stabilizing Mountains and Seas] and [Spiritual Ruins, Myriad Daos Connecting to the Profound], Li Fan naturally incorporated them into the construction of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. With his formation talent nearing its peak, they were integrated into the Profound Yellow heavens and earth almost seamlessly. The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, originally built on scattered ruins in the Mountain Above, suddenly felt much more stable, as if it had gained countless new roots. Although the distance was still vast, the feeling of imminent collapse was gone.

The inexplicable sense of crisis in his heart quietly receded, coupled with the effect of the Myriad Daos Connecting to the Profound Formation in isolating the power of Mountains and Seas, provided a more suitable environment for enlightenment and cultivation for the beings within the Profound Yellow Realm. Compared to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's initial birth, the difficulty of cultivation for its inhabitants had nearly halved. This also led to a brief period of explosive cultivation for the cultivators, with almost everyone achieving a minor realm increase within just over ten days. Those with outstanding talent even directly broke through a major realm. This naturally did not align with Li Fan's plan of "taking it slow." However, this time, Li Fan did not need to act personally. The Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao, sensing his intentions, actively adjusted, and this period of convenient cultivation quickly disappeared. The cultivators of Profound Yellow naturally noticed this change keenly. Those who missed it sighed in regret, those who benefited secretly rejoiced, and some had epiphanies, seeking to understand the changes in the world and await the next favorable opportunity. For a time, countless cultivators on the Profound Yellow land were stirred, and their thoughts were all connected to the consciousness of the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao. Heaven and man were in communication, with countless threads intertwining, which actually nourished the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao slightly, making the manifested girl appear much more "lively."

"This is the 'Heaven and Man Unite, Myriad Transformations Establish the Foundation'." Li Fan, looking down at the changes within the Profound Yellow heavens and earth, mused. "This period of favorable cultivation, whether for the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao or the Profound Yellow cultivators, is beneficial. It can be a permanent feature." "However, the duration each time cannot be too long, and the interval between each occurrence should not be regular. Everything should be random." "Let the cultivators of this world try their best to decipher the 'Will of Heaven'..."

As Li Fan pondered, the laws of the 'Gift of Enlightenment' for the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm were generated and deeply imprinted into the Great Dao of the Profound Yellow heavens and earth. Almost all cultivators' minds were drawn to this miracle called the 'Gift of Enlightenment.' With the help of this connection, Li Fan, as the master of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, could more easily control and grasp the minds of the Profound Yellow cultivators. In his vision, all sorts of bizarre and colorful illusions emerged from the minds of the cultivators, but they disappeared in an instant. Everlasting and ever-changing. If they had solidified, they could have filled the entire Profound Yellow Immortal Realm in mere moments. Fortunately, these colorful illusions were not physical entities and only appeared for an instant before vanishing.

"This is the so-called 'Thoughts'." "Hidden deep within everyone's heart, unseen and unknown by others." "Originally, only powerful beings like the Three Saints could catch a glimpse of it. But now, I can forcibly pry into it by utilizing the connection between the cultivators and this world."

As if discovering a new world, Li Fan's divine sense wandered through the boundless ocean of the Profound Yellow cultivators' thoughts.

"That fellow Zhao Si, his cultivation speed was always slower than mine. Last time, he actually had an epiphany during a great opportunity, not only surpassing me but also stepping into the Golden Core stage. Truly hateful! He has always been at odds with me. If he continues to fall behind, how will I live in the future? I must seize the next great opportunity..."

"My decision to hide my cultivation back then was indeed correct. When the monsters attacked and everyone was in despair, I suddenly made my move and turned the tide. From today onwards, I, Gao Zhi, will be the boss of this Desolate Python Mountain! I must find a way to kill all the men and keep only myself for pleasure. Anyway, this Desolate Python Mountain is isolated and sealed, and there's no hope of going out in this lifetime. Might as well indulge! The only thing to be wary of is that the strength of the surrounding monsters seems to be increasing synchronously?"

"Where is the Law Transmitter Immortal Venerable Elder? Ever since that anomaly occurred that day, the world has become too vast. Originally, my brothers in the Myriad Immortal Alliance were only a hundred miles apart. Now, I have traveled a hundred thousand miles without finding any trace of them..."

"Hahaha, my intuition was right, there really is a miraculous item underground. It's the [Empty Bamboo of Refinement] that I painstakingly cultivated and sought, but haven't had time to absorb and refine yet! Although the world has changed drastically, and the scale of this Empty Bamboo has expanded tenfold, from a single stalk to a continuous underground bamboo forest, my vital blood connection with it is still there! With this connection, I might be able to slowly refine it into my body and achieve the Foundation Establishment stage of the new era!"

"Yesterday, the monsters attacked, and we barely managed to repel them with our combined efforts. But food and resources have been depleted. How many more attacks can we withstand? Staying here any longer will likely lead to death. It's better to strike first, steal supplies, and flee!"

Countless Profound Yellow beings' thoughts intertwined. Some joyful, some angry. Some sad, some fearful. Although not all inner thoughts were exposed, they wove an incredibly grand symphony of inner voices. And the more Li Fan interacted with these beings' thoughts, the more he gradually sensed an abnormality within the Profound Yellow heavens and earth. It was like a mirror, silently enveloping all the Profound Yellow beings above. Reflecting all their thoughts into the mirror.

"Immortal Falling Realm..." A flash of surprise appeared in Li Fan's eyes. This illusory world, which was born alongside the original Profound Yellow Realm, had also expanded synchronously with the Profound Yellow Realm's sublimation and transformation. However, even with its extraordinary foundation, it could not keep up with the expansion fueled by the Great Dao of Longevity. The dark clouds of the Immortal Falling Realm were currently confined to the area above the original Profound Yellow Realm.

"The core of the Immortal Falling Realm is not from the Profound Yellow Realm..." "But after absorbing the thoughts of the cultivators of our Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, the Immortal Falling Realm seems to be undergoing an inexplicable change."

Li Fan did not let the situation develop further. With a thought, he intercepted the thoughts of all the cultivators in the area covered by the Immortal Falling clouds. It was like building a dam across a river upstream, completely absorbing the nutrient thoughts of cultivators by Li Fan. The Immortal Falling dark clouds, almost visibly, stopped their original transformation process. The dark clouds churned, and thunder rumbled. It seemed to be angered by Li Fan's insolent actions, roaring furiously. But it had lost its nourishment. And in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, a world created by Li Fan, it had no capital to contend with Li Fan. No matter how much resentment it held, it could only be helpless rage. The transformation of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was withdrawn. The Immortal Falling Realm returned to its original state. In fact, without the support of sentient beings' thoughts, its scale was even beginning to shrink. It was foreseeable that in the near future, it would completely disappear! The Immortal Falling Realm, which Li Fan had once considered a great enemy, became so easy to deal with once he could "observe" and, to a certain extent, control the thoughts of others!

Sensing the mortal danger, the Immortal Falling Realm did not resign itself to fate. It quickly began a path of self-salvation. In an instant, the internal structure of the Immortal Falling Realm was transformed. Originally, there were countless overlapping Immortal Falling illusions, existing together. But now, like a lotus flower, numerous petals protected the core stamen within. When nutrients from the outside were insufficient, the outermost Immortal Falling illusions would actively sacrifice themselves, transmitting the remaining nutrients inwards. This was to ensure that the innermost core area of the Immortal Falling Realm survived.

The secret self-exposure of the Immortal Falling Realm was something Li Fan had not anticipated. However, even now, with the ability to glimpse thoughts, even if the mutation of the Immortal Falling Realm was discovered. Under the cover of countless illusions, Li Fan could not distinguish the core secret hidden within the Immortal Falling Realm for the time being.

"Interesting." "Since it has exposed itself, don't even think about escaping."

Li Fan snorted coldly. He keenly sensed that the Immortal Falling Realm was attempting to transfer to another star system through the star gate of the Tai Yuan Realm. How could Li Fan let it succeed? With a thought, the Star Crossing Grand Formation was completely sealed. The two previously connected star systems were once again isolated. It was as if they were cut in half with a single blow. The Immortal Falling Realm was also cut into two halves by the closure of the teleportation formation. However, what surprised Li Fan was that the actual division did not seem to affect the Immortal Falling Realm. These two halves seemed to remain connected, and the core secret area of the Immortal Falling Realm was slowly transferring through this connection.

"Since this is the case..." Li Fan simply reopened the Star Crossing Grand Formation. And then, he reached out fiercely towards the star system on the other side! A projection of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm condensed in his hand instantly shattered. On the other side of the star system, the Tai Yuan Realm, and even the star system around the Tai Yuan Realm, as long as it was covered by the Immortal Falling Realm, were all brought over by Li Fan's claw!

With a roar, like the invasion of Dao Annihilation, the star system on the other side fell into complete silence and darkness due to the absence of a large area of stars. In fact, the sudden loss of the Tai Yuan star system greatly affected the stability of the surrounding star fields. Black energy emerged like bamboo shoots after rain. This was precisely the sign of Dao Annihilation approaching! But Li Fan did not care. The Tai Yuan star system was far from the High Wall. As long as the connection of the Star Crossing Grand Formation was severed, even if the other side was devoured by Dao Annihilation, it would not affect the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

At this moment, Li Fan looked at the Tai Yuan Realm captured in his hand, a faint smile playing on his lips. Then, he slammed it fiercely, and it was thrown onto the sky screen of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm! Like a muffled thunderclap, it echoed continuously in the sky. The beings of the Profound Yellow Realm looked up at the sky in unison, only to be astonished to discover that a bright moon had appeared in the sky inexplicably! Since the distance between heaven and earth was too vast, most beings could not discern the true appearance of this "moon." Only those cultivators who had died in the Tai Yuan Realm and were subsequently resurrected discovered something through their faint connection with the Tai Yuan Realm. However, they could not be sure for the time being.

Li Fan did not care about the thoughts of the Profound Yellow beings. He stared at the Tai Yuan Realm captured on the sky screen, feeling the Immortal Falling Realm, which was trapped and had nowhere to escape in desperation, and sneered again. "Let's see where you can run now!"

Instead of directly confronting the Immortal Falling Realm, which had become a trapped beast, Li Fan simply trapped it in a corner and blocked its reflection of the thoughts of all beings.

It turned out that without a foundation in reality, the Immortal Falling Realm was like a flower without nutrients, gradually withering. However, it was the legacy of an existence that had once amazed even the First Generation Grand Celestial Venerable. Although it showed signs of decay, the Immortal Falling Realm was not something that could disappear in a short time. Li Fan did not have the patience to wait slowly. "Let me give you a hand!"

The Immortal Falling Realm, born from the thoughts of sentient beings, grew with their thoughts. Therefore, it could also perish because of their thoughts. Under Li Fan's guidance, countless Profound Yellow beings, in a daze, all had a terrifying nightmare. In the dream, a world-ending catastrophe descended, engulfing everything in the world. Countless illusory world-ending tribulations surged towards the Immortal Falling Realm, invading it. Although they were merely nightmares in the hearts of cultivators, they could cause terrifying destruction in the Immortal Falling Realm! It was as if they were being eroded by wind and frost, and the illusory spaces on the outer layers of the dark clouds began to rapidly decay. The scale of the dark clouds continuously shrank. In just over half a day, only the innermost core illusion remained, struggling to survive.

However, at this point, Li Fan discovered that the effectiveness of his illusory world-ending calamity method had been greatly reduced. It seemed that this remaining illusion had strong resistance against the world-ending tribulations imagined by the Profound Yellow beings. "The core of the Immortal Falling Realm is not from the Profound Yellow Realm." "But... the Immortal Realm that once experienced the tribulation of Dao Annihilation!" A gleam flashed in Li Fan's eyes, discerning the reason.

Chapter 1563: Lord of the Immortal's Demise Realm

Although the thoughts of the Profound Yellow beings could not completely destroy the core of the Immortal Falling Realm, under Li Fan's manipulation, wave after wave of attacks constantly weakened it. The illusory world surrounding the core of the Immortal Falling Realm rapidly perished, allowing Li Fan to slowly discern the scene within the core of the Immortal Falling Realm. Large swathes of star fields were swallowed by darkness, depicting the scene of Dao Annihilation wreaking havoc. But this was merely the backdrop of the Immortal Falling Realm's core. What truly caught Li Fan's attention were the countless characters shining like brilliant stars in the sky, floating above the screen! Without truly entering the core of the Immortal Falling Realm, only observing from afar in reality, the boundary between reality and illusion caused these characters to distort to varying degrees. But with his past experience, Li Fan easily recognized the origin of these characters. True Immortal Seal Script! Each character represented a Great Dao in the heavens and earth!

"This floating..."

"Is it..."

Li Fan was slightly stunned, then realized: "The Boundless Star Domain, the Supreme Dao Scripture?"

Li Fan had seen this miraculous scene of the [Supreme Dao Scripture] spanning across the starry sky in Situ Xing's memories. Comparing them now, they were indeed extremely similar!

"Could it be that the master of the Immortal Falling Realm is actually that renowned [Sealing Dao Immortal]?" Li Fan's heart suddenly trembled. Even with Li Fan's current vision, upon considering this possibility, he couldn't help but feel startled. It was not without reason that the name Sealing Dao Immortal was so great. He inscribed all three thousand Great Daos with True Immortal Seal Script. It was said that half of the True Immortals in the original possibility were born after observing the Supreme Dao Scripture and receiving enlightenment from Sealing Dao. One could say that in the hearts of the original True Immortals, their reverence for Sealing Dao surpassed even Duke Shou Qiu and the Three Saints!

"In the past Immortal Realm, there were countless True Immortals."

"But let alone the Nameless realm, even ordinary True Immortals are rarely known by people in the lower realms. Only [Sealing Dao], even if one doesn't recognize True Immortal Seal Script, knows of its legend. Where does this kind of transmission come from..."

"One glance reflects Profound Yellow, forming an illusory Immortal Falling Realm that is almost identical to the real world. This illusion can not only evolve on its own but can also manifest from 虛 (xu - void) to 實 (shi - reality) in the real Profound Yellow Realm."

"This power is indeed beyond the capabilities of ordinary Nameless beings." The more Li Fan thought, the more he felt this possibility.

"There were rumors that Sealing Dao had already perished in the Immortal Realm, but all the Immortals did not believe it. If this Immortal Falling, is indeed Sealing Dao..." In a moment, countless thoughts flashed through Li Fan's mind. Without directly choosing to retreat, he continued to gaze towards the core of the Immortal Falling Realm.

In the tribulation scene of Dao Annihilation engulfing the Boundless Star Domain, the characters of the Supreme Dao Scripture seemed like pillars, supporting a safe area. The Immortals, like countless dots of light amidst the tribulation, all noticed the only safe place in the starry sky and rapidly fled towards the area protected by the Supreme Dao Scripture.

"It is said that this tribulation is the first outbreak of Dao Annihilation in the Primordial. Since then, the Primordial Immortal Realm has declined from its peak and ultimately perished completely." Li Fan commanded the Profound Yellow beings' thoughts to continue attacking and weakening the Immortal Falling Realm while simultaneously observing the scene within the core of the Immortal Falling Realm.

As expected of the [Supreme Dao Scripture], which could represent the three thousand Great Daos, its power was incomparable to the fake version Li Fan had created. Under its pillar-like support, the Dao Annihilation tribulation actually showed signs of subsiding!

"This is different from the records..." A doubt suddenly arose in Li Fan's heart. At this moment, a dark shadow suddenly appeared within the gleaming Supreme Dao Scripture. Seemingly with a clear purpose, it headed straight for a character in the Supreme Dao Scripture. It moved too fast and was hidden within the brilliance of the True Immortal Seal Script, making its appearance unclear.

As the dark shadow approached, that True Immortal Seal Script also began to shake violently. In a short while, as if a piece had been scooped out by a knife, this True Immortal Seal Script directly disappeared from the Supreme Dao Scripture!

This True Immortal Seal Script seemed to carry immense weight. With its support gone, the Boundless Star Domain, already precarious, became even worse. The starry sky was devoured by Dao Annihilation at an increasingly rapid pace, and the Supreme Dao Scripture, spanning across the sky, trembled uncontrollably due to the loss of control of the situation. Yet the dark shadow ignored it all, heading straight for the next True Immortal Seal Script!

The movement of the dark shadow attracted the attention of the surviving True Immortals in the Boundless Star Domain. They decisively attacked the dark shadow, wanting to stop its actions. But whether it was divine abilities, spells, or direct charges, as long as they approached within a thousand feet of the dark shadow, they would be teleported elsewhere in an instant. Some were tens of thousands of miles away, others were in the vicinity of the impending Dao Annihilation. The thousand-foot domain around the dark shadow seemed to have become an absolute forbidden zone, inaccessible to others!

The surviving True Immortals of the Boundless Star Domain tried various methods and means but could not get close, let alone stop it. They could only watch helplessly as the dark shadow stole the second True Immortal Seal Script.

With the loss of another True Immortal Seal Script, the Boundless Star Domain collapsed even faster. Seeing this, the surviving True Immortals no longer cared about stopping the actions and simply fled for their lives. Thus, the dark shadow stole characters with even greater impunity. Soon, the Supreme Dao Scripture became riddled with holes.

"The True Immortal Seal Scripts in the Supreme Dao Scripture are not simply representations of Great Daos. But why go to such great lengths, stealing them amidst the rampant Dao Annihilation, what is the purpose..." Just as Li Fan felt perplexed, another phantom appeared in the Boundless Star Domain at this moment!

On the Supreme Dao Scripture, the positions of the characters that had disappeared after being stolen suddenly emitted faint light again, repairing the characters. However, compared to the previous rich ink, they were extremely transparent, as if they could disappear at any moment.

Like giant pillars holding up the sky, with the appearance of this phantom, the rampant Dao Annihilation tribulation suddenly calmed down. The entire Supreme Dao Scripture erupted with unprecedented brilliance, as if welcoming its master's arrival!

"Sealing Dao Immortal!" Li Fan naturally recognized the identity of this phantom. Sealing Dao Immortal pointed a finger at the dark shadow, and countless tiny characters suddenly appeared around the dark shadow. Although still within a thousand feet, they were constantly advancing. The characters wove together, as if creating a traversable world and path out of the void and Dao Annihilation. Nine hundred and ninety-nine feet, nine hundred and ninety-eight feet... Inch by inch, they pressed towards the dark shadow!

However, the dark shadow seemed unconcerned about its predicament, even looking at Sealing Dao Immortal with a provocative, mocking gaze. Then it continued its stealing actions! Sealing Dao Immortal did not erupt in anger, but the speed at which he wrote characters quickened. The dark shadow was clearly not as calm as it appeared; its speed of moving and stealing True Immortal Seal Scripts within the Supreme Dao Scripture became much faster than before. The price was that the area around it was being lost at an increasingly rapid rate.

"Strange, why didn't Sealing Dao Immortal simply put away the Supreme Dao Scripture? Instead, he let the dark shadow steal from it?" As Li Fan watched the battle between the two powerful beings, a doubt flickered in his mind.

"Perhaps..." Li Fan suddenly thought of something, and his heart grew serious. And what happened next seemed to confirm his guess.

After stealing nearly thirty characters, Sealing Dao Immortal's inscribed True Immortal characters had already encroached within five feet of himself. The dark shadow finally chose to stop.

"Thank you, Fellow Daoist, for your generosity!"

"I shall remember [Dwelling Void]!"

"Hahahaha!"

The dark shadow laughed presumptuously, then suddenly expanded, like a drop of ink falling into clear water. After spreading, it quickly diffused outward. Not only did it reclaim the lost thousand-foot territory, but it also directly devoured the True Immortal characters written by Sealing Dao Immortal. However, judging from the churning scene below the dark shadow, [Dwelling Void] did not truly devour the inscription written by Sealing Dao, but rather temporarily suppressed it. Like boiling water, the phenomena in the dark shadow's area intensified.

In this process, the black color in the central area gradually faded, revealing a clear, mirror-like surface. This mirror seemed to reflect another world!

"Thief, don't run!" Seeing that the dark shadow was about to escape, Sealing Dao Immortal finally broke through the blockade of [Dwelling Void]. He directly appeared outside the mirror surface. Using his finger as a brush, he fiercely pressed down on the transparent mirror surface!

Time seemed to freeze at this moment. Li Fan vaguely saw scenes of endless, continuous immortal realms being born from Sealing Dao Immortal's fingertips, like mountains, pressing down towards the transparent mirror surface! Ripples arose, and the mirror seemed on the verge of shattering. However, at this moment, four more dark shadows appeared on the other side of the mirror! The five of them formed a bizarre symbol and jointly blocked Sealing Dao Immortal's finger! The ripples slowly subsided, and the mirror and the dark shadows disappeared as if they had never been there.

Sealing Dao Immortal stood there dumbfounded, seemingly unable to accept what had happened. Due to the loss of thirty True Immortal Seal Scripts, the Supreme Dao Scripture became incomplete. Amidst the invasion of Dao Annihilation, it could no longer resist. The Boundless Star Domain collapsed at an even faster rate than before.

From Sealing Dao Immortal's body, countless characters flew out, saving as many True Immortals as possible within his sight. And Sealing Dao Immortal himself remained in place. Until the Boundless Star Domain was on the verge of complete destruction, and the Supreme Dao Scripture, unfolded, gradually retracted into a half-unfolded scroll in Sealing Dao Immortal's hand.

"Realm of Life and Death, Five Venerables of the Same Tribulation." Sealing Dao Immortal looked towards the place where the dark shadow had disappeared, slowly uttering these eight words. With a forceful throw of the scroll in his hand, he cast it to an unknown location. Sealing Dao Immortal took a step forward, and his figure seemed to be swallowed by Dao Annihilation, also disappearing from the Boundless Star Domain.

...

The scene recorded in the core of the Immortal Falling Realm thus ended. It began again from the beginning, looping endlessly.

"The True Immortal Seal Scripts in the Supreme Dao Scripture are not merely depictions of Great Daos. They seem to be faintly connected to the true Great Daos of the Primordial Possibility! Like every branch and leaf of a towering tree connected to the countless roots underground!"

"The dark shadow named Dwelling Void did not just steal True Immortal Seal Scripts. It directly stole the Great Daos of the Primordial Possibility, stealing thirty at once!"

"No wonder Sealing Dao Immortal was so enraged. And no wonder the Primordial seemed to decline after this tribulation, losing all resistance to Dao Annihilation, destined for eventual destruction."

"The lack of Great Dao that I sensed, besides True Immortals proving the Nameless Dao and fleeing, was also due to others stealing them!" Li Fan's heart was shocked. The strength displayed by this dark shadow from beginning to end surpassed the realm of Nameless True Immortals. It could easily traverse possibilities, and was at least at the same level as Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai.

"However, even so, it was still forced into a desperate situation by Sealing Dao Immortal. In the end, it barely survived with the help of four other dark shadows. But their goal had been achieved. They took from the surplus to compensate the deficiency. Stealing others' Great Daos to supplement their own. What exactly is the [Realm of Life and Death]?" Li Fan's eyes narrowed.

Based on Li Fan's previous understanding, transcended powerhouses in the mortal world were all willing to gather together to discuss methods of salvation. Even continuing sparks of life, reversing the flow of time, and averting disaster seemed to be the common choice of all these powerful beings. However, Li Fan had long harbored doubts. It was impossible for everyone to be so "noble." A thousand people, a thousand faces. Especially when facing a life-or-death crisis, individual choices would tend to extremes.

"Indeed, besides the group who chose to save the world together, there are also extremely selfish individuals like the dark shadow."

"Their actions are essentially the same as Black Heavenly Physician and Evil Su Bai, obtaining resources from other possibilities to enhance themselves. However, they are more extreme and bolder, directly stealing the foundational structures of other possibilities..."

"Demolishing the east wall to patch the west wall. If one demolishes too much, they might indeed survive the great tribulation of Mountains and Seas merging." A glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. Instinctively, such actions were clearly more to his liking. However, since first learning about other possibilities, and now encountering various transcended powerhouses, only the so-called Five Venerables of the Same Tribulation acted like this. Clearly, in the mortal world, they were the minority.

"Moreover, such behavior of digging up everyone's foundation should absolutely not be allowed. Once discovered, it would likely be irreconcilable." Analyzing wisely, Li Fan temporarily suppressed the stirring in his heart.

"Sealing Dao Immortal pursued the Five Venerables of the Same Tribulation and disappeared, never to return. It seems the situation is not optimistic."

"However, speaking of which, the master of the Immortal Falling Realm does not seem to be Sealing Dao Immortal?"

"Who could it be?" Li Fan's gaze was fervent, looking towards the core of the Immortal Falling Realm. While harboring doubts, he couldn't help but feel a sense of relief. After all, if he really had to confront Sealing Dao Immortal, even just his remnant spirit after his demise, it would be extremely stressful.

"The one who could preserve the last scene before Sealing Dao Immortal's departure..." Li Fan thought of the half-unfolded scroll casually tossed by Sealing Dao Immortal.

"The Supreme Dao Scripture?" Li Fan's eyes lit up. "If the Supreme Dao Scripture truly possessed a spirit, it would definitely be able to reflect the events of Profound Yellow in a single glance."

"Furthermore, with the complete destruction of the Immortal Realm, and the disappearance of the foundation of the Supreme Dao Scripture and the Great Daos of the Immortal Realm, its demise was inevitable."

Chapter 1564: The First Star of Xuanhuang

Li Fan stared intently at the remnants of the Immortal Vanishing Illusion, trying to discern any trace of the Supreme Dao Scripture within. But alas, even as the Immortal Vanishing Illusion neared complete annihilation, he could not truly ascertain its origin.

"To pursue the routed enemy with the might of victory, one must not imitate the King of Chu and seek fame," Li Fan mused. After a moment of contemplation, facing the Immortal Vanishing Illusion, with only a sliver of light remaining under the concerted assault of the Profound Yellow beings' intentions, Li Fan harbored no reluctance. He issued the command for its final destruction.

The light grew dimmer, and finally, it vanished entirely from this world.

"The true Supreme Dao Scripture, destroyed so easily by my hand?" Li Fan's divine sense swept across the surroundings of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, confirming that no remnants of the Immortal Vanishing Illusion remained.

While he felt a slight sense of regret, Li Fan was also filled with a sense of unreality. He was a man of extreme suspicion, not just selfishness.

"The Immortal Vanishing Illusion, formed from the Supreme Dao Scripture, should have been a formidable foe. Even though the foundation of the Supreme Dao Scripture, the Primordial Immortal Realm, has been shattered, the Immortal Vanishing Illusion should not have been so fragile."

Having grown accustomed to adversity, a moment of smooth sailing made Li Fan’s suspicions resurface. As a precaution, Li Fan squinted his eyes and meticulously inspected every inch of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, from top to bottom. Finding nothing, he finally felt a measure of peace.

"My spiritual intuition has not given any warning either."

"It seems I was overthinking things."

Just as Li Fan let out a sigh of relief, he suddenly discovered that the Immortal Vanishing Illusion, which had utterly vanished moments before, had reappeared out of thin air above the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm! It was like a vigorous sprout, piercing the soil and emerging from underground.

Li Fan did not immediately act to eliminate it again. Instead, with a grim expression, he observed.
