The core of this newly born Immortal Vanishing Illusion still depicted the Boundless Star Domain and the Supreme Dao Scripture. However, the newly formed illusion surrounding the core reflected the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

This Immortal Vanishing Illusion was truly resilient, like a centipede that, though dead, still writhed. Not only had it survived the encirclement, but it had also advanced further.

"I had already sealed off any contact between the Immortal Vanishing Illusion and the Profound Yellow beings' intentions. How then did this new Immortal Vanishing Illusion come into being?"

With this question in mind, Li Fan dispatched a trace of his intention from the Great Celestial Venerable Immortal Puppet to enter the newly formed Immortal Vanishing Illusion. The Profound Yellow Great Celestial Venerable, possessing a higher "authority" over the Immortal Vanishing Illusion, had this rule remain even after its destruction and rebirth.

The moment the Great Celestial Venerable's intention entered the Immortal Vanishing Illusion, Li Fan sensed this fact.

"The grade of the Supreme Dao Scripture is far above the Profound Yellow Great Celestial Venerable."

"Yet, the Profound Yellow Celestial Venerable can restrain the Immortal Vanishing Illusion in certain aspects." Li Fan’s heart stirred, as if grasping a crucial point. The Great Celestial Venerable’s intention roamed within the Immortal Vanishing Illusion, and the scenes it witnessed confirmed his conjecture.

"So that's how it is."

"The core scene of the Boundless Star Domain is merely a facade. The true cornerstone of the Immortal Vanishing Illusion..." Li Fan looked at the various people and things within the new Immortal Vanishing Illusion. They corresponded almost one-to-one with the reality of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. But this was limited to the initial inhabitants of the Profound Yellow Realm. Those later incorporated, such as the Heavenly Law Realm beings, were not included.

"The true cornerstone of the Immortal Vanishing Illusion is [Profound Yellow Beings]!"

"As the Profound Yellow beings' intentions entered and shaped the Immortal Vanishing Illusion, the Immortal Vanishing Illusion also quietly entered the bodies of the Profound Yellow beings."

"The Supreme Dao Scripture has long since disintegrated, completing a certain degree of binding with the Profound Yellow beings."

"This is also why the Profound Yellow Great Celestial Venerable possesses a certain degree of authority to modify the Immortal Vanishing Illusion." Li Fan's gaze flickered, as if he had unraveled the truth of the Immortal Vanishing Illusion.

"Thus, the Immortal Vanishing Illusion has two bases for existence. One is the illusory scene of the Boundless Star Domain's core. The other is the intentions of the Profound Yellow beings. As long as either one exists, the Immortal Vanishing Illusion can continue to exist."

"To completely destroy the Immortal Vanishing Illusion, one would have to kill all the original Profound Yellow beings." Upon reaching this thought, Li Fan couldn't help but frown slightly. With his current strength, he could indeed achieve this. However, it would be akin to 'damaging a thousand enemies while losing eight hundred himself.' Not only would his carefully crafted spacetime anchor points be destroyed, but his plan to seal the Profound Yellow Immortals would also be greatly affected.

"If it's only to completely eliminate the hidden danger of the Immortal Vanishing Illusion, it might not be worth it." After weighing the pros and cons, Li Fan finally made a new decision. Previously, he had wanted to destroy the Immortal Vanishing Illusion because of its unknown nature. If its true foundation was unknown, it was impossible to guard against it. But now…

"The Supreme Dao Scripture may not necessarily be unusable by me."

"Even if you've disintegrated and hidden yourself within the Profound Yellow beings, I am still the Father of Profound Yellow. All Profound Yellow beings are within my grasp!"

With a single thought, Li Fan split into countless tiny intentions. When the miracle of the Profound Yellow Dao Enlightenment's Gift descended again, accompanied by the surging intentions of countless beings between heaven and earth, these small divided intentions quietly infiltrated the minds of the beings. Li Fan had once understood the profound grand formation of 'Forging Beings with Beings.' Though ants are small, when amassed in countless numbers, they can resist mountains and seas. Although Li Fan was the Father of Profound Yellow heaven and earth, upon close contact with the boundless sea of Profound Yellow beings' intentions, he felt as if he had suddenly plunged into a boundless ocean. He almost lost his direction.

However, Li Fan had personally entered the Infinite Sea several times and returned safely. Compared to the vast and boundless Infinite Sea, the sea of Profound Yellow beings' intentions was nothing. Within a few breaths, Li Fan adapted and began searching for the hidden traces of the Supreme Dao Scripture like searching for a needle in a haystack.

In reality, as if unaware of Li Fan's search, the Immortal Vanishing Illusion continued to repair itself instinctively. Even with Li Fan's active blockade and isolation, the growth rate of the new Immortal Vanishing Illusion was extremely fast. It seemed that after experiencing destruction and shedding its original form, it had become easier to grow. In just the time it takes to brew a cup of tea, it had recovered to one percent of its original size. However, after this point, the recovery speed of the Immortal Vanishing Illusion slowed down.

"Relying on the bedrock rooted within the Profound Yellow beings, it can only recover to this extent. To regain its full scale, it would require a continuous supply of nourishment from the Profound Yellow beings. But with my blockade, it can only reach this point." Li Fan sat beside the Immortal Vanishing Illusion, silently watching and waiting for the changes to occur. The Supreme Dao Scripture was hidden cleverly, but it was like a turtle in a jar, unable to escape. Capturing it was only a matter of time. And Li Fan had plenty of time.

Naturally, the Profound Yellow beings were unaware of the battle between Li Fan and the Supreme Dao Scripture. To them, being unable to enter the Immortal Vanishing Illusion was merely a part of the great changes in the Profound Yellow heaven and earth. What they truly cared about was a phenomenon that had recently traversed the entire Profound Yellow Immortal Realm: ninety-nine continuous mountain ranges, rising straight into the sky, reflecting Profound Yellow. Almost all Profound Yellow beings could witness this magnificent sight. After shining in the sky, these ninety-nine mountain ranges finally transformed into a world, soaring upwards again. Ultimately, they reached the edge of the firmament, visible to the naked eye, like a star hanging in the nine heavens! When cultivators attempted to use their divine sense to contact and sense this star, information about this star, 'Tianlu Star, Ji Wangxian!' would inexplicably flash in their minds. All cultivators who could perceive this information were profoundly shaken. For it represented the birth of the first Nascent Soul cultivator in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm after its heavens and earth underwent drastic changes! And the Nascent Soul of the new era possessed such astonishing power, far surpassing the Harmonious Dao and Longevity realms of the past, reaching an unimaginable level! One must know that the mountain ranges of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm were incomparable to those of the past Profound Yellow Realm. The combined size of these ninety-nine mountain ranges was already half the size of the former Profound Yellow Realm. And how strong would Ji Wangxian be, who attained Dao by mastering these continuous mountain ranges? While the cultivators felt fear, various ambitions also arose in their hearts. Who was Ji Wangxian? He was a familiar figure to the cultivators of the Profound Yellow Realm. He was the ancestor of the 'Myriad Merchants Association,' merely a merchant! Yet now, he had achieved Nascent Soul before countless prodigies and heroes. Dissatisfaction, curiosity, jealousy… these complex emotions arose in the hearts of the Profound Yellow beings. Their desire for cultivation and strength increased significantly. Everyone wanted to become the second brilliant star shining in the sky! Not just the Profound Yellow beings, but even Li Fan, the creator of Profound Yellow, was slightly drawn by this first rising star. "It's actually him who completed the breakthrough to Nascent Soul first." "Although there are reasons for my suppression of Su Bai and my teachings on enlightenment…" "But to achieve Nascent Soul before the ten Immortal Dao Sects is enough to show his extraordinary nature." With a thought, Li Fan knew the process of Ji Wangxian's advancement. "A ruthless person." "Indeed, without ruthlessness, nothing can be achieved," Li Fan raised his eyebrows, then praised him, which was rare. The Myriad Merchants Association, unlike other immortal cultivation sects. After the Profound Yellow Realm's heaven and earth underwent drastic changes, cultivators in other immortal cultivation sects had all returned to the same starting line. The previous class system was thus shaken. Many sects even fought amongst themselves over the issue of 'who would hold power in the new era.' However, within the Myriad Merchants Association, there was no such problem. Old Ancestor Ji Wangxian, even though he had returned to the mortal realm, still maintained absolute control over others. This was because the entire Ji family and the Myriad Merchants Association were creations of Ji Wangxian, tools for accumulating wealth and cultivating, serving him. The Ji family members were controlled by Ji Wangxian from birth. Just like Ji Zhaoxuan, whom Li Fan encountered in the Immortal Vanishing Illusion. Therefore, when the new era arrived, Ji Wangxian was not surprised but overjoyed. Whenever a Ji family member gained some insight into the new world, Ji Wangxian would directly devour it, digesting the insights of the other party. With the lives of thousands as food, Ji Wangxian's cultivation speed was unparalleled. He also ensured that he did not deplete his resources entirely, cultivating a large number of prodigies as reserves for future 'food.' Simultaneously, Ji Wangxian also organized his men to plunder other cultivators and process them into slaves using secret techniques, for cultivation sustenance. With the Profound Yellow Realm in turmoil and order collapsing, and without the constraints of the ten sects and rules, Ji Wangxian had found the perfect stage for his ambitions. Through this method, Ji Wangxian became the first Nascent Soul cultivator in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, transforming into a star and reflecting Profound Yellow. Henceforth, as long as the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm existed, he would be immortal and indestructible. Even in the face of Dao Annihilation, he would have a sliver of hope for survival. In a sense, Ji Wangxian of Tianlu Star’s ability to resist the calamity of mountains and seas surpassed even the so-called True Immortals of the past! Even though this resistance was largely built upon the foundation Li Fan had laid. Currently, besides Ji Wangxian, no other cultivators in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm knew about the benefits of transforming into a Profound Yellow star. And Ji Wangxian would not kindly share this secret with others. He only desired further progress. After all, with the creation of Nascent Soul, what about the subsequent stages of Spirit Transformation and Harmonious Dao? Ji Wangxian's exploitation and devouring became even more excessive. The Ji family had no room for resistance. "This is also a path of Great Dao cultivation." "It is a pity that relying entirely on others will ultimately limit one's achievements. One cannot forge their own path of transcendence." Li Fan commented. "However, my God Conferring List might have a place for him. Ji Wangxian is not skilled in cultivation and enlightenment, but in manipulating and deceiving others, I might even learn from him." Li Fan marveled at Ji Wangxian's methods. Putting aside past events, after achieving Nascent Soul, Ji Wangxian invented a new method. After becoming a star and achieving immortality, Ji Wangxian gathered all the Ji family members. Then, he implanted his flesh and blood essence into each of them, calling it 'the ancestor's gift.' This implanted flesh and blood essence could indeed aid cultivation, and with the characteristics of Tianlu Star, the Ji family members also possessed a semi-'immortal and indestructible' ability, greatly increasing their combat power. However, the greater role of the flesh and blood essence was for taxation. A large portion of the insights and cultivation gains of all Ji family members would be absorbed by Ji Wangxian. The higher the cultivation, the heavier the tax. Moreover, those implanted with flesh and blood would have their desires uncontrollably inflated, gradually eroding their ethics and morals, and spontaneously contributing to the Ji family's growth every night. Ji Wangxian's cultivation resources would continue to expand. In this burden, if anyone still managed to cultivate at a rapid pace, they would be specially targeted by Ji Wangxian. They would be helped to reproduce more outstanding descendants as future cultivation 'seed reserves.' At the same time, this genius himself would always be at risk of being devoured by Ji Wangxian. "This development model is indeed the most suitable for the current Profound Yellow Immortal Realm." "However, it needs to be restricted, otherwise, if he accumulates too much advantage, others will not be able to resist." Li Fan thought this and drew a circle in the air towards the ninety-nine mountain ranges. Moments later, countless sleeping spirits and monsters around the mountain ranges instantly awakened and surged towards the Ji family's territory. "Although it won't lead to immediate destruction, they will have to divert half of their energy to deal with the monster siege."

Chapter 1565: The Supreme Dao Book Appears

With Li Fan's current control over the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, everything that happened within this new world did not escape his calculations.

As Li Fan predicted, the rapid ascent of the Ji family was immediately curbed. The ferocious spirits and monsters were relentless, forcing even Ji Wangxian to dedicate a portion of his energy to dealing with them. However, having already transformed into a Profound Yellow Star, he possessed sufficient protective power, so the Ji family was not annihilated amidst the monster onslaught.

Perhaps the emergence of the first Profound Yellow Star spurred on other cultivators. Barely half a month later, the second Profound Yellow Star materialized. The one who achieved this feat was the Sect Master of the Supreme Dao Sect, Chen Qiandu! This was the same old Daoist whom Li Fan had glimpsed through Jiang Yingyue's eyes, the one who remained unmoved even when Li Fan presented his forged "Supreme Dao Scripture." Unlike Ji Wangxian's opportunistic path, Chen Qiandu's enlightenment was a genuine result of his own comprehension.

A phantom figure crossed the rippling water in the celestial dome, revealing the vision of the second Profound Yellow Star, the Crossing Star. The moment the Crossing Star appeared, all the disciples of the Supreme Dao Sect, scattered throughout the world due to the Profound Yellow Realm's upheaval, seemed to find their backbone once more. They all headed towards the Crossing Star. The light of the Crossing Star guided them, helping them avoid the vast majority of monster attacks on their journey. Thus, the Supreme Dao Sect became the first of the Ten Immortal Dao Sects to seemingly recover its foundational energy.

"This Chen Qiandu truly has some skill," Li Fan remarked, observing the Crossing Star beneath the Four Heavenly Gates from his vantage point. The entire process of the old Daoist's enlightenment unfolded in his mind in an instant. As the Sect Master of the Supreme Dao Sect, Chen Qiandu did not concern himself much with sect affairs. From the moment he became Sect Master, he had practically handed over all responsibilities to his junior brother, Duan Zhiyi, dedicating himself entirely to understanding the Dao and cultivation. The transformation of the Profound Yellow Realm did not significantly impact Chen Qiandu. Consequently, his "Path of Crossing" remained unchanged by the external environment; it followed his innate will. Even if he had to start anew from the Qi Refining stage, he remained calm and collected, crossing step by step.

"No wonder he so resolutely refused my Supreme Dao Scripture back then. I underestimated this person a bit," Li Fan mused, nodding slightly in appreciation. "This Path of Crossing already bears the semblance of a path of transcending merely crossing."

Then, Li Fan seemed to recall something and frowned slightly. "I remember that ten thousand years later in the Star Sea of Shuò, there was a region called the [Thousand Crossing Dojo], a gathering place for many surviving forces, akin to a sword domain. I imagine this person must have built it. Chen Qiandu has considerable potential. Perhaps his cultivation progress will soon surpass Ji Wangxian's."

With the first and second stars having already appeared, Li Fan turned his gaze towards Xuanyuan Tuo and Su Bai. Despite Li Fan's deliberate suppression, Su Bai's cultivation had already reached the pinnacle of Golden Core, just a step away from attaining Nascent Soul. And this was despite him not dedicating his entire focus to cultivation. Su Bai spent nearly half his day teaching the orphans from the dilapidated temple and maintaining order in Ningyuan City. Even so, his progress was remarkable, demonstrating his exceptional talent.

Compared to Su Bai, Xuanyuan Tuo seemed somewhat lacking. He hadn't even taken the first step in cultivation, Qi Refining. He merely remained in seclusion, occasionally looking up at the sky as if contemplating something. Li Fan, however, was not disappointed in his method of imparting knowledge. He had a vague premonition that Xuanyuan Tuo, though not yet cultivating, was brewing something significant. Much like the Profound Yellow's New Law in the past, once it emerged, it would be earth-shattering.

"The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's new law... I'm truly looking forward to it," Li Fan smiled faintly. Built upon the Infinite Sea and the Mountains Above, infused with the power of the Great Dao of Longevity, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's characteristics of infinity and longevity perfectly resolved the potential hidden dangers of developing a new cultivation method. No matter how much cultivation devoured the heavens and earth, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm could continuously regenerate itself. The heavens and earth, and the cultivators, no longer had irreconcilable contradictions. Instead, they shared a common goal: survival amidst the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation! "No longer a battle to the death, but rather shared prosperity and shared destruction."

As cultivators comprehended the Great Dao laws of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm and transformed into stars, adorning the celestial sky, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm itself underwent many profound changes due to the addition of these cultivators' stars. The most significant was that the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm became more stable with the integration of the cultivator stars. It was as if, during the process of building a house, Li Fan had used the Mountains Above, the Infinite Sea, and the Great Dao of Longevity as materials to lay the foundation of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. However, as this was the first time he had truly created an Immortal Realm, there were inevitably numerous loopholes. Within this grand framework, countless small "cracks" existed. As cultivators achieved enlightenment, these invisible minute gaps were gradually filled. "This is what is meant by 'using the human way to mend the heavenly way'." "The more prosperous the cultivation scene in this realm, the more stable my Profound Yellow Immortal Realm will become." Li Fan sat cross-legged in the ninth heaven, calmly observing the changes in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Time flowed by, and twenty years passed in the blink of an eye. The stars adorning the Profound Yellow celestial dome had increased to thirty-eight, but the first cultivator to reach the Nascent Soul stage had yet to appear. After these years of waiting, Li Fan's time of harvest had finally arrived. He had split countless divine senses that had now fully infiltrated and established themselves within the minds of all Profound Yellow beings. Essentially, all their thoughts were now completely under Li Fan's control. In the ninth heaven, situated just below Li Fan, above the cultivator stars and the Four Heavenly Gates, swirled a mass of distorted light. This was a phantom world created by Li Fan, imitating the Immortal Vanishing Realm, based on his observations of the cultivators' thoughts. Li Fan named it the [Great Illusionary Realm]. Here, cultivators could not only understand their thoughts and inner desires but also glimpse into the minds of others. They could even manifest certain fantastical creations into the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm! "This Great Illusionary Realm can only be entered by those stars in the heavens." "Below the stars, mortals cannot see or know." Li Fan's will was the law of the Profound Yellow Realm. As the Heavenly Dao flowed, the Great Illusionary Realm quietly changed, its light dimming, becoming more ethereal. Only cultivators' stars that were close could still detect its presence. It wasn't long before cultivators at the Nascent Soul stage discovered this mass of light and cautiously began to explore it. Each time they entered, it further strengthened the Great Illusionary Realm. Li Fan did not create the Great Illusionary Realm out of kindness for the Profound Yellow cultivators' cultivation. It was for the [Supreme Dao Record]! The Supreme Dao Record was hidden too deeply, and it shifted with the thoughts of living beings. Over the past twenty years, Li Fan had tried various methods to find it. While he had some success, the rendered Supreme Dao Records were always incomplete, even inferior to the fake version Li Fan had created. So, Li Fan changed his approach. Instead of digging directly, he installed a mirror in each being's mind, projecting all their thoughts simultaneously. This coalescence of projected consciousness formed the Great Illusionary Realm. Although the human heart is constantly changing, at any given moment, their thoughts are immutable. By observing the thoughts of all beings at a specific fixed moment, one could piece together the complete Supreme Dao Record. Under Li Fan's manipulation, the Great Illusionary Realm churned like a storm, light and shadow constantly shifting. In an instant, it felt as if millions of billions of changes had occurred. Through Li Fan's continuous adjustments, a majestic scroll, floating in the starry sky, finally appeared before him. Unlike the distorted and illegible True Immortal Seal Script seen in the Immortal Vanishing Realm, this Supreme Dao Record, reflected by the Great Illusionary Realm, had every word of True Immortal Seal Script rendered with perfect clarity! A scroll, spanning the starry sky, its Seal Script shining, truly resembling the Great Dao, illuminating the world. Li Fan saw familiar characters within it. Hunger, Ancient, Manifest, Return, Restrain... Primordial, Creation, Innate, Inaction... Some light images were very solid, while others appeared hollowed out, showing only a faint transparency. "This is the difference between proving the Nameless Dao." "I never expected that the number of those who proved the Nameless Dao would be so few." Li Fan swept through the True Immortal Seal Script recorded in the Supreme Dao Record and found that those who proved the Nameless Dao accounted for less than one in a hundred thousand. "Furthermore, there are those who have transcended and departed, and those who have been stolen." Li Fan observed carefully and discovered remaining traces in the parts of the Supreme Dao Record where characters were missing. Based on his experience in the Immortal Vanishing Realm, Li Fan first located the positions of the thirty-plus stolen characters. These characters were located towards the front of the Supreme Dao Record. They were not transparent but only bore faint imprints, their original forms now invisible. "As for those who proved the Nameless Dao but have departed..." Li Fan looked at these characters. Their shapes varied; some left only faint traces, while others had vanished completely. Some left relatively clear imprints. Li Fan compared them meticulously and mused, "This represents the different states of those who have transcended and departed." "Some have completely severed their connection with the Profound Yellow Realm. Others, like Duke Shou Qiu, left behind something akin to a Dao-Inheriting phantom, a remnant to support the Dao Annihilation." He believed these residual characters still had subtle connections with these nameless transcended beings. Li Fan did not delve too deeply, merely observing them from a distance. The Supreme Dao Record, spanning across the darkness of space, was vast and boundless. A brief perusal took Li Fan three years. "My previous guess was correct." "After the Immortal Realm's destruction, most of the True Immortal Seal Scripts recorded in the Dao Record are merely that – True Immortal Seal Scripts. The Great Daos they were connected to were either incomplete or had already been devoured by Dao Annihilation." "Therefore, most of the True Immortal Seal Scripts in this Scroll are invalid. Only the Great Daos that still exist in the lower realms hold value for comprehension." Li Fan's divine sense swept across the Supreme Dao Record, marking each valuable character. "I can faintly sense a connection between these characters and the outside world. Some point beyond the Primordial Possibility, while others remain within it. There are even True Immortals who have not proven the Nameless Dao but have gained insights in their respective paths." Li Fan's eyes flickered. "With this Supreme Dao Record, I might be able to capture them one by one." In Li Fan's vision, each character in the Supreme Dao Record had a fine thread behind it, connecting to a True Immortal in the outside world. Countless threads, dispersed in various locations. Li Fan examined them carefully, his gaze seeming to penetrate infinite time and space, focusing on the other end of the threads. "The surviving lower realm star seas of the Primordial are more numerous than I originally imagined." "However, some are simply too distant." "Compared to that, the Star Sea of Guang Wu is already considered adjacent." "But even just the areas near the High Wall are enough for me to digest for a while." According to the connections presented in the Supreme Dao Record, Li Fan had already classified the True Immortals behind them by strength. "When Profound Yellow Immortal Realm Harmonious Dao cultivators are born in large numbers, I can use them to capture them for me." After carefully marking everything, Li Fan finally refocused his attention on the Supreme Dao Record itself. Serving as a hunting indicator was merely a secondary use of the Supreme Dao Record. Its original purpose was, naturally, for enlightenment. "As expected of something created by the Dao Inscriber Immortal. It is far more exquisite than the True Immortal Seal Scripts I saw in my past reincarnations." "It even seems closer to the Great Dao itself than the True Immortal Seal Scripts manifested after the fall of the Nameless True Immortals," Li Fan marveled, staring at the character for 'Hunger' in the Dao Record. "However..." "There is no character for [Dao Inscription] in this Dao Record?" Li Fan's heart instinctively questioned. "Normally speaking, the Dao of Dao Inscription is also one of the Great Daos in this world. If this Supreme Dao Record were complete, this character should be included." "Yet, I cannot find it anywhere..." Li Fan snorted. "It seems that person, the Dao Inscriber Immortal, hid it." "How many True Immortal Seal Scripts like Dao Inscription are there, I wonder?" Li Fan stared at the thirty-odd stolen characters in the Supreme Dao Record. The threads behind them pointed to a place beyond the Primordial Possibility, a place called the [Realm of Life and Death]. Countless years may have passed, but this connection had not been severed. "With this guidance, I can reach the Realm of Life and Death directly. If I had the strength to traverse Mountains and Seas." "However, since Dao Inscription has vanished without a trace, there is no need for me to seek out further trouble." Li Fan shook his head slightly. Then, opening his mouth wide, he swallowed the Supreme Dao Record manifested by the Great Illusionary Realm directly into himself. The Great Illusionary Realm reverted to its original appearance, so as not to alert the Profound Yellow cultivators. Li Fan, alone, began to comprehend the countless True Immortal Seal Scripts within his mind. If enlightenment was an exam, then Li Fan now held the answer key. He only needed to follow the pattern to directly reach the Great Dao itself. Another ten years passed, and within Li Fan's body, a Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, a hundred times larger than the one in his previous life, quietly took shape.

Chapter 1566: No Need to Prove Longevity

The Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, woven with the ink-black clouds of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's nascent Ink Slaughter as threads and the countless True Immortal Seal Scripts recorded in the Supreme Dao Scripture as nodes, could almost be considered a miniature version of the complete Great Dao of the original possibility.

Except for the Great Daos that had already escaped and vanished, Li Fan mirrored all remaining Great Daos with the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net.

If it were the initial version of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net from his previous life, doing so would certainly have alerted the True Immortals still existing in the primordial world. But in this life, the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net did not mirror directly. Instead, it used the Supreme Dao Scripture as a relay for contact.

Therefore, it remained in a safe, hidden state.

With the initial establishment of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, Li Fan's strength also reached an extremely delicate realm.

Although he had not officially proven the Dao to become a True Immortal, through the Great Celestial Venerable Immortal Puppet, Li Fan could still invoke infinite power.

The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was forged on the Mountain Above. Li Fan, as the parent of Profound Yellow, thus possessed the aura of a True Immortal.

Inside his body, there was also the power of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's illusory projection formed by the feedback from the Sitting Heaven Technique. Now, with the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net centered around Ink Slaughter...

Although not a True Immortal, his strength was not comparable to ordinary True Immortals.

Even those who proved the Nameless Dao would not be Li Fan's opponent.

"In the Primordial, I have already reached the peak I could reach. Henceforth, all cultivation methods might slightly improve combat power, but they will be useless for the next step."

"Transcendence..."

After experiencing the tribulation of the Three Daos merging, Li Fan lost his memories and cultivation.

He was even forced to come to an unfamiliar time and space ten thousand years ago.

But even so, he only used a mere hundred years to constantly recover to his original state, and even reached an important node on his own cultivation path.

This was due to the foundation he had accumulated in his past reincarnations.

Although there were some minor disturbances, they ultimately did not affect the outcome.

Li Fan was destined to reach this step quickly.

"But how to truly take this step?"

Li Fan seemed to arrive at the center of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, surrounded by pitch-black starry sky, with only countless fine lines representing the Great Daos, crisscrossing each other.

Scanning them, Li Fan pondered the most suitable path for himself.

He had already begun seeking the answer to this question a long time ago.

But now, on the verge of breaking through, the answer remained vague.

"Logically speaking, when one's strength and realm reach my level, even if there is no answer in their heart for the moment, there should at least be a general direction to proceed. It is impossible to have no clear idea at all."

"This is because my path is too special. It is completely different from any other cultivator."

The anomaly of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net shattered around him, revealing the magnificent scenery of the Profound Yellow Realm.

"My current strength is almost eighty percent derived from this Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Once I attempt to take the path of transcendence and leave the possibility of the [Primordial] the moment I do, I will immediately sever my connection with the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. My foundation will be gone, like stepping into thin air and falling from a ten-thousand-foot building to a flat surface in an instant."

"To climb again would be no different from starting from scratch. Naturally, it would be extremely difficult."

"This is the downside of borrowing power. And it is only reasonable. After all, a hundred years is enough to show the incredible speed of cultivating from a mortal to a Nameless True Immortal. There is no such thing as a perfect thing in the world."

Li Fan was very clear in his heart.

However, even though he said so, he did not give up on finding a solution to the drawback.

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless, what can be used as a boat?"

According to Li Fan's previous thinking and behavior patterns, he would naturally seek the help of others to achieve his own transcendence.

However, the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas was different from before.

To cross it, one could only rely on oneself. It seemed there was no way to take shortcuts, which put Li Fan in a dilemma for a time.

However, Li Fan was not in a hurry.

Although True Transformation was still dormant, his foundation was stable. Before the Primordial was swallowed by Dao Annihilation, he had ample time to think.

Li Fan was exploring the answer for his future, and the cultivators of Profound Yellow were also doing the same.

The step from Nascent Soul to Divinity Transformation was even more difficult than all previous realms combined.

Even Ji Wangxian, who was exploiting his family members to the extreme, even Chen Qiandu, who had vaguely found his own path, even Su Bai, who had outstanding talent.

Facing this chasm, they could not help but feel a glimmer of despair.

Divinity Transformation was like this, what about the subsequent Harmonious Dao?

Even if they successfully achieved Divinity Transformation, how would they take the next step?

As long as the thought arose in the cultivator's heart, it was inevitably cast a shadow. If one could not emerge from this shadow, they might never be able to progress in their lifetime.

The gap between different realms was so huge, but this was not Li Fan deliberately making things difficult for Profound Yellow cultivators.

It was due to the special circumstances of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

Although the cultivators of Profound Yellow stood above the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm and gained an advantage out of thin air, they were essentially mortals.

From Qi Refining to Harmonious Dao, the entire cultivation process was actually the transformation from mortal to Nameless True Immortal.

The gap between each realm was naturally unimaginably large.

"There might be thousands of those who rank among the stars, but among these stars, only one in ten thousand can enter the God Conferring List! And among those on the list, only a very few can finally surpass the Four Immortal Gates and rank among the immortals!" Li Fan saw through the potential and upper limit of all Profound Yellow cultivators at a glance.

Without any other serendipitous encounters, most of them would be trapped in realms below Nascent Soul for their entire lives.

Seemingly tragic. However, compared to cultivators outside the Profound Yellow Realm, they were already incredibly fortunate.

At the very least, with the protection of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, they no longer had to worry about the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

"When the first Harmonious Dao cultivator is born in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, that will be the time when the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm officially connects with Mountains and Seas. I hope you do not keep me waiting too long."

Li Fan's gaze swept over a few figures below.

After the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net was initially formed, Li Fan also ceased suppressing Su Bai.

Without the suppression, Su Bai's true talent finally began to reveal itself, achieving the eighteenth star of Profound Yellow, the Tianjin Star.

The Nascent Soul star anomaly was precisely the range of one hundred thousand miles around Ningyuan City after its transformation.

All living beings within it were protected by Su Bai and would no longer be troubled by strange creatures.

As for the Transmission of the Law...

It still remained at the initial stage of cultivation.

A hundred years passed, and even the most devout followers of the Transmission of the Law had slowly forgotten it by now.

After all, there had been no news from the Transmission of the Law during these hundred years. Most of the Myriad Immortal Alliance cultivators believed that the Transmission of the Law had already perished in the changes of heaven and earth.

Otherwise, it would be difficult to explain why, in the guise of the Transmission of the Law, they had not yet transformed into a star.

WWW ●●CΟ

After all, three of the disciples of the Transmission of the Law in the past had already reached the Nascent Soul realm.

They only occasionally remembered the exceptionally brilliant Transmission of the Law Immortal Venerable when they were cultivating.

The cultivation path of New Law cultivators in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was even more difficult.

Nine out of ten were burst by the strange objects and grotto-heavens within their bodies.

A very small number of extremely talented individuals successfully re-mastered them, but when advancing to the next step, they faced almost a dead end.

Extracting the essence of heaven and earth to gain its spirit; sacrificing the soul of heaven and earth to merge with the Dao; reversing the principles of heaven and earth to prove longevity!

After Nascent Soul, there were three major realms. Although New Law cultivators had not yet met the conditions for cultivation in the past, they could at least imagine them in their minds. However, now...

There was not even room for imagination.

During the drastic changes of the universe, many grotto-heavens still existed and underwent transformation and sublimation along with it.

However, the essence of heaven and earth, the soul of heaven and earth, had directly disappeared from the sight of all New Law cultivators.

Without the necessary materials for cultivation, how could they cultivate?

The only thing that could support the New Law cultivators was that these materials had not truly disappeared, but rather their current realm was too low to detect them. Perhaps when their cultivation improved in the future, they would have further opportunities.

However, the reality was not as they wished.

The essence of heaven and earth is the change that heaven and earth will undergo.

The soul of heaven and earth is the one who upholds the Dao.

In the original Profound Yellow Realm, these two were the principles of the natural operation of the Profound Yellow heavens and earth, and they would naturally appear in the world.

But now, above the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao, there was a Creator, Li Fan!

Since the resources of strange objects and grotto-heavens could be continuously regenerated, how could Li Fan, the creator of the Profound Yellow Realm, possibly give away the authority of the Profound Yellow Realm?

Thus, Li Fan hid them.

If the New Law cultivators still followed the original cultivation method, it would truly be a dead end.

Li Fan had no intention of kindly reminding them.

He was more interested in seeing how the Transmission of the Law could change the New Law to make it function correctly within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

After observing carefully for a while, Li Fan discovered that the aura of the Transmission of the Law was fluctuating, showing signs of awakening.

And by probing the mind of the Transmission of the Law, Li Fan found that a violent storm was gathering in their consciousness.

Thunderclouds rolled, all centered around one thought.

"Do not prove Longevity, only prove Harmonious Dao!"

Li Fan stared at these words constantly echoing in the mind of the Transmission of the Law and could not help but narrow his eyes.

"It's a little interesting."

"It seems that he has vaguely sensed my existence as the ruler of this world."

Undoubtedly, the thoughts of the Transmission of the Law were extremely wise.

Not to mention that the foundation of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was the Infinite Sea and the Mountain Above, as well as the Great Dao of Longevity. The principles of Profound Yellow were the principles of Mountains and Seas and Longevity. It was by no means something that cultivators within the Profound Yellow Realm could reverse.

Not to mention that besides this, there was also Li Fan, the helmsman.

To reverse the principles of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was like contending with Li Fan for control of Profound Yellow. Even if an earth-shattering talent were to emerge from the countless beings in the Profound Yellow Realm.

Before they could successfully prove the Dao, Li Fan would decisively control them.

"Cut off one's own spirit to seek life."

"Not bad. Seemingly abandoning the most important step, in reality, by taking a step back, the horizon becomes wider, gaining room for survival."

Li Fan did not spare his praise.

He was even more looking forward to the complete deduction of the Transmission of the Law.

"If my prediction is correct, the original New Law was to solve the problem of cultivators being unable to cultivate. Then the current New Law is to solve the problem of cultivators' cultivation speed being too slow."

"The arrival of the New Law will bring great benefits to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm!"

In the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, all changes were under Li Fan's control. All the thoughts of the beings in Profound Yellow were also under Li Fan's watch.

Therefore, Li Fan could, to some extent, "foresee" the future scene of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

A smile appeared at the corner of his mouth, and Li Fan turned his gaze away with satisfaction.

He thought again about his path of transcendence.

"Sometimes, jumping out of the established framework and thinking from a different perspective might yield miraculous results."

As if sensing something in his heart, Li Fan's consciousness descended once more into that dark starry sky.

Wandering within the boundless Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, he forgot the passage of time.

Until he had personally treaded all the threads nine times.

A flash of spiritual light finally illuminated the surrounding dark starry sky.

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless, what can be used as a boat..."

"I have been desperately searching for the answer before, but I forgot that the boat was already built by me and has always been under my feet!"

"If I leave the Primordial, I will lose the reliance of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Then let's find a way to bring the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm into the Mountains and Seas!"

"The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm is not only my refuge boat for avoiding disaster, but also my boat for crossing!"

With this, Li Fan's mind instantly became clear.

As if he had understood everything, his laughter echoed throughout the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net.

And as his enlightenment occurred, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm also underwent inexplicable changes.

The heavens and earth trembled, and all things roared.

The strong tremors lasted for a full quarter of an hour.

All beings living within it felt a sense of imminent danger.

However, after the tremors subsided, this sense of danger quickly dissipated.

In the heavens and earth, only the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao remained immersed in that sense of fear.

Because it acutely sensed that the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, which originally had a foundation in the [Primordial] possibility, was completely "cutting" itself off from the Primordial.

If the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was originally a house built on the primordial land, then after the "cutting" was completed, it would become a wandering ship.

Although it was more free, it was also more dangerous.

The Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao undoubtedly preferred safety.

But the one who caused all this was Li Fan, the parent of Profound Yellow. Even with ten thousand unwillingness, it could only bear it silently.

Just for self-preservation, it instinctively unleashed various hidden potentials.

As a result, countless changes quietly occurred within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

For example, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm proactively began to differentiate into tentacle-like roots, exploring and rooting towards the surroundings along its foundation in the Mountain Above.

For example, more and more souls of heaven and earth were summoned to the vicinity of the Four Heavenly Gates.

Even though the connection with the Infinite Sea had not been officially opened, they were already preemptively sensing the infinite power, preparing for the formal connection with Mountains and Seas in the future.

For example, in the original Profound Yellow heavens and earth, there were still some residual, wandering immortal artifacts and fragments. In the past, the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao appeared very indifferent. Although it "digested" them proactively, it was only through the natural circulation of heaven and earth, slowly assimilating them.

But now...

Dao souls appeared near these immortal artifacts, collecting and imprisoning them.

Then, they actively "refined" them.

Although for the current Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, these residual immortal artifacts were not even comparable to supplementary medicine.

However, it could, to some extent, indicate the attitude of the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao.Chapter 1556: Refining the Profound Yellow Realm with Pills

As the memories of the previous Starving Immortal, or rather, the "Dao Devourer" from another possibility, flashed through Li Fan's mind, his skeletal remains transformed into streams of light, becoming another Heavenly Pillar.

Although it was only half a Heavenly Pillar, compared to what Li Fan had obtained previously, it undoubtedly represented a more fundamental condensation of the primordial Great Dao of "Starvation."

Li Fan did not uproot this Heavenly Pillar from the Immortal Ruins. Instead, he buried the half that sealed the Starving Immortal near it. He could sense that due to their mutual comprehension of the Great Dao of "Starvation," even though the cores of the two Heavenly Pillars were not from the same individual, there was still a tendency for them to merge.

"He could not achieve the Nameless Dao in life, yet he has a chance after death. It can be considered helping you fulfill your wish," Li Fan nodded to himself.

After temporarily settling the two Heavenly Pillars, Li Fan savored what he had just witnessed. Although the memories of the previous Starving Immortal were brief, there were three points that Li Fan found particularly noteworthy.

The first was the Dao of "Dao Devouring." Hidden within the Great Dao of "Starvation," its domineering desire to swallow mountains and drink seas was not Li Fan's illusion but the manifestation of this "Dao Devouring." Being able to devour an entire possibility Dao and turn it into one's own nourishment was undoubtedly an extremely terrifying existence.

"However, he overestimated himself and chose the wrong opponent. He had enough power to devour a single possibility. To face Mountains and Seas..." Li Fan sneered.

Without personally witnessing the Infinite Sea and the Mountain Above, one could not imagine their grandeur. Even the mortal world, encompassing all possibilities, was merely a corner of the Mountains and Seas. The previous Starving Immortal paid the price for his arrogance. After drifting for a long time in the Dao Annihilation, he embarrassingly arrived at the "Primordial," barely surviving. However, with the Three Saints of the Primordial present, he dared not act presumptuously. He had to change his guise, replacing "Dao Devouring" with "Starvation."

Although the two Dao paths had similarities, their power was clearly incomparable. His final fate was to be easily transformed into a pillar supporting the heavens.

The second point that concerned Li Fan was the "Immortal Coffin of Crossing Tribulations" that allowed the Starving Immortal to wander in the Dao Annihilation for so long. The Starving Immortal's remaining memories were not extensive, yet this Immortal Coffin was mentioned repeatedly. Clearly, the Starving Immortal deeply regretted the loss of the Immortal Coffin of Crossing Tribulations. A treasure that even a ruthless being like the Starving Immortal, who could destroy and devour single possibilities, cared so much about must possess its own mysteries.

"I wonder who stole this Immortal Coffin of Crossing Tribulations. Since the Immortal Realm is destroyed, if it still exists, it should be in some part of the lower stellar sea."

Although he had personally witnessed the destruction of the "Primordial," Li Fan had not yet explored all the surviving territories of the Primordial. His footsteps were currently limited to the High Wall, Suo Xing, and Guang Wu. The reasons for this were threefold: the obstruction of Dao Annihilation and the difficulty of travel; secondly, the forces that survived the destruction of the Immortal Realm were all formidable. In his previous life, the formidable weapons wielded by the Guang Wu Star Sea, such as Dao Swords, Dao Blades, and Dao Chronicle Projection Beads, all possessed world-destroying power. Guang Wu Star Sea was like this, and other star seas were as well.

Moreover, the backdrop of Dao Annihilation meant that these star seas were exceptionally repellent to outsiders. Exploring all the star seas of the Primordial was no easy task. Of course, the most crucial reason was that it was unnecessary. Li Fan's primary exploration objective in the future was to break free from the Mountains and Seas of the Primordial, and even to travel upstream to the Eternal Void. The High Wall, Suo Xing, and Guang Wu held no fundamental difference for Li Fan.

As for the last point that concerned Li Fan greatly, even causing him immense trepidation, it was the "Virtuous True Immortal." From the Starving Immortal's memories, Li Fan learned that this Virtuous True Immortal not only possessed extraordinary power but also acted entirely differently from the supreme experts Li Fan had encountered before.

The Duke of Shou Qiu, Emperor Tai Tian, Purple Robe, and the Three Saints were all powerful, but they all, to varying degrees, embodied the demeanor of "the strong" and acted according to certain rules. But this Virtuous True Immortal, despite his name, was utterly devoid of virtue in his actions! He habitually stood on the moral high ground to manipulate and control others, remaining indifferent to the lives and deaths of others. Anything that brought him benefit must be pursued; anything that threatened him must be ruthlessly destroyed...

Li Fan was all too familiar with this style of action! Although they had not yet met, Li Fan had a premonition that this Virtuous True Immortal would undoubtedly become his formidable adversary in the future!

"Interesting. Let's see who is more 'virtuous'!" The first-generation Immortal Puppet lightly stepped onto the ground of the Immortal Ruins. Under the sweep of the Dao Devouring power, the former ruins of the Immortal Realm were instantly shattered into countless fine particles and then rapidly devoured by the first-generation Immortal Puppet.

The Immortal Ruins would cease to exist in the future, leaving only two Starving Immortal Heavenly Pillars, one new and one old, to support the collapsing heavens of this place.

Using the body of the first-generation Immortal Puppet, Li Fan savored the essence of the Immortal Ruins. The entire Immortal Realm was carved out from the Mountain Above. Thus, as he slowly chewed, Li Fan's vision conjured images of vast, continuous mountain ranges.

"With this ability to gaze afar, one can indeed comprehend certain 'principles of mountains.' However, it is still far inferior to personally visiting the Mountains and Seas. Even Duke Shou Qiu's path of sitting on a mountain and gazing at the sea is vastly inferior."

Li Fan was not surprised by this, as he had only devoured an Immortal Realm. "It is like walking towards the mountain. The more you devour, the closer you get to the mountain."

The Immortal Realm was destroyed, and there were not many ruins left. Li Fan naturally turned his attention to the Immortal Domain Chess Pieces left behind by Sun Piaomiao. The temporal node of ten thousand years ago had subtle differences in the placement of the chess pieces compared to ten thousand years later, but they were all within the High Wall. During the three years he spent setting up traps and hunting the Starving Immortal, Li Fan had already collected them all.

The remaining disciples of the Medicine King Sect, overjoyed at having escaped the Immortal Ruins and regained new life, eagerly inquired about the situation from the cultivators ahead. To their shock, they discovered they had returned to the Profound Yellow Realm. Fortunately, the Ten Sects were now too busy dealing with the Myriad Immortal Alliance's offensive to bother with them. After much deliberation, the Medicine King Sect disciples, completely bewildered and terrified by what had happened, decided to join the Myriad Immortal Alliance. They thought that with their skills in treating illnesses, they could get by anywhere.

Instead, some peculiar elixirs that were previously considered unorthodox became their capital for survival.

Li Fan did not pay much attention to these matters. He had merely tossed the Medicine King Sect aside instead of devouring them, out of consideration for their past relationship. After unfolding the Immortal Domains and devouring them all with the Dao Devouring method, the first-generation Immortal Puppet temporarily reached its limit. Although the image of the Mountain Above vaguely seen had become clearer, the immense pressure from the approaching mountains followed closely behind, descending upon the first-generation Immortal Puppet.

Immortals were, after all, creations that connected Mountains and Seas. The infinity of the Sea and the height of the Mountain balanced each other, creating True Immortals. Now, with the first-generation Immortal Puppet using the Dao Devouring method to devour an entire Immortal Domain, the mountain had subtly overshadowed the sea within him. Li Fan vaguely sensed that certain unpredictable changes were occurring within the first-generation Immortal Puppet. He could not yet determine whether these changes were good or bad.

Resolutely stopping his continuous devouring, Li Fan attempted to harness the power of the Infinite Sea to counteract the mountain. Amidst the sounds of the sea tides, the oppressive feeling brought by the image of the Mountain Above finally receded, and the first-generation Immortal Puppet barely regained its ability to act.

"That feeling, as if I were about to be swallowed by the shadows of the continuous mountains, was very similar to the experience I had when the Three Daos merged," the first-generation Immortal Puppet sat cross-legged, meditating, while Li Fan meticulously pondered. After a long time, he finally confirmed.

"When the Three Daos merged, I was dissipated into an unknown collection of mysterious forces."

"But what the first-generation Immortal Puppet experienced just now was merely being submerged by the Mountain Above..." Li Fan thought of the Fallen Immortal Realm. The Fallen Immortal Realm contained only the Infinite Sea and no Mountain Above.

"If one were to disregard the consequences and push the Dao Devouring method to its extreme, could one create another Fallen Immortal Realm centered on the Mountain Above, counterpart to the existing one?" Li Fan narrowed his eyes and rapidly deduced, based on his past experience of the Three Daos merging.

If one could maintain their sanity while being submerged by the image of the Mountain Above, they should be able to see this counterpart Fallen Immortal Realm. The Immortal Ruins, the Immortal Domain Chess Pieces, all the Immortal Realm soils that he had devoured before, reappeared intact, but not in their real-world forms. Instead, they appeared as they were on the Mountain Above! Scattered like stars in the endless mountain ranges. Like distant stars in the darkness.

"Being far from the place where Mountains and Seas intermingle, thus in a sense, one can also evade the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation. However, the price..." Li Fan looked around like a ghost. Silence reigned in the mountains above. There was no sound of the sea representing life, only towering peaks.

"Absolute order and hierarchy."

"Life, here, is meaningless." Li Fan suddenly understood why all beings in Sun Piaomiao's prophecy about Mountains and Seas were born from the sea. Because the Mountain Above itself was inherently opposed to life.

"Even True Immortals can borrow the momentum of the mountains, but it does not mean merging with them. They merely stand upon them. Even the Three Saints of the Immortal Realm were like this."

"And the consequence of merging into the mountains..." The shadows of the mountains closed in from all directions. The scattered lands that he had devoured quickly disappeared into the endless mountains. Li Fan abruptly awoke from the illusionary deduction, a cold sweat breaking out on his forehead. Not out of fear, but out of a primal reverence for the Mountain Above that life possesses. The first-generation Immortal Puppet's body was covered in large swathes of shadows.

"Devouring mountains and seas is not mere hyperbole. It's just that one must simultaneously contend with the backlash from both mountains and seas."

"While devouring mountains and seas, one is also being devoured by them." Li Fan understood and connected the Infinite Sea to the first-generation Immortal Puppet to alleviate the pressure from the mountains. It took a full half-year to cleanse the shadows from the first-generation body. Li Fan could not help but sigh, "The two Saint Monarchs, Gui Hai and Lian Shan, were truly gifted. Even if one of them were missing, the so-called Immortal Dao, when cultivated to its extreme, would likely not end well."

"The only outcome would be to merge with Mountains and Seas, becoming one with them."

"But precisely because of the two Saints' heroic deeds, which opened up Mountains and Seas, the balance between them created a foothold for Immortals."

"However, consequently, having established a foothold within Mountains and Seas, one must also participate in facing the tribulations of Mountains and Seas themselves. The merging of Mountains and Seas, the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation..."

The Great Daos of the world are merely the principles of Mountains and Seas. Li Fan, through the Dao Devouring method, directly devoured the ruins of the Immortal Realm, bypassing the process of enlightenment and directly confronting Mountains and Seas. Although his cultivation speed was fast, the side effects were unbearable for ordinary people. It was fortunate that Li Fan had the True Transformation, allowing him to survive the calamity of the Three Daos merging and escape intact. In this lower-level "sinking," he could maintain his stability.

"All things merge into Mountains and Seas, and Mountains and Seas merge into something higher."

"Even Longevity and True Transformation, which are on par with Mountains and Seas, are within this merging sequence..." Li Fan thought of the legend of the Creator God again.

"This legend seems to vaguely point to the greatest truth within Mountains and Seas."

"The so-called Creator God created Mountains and Seas, birthed all things in the mortal world. But in the end, everything in the world will return to its origin."

"The mortal world fades, Mountains and Seas merge. This is the trend, the destiny that the beings within Mountains and Seas must face." In Li Fan's mind, the scene that once made even Mountains and Seas tremble appeared. A lone star hung high, like the single eye of a god, looking down.

"The True Immortals who traversed time and space, passing on sparks of life, were they rebelling against such a fate?" Li Fan stood in the dark starry sky, gazing beyond the "Primordial" and falling silent.

"With my abilities, I can even uncover this truth. Let alone those transcended powerhouses, and even the Three Saints..."

"Even so, they showed no hesitation or despair..."

"Truly remarkable!" Li Fan exclaimed from the bottom of his heart. If there was something guiding the merging of Mountains and Seas in the darkness, perhaps it was the will of the supposedly vanished "Creator God." To save the mortal world and reverse the trend of merging Mountains and Seas was essentially to contend with the Creator God. For an ant in the Mountains and Seas to raise its antennae and attempt to confront a lone star hanging outside the Mountains and Seas was already an unbelievable feat.

"When the sky falls, the taller ones will hold it up. Since they can still persist, let us endure a little longer..." Li Fan muttered, suppressing the unease in his heart. Half of Li Fan's unease stemmed from the trepidation after glimpsing the truth of Mountains and Seas. The other half, however, came from his distrust. Li Fan was never one to entrust his fate to others. Even if they were beings far more powerful than him, like Purple Robe, Shou Qiu, and the Three Saints. When it came to his own life and safety, Li Fan could not help but harbor doubts: "Can these people really do it?" Until the great trend of Mountains and Seas merging was completely reversed, this doubt would never dissipate. "Perhaps, in the end, I will have to step in myself to be at ease." Li Fan's gaze was deep, as if piercing through the fractured River of Time, reaching the very source of everything.

Chapter 1567: Dao One Devours Mountains and Seas

The Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, woven with the nascent Ink Slaughter clouds of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm as threads and the countless True Immortal Seal Scripts recorded in the Supreme Dao Scripture as nodes, could almost be considered a miniature version of the complete Great Dao of the original possibility.

Except for the Great Daos that had already escaped and vanished, all other Great Daos were mirrored by Li Fan with the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net.

If it were the initial version of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net from his previous life, doing so would certainly have alerted the True Immortals still existing in the primordial world. But in this life, the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net did not mirror directly. Instead, it used the Supreme Dao Scripture as a relay for contact.

Therefore, it remained in a safe, hidden state.

With the initial establishment of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, Li Fan's strength also reached an extremely delicate realm.

Although he had not officially proven the Dao to become a True Immortal, through the Great Celestial Venerable Immortal Puppet, Li Fan could still invoke infinite power.

The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was forged on the Mountain Above. Li Fan, as the parent of Profound Yellow, thus possessed the aura of a True Immortal.

Inside his body, there was also the power of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's illusory projection formed by the feedback from the Sitting Heaven Technique. Now, with the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net centered around Ink Slaughter...

Although not a True Immortal, his strength was not comparable to ordinary True Immortals.

Even those who proved the Nameless Dao would not be Li Fan's opponent.

"In the Primordial, I have already reached the peak I could reach. Henceforth, all cultivation methods might slightly improve combat power, but they will be useless for the next step."

"Transcendence..."

After experiencing the tribulation of the Three Daos merging, Li Fan lost his memories and cultivation.

He was even forced to come to an unfamiliar time and space ten thousand years ago.

But even so, he only used a mere hundred years to constantly recover to his original state, and even reached an important node on his own cultivation path.

This was due to the foundation he had accumulated in his past reincarnations.

Although there were some minor disturbances, they ultimately did not affect the outcome.

Li Fan was destined to reach this step quickly.

"But how to truly take this step?"

Li Fan seemed to arrive at the center of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, surrounded by pitch-black starry sky, with only countless fine lines representing the Great Daos, crisscrossing each other.

Scanning them, Li Fan pondered the most suitable path for himself.

He had already begun seeking the answer to this question a long time ago.

But now, on the verge of breaking through, the answer remained vague.

"Logically speaking, when one's strength and realm reach my level, even if there is no answer in their heart for the moment, there should at least be a general direction to proceed. It is impossible to have no clear idea at all."

"This is because my path is too special. It is completely different from any other cultivator."

The anomaly of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net shattered around him, revealing the magnificent scenery of the Profound Yellow Realm.

"My current strength is almost eighty percent derived from this Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Once I attempt to take the path of transcendence and leave the possibility of the [Primordial] the moment I do, I will immediately sever my connection with the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. My foundation will be gone, like stepping into thin air and falling from a ten-thousand-foot building to a flat surface in an instant."

"To climb again would be no different from starting from scratch. Naturally, it would be extremely difficult."

"This is the downside of borrowing power. And it is only reasonable. After all, a hundred years is enough to show the incredible speed of cultivating from a mortal to a Nameless True Immortal. There is no such thing as a perfect thing in the world."

Li Fan was very clear in his heart.

However, although he said so, he did not give up on finding a solution to the drawback.

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless, what can be used as a boat?"

According to Li Fan's previous thinking and behavior patterns, he would naturally seek the help of others to achieve his own transcendence.

However, the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas was different from before.

To cross it, one could only rely on oneself. It seemed there was no way to take shortcuts, which put Li Fan in a dilemma for a time.

However, Li Fan was not in a hurry.

Although True Transformation was still dormant, his foundation was stable. Before the Primordial was swallowed by Dao Annihilation, he had ample time to think.

Li Fan was exploring the answer for his future, and the cultivators of Profound Yellow were also doing the same.

The step from Nascent Soul to Divinity Transformation was even more difficult than all previous realms combined.

Even Ji Wangxian, who was exploiting his family members to the extreme, even Chen Qiandu, who had vaguely found his own path, even Su Bai, who had outstanding talent.

Facing this chasm, they could not help but feel a glimmer of despair.

Divinity Transformation was like this, what about the subsequent Harmonious Dao?

Even if they successfully achieved Divinity Transformation, how would they take the next step?

As long as the thought arose in the cultivator's heart, it was impossible to avoid being cast a shadow. If one could not emerge from this shadow, they might never be able to progress in their lifetime.

The gap between different realms was so huge, but this was not Li Fan deliberately making things difficult for Profound Yellow cultivators.

It was due to the special circumstances of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

Although the cultivators of Profound Yellow stood above the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm and gained an advantage out of thin air, they were essentially mortals.

From Qi Refining to Harmonious Dao, the entire cultivation process was actually the transformation from mortal to Nameless True Immortal.

The gap between each realm was naturally large and unimaginable.

"There might be thousands of those who rank among the stars, but among these stars, only one in ten thousand can enter the God Conferring List! And among those on the list, only a very few can finally surpass the Four Immortal Gates and rank among the immortals!" Li Fan saw through the potential and upper limit of all Profound Yellow cultivators at a glance.

Without any other serendipitous encounters, most of them would be trapped in realms below Nascent Soul for their entire lives.

Seemingly tragic. However, compared to cultivators outside the Profound Yellow Realm, they were already incredibly fortunate.

At the very least, with the protection of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, they no longer had to worry about the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation.

"When the first Harmonious Dao cultivator is born in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, that will be the time when the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm officially connects with Mountains and Seas. I hope you do not keep me waiting too long."

Li Fan's gaze swept over a few figures below.

After the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net was initially formed, Li Fan also ceased suppressing Su Bai.

Without the suppression, Su Bai's true talent finally began to reveal itself, achieving the eighteenth star of Profound Yellow, the Tianjin Star.

The Nascent Soul star anomaly was precisely the range of one hundred thousand miles around Ningyuan City after its transformation.

All living beings within it were protected by Su Bai and would no longer be troubled by strange creatures.

As for the Transmission of the Law...

It still remained at the initial stage of cultivation.

A hundred years passed, and even the most devout followers of the Transmission of the Law had slowly forgotten it by now.

After all, there had been no news from the Transmission of the Law during these hundred years. Most of the Myriad Immortal Alliance cultivators believed that the Transmission of the Law had already perished in the changes of heaven and earth.

Otherwise, it would be difficult to explain why, in the guise of the Transmission of the Law, they had not yet transformed into a star.

After all, three of the disciples of the Transmission of the Law in the past had already reached the Nascent Soul realm.

They only occasionally remembered the exceptionally brilliant Transmission of the Law Immortal Venerable when they were cultivating.

The cultivation path of New Law cultivators in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was even more difficult.

Nine out of ten were burst by the strange objects and grotto-heavens within their bodies.

A very small number of extremely talented individuals successfully re-mastered them, but when advancing to the next step, they faced almost a dead end.

Extracting the essence of heaven and earth to gain its spirit; sacrificing the soul of heaven and earth to merge with the Dao; reversing the principles of heaven and earth to prove longevity!

After Nascent Soul, there were three major realms. Although New Law cultivators had not yet met the conditions for cultivation in the past, they could at least imagine them in their minds. However, now...

There was not even room for imagination.

During the drastic changes of the universe, many grotto-heavens still existed and underwent transformation and sublimation along with it.

However, the essence of heaven and earth, the soul of heaven and earth, had directly disappeared from the sight of all New Law cultivators.

Without the necessary materials for cultivation, how could they cultivate?

The only thing that could support the New Law cultivators was that these materials had not truly disappeared, but rather their current realm was too low to detect them. Perhaps when their cultivation improved in the future, they would have further opportunities.

However, the reality was not as they wished.

The essence of heaven and earth is the change that heaven and earth will undergo.

The soul of heaven and earth is the one who upholds the Dao.

In the original Profound Yellow Realm, these two were the principles of the natural operation of the Profound Yellow heavens and earth, and they would naturally appear in the world.

But now, above the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao, there was a Creator-Li Fan!

Since the resources of strange objects and grotto-heavens could be continuously regenerated, how could Li Fan, the creator of the Profound Yellow Realm, possibly give away the authority of the Profound Yellow Realm?

Thus, Li Fan hid them.

If the New Law cultivators still followed the original cultivation method, it would truly be a dead end.

Li Fan had no intention of kindly reminding them.

He was more interested in seeing how the Transmission of the Law could change the New Law to make it function correctly within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

After observing carefully for a while, Li Fan discovered that the aura of the Transmission of the Law was fluctuating, showing signs of awakening.

And by probing the mind of the Transmission of the Law, Li Fan found that a violent storm was gathering in their consciousness.

Thunderclouds rolled, all centered around one thought.

"Do not prove Longevity, only prove Harmonious Dao!"

Li Fan stared at these words constantly echoing in the mind of the Transmission of the Law and could not help but narrow his eyes.

"It's a little interesting."

"It seems that he has vaguely sensed my existence as the ruler of this world."

Undoubtedly, the thoughts of the Transmission of the Law were extremely wise.

Not to mention that the foundation of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was the Infinite Sea and the Mountain Above, as well as the Great Dao of Longevity. The principles of Profound Yellow were the principles of Mountains and Seas and Longevity. It was by no means something that cultivators within the Profound Yellow Realm could reverse.

Not to mention that besides this, there was also Li Fan, the helmsman.

To reverse the principles of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was like contending with Li Fan for control of Profound Yellow. Even if an earth-shattering talent were to emerge from the countless beings in the Profound Yellow Realm.

Before they could successfully prove the Dao, Li Fan would decisively control them.

"Cut off one's own spirit to seek life."

"Not bad. Seemingly abandoning the most important step, in reality, by taking a step back, the horizon becomes wider, gaining room for survival."

Li Fan did not spare his praise.

He was even more looking forward to the complete deduction of the Transmission of the Law.

"If my prediction is correct, the original New Law was to solve the problem of cultivators being unable to cultivate. Then the current New Law is to solve the problem of cultivators' cultivation speed being too slow."

"The arrival of the New Law will bring great benefits to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm!"

In the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, all changes were under Li Fan's control. All the thoughts of the beings in Profound Yellow were also under Li Fan's watch.

Therefore, Li Fan could, to some extent, "foresee" the future scene of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

A smile appeared at the corner of his mouth, and Li Fan turned his gaze away with satisfaction.

He thought again about his path of transcendence.

"Sometimes, jumping out of the established framework and thinking from a different perspective might yield miraculous results."

As if sensing something in his heart, Li Fan's consciousness descended once more into that dark starry sky.

Wandering within the boundless Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, he forgot the passage of time.

Until he had personally treaded all the threads nine times.

A flash of spiritual light finally illuminated the surrounding dark starry sky.

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless, what can be used as a boat..."

"I have been desperately searching for the answer before, but I forgot that the boat was already built by me and has always been under my feet!"

"If I leave the Primordial, I will lose the reliance of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Then let's find a way to bring the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm into the Mountains and Seas!"

"The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm is not only my refuge boat for avoiding disaster, but also my boat for crossing!"

With this, Li Fan's mind instantly became clear.

As if he had understood everything, his laughter echoed throughout the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net.

And as his enlightenment occurred, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm also underwent inexplicable changes.

The heavens and earth trembled, and all things roared.

The strong tremors lasted for a full quarter of an hour.

All beings living within it felt a sense of imminent danger.

However, when the tremors subsided, this sense of danger quickly dissipated.

In the heavens and earth, only the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao remained immersed in that sense of fear.

Because it acutely sensed that the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, which originally had a foundation in the [Primordial] possibility, was completely "cutting" itself off from the Primordial.

If the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was originally a house built on the primordial land, then after the "cutting" was completed, it would become a wandering ship.

Although it was more free, it was also more dangerous.

The Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao undoubtedly preferred safety.

But the one who caused all this was Li Fan, the parent of Profound Yellow. Even with ten thousand unwillingness, it could only bear it silently.

Just for self-preservation, it instinctively unleashed various hidden potentials.

As a result, countless changes quietly occurred within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

For example, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm proactively began to differentiate into tentacle-like roots, exploring and rooting towards the surroundings along its foundation in the Mountain Above.

For example, more and more souls of heaven and earth were summoned to the vicinity of the Four Heavenly Gates.
