Although the connection with the Infinite Sea had not been officially opened, they were already preemptively sensing the infinite power, preparing for the formal connection with Mountains and Seas in the future.

For example, in the original Profound Yellow heavens and earth, there were still some residual, wandering immortal artifacts and fragments. In the past, the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao appeared very indifferent. Although it "digested" them proactively, it was only through the natural circulation of heaven and earth, slowly assimilating them.

But now...

Dao souls appeared near these immortal artifacts, collecting and imprisoning them.

Then, they actively "refined" them.

Although for the current Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, these residual immortal artifacts were not even comparable to supplementary medicine.

However, it could, to some extent, indicate the attitude of the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao.

Chapter 1568: Sneaking into the Merchant Immortal Ship

Before the Great Celestial Venerable Immortal Puppet, ripples arose. Amidst the shifting illusions, the image of a white cat could be faintly seen.

It existed for only a moment before leaping towards a certain direction and disappearing without a trace.

Watching the faint white line drifting in the starry sky, Li Fan followed its disappearance into the depths of the Suo Xing Sea.

"The image is somewhat different from Cat Treasure, but the aura and fluctuations are extremely similar. Its disappearance direction is…"

Li Fan stealthily followed Cat Treasure's trail, venturing deeper.

When the Display Character Technique's white line completely vanished, Li Fan had already arrived before a peculiar structure in the starry sky.

It resembled a planet covered in black metallic armor, lying quietly in front of him.

The material of this black metallic armor was unknown, yet it could evade the Great Celestial Venerable Immortal Puppet's divine sense. It had not been detected during the divine sense scan outside the Suo Xing Sea.

Only now, upon closer proximity, could this planet no longer hide its presence.

"Not just the material is special…"

After careful observation, Li Fan discovered the anomaly.

This peculiar creation before him was somewhat similar to the current Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. Its connection to the Primordial possibility had become extremely fragile, as if it could break at any moment and drift outwards, like a lone boat.

"Or perhaps, it is an immortal ship itself."

"Merchant Immortal Ship!" A strange light flashed in Li Fan's eyes as he recognized the origin of this strangely shaped planet.

"Previously, in Qin Zhuang's memories, I obtained information that Cat Treasure was a creation of the Merchant Immortal Ship. Although the Merchant Immortal Ship had long since disappeared after I left the High Wall, according to the memories of relevant personnel in the Suo Xing Sea, the Holy Merchant did possess creations similar to Cat Treasure. Qin Zhuang's memories were not mistaken."

"However, the actual performance of those creations was far inferior to Cat Treasure, which had instantly captured the Starving Immortal. They were barely enough to deal with ordinary True Immortals. Qin Zhuang's low cultivation level prevented him from distinguishing the differences."

"I initially thought it was merely a coincidence. The Holy Merchant created objects similar in appearance to Cat Treasure. Now it seems…"

Li Fan became intrigued.

He sent out a sliver of his consciousness, slowly approaching the Merchant Immortal Ship before him.

Wrapped in black metallic armor, the Merchant Immortal Ship seemed to exist in a gap between reality and illusion.

Even though his divine sense reached its location, it could not establish contact, as if this black planet were merely an illusion.

However, such a camouflage and defensive measure could not stump Li Fan.

"As long as it has not detached from the 'Primordial' possibility and leaped into the Mountains and Seas, it must be connected to the surrounding Great Daos."

Before Li Fan's eyes, the web of Great Daos suddenly appeared.

All beings in the world were within this net.

Although the Merchant Immortal Ship's contact with the net was extremely tenuous, like a dragonfly skimming water, with Li Fan's understanding of the Primordial Great Daos, he could pinpoint the subtle distortions in the Great Dao remnants caused by the Merchant Immortal Ship's lingering connections.

Following these clues, Li Fan soon located the true whereabouts of the Merchant Immortal Ship within the Primordial.

Strangely, it didn't exist solely in the Suo Xing Sea.

Instead, it was like countless scattered starlight, existing simultaneously in dozens of different star systems!

"The Merchant Immortal Ship is in a state of semi-separation from the Primordial, using dozens of support points as connections."

"And this black planet before me is one of the Merchant Immortal Ship's support points."

"This structure is even more rational than the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's flying ship form. When preparing to detach from the Primordial and leap into the Mountains and Seas, it can leverage these support points to facilitate its departure from the Primordial and search for other safe havens within the Mountains and Seas." Li Fan observed, his eyes lighting up.

He committed this peculiar structure to memory.

In the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao sensed Li Fan's will and obediently cooperated, undergoing corresponding evolutions. And in the shadows, the Dao Seed Worm was also quietly gathering towards the newly formed tendrils of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, undertaking further modifications.

The changes in heaven and earth were often immensely slow, requiring millions or even billions of years.

But when guided by a higher will and supported by sufficient energy, its evolution could be even faster than that of a single life form.

Not to mention the new round of drastic changes within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

After the Great Celestial Venerable Immortal Puppet deciphered the hidden secret of the Merchant Immortal Ship, it then attempted to send the wisp of differentiated consciousness into the black planet.

The black metal covering the exterior of the Merchant Immortal Ship seemed to possess a strong suppressive effect on divine sense. Even though the wisp of divine sense differentiated by Li Fan was close to True Immortal strength, it was still almost weakened to the point of being unable to sustain its existence.

Fortunately, its core was special, based on the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net. This allowed it to finally break through the outermost defenses of the Merchant Immortal Ship.

"Not only suppressing divine sense."

"Its physical defense capabilities are also formidable. At the very least, any strength below True Immortal level cannot inflict any damage upon it."

"Taking True Immortals as the benchmark…"

Li Fan had already understood that all the defensive measures set up by the Merchant Immortal Ship before him were designed with [Immortals] as hypothetical enemies.

"This black metal, capable of partially repelling Immortals, does not seem to be from the Primordial."

"At the very least, in the remaining starscape of the Primordial, only the Merchant Immortal Ship possesses this material now."

Although Li Fan had not traversed the entire Primordial, relying on the [Supreme Dao Scripture] left by the Dao Inscribing Immortal, he had a relatively accurate grasp of the remaining Great Daos in the Primordial.

The Dao principles involved in this strange black metal were not within the scope of the Supreme Dao Scripture!

"From another possibility."

Coupled with the fact that Cat Treasure, which had appeared earlier, later vanished into the Merchant Immortal Ship, Li Fan already had a vague guess in his heart.

However, it still needed to be confirmed.

The differentiated consciousness of the Great Celestial Venerable Immortal Puppet passed through the black metal defenses, and the vision suddenly became bright.

Brilliant stars constantly shifted and flowed, as if lost in an endless starry sky, making it difficult to discern direction.

Seeing this, Li Fan couldn't help but chuckle, "This formation is like showing off before Chibi."

Almost instantly, Li Fan identified the correct path among the innumerable stars and broke through the defensive formation.

The final layer of defense that appeared next surprised Li Fan.

A narrow and dark corridor stretched straight into the distance.

At the end of the corridor, a stooped figure seemed to be standing.

Li Fan surveyed the surroundings: "Either destroy this corridor and charge directly into the Merchant Immortal Ship, or I can only proceed along the corridor…"

If his true self had come, he could probably have destroyed the Merchant Immortal Ship with ease.

But the wisp of consciousness differentiated at this moment did not possess such power.

Therefore, he concealed himself as much as possible and quietly traversed the corridor.

The corridor itself held no other profound illusions. Soon, Li Fan reached the end of the corridor and saw the figure guarding the end of the corridor.

Beardless and hairless, appearing extremely old. Deep wrinkles covered his face like ravines, looking somewhat horrifying. The old man sat on a yellowish-brown wooden chair, hunched over, calmly staring at the corridor ahead.

Only his eyes seemed to retain vitality, vigilantly monitoring the surroundings.

Li Fan was unsure if the elder had discovered him.

Because the elder's eyes clearly lingered on Li Fan's location several times.

But for some reason, after only pausing for a moment, there were no agitated actions. He then turned his gaze elsewhere as if he hadn't seen anything.

Li Fan's consciousness drifted past the elder, and he clearly sensed the elder let out a sigh of relief.

"This person is rather interesting."

Thinking this, he passed through the three layers of defense and finally entered the Merchant Immortal Ship.

What he saw before him caused him to be slightly stunned.

It was a vast white space, filled with numerous humanoid puppets suspended in the air.

These puppets were all made of some kind of metal. Although they had no spiritual energy fluctuations, Li Fan could faintly sense their "heaviness."

"In terms of combat power alone, they are not weaker than ordinary Harmonious Dao cultivators."

"And…"

Li Fan could perceive that these humanoid puppets were scanning this vast white space non-stop. Besides the corridor Li Fan came from, there were a total of eighty-four other corridors, seemingly connecting to other star systems.

"These humanoid puppets likely share consciousness and have a special material. Individually, they are weak, but in large numbers, they could pose some trouble to ordinary True Immortals."

But Li Fan was no ordinary True Immortal.

Moving so openly under the watch of countless humanoid puppets, he broke through the blockade.

After leaving the white space, he officially entered the interior of the Merchant Immortal Ship.

Unlike the desolate scene Li Fan saw in the Profound Immortal Ship,

The interior of the Merchant Immortal Ship was teeming with vitality.

But this so-called vitality, in Li Fan's eyes, was somewhat bizarre.

Because among the people of the Merchant Immortal Ship he saw, more or less, they had lost some of their "living being" characteristics. A part of their body had been replaced by a strange blue substance.

This blue substance was neither like metal nor wood. It was as if it were purely made of radiance, possessing its own rhythm, emitting fluctuations rhythmically.

All the people of the Merchant Immortal Ship no longer communicated verbally.

As the blue radiance flickered, communication was completed. The efficiency of communication was extremely fast, and it seemed to have thus avoided deception and lies.

Each inhabitant of the Merchant Immortal Ship seemed to have an important task, hurrying with solemn expressions.

Li Fan followed an inhabitant whose blue transformation was most thorough into a crystalline building.

After passing through multiple verifications, this person seemed to have entered a space unique to himself.

The blue radiance flickered non-stop.

There were no outsiders. The fluctuations of the blue radiance were several times stronger than in public.

Li Fan could therefore roughly sense the content of his thoughts.

"In ten days, the parts for the 'Chen Yi' model must be submitted."

"But we are still far from the requirements from above."

As this person's thoughts shifted, hundreds of thousands of slightly different components appeared out of thin air before them.

Although their shapes varied subtly, they shared a common general form.

Li Fan observed for a long time but could not guess their specific use.

This blue-clothed merchant inhabitant, with unwavering focus, tested each of the hundreds of thousands of components.

Then, shaking his head slightly and sighing.

He waved his hand again, generating hundreds of thousands of other shaped components.

Conducting another round of testing.

Li Fan did not know how time was measured within the Merchant Immortal Ship. However, it was evident that this blue-clothed inhabitant was becoming increasingly anxious.

"Forget it, let's try it first."

He took a deep breath, dispelling all other components except one.

"Level Three Immortal Research, Sun Shengshen, applying for test of Chen Yi, component 18762." His head flashed with blue radiance.

Shortly after, it seemed his application was accepted.

Before him, a phantom appeared out of thin air.

Its image was that of a lifelike cat!

Sun Shengshen implanted the component he had created into the Cat Treasure phantom before him.

The Cat Treasure image enlarged continuously.

In an instant, it magnified a quadrillion times. After a moment, on a macroscopic level, the entire Cat Treasure could no longer be seen, just a landscape of countless stacked components.

And within it, there was a vacant spot glowing with blue light.

Sun Shengshen placed the component he had created into it.

The scene instantly retracted from the extremely minute details back to normal.

The Cat Treasure seemed to come alive.

"Testing first function, replication ability."

In the void, before Cat Treasure, a tattered piece of clothing appeared.

Although dilapidated, Li Fan keenly sensed residual array imprints on the clothing, indicating it was likely once a magical treasure.

A blue light beam shot out from Cat Treasure's eyes, locking onto the tattered clothing.

Three breaths later, the light beam shifted to another blank area.

A similar creation was slowly generated within.

Sun Shengshen watched nervously as the two pieces of clothing floated up and then instantly disintegrated into countless invisible particles.

Both magical treasures disappeared, leaving only a symbol.

Below the symbol, there was a downward-pointing arrow.

Although Li Fan had never encountered such a symbol before, like the True Immortal Seal Scripts, the moment he saw the symbol, he understood its meaning.

It represented the number 0.0028.

The moment the symbol appeared, Sun Shengshen was struck as if by lightning, his face turning ashen.

The blue light on his forehead weakened considerably, seemingly ready to extinguish at any moment.

After a long while, Sun Shengshen finally recovered.

Gritting his teeth, he began the second test.

"Evolution."

In the void, where the tattered clothing had appeared before. This time, a white snake appeared.

Cat Treasure's eyes again emitted light, locking onto the white snake.

Within the light beam, the white snake was frozen as if encased in ice.

And when the light beam receded, the white snake let out a sharp cry, its body writhing incessantly, seemingly in great pain.

And at its forehead, it seemed horns were about to emerge from its flesh. Its scales all over its body also became more divine.

The white snake transforming into a dragon lasted for thirty breaths.

After thirty breaths, the white dragon was again frozen still.

Similar to the clothing before, it was decomposed into countless fine particles of light.

A moment later, a symbol appeared before Sun Shengshen.

This time, the arrow next to the symbol pointed upwards.

Sun Shengshen couldn't help but breathe a sigh of relief.

Li Fan clearly saw that this symbol represented the number 0.003.

"Next is the final test."

"Spirit Transformation."

Cat Treasure's eyes again emitted blue radiance.

But this time, the light locked onto Sun Shengshen himself!

Chapter 1569: Seeing Cat Treasure in the Immortal Ship

The moment he was engulfed by the blue light, as if suddenly realizing something, Sun Shengshen's face instantly turned extremely pale. It was as if something terrifying was about to happen to him.

The light beam stayed on him for three breaths before shifting to an adjacent area.

The blue light surged like tides, and after a while, a human figure emerged from within.

Its physique, appearance, and even facial expression were exactly the same as Sun Shengshen's!

The blue light locked onto the new and old Sun Shengshen. Similar to the previous two test procedures, another symbol materialized in the void.

Representing 0.00041.

Next to the symbol, there was an upward-pointing arrow.

The moment the arrow appeared, the two Sun Shengshens displayed different expressions on their faces.

The original Sun Shengshen's face was paper-white, his eyes filled with despair.

While the newly born Sun Shengshen secretly breathed a sigh of relief, a glint of luck flashing in his eyes.

Time seemed to freeze.

The original Sun Shengshen, under the blue illumination, instantly disintegrated into countless invisible particles and vanished.

While the newly born Sun Shengshen replaced him, taking over his work.

Li Fan keenly observed that a small portion of these particles attached themselves to this newly born Sun Shengshen.

He seemed to have no memory of the previous experimental cycle. After standing blankly for a moment, the blue light on his head began to glow, displaying the same words: "In ten days, the parts for the 'Chen Yi' model must be submitted. But we are still far from the requirements from above."

The process then repeated like a loop.

Thinking, designing new components, then testing.

"Level Three Immortal Research, Sun Shengshen, applying for test of Chen Yi, component 18762."

However, in this experiment, the replica created by Cat Treasure, after testing, displayed a symbol representing 0.00036, with a downward-pointing arrow next to it.

Thus, this Sun Shengshen was spared.

"The efficiency of Spirit Transformation and replication has actually decreased so much. Where is the problem?"

Sun Shengshen looked at his replica, and the blue light attached to his head erupted violently. The light was like a blade, decomposing the replica, and then observing it inch by inch.

After the blue light subsided, Sun Shengshen began designing the next round of components.

WWW＿＿￠〇 Li Fan spent a full half-year in this space, witnessing over thirty cycles.

Sun Shengshen's life seemed to consist only of designing and experimenting. Apart from scheduled outdoor breaks and interactions with other merchant inhabitants, all other time was spent in this repetitive cycle.

And he remained completely unaware of his cyclical fate, only realizing it at the last moment before being destroyed by the blue light beam each time.

But this did not affect the more capable replicas taking his place and conducting the next round of design experiments.

"The three tests directly correspond to Cat Treasure's three exhibited abilities: 'Item Replication, Living Being Mimicry, Marrow Cleansing and Bone Changing.'"

"Sun Shengshen is responsible for only one of Cat Treasure's countless components. The entire Merchant Immortal Ship likely has countless individuals like Sun Shengshen."

"By making minor improvements to each component, the overall capability of the crafted Cat Treasure is continuously advanced. The ultimate goal…"

"To approach or even reach the true Cat Treasure!"

Thinking of this, Li Fan became even more interested in the lord of the Holy Merchant.

It was a pity that although everyone in the Merchant Immortal Ship seemed to communicate through thoughts and be equal, this was clearly only an appearance.

Li Fan had been lurking in the Merchant Immortal Ship for a full half-year. Besides monitoring Sun Shengshen daily, he had also explored other areas. He encountered all merchant ship inhabitants who were like Sun Shengshen, locked in repetitive labor.

As for those truly responsible for the operational order of the Merchant Immortal Ship, or those who shaped this workflow, Li Fan had not seen any of them.

It seemed that although they were all on the Merchant Immortal Ship, these two groups lived in different worlds.

"These people are quite good at hiding."

After searching fruitlessly, Li Fan finally turned his attention to the ubiquitous Cat Treasure creations within the Merchant Immortal Ship.

"Seemingly, each cyclical laborer's space contains a Cat Treasure, used for experimental participation at any time. In reality, all these Cat Treasure creations are the same one."

Returning to Sun Shengshen's location, when another experimental cycle began and the Cat Treasure phantom fully manifested, Li Fan's consciousness subtly attempted to infiltrate it.

"Since it can effectively display three major functions, it means that even if Cat Treasure's true body is not in this world, it must have a connection."

Li Fan's infiltration in this step was extremely cautious.

Even though the Cat Treasure creation on the immortal ship was far inferior to the real Cat Treasure, it had already possessed all of Cat Treasure's characteristics. The real Cat Treasure could instantly suppress the Starving Immortal, while this imitation on the immortal ship could contend with ordinary True Immortals. It should not be underestimated.

Moreover, Li Fan was not here in person, but only a wisp of consciousness from the Great Celestial Venerable Immortal Puppet.

If exposed, it would alarm the Merchant Immortal Ship, which would be detrimental.

Li Fan's guess was correct.

The Cat Treasure creation before him did indeed have a subtle, almost imperceptible connection with the real body, but only at the moment Cat Treasure's functions were activated.

At other times, even though the Cat Treasure image was constantly displayed, it was merely a simple phantom projection.

The connection between Cat Treasure's manifested power and its true body was fleeting. However, Li Fan accurately captured it each time.

Instead of rushing into the connection immediately, he patiently witnessed thousands of descents and disappearances. After ensuring there were no sudden changes or potential traps, Li Fan followed the power of Cat Treasure's descent and disappearance, stealthily infiltrating its true body's location.

A space of darkness.

Gazing into the distance, one could vaguely see the transparent boundary of this space, like glass.

An orange cat lay quietly in the void, deep in slumber.

Ninety-nine blue chains completely bound the cat.

Vaguely visible, countless flowing symbols flowed from the orange cat towards the other end of the chains extending into the void.

And beside this slumbering black cat, another cat sat quietly.

This cat's appearance was identical to the Cat Treasure creation on the Merchant Immortal Ship.

It stared intently at its "fellow," occasionally drawing closer to sniff and observe. However, it seemed afraid of waking the orange cat, not daring to get too close, maintaining a distance.

Li Fan had once meticulously carved countless wooden statues of Cat Treasure to overcome his fear of Cat Treasure, then burned them all.

This imprisoned orange cat, although its appearance was extremely similar to Cat Treasure, almost identical, Li Fan could tell the subtle difference between the two by intuition.

"It looks very similar, yet it's not."

Li Fan felt slightly relieved.

Neither the orange cat nor the immortal ship cat seemed to have detected Li Fan's infiltration.

They continued their original actions.

Periodically, the immortal ship cat would attempt to learn the sleeping posture of the orange cat. Not only its form but also its appearance and even its expression began to change towards the other.

But for some reason, this transformation and learning could not last long. Almost every time, it only lasted for about ten breaths before the immortal ship cat returned to its original state.

However, it showed no signs of giving up, persistently learning.

Li Fan noticed that each change made by the immortal ship cat was closer than before.

"This should be the result of the efforts of countless Sun Shengshens."

"But this cat…"

Li Fan felt a strange sensation.

This immortal ship cat, although a replica of the true Cat Treasure, inexplicably had eyes that seemed more intelligent than the real Cat Treasure.

Like…

A human!

And the change that occurred with the immortal ship cat soon afterward completely verified Li Fan's guess.

After another round of learning and transformation, seemingly feeling a bit tired.

The immortal ship cat yawned, and then transformed from a cat back into a human form!

"I've gotten used to staying in a cat's body, so it's a bit uncomfortable in human form,"

said a refined youth who looked about fifteen or sixteen, with a hint of self-mockery.

As the youth resumed human form, rows of blue figures appeared one after another.

"Master!" The blue figures all bowed respectfully to the youth.

The youth merely nodded slightly, his expression indifferent.

"Is there any news from that side?" the youth asked.

"The last contact was more than half a year ago. They promised to send another one, but we haven't seen it. And there has been no further response from their end," replied one of the blue figures.

The youth frowned slightly, one ear instantly transforming into a cat ear. After twitching slightly, the youth chuckled, "You don't need to speculate. It was sent. However, some problems occurred when it arrived here, and it broke free. It must be hiding somewhere on the ship."

The figures around him flashed with blue light, seemingly astonished.

The youth waved his hand dismissively, smiling, "Don't worry. With [Loquat] here, the newly arrived one won't escape. It's probably hiding somewhere on the ship."

The blue figures were greatly shocked and repeatedly said, "We have failed in our duty, please punish us, Master."

"Heaven-Stealing Cat is extraordinary. Even if it appeared openly before you, you might not have noticed it. If it wanted to hide, how could you possibly discover it? What fault is yours?" the youth said calmly.

"If Heaven-Stealing Cat did not possess such power, why would I go to such lengths, even risking myself to learn from it?"

The blue figures around looked ashamed and lowered their heads.

The youth himself seemed unconcerned, "Let's go, accompany me to meet this newcomer."

With a wave of his hand, a rift instantly appeared in the space.

The youth stepped out, followed by the others.

Li Fan also quietly attached himself to one of the blue figures and left.

However, before leaving, Li Fan seemed to sense that the imprisoned orange cat named Loquat trembled slightly.

"It's not an illusion."

"Interesting," Li Fan mused inwardly.

The youth led the group to a completely different area from where Sun Shengshens were located below.

Thousands of buildings, like stars, floated in the starry sky.

From a distance, the style of these buildings resembled that of the Profound Immortal Ship.

The beings living within had partially blue bodies, but the majority were still human in appearance.

The moment the youth appeared in the starry sky, they all perceived it.

"Greetings, Holy Master!"

They shouted in unison, bowing their heads.

"Since you have the guts to come here, why hide?" the youth sneered, speaking to a lush green tree floating in the starry sky.

Li Fan recognized that, unlike the Ruomu tree, this tree did not contain life force but death aura. However, when the death aura condensed to its extreme, it presented an appearance of vibrant life.

As the youth spoke, the leaves rustled.

A moment later, a black and white cat jumped down from the top of the large tree.

The black and white cat sniffed the air, seemingly sensing something. It let out a low growl towards the youth, then crouched low, preparing to pounce.

The youth instantly transformed into the appearance of the imprisoned orange cat.

The black and white cat was momentarily stunned by this.

"Attack!"

The change lasted only an instant before the youth reverted to human form.

And his surrounding blue figures, without needing his instruction, had already begun their attack in unison, even before he spoke.

A tattered garment, like a real cultivator, unleashed streaks of black lines. Although most of the black lines were absorbed and assimilated by the black and white cat the moment they approached, a small portion survived. They landed on the black and white cat, weaving into clothes.

A broken suona played a high-pitched note, drowning out all of Cat Treasure's sounds. But it suppressed far more than just sound. The light beams emitted from the black and white cat's eyes dimmed amidst the suona's melody.

A battered wooden staff, seemingly on the verge of breaking, unleashed countless transparent figures when swung. These figures all bore expressions of pity. Although they had lost their eyes, they precisely targeted the enemy. Fearlessly, they launched kamikaze attacks.

An ordinary-looking stone, as if it could appear in any river, was thrown. Although not aimed at the black and white cat's location when thrown, it always landed precisely on the black and white cat's head.

…

The merchant ship inhabitants unleashed their full might.

They used no divine abilities or spells, relying entirely on strange and peculiar artifacts.

But under the siege of these strange artifacts, the black and white cat was utterly unable to retaliate, passively taking blows. Even its meows were suppressed by the suona.

This bizarre scene shocked Li Fan, who was observing in secret.

"These objects…"

"They are imbued with Great Daos that I have rarely seen. They are all from other possibilities."

"And they are not weak!"

Li Fan instinctively became more cautious, hiding himself further.

He recalled the conversation between the Holy Merchant Lord and the merchant inhabitants earlier.

"The Merchant Immortal Ship likely has assistance from other possibilities?"

"Cat Treasure is suspected to be one of the Heaven-Stealing Cats. The opposing side was able to capture and send it here, so their strength must not be underestimated. However, why did they choose to help the Merchant Immortal Ship? What is their motive?"

Li Fan thought about this.

Chapter 1570: Immortal Corpse Restoration Point

The Cat Treasure at this time was clearly much weaker than the one Li Fan had encountered in his reincarnation cycles.

Even though the various artifacts wielded by the Merchant Immortal Ship inhabitants were extraordinary, with the power it displayed in leaping up and suppressing the Starving Immortal, it should not have been in such dire straits.

Being beaten by the Merchant Immortal Ship inhabitants, the black and white cat's situation seemed increasingly dire. However, Li Fan discovered that the black and white cat, while seemingly battered, had not actually sustained any real injuries.

And the youth called the [Holy Master], apart from transforming into an orange cat at the beginning, had not made any other moves. He merely watched the unfolding events.

"The attacks from the Merchant Immortal Ship inhabitants are fierce, but they are ultimately inconsequential for capturing Cat Treasure. The key likely lies with him." Li Fan thought, recalling the blue chains that suppressed the orange cat.

Li Fan's intuition had always been accurate.

After being beaten for a period, the black and white cat, though in pain, surprisingly adapted to the artifact attacks from the Merchant Immortal Ship inhabitants. Its low growls gradually became comparable to the suona's drumming. Its fur began to stand on end. Its eyes fixed on the merchant ship inhabitants who were beating it, glints of ferocity flashing within.

Just as the situation was about to turn, the Holy Merchant Lord finally made a move.

And his method of attack was quite peculiar.

He transformed into a cat again, but this time not the orange cat used for luring, but a phantom cat composed purely of blue light. The blue light rippled and shimmered, ethereally dreamlike. Its size was also hundreds of times that of a normal Cat Treasure.

"Meow~"

With a low meow, the blue phantom exploded into billions of fine threads, all surging towards the black and white cat.

Unlike facing the previous attacks, the black and white cat now clearly sensed fear. Its fur bristled, its back arched. It let out sharp explosions, repelling all incoming attacks.

With a fierce swipe of its claws towards a nearby spot, the dead aura-condensed great tree it had hidden behind earlier was instantly shattered. As if absorbed by it, the blackness on the black and white cat's body intensified.

Simultaneously, the black and white cat's tail swept towards the distance.

Li Fan vaguely saw that at least tens of thousands of Holy Merchant inhabitants instantly lost all signs of life, absorbed by the black and white cat.

In an instant, after absorbing a large amount of life and death aura, the black and white cat's pupils turned black and white. The black and white cat flew gracefully, like a monk's kasaya. The black and white cat then, like a human, sat cross-legged in the void of the battlefield.

With a pointed finger towards the front,

The next moment, as if infinite life and death ensued, boundless life and death aura surged from within the black and white cat. Or rather, this single gesture stirred the very essence of life and death that already existed in the world, completely disrupting it.

The Great Dao of Life and Death was the foundation of all things' existence and development. At this moment, its disturbance was like the sudden appearance of a storm, distorting the life and death of all things.

The various artifacts were scattered by the storm. The billions of blue threads were forced back to their original forms.

And the black and white cat remained motionless at the center of the storm.

Watching as the living perished and the dead vanished within the storm.

The blue figures of the Merchant Immortal Ship, although having a special life form, still belonged within the category of [living beings]. Caught off guard, they were swept away by the storm and perished.

Only the Holy Merchant Lord, transformed into a blue light cat, survived.

The situation had dramatically reversed, yet the blue light cat's face showed no sign of panic. Even as the storm of life and death threatened to spread outwards and engulf this entire starry sky.

Indifferently watching the black and white cat in the center of the storm, the Holy Merchant Lord, transformed into blue light, suddenly expanded a hundredfold. Covering the entire area of the life and death storm.

Within the storm, strands of blue light flickered incessantly like lightning. They were not annihilated within the storm of life and death but grew stronger with the passage of time.

Slowly dyeing the chaotic region blue.

The storm of life and death continued to spread outwards, forcing Li Fan's hidden consciousness to retreat further and further.

"This divine ability has some Cat Treasure characteristics."

"An attack at the Great Dao level, shaking the foundation of order. If allowed to spread without restraint, it could even devour an entire possibility…"

The black and white storm of life and death swept across almost the entire starry sky.

Finally, the once vibrant Merchant Immortal Ship had turned into a dead land.

Only the life auras of more than a hundred beings survived this calamity.

But the countless dense blue threads covering the area like a net, and the black and white cat in the center, tightly bound and slumbering, indicated the victor of this battle.

The storm subsided, and the blue threads slowly retracted.

The black and white cat met the same fate as the orange cat, being suppressed and imprisoned.

The young Holy Merchant Lord resumed his human form, looking at the now silent and dead starry sky without any emotional fluctuation.

The next moment, a change occurred.

A strange fluctuation suddenly descended, sweeping across the entire space.

Then, the beings who had disappeared and perished all returned to their original states.

Within mere moments, life reappeared in this starry sky!

It was only then that the Holy Merchant Lord's face showed a faint smile.

"This is…"

Li Fan, witnessing the drastic changes, felt a tremor in his heart.

Because this scene was overwhelmingly familiar.

"It's very much like [True Transformation]."

"But there's no aura of the change between true and false."

"That fluctuation just now, it came from…"

Li Fan looked up towards the location above this space.

The Holy Merchant Lord and the resurrected inhabitants of the immortal ship began to examine their spoils.

However, Li Fan did not follow them back. Instead, he quietly flew towards the location where he had sensed the fluctuation.

Although not directly above the spatial structure, Li Fan, with his extremely keen perception, successfully found the source of the fluctuation.

A bone-white skeleton lay tilted, apparently dead.

The direction its hollow eye sockets gazed was towards the Merchant Immortal Ship below.

From this skeleton, Li Fan felt a faint sense of danger.

He did not approach, merely observing from a distance.

With his vast experience, he could not discern the foundation of the Great Dao contained within this skeleton for the moment.

But undoubtedly, it was this skeleton that had "restored" the immortal ship in an instant.

"The change between true and false is the creation of something from nothing. This Dao, however, restores things to their original state."

"Even under the change between true and false, the status of this Dao is extremely high. More importantly, I can sense that it is not something external, but a Dao inherent in the [Primordial]."

"And it is actually controlled by the Merchant Immortal Ship?"

"Judging by its aura, it seems to have been here for a long time."

Li Fan recalled Xuan Shang Immortal Ship's description from Jian Dao Sheng.

"Xuan Shang Immortal Ship escaped from an experimental field guarded by Immortal Realm observers."

"As an NPC, escaping the control of the Immortal Realm is already enough to explain their extraordinary nature."

"It seems that Xuan Immortal Ship, as the losing side in a schism, has far inferior foundations compared to Merchant Immortal Ship. It's just that they are unaware of it."

Chapter 1571: Undying and Unkillable

Li Fan possessed the Supreme Dao Scripture, and theoretically, all existing Dao information in the Primordial was within his grasp. However, the Dao principles condensed by the skeletal remains before him, like the Dao of Inscription, were not present within it!

"Understanding this Dao will allow my grasp of the transformation between True and False to reach a higher level," Li Fan immediately felt a premonition.

However, he did not rashly attempt to seize it.

This immortal skeletal remains must be extremely important to the Merchant Immortal Ship. Yet, there were no defenses whatsoever around the skeletal remains. Even the blue light power of the Holy Merchant Lord did not appear.

"This can only mean that the power of the skeletal remains itself already exceeds the sum of all defensive forces the Merchant Immortal Ship can wield. There is no need for defenses." The faint sense of crisis lingering in his heart never subsided.

Li Fan stared intently for a long time, unable to determine whether the skeletal remains before him were alive or dead.

After pondering for a moment, Li Fan finally made up his mind.

In this situation, the Great Celestial Venerable Immortal Puppet could no longer handle it. He had to act personally!

"For safety's sake, I will not easily step outside the High Wall. But I can still send out the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net."

With a flicker of Li Fan's intention, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm quietly trembled. The invisible great net covering it began to penetrate and extend outwards.

Li Fan was no stranger to the Suo Xing Sea beyond the High Wall. In his previous life, he had even jointly established the Suo Xing Sea – High Wall system with Cheng Dao. Especially at this current point in time, the Suo Xing Sea Dao Net had not yet been established. Therefore, the covert erosion by the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net proceeded exceptionally smoothly.

However, after all, this starry sky was still in the chaotic era where True Immortals and cultivators coexisted. The further away from the High Wall, the weaker the support from the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, and the easier it was to be detected. Li Fan did not expand blindly, focusing only on the location of the Merchant Immortal Ship.

According to his observations during his stealthy infiltration, the entrance passage of the Merchant Immortal Ship in the Suo Xing Sea changed periodically. However, perhaps because the Merchant Immortal Ship had recently expended most of its energy in capturing and studying the black and white cat, this entrance Li Fan had discovered showed no signs of changing.

The tendrils branched out from the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net thus smoothly infiltrated.

It is worth mentioning that the old man guarding the entrance to the passage seemed to have perceived the arrival of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net. There were subtle changes in his expression, but as before, he ultimately chose to act as if nothing had happened.

"This person is quite interesting."

Li Fan did not entangle with him. The Myriad Phenomena Dao Net extended all the way, merging with the differentiated consciousness.

A phantom image of Li Fan slowly took shape within the tendrils of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net as it writhed.

"No matter how high the Dao's status, it cannot escape the fate of the merging of Mountains and Seas."

Li Fan gazed at the immortal skeletal remains before him. As his gaze fell upon it, the newly formed Ink Slaughter, like fierce wolves and tigers, rapidly approached.

Having been nurtured for a hundred years within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm and infused with the rhythm of the Great Dao of Longevity, the newly formed Ink Slaughter materialized in the world for the first time. Even Li Fan himself did not fully know its power.

The black dots of Ink Slaughter, like surging tides, heavily enveloped the reclining immortal skeletal remains.

Li Fan then manipulated the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net to seal off the surrounding space, ensuring that even if there was a violent upheaval here, the Merchant Immortal Ship would not be able to detect it immediately.

The Myriad Phenomena Dao Net acted like a mirror, reflecting everything around it.

Li Fan keenly sensed that this immortal skeletal remains had a strand of connection with the outside world.

But it was merely one strand of connection.

"It seems that the Merchant Immortal Ship's utilization of this skeletal remains is not very high. Perhaps they merely mechanically trigger its Dao principles."

As Li Fan pondered, the torrent of Ink Slaughter had already completely consumed the reclining immortal skeletal remains.

"Hmm?" Li Fan felt a moment of astonishment.

In his imagination, even the newly formed Ink Slaughter, no matter how powerful, should not have been so utterly defenseless against this immortal skeletal remains. Given its ability to constantly reverse and restore, it should have at least held out for some time.

"Why is this so?"

Li Fan frowned and recalled the newly formed Ink Slaughter.

Where the reclining immortal skeletal remains had been was indeed completely empty. The Ink Slaughter should have devoured the skeletal remains.

But strangely, as if it had swallowed air, the Ink Slaughter showed no change, as if it had not swallowed anything.

"The newly formed Ink Slaughter can not only devour and annihilate all Great Daos, but it can also revert the devoured Great Daos, turning them into materials for weaving the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net."

Li Fan gently stroked the constantly shifting ink-colored mass beside him, confirming that this ability of Ink Slaughter had not disappeared.

"So..."

Realizing something, Li Fan refocused his gaze on the spot where the reclining immortal skeletal remains had vanished.

He began to count the time in his heart.

Ninety-nine breaths later, without any warning, the skeletal remains that had been devoured by Ink Slaughter reappeared in the area.

It was still reclining quietly. Only this time, the hollow eyes of its skull were not looking at the Merchant Immortal Ship below.

But at Li Fan!

Sensing the sudden chill in Li Fan's heart, the Ink Slaughter beside him spontaneously surged forward, guarding Li Fan.

Extremely vigilant, but after a long time, Li Fan did not receive the anticipated counterattack.

After observing for a while longer and confirming that this bizarre immortal skeletal remains posed no threat, Li Fan once again released the Ink Slaughter. He directed it towards the skeletal remains.

The result was the same.

The skeletal remains were devoured without any resistance.

But after ninety-nine breaths, it reappeared out of thin air. Its eyes were still locked onto Li Fan.

Li Fan snorted coldly and tried again.

This time, the Ink Slaughter clouds persistently covered the area where the skeletal remains were, and did not withdraw even after the skeletal remains disappeared.

As the ninety-nine breaths approached, Li Fan held his breath, carefully observing the changes within the Ink Slaughter clouds.

In the area of Ink Slaughter, the skeletal remains did not appear.

But Li Fan inexplicably had a bad feeling.

Suddenly turning around, he discovered that the immortal skeletal remains had, at some unknown point, appeared beside him.

Its posture had changed, no longer reclining but sitting up, cross-legged.

Its skeletal right palm supported its head, as if it were looking at Li Fan with interest!

Li Fan instinctively retreated.

He stopped only after reaching a safe distance in his mind.

The immortal skeletal remains did not stop him; its hollow eyes calmly observed Li Fan.

Li Fan could now finally confirm that the skeletal remains before him was alive!

Or rather, it was in a peculiar, incomprehensible state that could not simply be measured by life or death.

"Greetings, senior!"

Li Fan shamelessly cupped his hands slightly in greeting, completely ignoring his previous brazen attack.

The immortal skeletal remains naturally showed no reaction, appearing as just a mere skeleton.

The scene suddenly fell into a static stalemate.

Li Fan believed that if he retreated now, the immortal skeletal remains would not stop him. But to leave like this would truly be like returning empty-handed from a treasure mountain.

"Since there is no immediate threat, let's test it further."

Li Fan decided to disregard the changes in the immortal skeletal remains and repeatedly drove the newly formed Ink Slaughter clouds to engulf it. Then, again and again, he watched the skeletal remains regenerate in the void.

"Ink Slaughter is a simulation of the calamity of merging Mountains and Seas. Yet this skeletal remains can repeatedly recover, ignoring the power of Ink Slaughter. How is this achieved?"

Even after observing the process of the immortal skeletal remains' reappearance hundreds of times, Li Fan could not find an answer.

"It completely defies common sense."

Li Fan even began to wonder if the newly formed Ink Slaughter had weakened.

But the facts were before him. No matter how inconceivable, there must be a principle behind it.

"Theoretically, Ink Slaughter can devour all Great Daos in the mortal world."

"However, there is one Dao that can ignore Ink Slaughter..."

Chapter 1572: Eternal Eternal Transformation Dao

Li Fan felt increasingly bewildered.

After all, [Ink Slaughter] was the "answer" that the people of the Immortal Realm had placed their hopes on to counter the tribulation of Mountains and Seas merging. Ever since Li Fan had coincidentally recreated the power of the Ink Slaughter Immortal Soul, it had been almost unfailingly effective and invincible.

Yet now, this skeleton hidden within the Merchant Immortal Ship could ignore the encroachment of Ink Slaughter!

If Li Fan could grudgingly accept its ability to resist Ink Slaughter during a stalemate, the current situation, which was an almost one-sided suppression, was utterly incomprehensible to him.

"Either this Dao is not within the mortal world, transcending Mountains and Seas."

"Or…"

The Ink Slaughter clouds churned, like angry hounds, determined to devour the Immortal Skeleton, but their actions were destined to be futile.

It was submerged by the clouds, disappearing, only to reappear quietly shortly after.

This cycle repeated.

Li Fan suppressed his doubts for the moment and patiently continued to observe.

The Dao imbued within this skeleton, though of high standing, could not possibly transcend Mountains and Seas.

Having cultivated through countless reincarnations, Li Fan was confident in his ability to discern this.

So why could it evade Ink Slaughter’s erosion?

Watching the cyclical scenes in the arena, Li Fan became immersed, losing track of time. Suddenly, a thought stirred in his mind.

He stared at the churning Ink Sea before him and mused, "What Ink Slaughter cannot devour, other than things beyond its capabilities…"

"Is itself."

"Could it be…"

Li Fan's thoughts returned to the first time he encountered the Grand Master of Heaven's Capital.

Through the myriad phantoms within the Grand Master's body, Li Fan had understood the two cornerstones of Ink Slaughter: Tai Yi and Eternal.

It was the intertwining of these two divine powers, Change and Unchange, that created a force capable of resisting the merging of Mountains and Seas.

"At that time, I tried to use Ink Slaughter to kill the Grand Master. However, he dissolved it with just two simple sentences."

"‘Please, Master, disperse; please, Uncle-Master, disperse.’"

"‘Tai Yi is the Master of Wuji; Eternal is the Uncle-Master of Wuji.’"

"Uncle-Master implies seniority. Although Eternal is not one of the Three Saints, being called Uncle-Master by Wuji means that his strength and status are not insignificant."

"The Great Dao contained within this skeleton before me is not [Tai Yi]."

A thousand thoughts flashed in an instant. Li Fan recalled the Merchant Immortal Ship, which had been completely destroyed moments ago, and its instantaneous restoration under the skeleton's gaze.

His heart finally had an answer.

"The Dao of Eternity…"

Before identifying it, no matter how he observed, he couldn't discern its true nature. But after recognizing its origin, it was as if layers of disguise were stripped away from the skeleton.

It no longer appeared as a skeleton.

Instead, it manifested its true form: a smiling, round-faced, benevolent-looking middle-aged man!

However, he appeared to be in slumber, his eyes tightly closed. He seemed indifferent to the outside world.

"I had previously come into contact with and gained insights into the two Daos of [Tai Yi] and [Eternal] with the help of the Grand Master. But that was merely my understanding of them. Just as I mistook Tai Yi for illusionary birth, my understanding of [Eternal] was also flawed. That's why I didn't recognize Eternal when it was right before me."

Li Fan gazed at the round-faced middle-aged man not far away. In his daze, he seemed to see an existence that was unchanging from antiquity to the present. He sat there quietly, as if time and space were condensed together. As the surrounding years flowed by, he remained utterly unchanged.

The Dao of Eternity was undoubtedly one of the supreme Daos in the Primordial. Just looking at it, countless insights surged into Li Fan's mind as if inspired.

Li Fan's comprehension was already not weak. Now, with the augmentation of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net and the Supreme Dao Scripture, he had a pre-existing advantage in comprehending all Daos in the Primordial.

Yet, while observing [Eternal], even though countless insights arose moment by moment, they were all as fragile as bubbles, lasting only a moment before quietly bursting and disappearing.

No matter how hard Li Fan tried, the result remained the same.

The faint smile on the round-faced middle-aged man's face seemed to silently remind Li Fan that the Dao of Eternity belonged, and would forever belong, only to Him.

Finally realizing this, Li Fan, not lacking in judgment, decisively ceased his attempt at enlightenment for the time being.

He waved his hand, retracting Ink Slaughter, but did not retreat from this space.

After further observation, he became even more certain of his previous judgment.

"Although Eternal is still alive, its state is rather peculiar."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes and observed for another half-day, finally gaining some understanding of this strangeness.

"The Dao of Eternity still persists. However, the True Immortal who attained this Eternal Dao…"

"His consciousness seems to have dissipated. What maintained his actions just now was merely instinct."

"What stands before me is not so much the [True Immortal of Eternity], but rather the [Dao of Eternity] itself. However, it's different from the original Dao of Eternity; it's now a version modified, or rather, merged, by the True Immortal who attained it."

Although he couldn't fully comprehend the reason for this bizarre scene, Li Fan had some guesses.

"It probably has something to do with [Eternal] itself."

"If one has independent consciousness, it would be difficult to maintain a truly eternal state. Only by completely merging one's will into the pure Dao can the prerequisite for eternity be established. In some cultivation worlds, the highest realm for cultivators is not ascension, but merging with the world's Heavenly Dao."

"This alternative 'merging with Dao,' although it allows cultivators to transcend themselves and become as powerful as the world, extinguishes their individual will, turning them into machines that maintain the operation of the Heavenly Dao."

"Eternal's current situation is somewhat similar to this ‘merging with Dao.’"

After observing for a long time, Li Fan conducted several experiments and managed to tentatively verify his judgment.

"It has no inherent offensive capability, but it consistently maintains its Dao characteristics."

"It will react to external stimuli, so it's correct."

Thus, Li Fan, who had been shocked by the sudden manifestation of the Eternal Dao, began to stir again.

In a sense, the [Eternal] before him was a materialized Dao. Moreover, this Dao was highly independent and powerful, impossible for others to comprehend.

"But it can be stimulated and used." Recalling the scene where Eternal restored the destroyed Merchant Immortal Ship, Li Fan's eyes lit up.

"With this in hand, it's equivalent to having a portable Minor True Transformation armor. It's no wonder the Merchant Immortal Ship has survived the tribulation of the Immortal Realm's destruction to this day, and has always been ahead of everyone else. Escaping the High Wall, escaping the Primordial. It is precisely because they have Eternal as a fallback that they have the confidence to attempt various seemingly extremely dangerous and irrational experiments."

Although Li Fan harbored ulterior motives towards the Dao of [Eternal], successfully stimulating Eternal's power, like the Merchant Immortal Ship, was not an easy task.

The Merchant Immortal Ship had possessed Eternal for countless years, and all they could do now was make it open its eyes and restore the Immortal Ship.

Li Fan, having just arrived and unable to comprehend it due to Eternal's nature, achieving the Merchant Immortal Ship’s level of application in such a short time seemed like a foolish dream.

After trying various methods with no practical effect, Li Fan changed his approach.

The Immortal Skeleton of Eternity was independent, self-contained, and indestructible.

However, since the Merchant Immortal Ship could wield Eternal's power to restore the destroyed Immortal Ship, it indicated a certain connection between the Merchant Immortal Ship's space and this Eternal Immortal Skeleton.

"Since studying it myself is not working, I'll learn by stealing."

Unable to comprehend the Dao of Eternity, Li Fan was confident in his ability to break through the mysterious connection created by the Merchant Immortal Ship.

With a thought, the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, led by Ink Slaughter, reappeared. However, this time, its target was not the Eternal Immortal Skeleton.

But everything else in this space besides the Eternal Immortal Skeleton.

The ink tide surged, sweeping inch by inch, ensuring no omissions.

Like a great wave sifting sand, the surging clouds revealed everything hidden in this space.

Li Fan thus saw through the Merchant Immortal Ship's methods.

What was used to forcibly establish a connection with the now "Dao-ized" Eternal, making the Merchant Immortal Ship's space attract the attention of the Eternal Immortal Skeleton.

It was a prayer mat!

The prayer mat looked unremarkable, seemingly woven from purple bamboo.

"Hmm? This prayer mat looks somewhat familiar?"

After a moment of stunned silence, Li Fan quickly found its origin in his memory.

It was the prayer mat from the vision of Grand Master of Heaven's Capital, where his Master [Sage Monarch Tai Yi] sat!

Compared to the memory from the Grand Master's vision, this prayer mat seemed to have endured many tribulations and looked quite worn. However, its unique rhythm had not changed.

As Li Fan stared for a long time, he seemed to see a blurry figure of [Tai Yi] from this prayer mat!

Chapter 1573: Dao Refines Mountains and Seas Together

The prayer mat floated quietly, as if Sage Monarch Tai Yi himself were present!

Even Li Fan's heart trembled uncontrollably at the sight of this phantom.

"No wonder the Merchant Immortal Ship could attract [Eternal]'s attention with this."

Suppressing the instinctive tremor in his body, Li Fan carefully examined the purple prayer mat.

"Why would something belonging to Sage Monarch Tai Yi appear in the lower realm?"

According to the memories of Grand Master of Heaven's Capital, Sage Monarch Tai Yi might have foreseen the outcome of the Primordial being inevitably swallowed by Dao Annihilation. Like the other two Saints, he retreated and chose to no longer concern himself with the affairs of the Primordial.

However, when Tai Yi departed, all items within the Palace of Tai Yi remained as they were, without being taken. Only a phantom image was left to provide guidance.

And his disciple, Grand Master of Heaven's Capital, continued to treat the phantom image as his master, just as before.

Until the vast tide of Dao Annihilation thoroughly engulfed the Primordial Immortal Realm. Grand Master of Heaven's Capital fled in panic, and under the guidance of the phantom image, discovered the origin of Ink Slaughter hidden beneath the Source Dao State of the Profound Yellow Realm.

"Back then, the Grand Master was only concerned with escaping and did not have time to take any items from the Palace of Tai Yi. After all, besides the phantom of Tai Yi, everything else was ordinary."

"But for others, it was different. Tai Yi, as one of the Three Saints of the Immortal Realm, held an incomparably noble status. Any item in the Palace of Tai Yi could be a priceless treasure, especially those near Sage Monarch Tai Yi…"

"It seems someone, at the critical moment of the impending Dao Annihilation, not only did not flee but also infiltrated the empty Palace of Tai Yi and plundered it."

Li Fan couldn't help but feel curious about this audacity.

"This prayer mat, obtained at such great risk, is here, yet the person who acquired it is nowhere to be seen. Could they have already met their demise?"

Li Fan was certain that there were no undiscovered areas left within the entire Merchant Immortal Ship. The two Cat Treasures and the Eternal Immortal Skeleton were the Merchant Immortal Ship's greatest hidden secrets.

"Perhaps the presence of the Eternal Immortal Skeleton here is also related to this person."

"Only the Lord of the Holy Merchant knows the answer."

Li Fan did not immediately confront the Holy Merchant for now, but kept his target fixed on the Eternal Immortal Skeleton.

The Dao of Eternity might play a crucial role in Li Fan's next plan.

"With the power of Eternity, when the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm collides with Mountains and Seas, there will be more time for buffering," Li Fan mused, his appearance and form simultaneously transforming.

Moments later, he had changed from his original appearance to that of Grand Master of Heaven's Capital's disciple!

Not only his physical form and appearance, but even the power of [Wuji] surging within him, innate to the Grand Master, was displayed!

"Tai Yi came before the Immortals, Wuji came before Tai Yi…"

Li Fan chanted softly, smiling as he bowed to the Eternal Immortal Skeleton before him.

"Greetings, Uncle-Master!"

The smiling, round-faced man suddenly opened his eyes.

His gaze shifted from the Tai Yi prayer mat below, focusing on Li Fan.

Under the gaze of the Eternal Dao, Li Fan felt no panic. After all, his current state could not be considered a "disguise."

The true Grand Master of Heaven's Capital had been suppressed by him and turned into a Heavenly Pillar. What was manifested in the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net now was the true [Wuji]!

It was merely a change in the core.

But it was clear that the now "Dao-ized" [Eternal] could not distinguish between the previous and current Wuji. In its eyes, the person before it was its long-unseen junior disciple.

Although there was no gesture like nodding, Li Fan already felt the "favor" emanating from the other party.

A warm power enveloped Li Fan.

Like a straw cloak put on in a storm, the moment Li Fan was protected by the power of Eternity, he felt an unprecedented sense of security arise in his heart.

It seemed that even if Dao Annihilation descended, he would not need to worry.

"It's not just an illusion. The Dao of Eternity can indeed resist Dao Annihilation to a certain extent."

Li Fan extended his hand, gently caressing this invisible "outer garment" on his body.

However, his gaze drifted into the distance, beyond the Primordial possibility.

"Capable of being brothers with the Three Saints, it must not be weak. Another existence spanning multiple possibilities. Although it has not reached the realm of the Three Saints where all worlds exist simultaneously, it is not far off."

"However, this 'unification of all selves' of the Dao of Eternity is somewhat different from what I encountered before with Black Heavenly Physician, Evil Su Bai, and others."

Through the eternal cloak he was now wearing, Li Fan could vaguely sense the Dao of Eternity shining brightly in other possibilities. It was like a thread, spanning across Mountains and Seas, connecting across multiple possibilities.

After gazing for a long time, he finally withdrew his gaze and looked back at the round-faced man before him, who had merged with the Dao.

"The Eternal beings who merged with Dao in other possibilities are not him."

"But rather all sorts of strange and varied beings. Perhaps a stubborn stone, perhaps the strongest in a world, or perhaps an evergreen tree."

"But their ultimate outcome is the same. Merging with the Dao of Eternity, completely integrating into it."

"When all existent possibilities give birth to an Eternal being, that will be the moment the [Dao of Eternity] is truly forged."

Thinking of this, Li Fan faintly felt a sense that.

It seemed that the ones cultivating the Dao of Eternity were not the cultivators in countless possibilities, but the [Dao of Eternity] itself!

A faint chill rose from the depths of Li Fan's heart.

"Perhaps at that time, the forged Dao of Eternity will be able to rival Mountains and Seas to some extent."

After understanding the power of the Dao of Eternity, Li Fan's resolve became even firmer.

In the guise of the Grand Master, he bowed again, "This place is humble, I hope Uncle-Master will condescend to move."

"So that Nephew can serve you."

Wuji preceded Tai Yi was not just Grand Master of Heaven's Capital's boast.

Compared to the Tai Yi prayer mat, the Wuji nephew clearly held greater importance in Eternal's heart. This time, as Li Fan spoke, the round-faced man did not hesitate at all. He transformed into a ball of light and attached himself to Li Fan.

As long as Li Fan returned to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, he could bring the Dao of Eternity, the greatest foundation of the Merchant Immortal Ship, back with him.

It seemed incredibly easy, almost like a joke. But one must realize that if Li Fan did not possess the power of Wuji, he would not have been able to complete this task at all.

Even using the change between True and False would yield the same result.

"This is specialization, treating the symptoms with the right medicine."

To avoid unnecessary complications, Li Fan did not delay. He quickly retracted the tentacles of the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net that had infiltrated, carrying the Dao of Eternity with him, and rapidly returned.

Before leaving, Li Fan especially left behind the "outer garment" that Eternal had conferred upon him earlier.

It served as an Eternal shell to deceive the people of the Merchant Immortal Ship.

Just as Li Fan thought he had undetected his theft and was about to leave the Merchant Immortal Ship,

"Senior, please take me with you!"

The old man guarding the entrance suddenly shouted.

Chapter 1574: The Origin of the Divine Witch Realm

At the entrance of the Merchant Immortal Ship, the old man without beard or hair, sitting on a yellowish-brown wooden chair, actually stood up.

His posture was no longer hunched, and without waiting for Li Fan's consent, he rapidly approached as the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net retracted.

His plea, "Senior, please take me with you!" was directed at Li Fan.

However, the old man's gaze was fixed on the Dao of Eternity within the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net. In his eyes, which were as dark as if devoid of any light, a complex emotion was revealed.

There was both uncontrollable longing and a sense of restraint.

The round-faced man representing the Primordial Dao of Eternity seemed to completely ignore the elder, showing no change from beginning to end.

However, Li Fan did not pretend not to see.

Pausing slightly, Li Fan examined the elder and asked, "You are not a citizen of the Holy Merchant?"

The elder's gaze finally shifted away from Eternity, and he bowed slightly to Li Fan, replying solemnly, "No, no. I hope Senior will understand. I came to the Merchant Immortal Ship many years ago specifically to follow in Eternal's footsteps. Now that Eternal is moving, I naturally must follow."

Li Fan's interest was piqued upon hearing this. The Myriad Phenomena Dao Net enveloped them both, and they began to retreat towards the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm within the High Wall.

Facing the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net's embrace, the elder did not resist, allowing Li Fan to do as he pleased.

During the journey back, he answered Li Fan's questions truthfully and without omission.

"When did you arrive at the Merchant Immortal Ship?"

"It has been too long, and I cannot quite recall. However, at that time, the Immortal Ship was not yet an Immortal Ship, but a grotto-heaven within the cultivation world. Later, the grotto-heaven detached itself from the world and abandoned it, thus becoming the Xuan-Shang Immortal Ship. Later, as the Immortal Ship drifted through the sea of stars, its wanderings were unstable. Finally, due to disagreements, it split into two during a civil war. The victor became Shang, and the loser became Xuan. I then followed the split Shang Immortal Ship, passed through the High Wall, and arrived in a new star field…" the elder said slowly and unhurriedly.

"You are not a True Immortal, with mortal eyes and flesh, how can you perceive the Dao of Eternity?" Li Fan saw clearly. Although the elder before him was quite mysterious, he did not possess the aura connecting him to Mountains and Seas; he was a pure mortal cultivator. This was also the primary reason Li Fan felt at ease allowing him to approach.

"To inform Senior, I hail from the world of [Divine Witch]. I am naturally gifted with keen insight into all manner of Great Daos. Thus, I was able to recognize the Dao of Eternity, hidden in plain sight, at a glance." the elder replied humbly.

"Divine Witch Realm?"

Li Fan was slightly stunned upon hearing this. Immediately, an image appeared in his mind: twelve solemn palaces stood amidst the clouds, arranged in a circle, occupying the sky of the world. Each palace enshrined a statue. Countless cultivators on the ground, like ants, knelt and prayed.

He flipped his hand and took out the Azure Nether Pearl, asking, "Do you recognize this object?"

After only a moment, the elder recognized the object from his homeland. His emotional reaction was even greater than when he saw the Dao of Eternity being taken away: "This… This is the Azure Nether Sacred Pearl?"

The elder wished to examine it further, but Li Fan had already put the Azure Nether Pearl away.

"I hope Senior will forgive my失态 (shītài - losing composure). Seeing this object brought back memories," the elder said with a sense of loss.

"Tell me about it."

"The Azure Nether Sacred Pearl is one of the twelve Sacred Artifacts of our Divine Witch Realm. The twelve Sacred Artifacts were refined by the twelve Divine Witches, who gathered Great Daos from all realms and fused them with their own essence blood. The Twelve Divine Witches already existed before the Immortal Realm was created. Each of them possessed unimaginable supreme power, not inferior to True Immortals. It is said that after the Immortal Realm was established, to glimpse the secrets of the Immortal Realm, the Divine Witches sent their Sacred Artifacts as substitutes to enter the Immortal Realm, thus opening the path to ascension for the countless beings of the Divine Witch Realm."

"Later, when the great tribulation descended and the Immortal Realm collapsed, the Divine Witch Realm could not avoid such a disaster. The Twelve Divine Witches joined forces to save the world, buying the last sliver of escape time for the living beings. I followed the teleportation channel opened by the Divine Witches and miraculously managed to escape…"

"The channels opened by the Divine Witches could lead to a place within this sealed High Wall?" Li Fan chuckled, interrupting him.

At this moment, the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net brought them both, along with the Dao of Eternity, back to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

However, the elder from the Divine Witch Realm could no longer answer Li Fan's question.

The moment he entered the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, the elder from the Divine Witch Realm froze as if petrified.

Cultivators from the Divine Witch Realm resonated with the Great Dao through their primordial spirits, manipulated the Great Dao, and even replaced the Great Dao. They possessed a natural keen perception of the world's Great Daos. Therefore, the moment he entered the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, the elder saw that this realm had high heavens and deep earth, a flourishing new Great Dao, a scene full of vitality.

The elder had never been to the Immortal Realm, but judging by this realm, it might not be inferior to the former Immortal Realm!

He greedily looked around. As if desperate, every corner of the Profound Yellow realm seemed to be filled with rare treasures.

And his extremely aged appearance, accompanied by his observation, began to gradually regain its youth.

While the elder was observing the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, Li Fan was also observing the elder.

He had already received the Dao of Eternity atop the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's celestial dome and settled it properly. Li Fan, now with ample time, was closely examining this cultivator from the Divine Witch Realm with great interest.

It was clear he was comprehending Dao.

But the process was different from that of ordinary cultivators.

Li Fan could tell that within this short time since entering the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, this person's comprehension of the various Great Daos in heaven and earth had not deepened. The reason for his rejuvenation was simply that he was directly drawing power from the myriad Daos in nature.

As the Father and Mother of Profound Yellow, Li Fan could acutely sense that the Great Daos of the Profound Yellow realm had weakened slightly because of this Divine Witch Realm cultivator's absorption.

Even though the absorbed amount was negligible, it had undeniably occurred.

"It's somewhat similar to the ability of the newly born Ink Slaughter. It steals abilities, but much weaker, yet it can simultaneously lock onto all intertwined Daos in the world in an instant…"

"It truly has some skill."

Li Fan let out a cold snort and directly severed the connection between him and the Profound Yellow Great Dao.

As if his eyes were instantly blinded and his throat fiercely choked, the Divine Witch Realm cultivator let out a scream.

Soon, he realized that his impolite actions had angered Li Fan. He immediately knelt down and repeatedly kowtowed, begging for forgiveness.

"It wasn't intentional, Senior. It was my instinct acting uncontrollably."

"Please do not be angry, Senior, please do not be angry!"

Li Fan could see that the other party was not lying.

However, this unique constitution of the Divine Witch Realm cultivator truly piqued his curiosity.

Disregarding the elder's cries of mercy, Li Fan suppressed and sealed him. Then, he sent a wisp of his divine sense into the other party's body to observe carefully.

As if entering the Azure Nether Pearl once again, Li Fan's eyes were presented with the image of twelve grand halls standing majestically in the sky.

Chapter 1575: Profound Yellow Engraves Eternity

The palaces enshrined twelve Divine Witches. Eleven of them were hidden within gray mist, their true appearances indiscernible. The remaining one, with three eyes and four arms, had a serene expression. The two eyes on either side were like deep, bottomless cold abysses, while the vertical eye in the center seemed to reflect countless beings from the Divine Witch Realm.

The elder guarding the entrance of the Merchant Immortal Ship was one of the beings reflected in its eyes!

Li Fan faced this so-called Divine Witch without fear.

Despite being named "Divine," as Li Fan stood before it, its eyes could not reflect Li Fan's figure.

Li Fan was able to observe carefully.

After careful study, he concluded: "Although the Twelve Divine Witches are deceased, their enshrined seats within the beings of the Divine Witch Realm have not vanished. Cultivators of the Divine Witch Realm can activate various Divine Witch seats, worshipping and communing with them. They can usually only choose one. Upon activation, they can borrow the power of the Divine Witch to a certain extent. Glimpsing and comprehending the Dao, and drawing power from the Dao, is merely the most basic ability."

Li Fan attempted to send his divine sense into the Divine Witch seat above the Azure Nether Pearl. However, to him, these magnificent structures were merely illusions, nonexistent. He passed right through them, unable to enter.

He could only ascertain the various abilities obtained by Divine Witch Realm cultivators through their memories of worshipping the Divine Witch.

"The three-eyed Divine Witch, Cang Ming Xu, controls the cycle of life and death in the Divine Witch Realm. Therefore, this Divine Witch Realm cultivator named Wu Xin can defy old age and near death. He can capture souls, perceive grudges, and hear disasters…"

"All these abilities, though not exceedingly powerful, have the advantage of being obtained through a mere act of worship. They become his unique [skills] and can also be integrated into his cultivation methods, complementing each other."

"These numerous Divine Witch seats, projected by the Divine Witches into the cultivators of the Divine Witch Realm, appear to be a dispersal of their power. In reality, they are similar to anchors. Even if the Divine Witches were to perish temporarily, as long as any living beings of the Divine Witch Realm survive on the mortal plane, with continuous propagation and worship, these Divine Witches have the opportunity for resurrection."

"The Divine Witch Realm was created by the Twelve Divine Witches united. All laws within the realm are controlled by the Gods…"

Li Fan vaguely felt that, in a certain sense, the Divine Witch Realm he glimpsed in Wu Xin's memories shared many similarities with the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm he had created.

However, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's standing was far superior to the Divine Witch Realm, and there was only Li Fan, the sole master of Profound Yellow. But the Divine Witch Realm had originated very early and had a continuous lineage for tens of billions of years. There were indeed many aspects Li Fan could learn from.

For instance: When beings were in the Divine Witch Realm, they could perhaps guarantee their loyalty to the Divine Witches. However, once they left the Divine Witch Realm, went to other worlds, or even ascended to the Immortal Realm, how could they ensure their continued loyalty to the Divine Witches? The answer lay in the Divine Witch seats within the beings.

The Divine Witch seats were essentially projections of the Divine Witches' power, combined with the life essence of the beings. As the power of Divine Witch Realm cultivators grew, the Divine Witch seats would become more solidified. Simultaneously, they would bind more deeply with the cultivators. If a cultivator betrayed the Divine Witches, it would be equivalent to betraying the foundation they had been strengthening since their cultivation began. At best, their cultivation would be destroyed; at worst, they would die and their Dao would perish. Even True Immortals were no exception.

Another example: Due to the Divine Witches' favor, the lifespan of beings in the Divine Witch Realm was extremely long. However, the Divine Witch Realm was not connected to Mountains and Seas and did not possess infinite attributes. To ensure the eternal prosperity of the Divine Witch Realm, a "reset" would occur every ten million years.

This was a world-ending tribulation decreed by the Twelve Divine Witches. Below the Divine Witches, all beings were equal and had to face the tribulation. Among hundreds of millions of creatures, only ninety-nine individuals with the greatest fortune and strength could survive. The next era of civilization would begin with these ninety-nine individuals.
