In this way, like a great wave sifting sand, through repeated resets, the "aptitude" of Divine Witch Realm cultivators showed a stable upward trend.

Of course, there were cultivators who attempted to break free from this cruel cycle of destruction and reincarnation, but in the face of the will of the Twelve Divine Witches, all resistance was futile.

…

"The Profound Yellow Immortal Realm is the foundation for my crossing of Mountains and Seas. It truly needs to be managed properly. I was too kind before. My methods were akin to laissez-faire. While currently the time is short and my strong control has prevented any major issues, it might not be the same in the future."

"After all, all sorts of unpredictable beings have tried to meddle in the Profound Yellow Realm."

Li Fan was a humble person. He did not shy away from praising those superior to him and would promptly learn from advanced experiences.

"The beings of Profound Yellow only know of the drastic changes in heaven and earth, but not of their Profound Yellow Father and Mother behind it."

"Coincidentally, with [Eternal] illuminating Profound Yellow, I can announce my divine name."

Li Fan’s divine sense withdrew from Wu Xin’s body.

He looked towards the Eternal Dao seated in the celestial dome.

After seven days of active adjustment, bringing the overall state of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm to its optimal condition. Li Fan once again transformed into the phantom image of the Grand Master.

"This realm was crafted by Nephew. If Uncle-Master is satisfied, you may reside here permanently."

A moment later, the round-faced man slowly opened his eyes upon hearing this.

In that instant, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm seemed to be frozen, entering a brief period of stillness. The round-faced man closed his eyes, and the ice seal was broken.

This was followed by continuous, intense tremors.

Heaven and earth rumbled, and strange phenomena appeared in the sky. However, what was displayed were not scenes from within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

It was clearly the sights Eternal had witnessed in other possibilities.

As the [Eternal] was engraved, Li Fan, the Lord of Profound Yellow, remained vigilant, even as [Eternal] descended.

Although Eternal had almost no consciousness of its own and acted merely on instinct, mechanically, it was an existence capable of traversing Mountains and Seas. Li Fan needed to take precautions to prevent its influence in the Profound Yellow Realm from surpassing his own and making it the new Lord of Profound Yellow.

As Eternal descended and influenced the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, a mysterious figure exuding an immortal aura also appeared in the minds of all Profound Yellow beings.

Almost instantly, all Profound Yellow beings learned the identity of this figure.

The source of the anomaly in the Profound Yellow Realm, the Father and Mother of Profound Yellow Heaven and Earth.

The Primordial Profound Yellow Controlling the Heavens and Skies Saint!

Irresistibly, all beings felt an urge to prostrate themselves.

Their bodies moved uncontrollably, and amidst the slight tremors of heaven and earth, they slowly bowed down.

And as they bowed, the figure in their hearts transformed from an illusory being into a real one, truly taking shape.

It was like a divine statue erected in the spiritual platform.

With just a thought, it could be perceived again at any time.

Worshipping and bowing to the Saint was like facing countless Great Daos of heaven and earth.

A single bow was worth more than three years of enlightenment!

Unfortunately, after the bow, the Saint's divine statue became wispy again, requiring sincere faith in one's heart to recongeal.

The descent of the [Primordial Profound Yellow Controlling the Heavens and Skies Saint] instantly changed the landscape of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

In less than half a day, over a hundred Grotto-Heaven Stars appeared.

And the first "God Transformation" cultivator in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm was born!

Chapter 1576: The God-Enshrined Name Endures for Eternity

This first cultivator to achieve the God Transformation realm was none other than Su Bai!

High above, the Heavenly Benevolence Star erupted with a radiance thousands of times brighter than usual, resembling a second great sun, casting the sky of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm in pure, blinding white.

All other stars vanished, leaving only the Heavenly Benevolence visible!

As the myriad phenomena of the Heavenly Benevolence Star drew the gaze of all beings in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, a thin thread shot upwards from this resplendent star, piercing the heavens and ascending towards the realm beyond the sky.

If the beings of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm could still sense the anomalies of the Heavenly Benevolence Star, then what occurred in the celestial realms beyond was far beyond their comprehension.

They could only watch the Heavenly Benevolence Star shine, gazing upwards in silent anticipation of the outcome.

The dazzling light, comparable to a great sun, lasted for a full hour. As the radiance began to recede and the thread ascending beyond the heavens gradually returned, a majestic, colossal figure suddenly materialized in the celestial expanse.

This figure was so immense that the entire sky of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm could not contain its form; only its upper body, seated grandly, could be glimpsed.

Before all beings realized the true identity of this magnificent figure, their bodies instinctively knelt in reverence.

Thus, they understood who it was:

The Primordial Profound Yellow Controlling the Heavens and Skies Saint Venerable!

All beings trembled, their souls surging. As if witnessing the Dao, their minds became frozen in fear, yet their bodies seemed to be drawn and disintegrated by the mere appearance of the Saint Venerable's phantom.

They realized this was no illusion. It was because the Profound Yellow Saint Venerable was too powerful. They could not withstand the divine might of the deity; just as ice and snow inevitably melt under the sun's glare, before the magnificent [Primordial Profound Yellow Controlling the Heavens and Skies Saint Venerable], they were less than ants. Even a slight fluctuation in its aura would be unbearable, causing their annihilation.

The reason they were still alive was that something stood between the Profound Yellow Saint Venerable and the beings.

It was a scroll, unfurled and boundless, floating in the expanse.

The scroll was initially blank, but now, it bore the first name.

Su Bai!

Originally, a name was merely a designation. You could be called Su Bai, I could be called Su Bai, anyone could be called Su Bai.

But from the moment this name appeared on the [Investiture of the Gods], the designation of "Su Bai" became specific throughout heaven and earth.

It was, and could only be, that resplendent Heavenly Benevolence Star!

Those who shared the name Su Bai in the world had already vanished like dust, leaving no trace of their past existence, nor even any imprint in the memories of their closest kin.

And in the future, no second Su Bai would emerge.

This was the God Transformation realm of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm: entering the Saint Venerable's discerning gaze and receiving an eternal name!

Of course, receiving an eternal name was merely the most direct and perceivable enhancement for outsiders after achieving God Transformation. The earth-shattering changes truly occurring within their own bodies were known only to the individuals themselves.

The Saint Venerable's grand likeness finally slowly dispersed.

And without the Saint Venerable's radiant gaze, although the Investiture of the Gods remained floating in the celestial realm, it was beyond the sight of all beings. Only cultivators who had transformed into stars at the Nascent Soul stage could vaguely perceive its trace.

Thus, their ambition to advance grew even stronger. Those who could cultivate to this realm naturally possessed a certain pride. If Su Bai could advance to God Transformation, why couldn't they? With the birth of the first God Transformation cultivator in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, the emergence of the second and third would not be far behind.

Su Bai seemed to have become a bridge, shortening the vast chasm between the Nascent Soul and God Transformation realms in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

Other cultivators displayed their unique abilities, eager to become the second name on the Investiture of the Gods.

As for Su Bai himself, he showed no joy in achieving God Transformation. Instead, his face contorted in pain, deep in self-reproach.

"After the great changes in heaven and earth, the number of living beings in the world has multiplied countless times. Among them, how many shared my name and surname..."

"And now, they have all died because of me." Su Bai's face turned pale, his body trembling uncontrollably.

"Saint Venerable, can the strong disregard the lives of the weak? Can the strong do whatever they please? Is this truly the right way?" After a long while, Su Bai finally emerged from his remorse and self-reproach. Then, a question arose in his heart.

He looked up towards the highest heavens, directly asking the Profound Yellow Saint Venerable.

However, he received no answer from the Saint Venerable.

Instead, he learned an unexpected piece of news that turned his face pale again, and his heart turned cold.

"The Tribulation of Profundity? The heavens and earth will be reopened, and all beings will perish. Only those whose names are recorded on the Investiture of the Gods will be able to escape this tribulation..." Su Bai was immediately struck as if by lightning.

Having already entered the Investiture of the Gods, he should have felt fortunate, free from calamity. But when he thought of the countless beings below who would turn to dust in the coming great tribulation, Su Bai felt suffocated.

"Is there… is there no way to prevent this catastrophe?" he asked instinctively.

The Saint Venerable did not respond.

Only the cold Investiture of the Gods, hanging high in the sky, reflected the myriad beings of Profound Yellow.

"There must be a way. There must be a way..." Su Bai muttered to himself, his gaze gradually shifting from confusion to determination, fixed upon the heavens beyond.

His thought was simple: as long as he could meet the Profound Yellow Saint Venerable face-to-face, perhaps he could persuade Him to retract the decree of world destruction.

"Only by merging with the Dao can one cross this invisible boundary."

"Merging with the Dao..." Su Bai narrowed his eyes, once again sensing the myriad Great Daos in the world.

This time, his desire to delve deeper was a million times stronger than before.

...

"As expected, Su Bai is still Su Bai."

Having seen Su Bai's entire transformation from beginning to end, Li Fan couldn't help but sneer.

"Wanting to save the world, how much can one save? Without the Great Tribulation of Profundity, there is the Tribulation of Mountains and Seas. His own strength is not enough, yet he still wants to overthink things." Li Fan naturally could not empathize with Su Bai.

But if it could make Su Bai accelerate his cultivation and completely exhaust his potential, Li Fan would not prevent him from changing his mindset.

"After the integration of the Dao of Eternity, the sturdiness of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm has increased by at least thirty percent. And this effect will only grow as more names are added to the Investiture of the Gods."

In fact, this was an unexpected bonus.

When Li Fan, under the guise of [Tai Yi], drew the gaze of Eternity and it glanced at the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, carving a trace of eternal attribute into the world, the Dao of Eternity subsequently closed its eyes.

Li Fan was already quite satisfied with this outcome. He then proceeded to project his divine manifestation onto the hearts of all Profound Yellow beings.

As for later, when a cultivator broke through to God Transformation and had their name inscribed on the Profound Yellow Investiture of the Gods, it was all within Li Fan's plan.

However, what Li Fan had not anticipated was that after Su Bai ascended the Investiture of the Gods, Eternity, which had already closed its eyes and ceased its involvement in worldly affairs, unexpectedly opened its eyes again!

Although the duration of its gaze was much shorter than when Li Fan had summoned it, it still added another layer of eternal attribute to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

"I wonder if Eternity reopened its eyes because of [Su Bai], or simply because of the emergence of a pure genius in this world."

"However, as soon as the next person appears on the Investiture of the Gods, we should be able to determine this."

Li Fan's divine sense swept across the entire Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, locking onto potential candidates.

Most were as expected.

Only one was a slight surprise to Li Fan.

Although this person was currently only at the Foundation Establishment stage, in Li Fan's estimation, they might even rank among the top three on the Investiture of the Gods.

"This speed of comprehending the Dao..."

"It wasn't there before. Did it only manifest now?"

"Is it because of Eternity's inclusion? Or..."

The person Li Fan was focusing on was a thin man named Zhang Shangzhi. While he appeared righteous, a hint of inexplicable陰翳 (yīn yì - gloom/shadow) flickered in his eyes from time to time.

Upon observing his inner world more closely, Li Fan finally understood why this person's innate talent for comprehending the Dao had suddenly surged.

The so-called talent for comprehending the Dao was, in reality, the affinity with various Great Daos.

Before this, Zhang Shangzhi's talent for comprehending the Dao was mediocre. Even now, it remained so.

The reason for the earth-shattering change in an instant was the formal manifestation of the [Primordial Profound Yellow Controlling the Heavens and Skies Saint Venerable]!

The Profound Yellow Saint Venerable was Li Fan, the Father and Mother of Profound Yellow!

The greatest Dao in this world, the Dao above all Daos!

And Zhang Shangzhi, due to his excellent compatibility with Li Fan—acting ruthlessly to achieve his goals, never trusting anyone from the bottom of his heart, and possessing a cold, robotic indifference—shared almost identical traits and thought patterns with Li Fan.

If Li Fan hadn't known for certain that there were no blood relatives of his within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, he would have almost thought that Zhang Shangzhi was his own flesh and blood.

Having understood the truth, Li Fan was speechless.

The reason Zhang Shangzhi's cultivation had advanced by leaps and bounds was simply because he was "lucky" to be like Li Fan.

"Outside the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, he would be useless. After all, he has no True Transformation, nor does he possess infinite spiritual essence." Li Fan shook his head slightly.

He did not intend to pay excessive attention, nor did he plan to interfere deliberately.

The Heavenly Dao was unpredictable; everything would take its natural course.

After settling the Dao of Eternity in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, Li Fan intended to return to the Merchant Immortal Ship to retrieve the two Cat Treasures. However, the matter of Zhang Shangzhi suddenly made him recall something else.

"The principles of Profound Yellow and Mountains and Seas are interconnected."

"So-called talent might merely be a certain degree of similarity to certain beings."

Chapter 1577: The Holy Dynasty Reflects the Ancient Ages

"Perhaps, the so-called disparity in talent among cultivators in the Mountains and Seas is merely a degree of similarity to that [Creator God]." Li Fan mused leisurely.

With Eternity residing within, the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm became even more stable, and in turn, it fed back to Li Fan. Within the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, it was as if refined gold had been implanted, forming stable support. Even if it extended far beyond the High Wall, there would be no significant attenuation.

Therefore, this time when Li Fan re-entered the Merchant Immortal Ship, the projection of his true self, enshrouded by the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net, could exert nearly half of his original strength.

"Although Eternity forms its own Dao, and cannot be comprehended by others, it can be borrowed."

"Just like adding heavenly treasures and earthly materials during the process of refining artifacts or elixirs."

With this thought, Li Fan once again infiltrated the Holy Merchant.

The inhabitants of the Merchant Immortal Ship were still engrossed in studying the newly captured Cat Treasure. Moreover, with the mask of Eternal "outer wear" that Li Fan left behind, they had not even discovered the loss of the [Dao of Eternity].

On the other hand, the disappearance of Wu Xin, who was responsible for guarding the entrance of the Merchant Immortal Ship, caused quite a stir. After all, Wu Xin had been on the Merchant Immortal Ship for who knew how many years, undoubtedly an elder figure. The Lord of the Holy Merchant personally investigated the scene but could not ascertain the true reason for his disappearance.

After careful consideration, the Lord of the Holy Merchant only ordered that the location of the entrance channel be changed, rather than choosing to seal all entrances.

This, in turn, gave Li Fan another opportunity to infiltrate.

Skillfully arriving at the space where the Cat Treasure was imprisoned, the situation was vastly different from when Li Fan had left.

The orange cat was still tightly bound by countless blue chains. Beside it, the recently captured black and white cat could move freely, weaving around the orange cat, occasionally sniffing and meowing softly.

The orange cat, however, remained extremely indifferent to its "companion," its eyes tightly closed, motionless.

Occasionally, a burst of orange-yellow light would erupt from its body, forcefully resisting the bindings of the blue chains and repelling the approaching black and white cat.

Li Fan subtly sensed that within this group of orange-yellow light contained unparalleled, warm vitality. If the black and white cat's power was the cold energy of the Dao of Life and Death, then the orange cat's body contained pure condensed life force. Because the gathered life force was so immense, its outward manifestation of power even surpassed that of the black and white cat.

And as the orange cat was forced to unleash its orange-yellow light, countless shallow blue symbols simultaneously flashed within the Merchant Immortal Ship's space, stealing the vital energy from the orange-yellow light.

Following this, Li Fan saw that the black and white cat's body gained a few streaks of orange-yellow fur.

"This black and white cat is likely not the Cat Treasure itself, but a transformation of the Holy Merchant Lord," Li Fan mused inwardly.

Indeed, as Li Fan predicted.

With different colored hues of orange and black and white appearing on its body, the black and white cat's form suddenly flickered with strange light and shadow, constantly shifting between human and cat forms.

Finally, with a muffled grunt, the Holy Merchant Lord revealed his true form.

The orange cat, which had been lying quietly, suddenly opened its eyes. It crouched low, emitting a resounding growl towards the Holy Merchant Lord. The surrounding countless blue chains seemed unable to restrain it, shaking violently. Many chains even directly shattered, scattering into countless specks of light.

It was evident how much the orange cat hated the Holy Merchant Lord.

The Holy Merchant Lord, however, remained rather calm. With a gentle wave of his hand, layer upon layer of light-colored barriers sealed and enveloped the orange cat, ultimately forming a sphere of light that completely encapsulated the Cat Treasure. The disturbance ceased.

Immediately after, figures began to appear one after another; they were the citizens of the Holy Merchant involved in the Cat Treasure research.

"As expected of one of the Seven prototypes of Heaven-Stealers, [Loquat]'s strength is still far superior to [Bai Qian]. We only took a few days to analyze Bai Qian, but for [Loquat], we've always been somewhat helpless," the Holy Merchant Lord said with great emotion, looking at the thoroughly wrapped sphere before him.

"The reason this time's research on Bai Qian went so smoothly was thanks to the analysis of Loquat in the past. It's a shame that it would be almost impossible to capture a third Cat Treasure. If we had new Heaven-Stealing Cats for research..."

The Holy Merchant Lord chuckled, "Who says it's impossible?"

The people around them exchanged glances, most showing hesitation.

"Heaven-Stealing Cats are vengeful. After capturing two without them noticing, it was already great fortune. If we act again, we might not be so lucky..."

The Holy Merchant Lord waved his hand: "I am aware of the risks. Although the Holy Merchant Dynasty is formidable, it is merely one great force among the Mountains and Seas. With the Holy Emperor as the supreme being, they are at odds with other powerhouses. Although we are no match for the Holy Dynasty, there are those in the Mountains and Seas who can contend with them. Our act of capturing Cat Treasures is precisely our pledge of allegiance to them!"

The citizens of the Immortal Ship finally understood: "Holy Master, have you already made contact?"

"The Annihilation of the Dao is imminent. Even with Eternity's protection, it is unlikely to last long. What else can we do but make preparations? The past Holy Masters risked their lives crossing to other possibilities, precisely to seek a sliver of hope for survival!" The Holy Merchant Lord said with a solemn expression.

The citizens of the Immortal Ship were filled with excitement, some even shedding tears on the spot.

Amidst their heartfelt praises, Li Fan finally understood that after the Merchant Immortal Ship had leaped beyond the High Wall and barely escaped the world-ending catastrophe of the Immortal Ruins,

The entire Immortal Ship had maintained a strong sense of crisis.

Through some unknown channel, upon learning the truth of the Immortal Realm's destruction, they resolved to escape this land affected by the Annihilation of the Dao as much as possible.

Later, the first Holy Merchant Lord, who had led the Xuan-Shang Immortal Ship away from the cultivation world, discovered a method to traverse to other possibilities. However, the safety of those possibilities was unknown.

Thus, he ventured forth alone to investigate.

Since then, this had become a tradition of the Merchant Immortal Ship. Every successive Holy Merchant Lord had to shoulder the responsibility of exploration, venturing into different possibilities to find those that were relatively safe.

Among them, some never returned. But others were still alive.

Only within the Holy Merchant did they possess the method to communicate with these predecessors. Thus, the other inhabitants of the Immortal Ship knew little about matters beyond the original possibility.

And it was precisely because of the sacrificial exploration efforts of the successive Holy Merchant Lords that the Merchant Immortal Ship, even without leaving its original location, had a basic understanding of the myriad possibilities within the Mountains and Seas.

In fact, they knew more than Li Fan.

Li Fan, eavesdropping from the side, nodded secretly: "Standing on the achievements of countless generations. This is the true foundation of the Merchant Immortal Ship. No wonder they were able to escape successfully before the original possibility was destroyed."

Li Fan stared at the Holy Merchant Lord, who was currently boasting eloquently nearby. The desire to thoroughly examine the memories within his mind was almost uncontrollable.

In his view, this Holy Merchant Lord could definitely be considered a living map.

As if sensing Li Fan's malice, the Holy Merchant Lord's boastful speech suddenly stopped. He frowned, looking around suspiciously.

However, he could not detect the source of the fleeting unease in his heart.

"Could it be... the Cat Treasure acting up?"

The Holy Merchant Lord cautiously re-examined the orange cat Loquat, finding no signs of it breaking free. As Li Fan suppressed the malice in his heart, his unease gradually subsided.

He then returned to the previous topic: "That [Holy Emperor of Tai Wei], in his attempt to expand the Holy Dynasty across all Mountains and Seas, projects his power across countless possibilities. Any entity that bears a similar form will be influenced by him, becoming a so-called Holy Emperor."

"If, by chance, a Heaven-Stealing Cat on a mission is present in this possibility, the Holy Emperor will receive aid from the Heaven-Stealing Cat, and there will be a high probability of unifying the possibility and establishing a Holy Dynasty. At that moment, the [Holy Emperor of Tai Wei]'s true consciousness will awaken, and the pseudo-Holy Emperor influenced by this projection will ascend to become the true one."

The Holy Merchant Lord slowly explained the methods of the [Holy Emperor of Tai Wei], and the citizens of the Immortal Ship were filled with awe.

"We originally thought that Heaven-Stealing Cats were already great fortunes from heaven. Now it seems that these creations are merely part of the myriad schemes of that colossal Holy Dynasty."

"Compared to the Tai Wei Holy Dynasty, a massive entity, our Immortal Ship is like an ant. Yet, we repeatedly manage to snatch pieces from this behemoth. This is truly too dangerous!"

The Holy Merchant Lord heard the discussions of his subordinates and, after allowing them to calm down, continued: "The Tai Wei Holy Emperor is indeed powerful. But his actions are overly domineering. Most of the powerful beings in the Mountains and Seas have united in the [Other Shore] to discuss countermeasures against the Dao Annihilation tribulation. As for those unwilling to participate, they merely carve out separate territories and maintain a distance from the Other Shore."

"This Tai Wei Holy Emperor not only has no intention of joining the Other Shore but also acts willfully, expanding his Holy Dynasty without any regard. It is said he has repeatedly clashed with powerful beings from the Great World of the Other Shore, making many enemies."

"We are currently not qualified or capable of venturing to the Other Shore. However, those who are at odds with the Tai Wei Holy Emperor, and who are safe for a long period of time in other possibilities..."

The Holy Merchant Lord smiled slightly, appearing confident.

This elicited continuous praise from the citizens of the Immortal Ship.

"But before we offer the Heaven-Stealing Cat as a pledge of allegiance, it is best that we complete its research to the best of our abilities."

"Even if we cannot completely decipher it, we must push it to the limits of our capabilities."

"After all, relying on others is not the right path. Regardless of anything else, only the power that we can grasp ourselves can be the capital for our survival. Esteemed sirs, do not forget how the Xuan-Shang Immortal Ship escaped from its homeland back then." the Holy Merchant Lord said sternly.

...

"Tai Wei Holy Emperor? Holy Dynasty?" Li Fan heard the discussions of the Immortal Ship's inhabitants and the image of Li Ping resurfaced in his mind.

"So that's how it is. I misunderstood."

"The birth of the Holy Emperor, the Cat Treasure's closeness, were not because there was an original [Li Fan] in other possibilities. It was because the clone I derived had a strong compatibility with the Tai Wei Holy Emperor, and thus was subtly influenced by him."

Li Fan recalled now. The loss of control over the Holy Emperor clone was not instantaneous, but a gradual process. Even at first, the Cat Treasure was indifferent to the Holy Emperor. As their interactions increased, it became more intimate, even becoming obedient.

"The Tai Wei Holy Emperor, seated in the Holy Dynasty, reflecting countless possibilities. Even within the High Wall erected by the Guardian Duke, he is difficult to avoid influencing. His power is evident." Li Fan was secretly shocked.

"This method of cultivation of the Tai Wei Holy Emperor is also a form of unification of all selves. However, compared to Evil Su Bai and Black Heavenly Physician, who devoured their other selves from different possibilities, it is even superior!"

"It's not just about the self, but a degree of similarity, all within the scope of fusion. And what is devoured is not just a single individual, but an entire Holy Dynasty as a unit..."

Li Fan could almost imagine that if the Tai Wei Holy Emperor truly succeeded in spreading his Holy Dynasty across all Mountains and Seas, he might even possess power comparable to the Mountains and Seas themselves.

"However, doing so would strip away the living space of other powerhouses. Even if the Guardian Duke and Zi Yi are extremely righteous, it would be difficult for them to submit to the Tai Wei and acknowledge him as their lord."

The Dao of Eternity, the Tai Wei Holy Emperor, these newly discovered powerhouses in the Mountains and Seas, broadened Li Fan's perspective once again.

"Indeed, it is not surprising that all sorts of powerhouses emerge in the countless possibilities of the Mountains and Seas."

"But conversely, every existence that reaches the pinnacle of the Mountains and Seas possesses unique characteristics and has walked a path distinct from others..."

As Li Fan pondered, the inhabitants of the Merchant Immortal Ship, after a brief respite, resumed their research on the Cat Treasure.

This time, the orange cat Loquat's resistance was even stronger.

The blue chains binding it vibrated more intensely, seeming on the verge of shattering at any moment.

But the Holy Merchant Lord remained unperturbed.

He had long been accustomed to the various situations that arose during experiments. In his view, with the protection of the Dao of Eternity, even if the Merchant Immortal Ship were instantly reduced to dust, it could be restored in an instant.

Therefore, he not only did not stop but also continued to draw energy from the Merchant Immortal Ship, intensifying the confrontation with the orange cat.

The Immortal Ship inhabitants watching were already accustomed to this.

There was no fear on their faces.

Only the joy of transforming the power of the Heaven-Stealing Cat into their own.

Finally, the intensity of the power struggle reached a critical point.

A destructive wave erupted, surging forth.

Chapter 1578: The Seven Divine Medicines of Heaven-Stealing

From the darkness, a piercing light erupted, instantly turning everything in its path to ash.

"Eternity!"

Witnessing the annihilation of the Merchant Immortal Ship's billions of life forms before his eyes, the Holy Merchant Lord showed no panic, merely calmly uttering the word.

One breath. Two breaths. Three breaths.

As the intense radiance gradually dimmed and subsided, the scene of the Merchant Immortal Ship returning to its original state, which the Holy Merchant Lord had anticipated, did not occur.

A look of suspicion began to surface on the Holy Merchant Lord's face.

However, he did not immediately consider the possibility of the Dao of Eternity failing.

Instead, he called out to [Eternity] again.

His response was only the silent, dead void before him.

Panic began to set in the Holy Merchant Lord's heart.

He repeatedly called out, even taking the Tai Yi prayer mat and personally going to the side of the Eternal Immortal Skeleton.

His body trembled as he pointed to the location where the Merchant Immortal Ship had been.

The Eternal Immortal Skeleton, naturally, offered no response.

The Holy Merchant Lord had already realized what had happened, but he was utterly unable to accept it. His reason gradually slipped away, and he even began to attack the Eternal Immortal Skeleton.

"Damn it, damn it, damn it..."

"Restore it for me!"

An endless stream of blue symbols surged from his body, like a raging storm, crashing towards the Immortal Skeleton.

This strike, born of the Holy Merchant Lord's fury, caused the silent starry sky to reverberate once more. Like a stone cast into calm water, ripples of blue spread outwards.

And the Eternal Immortal Skeleton, which had existed within the Immortal Ship for millions of years and had become its foundation, actually shattered like a bubble amidst this turmoil and vanished without a trace.

The Holy Merchant Lord stood frozen, completely stunned.

The Dao of Eternity could not possibly be so easily destroyed by him. His strength was far from reaching that level. Therefore, there was only one answer.

The skeleton he had just destroyed was not [Eternity]!

The true Eternal Immortal Skeleton had disappeared at some unknown time!

Almost instantaneously, the Holy Merchant Lord linked this to the sudden disappearance of the Immortal Ship's gatekeeper, Wu Xin, not long ago.

Eternity had been hidden within the Immortal Ship for millions of years without incident. Now, coinciding with Wu Xin's disappearance...

"Aaaaaahhhhh!"

The Holy Merchant Lord's eyes turned scarlet with extreme rage. Countless familiar faces flashed through his mind. The thought that he himself had destroyed the entire Immortal Ship and its billions of inhabitants nearly crushed his consciousness with unimaginable guilt and self-reproach.

"Wu Xin, I will kill you! I will kill you!"

"Kill, kill, kill!"

Within mere breaths, the Holy Merchant Lord, once a figure of great strategy and ambition, descended into madness. His mind was consumed by a single thought: to kill Wu Xin and exact revenge.

But Wu Xin had long since been suppressed by Li Fan within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

No matter what methods the Holy Merchant Lord employed, he could not find Wu Xin's trace.

Thus, he descended into even more impotent rage, wanting to destroy everything before him.

Disoriented, he left the original star system of the Merchant Immortal Ship and headed towards the Suo Xing Sea.

The massive shockwave caused by the destruction of the Merchant Immortal Ship had also attracted the attention of cultivators within the Suo Xing Sea.

The two parties encountered each other, and a senseless battle ensued.

The Holy Merchant Lord, devoid of reason, attacked indiscriminately. After catching the cultivators of the Suo Xing Sea off guard and suffering heavy losses, their tempers flared, and they united, vowing to kill this madman.

"That's why I say, never place too much importance on external things. My entire family perished in the battle between Kou Hong and Daoist Xuan Zi back then, yet I merely laughed it off. If I had been consumed by grief and despair at that time, would I be where I am today?" Li Fan commented from afar, watching the unfolding drama with an air of detachment.

Although the Holy Merchant Lord had gone mad, his knowledge of the various possibilities within the Mountains and Seas was still of immense value. Li Fan naturally would not let him off so easily.

"Let them fight until both sides are wounded. Then, I will deal with them together."

Neither the Holy Merchant Lord nor the Suo Xing Sea were forces to be easily defeated or suppressed.

Li Fan temporarily withdrew his gaze and looked towards the original location of the Merchant Immortal Ship.

After the intense explosion, the entire star system had turned into a dead zone, seemingly devoid of any remaining existence.

But Li Fan knew that Loquat and Bai Qian, the two Heaven-Stealing Cats, had not escaped.

They were still hiding in this area.

"Come out." Li Fan revealed his hidden form and spoke faintly to the empty star system.

The two Heaven-Stealing Cats showed no reaction.

Li Fan chuckled disdainfully. They were actually playing hide-and-seek with him...

With a grab of his hands, the entire star system before him was severed and transformed into a square cage.

As the Myriad Phenomena Dao Net rapidly contracted, Li Fan took this cage, along with the Cat Treasures within, back to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

He left behind a wisp of his divine sense to monitor the situation in the Suo Xing Sea, ready to intervene at any moment.

As if sensing the environment within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, which was starkly different from the ordinary star systems, the two hiding Heaven-Stealing Cats immediately emerged upon arrival.

"This method of hiding..." Li Fan's eyes flashed.

The bodies of the Heaven-Stealing Cats seemed to completely dissolve, merging with their surroundings, becoming a part of the Great Dao of heaven and earth, thereby achieving perfect concealment.

Even though Li Fan knew they were hiding there, he could not discern them.

However, this camouflage by the Cat Treasures was clearly not applicable to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, hence the exposed flaw upon entering this place.

"But this does not mean they cannot hide within this realm. It only means they need some time to adapt..."

Li Fan observed the two Heaven-Stealing Cats before him, one orange and one black and white, noticing that their bodies were undergoing changes corresponding to the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm's environment at an incredibly terrifying speed.

This adaptability was something Li Fan had only witnessed in the newly born Ink Slaughter.

"Loquat's rate of change is even faster than Bai Qian's."

"These are the so-called Seven Prototypes of Heaven-Stealing."

The two Heaven-Stealing Cats huddled together, warily observing Li Fan from a distance.

As their bodies began to slowly integrate into the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, even Li Fan, the Father and Mother of Profound Yellow, felt these two cats becoming more pleasing to the eye. If Li Fan felt this way, let alone the Profound Yellow Heavenly Dao.

The invisible hostility towards external invaders that permeated heaven and earth inexplicably dissipated.

The two Heaven-Stealing Cats thus easily transitioned from being outsiders to being favored by heaven and earth.

This was clearly the effect brought about by the self-evolution of the Cat Treasures.

"If the Heavenly Physician had possessed such means back then, there would have been no need for him to reincarnate as the Heavenly Demon." Li Fan marveled at the unbelievable nature of the Cat Treasures' transformation, observing every subtle change.

Only as the Father and Mother of Profound Yellow did he truly understand how incredible this transformation was.

When they were in the Suo Xing Sea, due to being in a lower-realm star system, the power of the two Heaven-Stealing Cats was merely at the level of Nameless True Immortals. But now...

As if a cultivator ascending to the Immortal Realm, the Heaven-Stealing Cats rapidly transformed. The aura emanating from their bodies surpassed that of ordinary Nameless True Immortals.

And this upward trend showed no signs of stopping, as if they were ascending further towards the realm of transcendence!

"Rather than saying they advanced to this level in such a short time, it's more accurate to say that the level set for Heaven-Stealing Cats when they were created was at this standard. They are now merely returning to their original state."

"Being entrusted with important tasks by the Tai Wei Holy Emperor and dispatched to other possibilities, it is not surprising that they possess the power of transcendence. After all, the definition of transcendence is the ability to traverse Mountains and Seas and travel freely to other possibilities."

"However, this is only in terms of realm. The Heaven-Stealing Cats' method of traversal is more like a clever shortcut. Compared to transcendent cultivators, their actual combat power is undoubtedly far inferior."

While the Heaven-Stealing Cats were adapting to the environment and integrating into the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, Li Fan was also using the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm to perceive these two Heaven-Stealing Cats.

Just as he had seen through the true nature of the Merchant Immortal Ship's Eternal Immortal Skeleton, as his understanding of the Cat Treasures' essence deepened, the images of the orange and black and white Cat Treasures before him also began to change.

Cat fur receded, cat skin dissolved, cat bones vanished.

Their core essence was revealed to be two plants!

Or rather, they were medicinal herbs!

This corresponded to their names:

One was Loquat, the other was Bai Qian!

*Boom!* The images of the two medicinal herbs instantly exploded, and Li Fan felt a slight dizziness in his head.

After a moment, he faintly glimpsed a towering figure.

Its form was imposing, but its face could not be seen. It held up Loquat and Bai Qian, or perhaps other medicinal herbs.

Upon closer inspection.

And the medicinal herbs that had passed through its hands were all instantly reborn, gaining all kinds of divine effects that were previously unattainable.

Before the figure, countless medicinal herbs were scattered.

Among them, seven were particularly radiant.

"The Seven Prototypes of Heaven-Stealing, they are the Seven Divine Medicines of Heaven-Stealing..." Realizing this, Li Fan suddenly understood.

Since their essence was that of medicinal herbs, the greatest efficacy of the Cat Treasures naturally related to medicine.

The functions of imitating living beings and replicating items were merely basic abilities bestowed upon the Cat Treasures after their creation.

Chapter 1579: Tai Yi Transforms into Ink Slaughter

The true divine efficacy of the Heaven-Stealing Cats corresponded to their names.

Perceiving Heaven as Humanity Sees.

The medicinal effects of past medicinal herbs on the human body transformed into the corresponding effects on Heaven when embodied by the Heaven-Stealing Cats.

The cycle of life and death for all things, like the ebb and flow of the world's breath. Bai Qian governs life and death, rectifying the natural order.

In the Primordial Era, there was the Great Saint Jing Fen, who regulated the dissipation and annihilation of the Dao, ensuring the eternal existence of the Immortal Realm. The Tai Wei Holy Dynasty, with just a dose of [Bai Qian], could achieve nearly half the efficacy of Great Saint Jing Fen.

The Great Dao ascended, without beginning or end. Loquat, intercepts the Dao of Life and nurtures all things. In the Profound Yellow Realm, there was a tree named Ruo Mu, which governed the life force of all realms. However, Ruo Mu's life force originated from the Profound Yellow Realm itself. As the Profound Yellow Realm flourished, Ruo Mu naturally prospered without worry. But if the Profound Yellow Realm weakened, Ruo Mu would also wither and fade. Yet, [Loquat]'s life force was intercepted from the Dao itself. It leaped beyond the limitations of a single possibility, and wherever the Dao flowed, Loquat could intercept the Dao and bring forth new life.

A dose of [Loquat] could ensure a world's life force, unyielding for ten thousand generations!

...

Li Fan was greatly shaken by the efficacy of the Heaven-Stealing Divine Medicines and couldn't help but look at the other medicinal herbs.

The majestic figure standing before countless medicinal herbs was undoubtedly the Tai Wei Holy Emperor. As if sensing Li Fan's prying gaze, His form subtly shifted, and His gaze met Li Fan's.

Time seemed to freeze at this moment, entering a state of stillness.

Perhaps it was due to Li Fan's habitual [Illusion is True] divine protection, or perhaps [Returning to Truth] had fallen into slumber, and the power of the Dao of Longevity had been expelled from Li Fan's body.

In any case, the Tai Wei Holy Emperor did not detect Li Fan's peculiarity from this fleeting eye contact.

However, He did not sever Li Fan's line of sight.

Instead, He seemed to smile slightly, and with a grand gesture, generously allowed Li Fan to look to his heart's content.

The scene before Li Fan's eyes suddenly magnified countless times.

Countless Heaven-Stealing Divine Medicines, densely packed like continuous dark clouds, covered the entire field of vision.

Not only ordinary medicinal herbs, but even the Seven Divine Medicines of Heaven-Stealing that Li Fan had seen shining brightly before, were present in countless numbers, impossible to count!

Only then did Li Fan realize.

What he was seeing was clearly vast expanses of medicinal gardens! Each type of Heaven-Stealing Divine Medicine was planted by the Tai Wei Holy Emperor in its corresponding medicinal garden. Endless and magnificent!

It was through these endless divine medicines grown in the medicinal gardens that the Tai Wei Holy Emperor had created and established the Tai Wei Holy Dynasty that spanned across Mountains and Seas.

And the reason He displayed His secrets so generously when Li Fan peeked was precisely due to His imperial demeanor!

"This is not some Tai Wei Holy Emperor; he is simply the Green Emperor!"

Li Fan's heart nearly became lost in this boundless ocean of divine medicines. He discovered that his inner being was subtly showing signs of being swayed by the Tai Wei Holy Emperor's demeanor.

He quickly and actively withdrew his gaze.

After a long while, his emotions finally began to calm down.

"I never expected the Tai Wei Holy Emperor to have become so powerful. Merely for a moment of my peeking through the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm at just one of His countless medicinal herbs, He could simultaneously sense my situation."

"He knew that I had suppressed and imprisoned the two Heaven-Stealing Cats. But..."

"The Heaven-Stealing Divine Medicines are inexhaustible in the Tai Wei Holy Dynasty..."

The gap between powerhouses like the Tai Wei Holy Emperor became visually apparent. Li Fan inevitably felt a faint sense of defeat.

He even harbored thoughts of "surrendering."

At Li Fan's current realm, his heart was like a clear mirror; the origins of all thoughts were completely under his control. Li Fan naturally knew that these were the Tai Wei Holy Emperor's methods of intimidation and one of the reasons He deliberately revealed the [Holy Emperor's.”. “Medicinal Garden.”

"If it were an ordinary person, after just one glance, they would likely be utterly subdued by the Holy Emperor's might and voluntarily seek refuge with the Tai Wei."

"Even transcendent cultivators would probably be unable to escape such influence."

"Fortunately..."

A faint cold glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes. He quickly crushed and removed all aberrant thoughts from his mind, restoring his normal composure.

"Although the Tai Wei Holy Emperor is powerful, He has not yet reached the level of being equivalent to the Mountains and Seas. I have even abandoned the Dao of Longevity, which is comparable to the Mountains and Seas. How could I be intimidated and bewitched by you?"

With a cold snort, although he was not Tai Wei Holy Emperor's match, it did not prevent Li Fan from using the Holy Emperor's medicinal herbs to his advantage.

Having understood the background of the Heaven-Stealing Cats, Li Fan acted without reservation.

"Ink Slaughter!"

Black ominous clouds rolled in, surrounding the two Heaven-Stealing Cats.

As if sensing the imminent fatal crisis, the fur of the two Heaven-Stealing Cats stood on end, and they let out low growls. As the Ink Slaughter ominous clouds continued to approach and they discovered they could not resist its erosion,

After a moment of hesitation, the two Heaven-Stealing Cats finally made a decision.

With high-pitched cries, the two Heaven-Stealing Cats transformed into black and white and orange-yellow balls of light respectively.

The two balls of light drew closer to each other, hesitated briefly, and then quickly merged.

The black and white radiance integrated into the orange-yellow,

This did not dilute the orange-yellow color but instead made it even more dazzling.

"This is using medicine to supplement medicine, advancing Heaven-Stealing further!"

Li Fan, well-versed in medicinal properties, saw the transformation of the two Heaven-Stealing Cats and, after a short while, understood the reason.

Concurrently, the Loquat, after consuming Bai Qian, transformed again.

Within its orange-yellow fur appeared some black and white stripes. Its overall physique had also grown significantly larger.

It no longer resembled a cat but rather a newborn tiger!

Facing the tide-like assault of the Ink Slaughter ominous clouds, Loquat remained undaunted. With a soft roar, it unleashed a large amount of vital yellow light from its body, which acted like a dike, temporarily holding back the Ink Slaughter's encroachment.

Seeing Ink Slaughter falter, Li Fan was not alarmed but delighted.

"This is the power of crossing the Mountains and Seas by carrying the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation! Using medicine to supplement medicine, this Heaven-Stealing Cat, Loquat, has truly reached the realm of transcendence."

With the protection of its orange-yellow light, Loquat charged through the Ink Slaughter ominous clouds, showing signs of breaking free. Even though the Ink Slaughter ominous clouds churned like boiling water, they could not subdue it for the time being.

If not for the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm acting as support, Loquat would likely have already broken through the Ink Slaughter's blockade.

"While it cannot completely negate the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation, it possesses enough self-strength to find a safe haven before being consumed by Dao Annihilation."

"This is the fundamental principle of crossing the Mountains and Seas."

"The stronger one's power, the longer one can remain within Dao Annihilation, and the more at ease one can traverse the Mountains and Seas."

Li Fan recalled the Tongtian Great Dao displayed by Zi Yi earlier, and the fragment of a transcendent remnant fished up from the Guangwu Star Sea. Comparing and contrasting these with the scene before him, all the past incomprehensible mysteries now erupted in his mind like an explosion.

Facing Loquat, which possessed the realm of transcendence, Ink Slaughter was at a disadvantage. However, its ability to devour and analyze had not failed.

Vast amounts of knowledge regarding the Heaven-Stealing Divine Medicines and the medicinal properties of Loquat gradually surfaced in Li Fan's mind through Ink Slaughter.

"This can be considered Loquat's Dao of Transcendence."

"Unfortunately, this principle only applies to medicine and cannot be used for humans."

Despite its severe limitations, Li Fan did not reject it. He still regarded it as a rare insight and pondered it carefully.

"Although I cannot use Loquat's medicinal properties for myself, I can still integrate them into my Profound Yellow Immortal Realm through the Dao Refining Medicine King Scripture!"

"Since it is a medicinal herb, no matter how extraordinary, it is still a medicinal herb in the end. Returning to its rightful path is your destiny!"

Loquat, indeed one of the Seven Prototypes of Heaven-Stealing, possessed seemingly boundless intercepted life force. In the Ink Slaughter ominous clouds, it charged left and right for a full thirty-three days, yet showed no signs of weakening.

And Li Fan, through Ink Slaughter's absorption, had grasped Loquat's medicinal properties with about seventy to eighty percent accuracy.

At this point, with a cold finger directed at the orange cat within the ominous clouds, Ink Slaughter churned and instantly transformed into a colossal alchemy furnace!

Although its form had merely changed, the limiting effect on Loquat seemed to increase hundreds of times.

The immensely vital and swift-moving orange cat seemed to have its limbs bound. It could no longer move with its previous speed, only laboriously attempting to continue its charge.

Moreover, the surrounding protective orange-yellow light, as if blown by a strong wind, was no longer steady but swayed precariously, appearing on the verge of disintegration.

The Ink Slaughter Alchemy Furnace stood in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, beyond the heavens.

Li Fan personally oversaw the process. First, he invited "Uncle-Master" Eternity to cast a glance.

Then, with swift strokes, he wrote a phantom scripture and cast it into the Ink Slaughter Alchemy Furnace.

This scripture was the "[Primordial Beginning of Mountains and Seas]," obtained from Shan Hua in his previous life!

The Primordial Beginning of Mountains and Seas was born from the observation of Great Sage Lian Shan and Great Sage Gui Hai's process of creating the Immortal Realm from nothing by Sage Monarch Tai Yi. It contained the principles of Mountains and Seas as well as the Dao of Tai Yi.

The foundation of Ink Slaughter was precisely [Tai Yi] and [Eternity].

At this moment, both foundations were further strengthened under Li Fan's direction. Although it was not equivalent to the two great powerhouses acting personally, it was akin to a degree of "borrowing" their power.

Like adding fuel to a raging fire, the power of the newly born Ink Slaughter instantly expanded several times over.

The alchemy furnace solidified, appearing lifelike, as if transformed from nothingness into reality.

The ink-colored light surged, instantly engulfing the last trace of orange-yellow within the furnace.

Before the strengthened version of the newly born Ink Slaughter, even Loquat, at the transcendent realm, could only face suppression.

The newly born Ink Slaughter, born within the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm,

But now, having received the augmentation of the two primordial powers, it had already subtly transcended the limitations of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

Fortunately, Li Fan acted as the moderator and helm, able to withdraw the support of Eternity and Tai Yi at any time. Otherwise, after devouring Loquat, it might have further advanced and even consumed the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm along with it.

"It's akin to seeking a tiger's skin, but it must be done."

Ink Slaughter was not Li Fan's only trump card. With a thought, numerous constantly moving black dots appeared throughout the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, converging towards the heavens beyond.

Compared to the ominous clouds of Ink Slaughter, visible to all, these black dots could only be seen by Li Fan.

They were the Dao-One Worms!

"Ink Slaughter is, after all, a creation of others. It has many uncontrollable factors and poses too great a hidden danger."

"Whereas the Dao-One Worms are something I created from nothing, entirely through my own efforts."

"Loquat can devour Bai Qian, the Dao-One can devour Mountains and Seas. Ink Slaughter resembles the annihilation of Dao..."

"The Dao-One can transform into Ink Slaughter!"

As Ink Slaughter transformed into an alchemy furnace, focusing on refining the Heaven-Stealing Cat within,

Unbeknownst to it, the Dao-One Worms on the exterior of the alchemy furnace were also attempting to erode it!

Li Fan could see that the erosion and assimilation progress of the Dao-One Worms was extremely slow.

But their actions were not in vain.

Li Fan had secretly shared his understanding of the Dao of Ink Slaughter with these Dao-One Worms, slightly accelerating their assimilation speed.

However, the perception of Ink Slaughter by the Dao-One Worms was likely different from Li Fan's.

Therefore, Li Fan's assistance yielded only a minimal effect.

"But it doesn't matter. Since it has begun, it's already half a success."

Li Fan continued to stimulate Ink Slaughter, causing it to focus its attention on dealing with Loquat, creating greater space for the Dao-One Worms to erode.

And Ink Slaughter did not disappoint.

Black smoke billowed, completely devouring the last remnants of orange-yellow within the alchemy furnace.

Next, as Li Fan had predicted.

After completely devouring Loquat, Ink Slaughter did not stop.

The alchemy furnace expanded, seeking to encompass the entire celestial realm beyond the heavens of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm.

Fortunately, Li Fan had prepared for this and promptly withdrew the support of both Eternity and Tai Yi.

Having lost the support of the two primordial powers, the expanding Ink Slaughter instantly returned to its original form.

The anomaly also ceased.

Under Li Fan's gaze, it finally calmed down.

The ominous clouds churned, spitting out wisps of orange-yellow light.

It transformed into an orange-yellow pill, almost golden in color.

"This is Loquat's intercepted Dao of life force..."

A hint of variegation appeared in Li Fan's eyes.

He toyed with it in his hand for a long time, but Li Fan did not swallow it. Instead, he crushed this pill of Intercepted Loquat's Life Force. He then scattered it across the Profound Yellow world and heavens.

That day, a brilliant sunset glow, illuminating half the sky, appeared in the heavens of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm. It did not dissipate until the moon had climbed to its zenith.

From then on, the evolution of life force in the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm quietly changed.

The beings in the heavens and earth remained unaware of this, as currently, neither the quantity nor the quality of life force had shown any significant change.

"Once the calamity descends, the difference will become apparent."

"Even if I were to bring about a world-ending catastrophe, annihilating all life except those whose names are recorded on the Investiture of the Gods, under normal circumstances, without my deliberate manipulation, it would take approximately three years for the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm to recover from utter desolation and become vibrant once more."

In Li Fan's eyes, the terrifying recovery scene of the Profound Yellow Immortal Realm, enhanced by the Intercepted Dao of Life force, appeared.

"Intercepting Dao, Intercepting Dao..."

"Where does this intercepted life force originate from?"

Li Fan looked beyond the Profound Yellow Realm.

In his perception, there was indeed a faint, ethereal life force, like celestial music, drifting from afar.

But it arrived without any precursor, its source completely untraceable.

After observing for a long time, Li Fan finally had a dawning understanding.

"It is not stolen from other possibilities. Rather, it originates from the Dao itself."

"From the flow of [Dao's Birth and Death]..."

"As long as the Great Dao continues to exist and has not entered a state of寂灭 (jì miè - extinction), this Loquat's Intercepted Dao of Life can continuously obtain life force."

"This is the essence of the Heaven-Stealing Divine Medicines..."

Recalling the [Tai Wei Holy Emperor's Medicinal Garden] filled with countless other medicinal herbs, Li Fan's understanding of the power of the arrogant Tai Wei Holy Emperor deepened once more.
